paQca skanDaka viBAzA / namaH budDAya / paQca skanDAH ityAdi prakaraNa AramBaH / sa ca Darma sva sAmAnya lakzaNa vyutpatti arTam / nanu ca yoga AcAra BUmi Adizu SAstrezu Darma lakzaNam nirDAritam eva iti punar tat nirDAraNAya yatna vEyarTyam
# # / / rgya gar skad du / / panytsa skan dha pra ka ra na bi bh'a shyam / / bod skad du / / phung-po #  lnga'i rab tu byed-pa #  bye-brag #  tu bshad-pa #  / / bam po dang-po #  / / sangs-rgyas #  dang sbyang-chub-sems-dpa' #  thams-cad-la #  phyag 'tshal lo / / phung-po #  lnga zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rab tu byed-pa #  ci'i-phyir #  rtsom zhe na / / chos-thams-cad #  kyi rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  rtogs-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro / / rnal-'byor-spyod-pa'i-sa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bstan-bcos #  dag las chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  dpyad zin na yang de dpyad-pa #  don-med-pa # r mi 'gyur ram /
na vEyarTyam udGawita jQa vineya arTi tvAt
# don-med-pa # r mi 'gyur te / / mgo smos-pa # s go-ba #  gdul-ba # 'i don-gyi-phyir #  ro /
udGawita jQAH hi diS mAtreNa tad samBavinoviSezAt niravaSezAn avabodDum samarTAH iti saFkzepa uktim eva bahu manyante na vistara uktim
# mgo smos-pa # s go-ba #  ni phyogs tsam gyis de rtogs-pa # 'i khyad-par #  rnams ma-lus-par #  khong-du-chud-pa # r nus-pa # s mdor bshad-pa #  nyid la dga'i / / rgya-cher #  bshad-pa #  la ni ma yin no /
atas ca saFkzipta ruci sattva anugrahAya idam prakaraNam ArabDam iti
# de'i-phyir #  mdor-bsdus-pa #  'dod-pa # 'i sems-can #  la phan-gdags-pa # 'i phyir rab tu byed-pa #  'di brtsams so /
aTavA gRhasTAnAm bahu kRtya vyApRta tvAt vistara granTezu aBiyoga asamBavaH / manasikAra aBiyuktAnAm ca pravrajitAnAm api vistara granTa aBiyogaH vikzepAya eva iti uBayezAm api Darma lakzaNa vyutpatti arTam iha prakaraNe Darma lakzaNam samAsena uktam iti na asti tad AramBa vEyarTyam
# yang-na #  khyim-na-gnas-pa #  rnams bya-ba-mang-po #  la zhugs-pa # 'i phyir le'u grangs rgya-cher #  byas-pa #  rnams la mngon-pa # r brtson mi srid-pa #  dang rab-tu-byung-ba #  yid-la-byed-pa #  la mngon-pa # r brtson pa rnams kyang le'u grangs rgya-cher #  byas-pa #  la mngon-pa # r brtson par byas-na #  g-yeng bar 'gyur-ba # s / / de-gnyi-ga # s chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  rtogs-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir rab tu byed-pa #  'dir chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  mdor bshad de /
aTavA saFkzepeNa Darma lakzaNa vyutpannAH ayatnena Darma lakzaNa vistara pratipatti samarTAH Bavizyanti iti atas yoga AcAra BUmi AdInAm vistara granTAnAm praveSa BUtam idam AcAryeNa prakaraNam kRtam iti
# de-ltar-na #  de brtsams pa don-med-pa # r mi 'gyur ro / / yang-na #  chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  mdor-bsdus-pa #  rtogs-nas #  chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  rgyas-pa #  yang bsgrim mi-dgos-pa # r rtogs nus-pa # r 'gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  slob-dpon #  gyis rnal-'byor-spyod-pa'i-sa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i le'u grangs rgya-cher #  byas-pa #  rnams la 'jug-par-'gyur-ba # 'i rgyur rab tu byed-pa #  'di mdzad do /
kim punar Darma lakzaNa vyutpattyA vinA na siDyati yatra AcAryaH Darma lakzaNa nirdeSam prati Adriyate
# chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  rtogs-pa #  med-pa # r ci-zhig #  mi 'grub na / / 'di-ltar #  slob-dpon #  gyis chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  bstan-pa # r gus-par #  mdzad ce na /
citta ekAgra tA saFkaTya niScayezu ca praSna vyAkaraNa kOSalam
# sems rtse gcig-tu #  bya-ba #  dang 'bel-ba'i-gtam #  brtsal bar nges ba rnams la dris-pa #  lung bstan-pa #  la mkhas-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir te /
taTA hiDarma lakzaNa kRta paricayasya sandeha aBAvAt yaTezwam Alambane cittam ekAgrIBavati na anyaTA
# 'di-ltar #  chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  la byang-ba # r byas-na #  the-tshom-med-pa # 'i phyir ji-ltar-'dod-pa #  bzhin-du #  dmigs-pa #  la sems rtse gcig-tu #  'gyur gyi gzhan-du #  ni ma yin no /
Darma lakzaNa pravicayAt ca prajQA prakarza gamanAt vESAradyam pratilaBate
# chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa # s kyang shes-rab #  mchog-tu-'gyur-ba # s mi-'jigs-pa #  thob ste /
viSAradaH ca sa aFkaTya niScayezu sarva praSna tad vyAkaraNa nirdeSa samarTaH Bavati na anyaTA
# 'jigs-pa-med-pa #  ni 'bel-ba'i-gtam #  rnam-par-nges-pa #  rnams la dris-pa #  de thams-cad-du #  lung ston nus-pa # r 'gyur gyi gzhan-du #  ni ma yin no /
paQca skanDAH iti nyUna atirikta pratizeDena saFKyA avaDAraNam
# phung-po #  lnga zhes-bya-ba #  ni mang nyung dgag-pa # 'i phyir grangs nges-par #  gzung-ba # 'o /
nirviSezaNa skanDa Sabda prayogAt sa Asrava anAsrava skanDa upAdAnam / paQca eva skanDAH na nyUnAH aDikA vA
# phung-po # 'i sgra bye-brag-med-par #  smos-pa # s zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa # 'i phung-po #  gzung-ba # r bya'o / / phung-po #  ni lnga kho-na #  ste /
Atma AtmIya grAha vastu pradarSana arTam prAyeNa hi bAlAn aMvijQAnaH eva Atma grAhaH Sezezu rUpa Adizu AtmIya grAhaH
# bdag dang bdag-gi # r 'dzin-pa # 'i gzhi rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / mang-ba # 'am nyung-ba #  ma yin te / / byis-pa #  dag ni phal-cher #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid la ni bdag tu 'dzin / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  ltag ma rnams la ni bdag-gi # r 'dzin te /
taTA hi bAhya ADyAtmikasya rUpasya karaNa tvena karma tvena vA AtmanA sambanDaH iti rUpa skanDaH AtmIya grAhaH
# 'di-ltar #  phyi dang nang gi gzugs ni byed-pa #  dang las su bya-ba # r bdag dang 'brel to snyam-du #  gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  la bdag-gi # r 'dzin to /
SuBa aSuBa anAMkarmaNAm vedanA vipAkaH tAm ca AtmA saMvedayate iti vedanA skanDaH AtmIya grAhaH
# las dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  rnams kyi rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  de bdag-gis #  yang-dag-par-myong-ba # r byed do snyam-du #  tshor-ba'i-phung-po #  la bdag-gi # r 'dzin te /
tatra SuBAnAm karmaNAm suKaH anuBavaH vipAkaH / aSuBAnAm karmaNAm duHKaH / uBayezAm aduHKa asuKaH
# de-la #  bde-ba-myong-ba #  ni las dge-ba #  rnams kyi rnam-par-smin-pa # 'o / / sdug-bsngal #  ni las mi-dge-ba #  rnams kyi'o / / sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa #  ni gnyi-ga # 'i'o /
atra cAlaya vijQAna samprayukta upekzA eva parama arTataH karma vipAkaH SuBa aSuBa karma vipAka tvAt AlayavijQAnasya
# 'dir ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  dar mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  btang-snyoms #  nyid yang-dag-par #  na las kyi rnam-par-smin-pa #  ste / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid las dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
suKa duHKayoH tu vipAka ja tvAt vipAka upacAraH
# bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  gnyis ni rnam-par-smin-pa #  las 'byung-ba # 'i phyir rnam-par-smin-pa # r gdags-pa # 'o /
dRzwa Sruta mata vijQAtezu arTezu AtmanaH saQjQAt vAreNa saMvyavahAraH pravartate iti saQjQA skanDaH AtmIya grAhaH
# mthong-ba #  dang thos-pa #  dang bye-brag-phyed-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i don rnams la bdag-tu-'du-shes #  pa'i sgo nas tha-snyad-'dogs-pa # r byed do snyam-du #  'du-shes-kyi-phung-po #  la bdag-gi # r 'dzin to /
kuSala akuSala Adizu saMskArEH Atma aBimatasya cittasya preraNAt saMskAra skanDaH AtmIya grAhaH iti paQca eva skanDaH
# bdag tu 'dod-pa # 'i sems ni 'du-byed-rnams #  kyis dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la 'jug-par-byed-pa # s 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po #  la bdag-gi # r 'dzin te / / phung-po #  ni lnga kho-na # 'o /
aTa kasmAt skanDAnAm iyam eva AnupUrvI
# 'o na phung-po #  rnams kyi go-rims #  'di ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
yaTA OdArikataH
# ji-ltar #  rags-pa # 'i rim bzhin te /
tatra sarva OdArikam rUpam sa pratiGa tvAt paQca vijQAna kAya ASraya tvAt zaX vijQAna vizaya tvAt / atas AdO= OdArikam rUpam uktam
# de-la #  gzugs ni thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs lnga'i gnas-su-gyur-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  drug gi yul yin pa'i phyir thams-cad #  pas ches rags te / / de-bas-na #  gzugs dang-por #  brjod do /
triByaH pracAra OdArika tayA OdArikatara AvedanA / taTA hi adeSa sTAm api saQjQA Adi vat pracArOdArika tvAt deSa paricCedena tAm eva vyapadiSanti na saQjQA AdIn haste mevedanA Sirasi me vedanA iti / atas rUpa anantaram uktA / dvAByAm OdArikatara Asan jQAna nimitta udgrahaNa Atmaka tvena sulakzya tvAt / vijQAnAt saMskArAH OdArika tarAH saMskaraNa lakzaNa tvena suKa avaboDa tvAt
# tshor-ba #  ni gsum po dag-pa # s rgyu-ba #  rags-pa # 'i phyir ches rags-pa #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  'du-shes #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  yul na mi gnas kyang nga'i lag-pa # r tshor ro / / nga'i klad par tshor ro zhes rgyu-ba #  rags-pa # 'i phyir yul yongs su chad-pa # s de-nyid-la #  brjod kyi / / 'du-shes #  la-sogs-pa #  la ni ma yin te / / de'i-phyir #  gzugs kyi 'og-tu #  brjod do / / 'du-shes #  ni mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  rtogs-par-sla-ba # 'i phyir gnyis po dag-pa # s ches rags so / / 'du-byed #  ni 'du-byed #  pa'i mtshan-nyid #  yin-pas #  khong-du-chud-pa # r sla-ba # 'i phyir / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  las ches rags so /
sarva SUkzma tvAt vijQAnam sarva paScAt uktam
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni thams-cad #  pas phra-ba # 'i phyir kun gyi tha-ma # r brjod do /
rUpa skanDaH iti samAna aDikaraNaH vA syAt zazWI tatpuruzovA
# de-la #  gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  gzhi mthun-pa # 'am / / de'i skyes-bu # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba # r 'gyur grang na /
na Bavet samAna aDikaraNaH adravya tvAt skanDasya
# gzhi mthun-pa #  ni ma yin te / / phung-po #  rdzas su med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yasmAt skanDa SabdaH rASi paryAya vacanaH tasmAt rASi vat prajQapti santaH skanDAH iti / tatas ca sAmAnADikaraNya aBAvaH / zazWI tatpuruzaH api na prApnoti
# gang-gi-phyir #  phung-po # 'i sgra spungs ba'i rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa # 'i tshig yin pa de'i-phyir #  phung-po #  rnams ni spungs pa bzhin-du #  btags-pa'i-yod-pa #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  na gzhi mthun-pa #  nyid med do /
sambanDaH hi dvayoH para sparavi Binna rUpayoH Bavati devadattam Atula vat
# de'i skyes-bu # 'i phyir-yang #  mi 'gyur te / / phan tshun tha-dad-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yod-na #  'brel-par-'gyur-ba # s / / lha sbyin gyi zhang po zhes-bya-ba #  lta-bu #  yin la /
sambanDa arTA ca iyam zazWI rUpa skanDayoH iti rUpAt anyaH eva skanDaH prApnoti / na ca etat izyate prajQapti sataHsu upAdAnAt tattvAni tvena avAcya tvAt
# gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i kyi [?] 'di ni 'brel-ba # 'i don yang yin-pas #  gzugs las phung-po #  gzhan nyid-du #  'gyur na / / btags-pa'i-yod-pa #  ni rang-gi #  rten las de nyid dang gzhan-du #  brjod du me dpa'i phyir de'ang mi 'dod do /
na eza dozaH
# 'di ni nyes-pa #  med de /
aBede api zazWI dRzwA tattva anyatvena avAcye ca pratimAyAH SarIram rUpasya prAgaBAvaH iti / na hi pratimA SarIrAt anyA
# tha-dad-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  dang de nyid dang gzhan-du #  brjod-du-med-pa #  la yang drug-pa #  mthong-ste #  / / gzugs su byas-pa # 'i lus dang gzugs kyi snga na med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / gzugs su byas-pa #  ni lus-las #  gzhan ma yin no /
prAc aBAvaH api nirUpa AKya tvAt tattva anyatvena avAcyaH svarUpa nibanDana tvAt tattva anyatvayoH / anya vastu grahaNa apekzam niHsvaBAva tvAt yatra grahaNam eCe ape AKBh / BiDAnam ca tat upAdAna vyatirikta svaBAva aBAvAt prajQapti sat / taTA eva ca skanDa arTaH iti prajQaptisan= ucyate / atas ca tattvAni tvena avAcya tve api sva upAdAnAt zazWI na viruDyate / tatas ca zazWI tatpuruzaH eva atra / rUpam katamat
# snga na med-pa #  yang dngos-po-med-pa # 'i phyir gzugs las de nyid dang gzhan-du #  brjod du med de de nyid dang gzhan yin pa gnyis kyi rgyu ni rang-gi #  ngo bo yin pa'i phyir ro / / rang-bzhin #  med-pa # 'i phyir dngos-po #  gzhan 'dzin-pa #  la ltos-pa #  ste / / gang zhig gang-la #  'dzin-pa #  dang brjod-pa-'jug-pa #  de ni rten dang tha-dad-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  med-pa # s btags-pa'i-yod-pa #  nyid de / / don-du #  ma-yin-pa # s btags-pa'i-yod-pa #  nyid ces bya'o / / de'i-phyir #  rang-gi #  rten las de nyid dang gzhan-du #  brjod du med kyang kyir 'gal-ba #  med do / / de'i-phyir #  'dir de'i skyes-bu # 'i kyi [?] nyid do / / gzugs gang zhe na /
catvAri mahABUta anicatvAri ca mahABUtAni upAdAya / nanu caskanDAnAm prakRta tvAt katamat rUpam iti asambadDaH praSnaH / na asambadDaH skanDAnAm niHsvaBAva tvAt tad svaBAva vyapadeSena nirDAraNam aSakyam kim tarhita dupAdAna nirDAraNena eva iti / atas rUpam katamat iti praSnaH na rUpa skanDaH iti / rUpasya kArya kAraNa BAvena Beda pradarSana arTam Aha catvAri mahABUtAni ityAdi
# 'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  dag dang 'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  dag rgyur-byas-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la phung-po #  smos-pa # 'i skabs su gzugs gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba # 'i 'dri-ba #  'di 'brel-ba #  med do zhe na / / 'brel-ba #  med-pa #  ma yin te / / phung-po #  rnams ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # 'i phyir / / de'i-ngo-bo-nyid #  brjod-pa # s ni dmigs kyis dbye-ba # r mi nus kyi / / 'on-kyang #  de'i rten dmigs kyis phye-ba # s 'gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  gzugs gang zhe na zhes 'dri'i / / gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  ni ma yin no / / rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # 'i dngos-po # r gzugs kyi dbye-ba #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir /
taTA hi sarva ANi mahABUtAni sarvasya upAdAya rUpasya kAraNam sarvam ca upAdAya rUpam sarvezAm mahABUtAnAm kAryam
# 'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  dag dang zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  smos te / / 'di-ltar #  'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  po thams-cad #  ni rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  thams-cad-kyi #  rgyu yin la / / rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  thams-cad #  ni 'byung-ba-chen-po #  thams-cad-kyi #  'bras-bu #  yin no /
mahat tvaMBUtAnAm sarva upAdAya rUpa ASraya tvena OdArika tvAt
# 'byung-ba #  rnams kyi chen-po #  ni rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  thams-cad-kyi #  rten yin-pas #  gtos che-ba # 'i phyir ro /
aTavA sarva rUpa Adi samudAyezu kAWinya Adi sadBAvAt mahA sanniveSa tvAt mahat tvam / BUta tvam tu punar ezAm viviDa upAdAya rUpa nirvRttO tEH tEH prakArEH Bavanti iti BUtAni
# yang-na #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  'dus-pa #  thams-cad-la #  srab la-sogs-pa #  yod-pa # 'i phyir ram / / gnas-pa #  tha gru che-ba # 'i phyir chen-po # 'o / / de-dag #  gi 'byung-ba #  ni rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  sna-tshogs #  'grub-pa #  na de-dang-de-dag #  gi rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba # s 'byung-ba #  rnams so /
sarva sattva karma ADipatya AdO saMsAre na kadAcid na aBUvan= iti BUtAni / na ca anyezAm BUta tva prasaFgaH mahiza Adi vat rUXi Sabda tvAt
# yang-na #  sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi las kyi dbang gis thog-ma-med-pa # 'i 'khor-ba #  nas nam yang ma-byung-ba #  ma-myong-ba # s 'byung-ba #  rnams so / / gzhan dag la yang-'byung-ba #  nyid thal-ba # r mi 'gyur te / / ming grags-pa #  yin-pas #  sa steng nyal la-sogs-pa #  bzhin no /
tAni punar catvAri eva na nyUna aDikAni asAmarTya apArTaka tva prasaFgAt / BOtikasya hi avaDRti sneha pAcana vyUhana mAtrakam eva kAryam
# de-dag #  ni bzhi kho-na #  ste / / mi-nus-pa #  dang mi-dgos-pa #  nyid-du #  thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir mang-ba # 'am nyung-ba #  ma yin no / / 'byung-ba # 'i bya-ba #  ni brten-pa #  dang sdud-pa #  dang smin-par-byed-pa #  dang skyod-pa # r byed-pa #  tsam du zad de /
tasya ca etAvadBiH eva parisamApta tvAt anyasya ca karaNIyasya aBAvAt catvAri eva BUtAni
# de-dag-nyid #  kyis de'i bya-ba #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  dang bya-ba #  gzhan med-pa # 'i phyir-'byung-ba #  dag ni bzhi kho-na # 'o /
nanu caDRti Adi vat avakASam api upAdAya rUpasya kAryam
# brten-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  nam-mkha' # i bya-ba #  ni go 'byed-pa #  yin te /
tad cAkASena kriyate iti pRTivI Adi vat AkASasya api mahABUta tva prasaFgaH / na etat evam / kim kAraNam / na hi AkASam nAma kiQcid asti anyatra sa pratiGa rUpa aBAva mAtrAt / avakASam ca sa pratiGam eva vastu svasmin= avakASa ISa pratiGasya eva tasmAt apasaram dadAti na AkASam / na hitasmAt pradeSAt rUpa vat AkASam apasRtam ititasya avakASa dAnam na yujyate
# de-yang #  nam mkhas byed-pa # s na sa la sogs ba bzhin-du #  nam-mkha' #  yang-'byung-ba #  chen-po #  nyid-du #  thal-ba # r 'gyur ram / / de ni de-ltar #  mi 'gyur te / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na / / thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i gzugs-med-pa #  tsam ma-gtogs-par #  nam-mkha' #  zhes-bya-ba #  ci-yang #  med do / / thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo-bo-nyid #  de nas song-ste #  / / rang-gi #  go der thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  la go 'byed-pa # r zad kyi nam mkhas ni ma yin te / / gzugs ltar nam-mkha' #  phyogs de nas song-ba #  med-pa # s de go 'byed ces byar mi rung ngo /
sa pratiGam ca rUpam sva deSe anya rUpasya utpattim pratibaDnAti / na AkASam / tasmAt yatra yasya ayasmin sati avakASa aBAvaH yasmin= asati tasya tatra avakASaH iti tena eva tasmAt sTAnAt apasaratA tasya avakASaH dattaH na AkASena iti
# thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i gzugs ni rang-gi #  phyogs su gzugs gzhan 'byung-ba # 'i bgegs byed kyi nam-mkha' #  ni ma yin no / / de-lta-bas-na #  'dir gang na gang yod-na #  ni go phye-ba #  med la / / de na de med na ni der go phye-ba #  yod-pa # s de'i-phyir #  de nyid gnas de nas song-nas #  go phye-ba #  yin gyi nam-mkha' #  ni ma yin no /
tasmAt na AkASam pRTivI Adi vat mahABUtam
# de-bas-na #  nam-mkha' #  ni sa la-sogs-pa #  ltar 'byung-ba-chen-po #  ma yin no /
catvAri ca mahABUtAni upAdAya iti catvAri ca mahABUta anirUpam catvAri ca mahABUtAni upAdAya rUpam iti uBaya trApi caSabdaH sambaDyate
# 'byung-ba #  bzhi dag rgyur-byas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  dag gi gzugs dang 'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  dag rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra gnyi-ga # r yang sbyar ro /
paQca prakAreNa janana niSraya pratizWA upastamBa bRMhaNAnAm hetu BAvena BOtikaMBUtAni upAdattaH iti upAdAya SabdaH hetu arTaH tat yaTA inDanam upAdAya agniH Bavati iti tena nimittena iti gamyate
# skyed-pa #  dang brten-pa #  dang gnas-pa #  dang ston-pa #  dang 'phel-bar-byed-pa #  rnams kyi rgyu'i-dngos-po #  rnam-pa-lnga # s 'byung-ba #  rnams kyis 'byung-ba-las-gyur-pa #  gzung ngo / / rgyur-byas-pa # 'i sgra ni rgyu'i don te / / dper-na #  shing rgyur byas-na # s me byung ngo zhes byas-na #  rgyu-de-las-byung-ba # r shes-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
tatra janana hetu tvam tEH vinA tat anutpatteH / niSraya hetu tvaMBUta vikAre tad pratizWita upAdAya rUpa vikRti anuviDAnAt
# de-la #  skyed-pa # 'i rgyu ni de-dag #  de med-pa # r de mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / rten gyi rgyu ni 'byung-ba #  'gyur na de-la #  brten-pa #  rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  kyang rjes su 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sTAna hetu tvam BUtAnAm sadRSa santAna utpattO BOtikasya api sadRSa santAnAn ucCeda hetutvAt / upastamBa hetu tvaMta dvaSena anucCedAt
# gnas-pa # 'i rgyu ni 'byung-ba #  rnams rgyun 'dra-bar-'byung-ba #  ni 'byung-ba-las-gyur-pa #  yang 'dra-ba # 'i rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rton-pa # 'i rgyu ni de'i stobs kyis rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
bRMhaNa hetu tvam BUta vRdDa Ota tad ASrita upAdAya rUpa vRdDeH
# 'phel-bar-byed-pa # 'i rgyu ni 'byung-ba #  'phel na de-la #  rten-pa #  rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  kyang 'phel-ba # 'i phyir ro /
pRTivI DAtuH ityAdi vyAkaraNa MsvalakzaNa upAdAya rUpa DAraNAt pRTivI AdayaH eva DAtavaH / pRTivI Adi grahaNaMcakzuH DAtu AdiByaH parasparataH ca vyavacCeda arTam
# sa'i-khams #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  bshad-pa #  la rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  dang rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  'dzin-pa # 'i phyir sa la-sogs-pa #  nyid khams so / / sa la-sogs-pa #  smos-pa #  ni phan tshun dang mig gi khams la-sogs-pa #  dag las rnam-par-dbye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
DAtu grahaNam lOkikeByaH pRTivI AdiByaH viSezaNa arTam
# khams smos-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-pa # 'i sa la-sogs-pa #  las bye-brag-tu-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
pRTivI AdayaH hi lOkika SAstra prasidDi Bedena dviDA izyante
# sal sogs-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-pa #  dang bstan-bcos #  las grags-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-gnyis #  su 'gyur te /
tatra lOkikAH varNa saMsTAna Atmaka tvAt sAMvyavahArikAH iti na DAtavaH
# de-la #  'jig-rten-pa # 'i ni kha-dog #  dang dbyibs kyi bdag-nyid #  du kun du tha-snyad-'dogs-pa #  yin pa'i phyir khams ma yin no /
SAstrIyAH punar KakKawa Adi svaBAva sadBAvAt pAramArTika tvAt DAtavaH
# bstan-bcos #  las byung-ba #  rnams la ni sra-ba # l sogs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yod-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  dag-pa # r na khams yin no /
BUta vat pRTivI DAtu AdayaH api svarUpa nirdeSam antareNa na vijQAyante iti punar api praSnaH pRTivI DAtuH katamEti Adi / KakKawa tvam / iti BAva pratyayaH atra sva arTikaH / KakKawam eva KakKawa tvam na hi atra BAva antaram asti / KakKawaH KaraH krUraH iti paryAyAH
# 'byung-ba #  bzhin-du #  sa'i-khams #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo-bo-nyid #  kyang ma bshad-pa # r mi-shes-pa # s yang sa'i-khams #  gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dris so / / sra pa nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  la nyid ni sra-ba #  kho-na #  sra-ba-nyid #  de 'di-la #  don gzhan ni med do / / sra-ba #  dang mkhrang ba dang 'thas pa ni rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa # 'o /
snehaH ap DAtuH iti saMSraya Atmaka tvAt drava / tvAt vA snehaH
# chu'i-khams #  gang zhe na / / gsher-ba #  nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'du-ba # r byed-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin pa dang rlan-par-byed-pa # s gsher-ba # 'o /
dAhaka tvAt UzmA tejaH DAtuH / vAyu / DAtuH laGu samudIraNa tvam iti / laGu tvam vAyuDAtuH iti ucyamAna OpAdAya rUpasya api BUta tvam prasajyeta / IraNam vAyuDAtuH iti ucyamAne karma eva asya nirdizwam syAt na svarUpam iti atas asya laGu tvAt upAdAya rUpAt karmaNaH cavyavacCeda arTam evam uktam laGu samudIraNa tvam vAyuDAtuH iti / samudIraNa tvam punar BAva srotasaH nErantaryeNa deSa antara utpatti hetutvam / ete ca pRTivI ap tejaH vAyu DAtO= OpAdAya rUpeNa iva parasparataH api avinirBAga vartinaH iti kaTaMvijQAyate / karmataH
# me'i-khams #  ni sreg-par-byed-pa #  yin-pas #  tsha-ba # 'o / / rlung-gi-khams #  ni yang zhing g-yo-ba #  nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  la yang-ba-nyid #  rlung-gi-khams #  yin no zhes brjod na ni rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  la yang-'byung-ba #  nyid thal-ba # r 'gyur ro / / rlung-gi-khams #  g-yo-ba # 'o zhes brjod-pa #  ni de'i las nyid bstan-pa # r 'gyur gyi / / rang-gi #  ngo bo ni ma yin te / / de'i-phyir #  de-yang #  ba rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  dang las rnam-pa # r gcod-pa # 'i phyir rlung-gi-khams #  ni yang zhing g-yo-ba # 'o zhes de-skad #  ces brjod do / / g-yo-ba #  ni dngos-po # 'i rgyun yul gzhan-du #  'byung-bar-byed-pa # 'i rgyu yin no / / sa dang chu-dang-me #  dang rlung-gi-khams #  de-dag #  dang rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  phan tshun tha dad du mi-'jug-pa # r ci mngon zhe na /
atas eva ca ezAm DRti saFgraha pakti vyUhanAni kAritram uktam / kaTam nAma ezAm svarUpataH anupalaByamAnAnAm api upala Adizu kAryataH sattvam anumIyeta iti
# las las mngon te / / de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  gi las ni brten-pa #  dang sdud-pa #  dang smin-par-byed-pa #  dang skyod-pa # r byed-pa #  brjod do / / de-dag #  gi rang-gi #  ngo bo mi dmigs kyang rdo la-sogs-pa #  la yod-pa # r las las ji-ltar #  rjes su dpag ce na /
taTA hi upala Adizu saFgraha pakti vyUhaneByaH jala anala anila anAMpRTivI DAtunA sAhacaryam vijQAyate
# 'di-ltar #  rdo la-sogs-pa #  la 'dus-pa #  dang skam pa dang g-yo-ba #  rnams yod-pa #  las chu-dang-me #  dang rlung rnams sa'i-khams #  dang lhan-cig #  'jug-pa # r mngon no /
apsu kAzWa sanDAraNa patra dala pAka uzNa tA avacalaneByaH kziti anala anilAnAm abDAtunA / agnO jvAlA AdInAm sTErya sampiNXita preraNeByaH kzitija lAnilAnAm tejasA
# tshul yang shing 'degs-pa #  dang padma'i 'dab ma rgyas-pa #  dang chu g-yo-ba #  rnams yod-pa #  las sa dang me dang rlung rnams chu'i-khams #  dang lhan-cig #  rgyu-ba # r mngon no / / me la yang me-lce # s 'degs-pa #  dang 'dus-pa #  dang g-yo-ba #  rnams yod-pa #  las sa dang chu dang rlung rnams me-dang-lha # n cig 'jug-pa # r mngon no /
vAyO sanDAraNa vastra Adi SozaNa avisAreByaH kziti udaka analAnAm vAyuDAtunA sAhacaryaMvijQAyate
# rlung la yang 'degs-pa #  dang mi 'gyes-pa #  dang gos la sogs bskam bar byed-pa #  yod-pa #  las / / sa dang chu-dang-me #  rnams rlung-gi-khams #  dang lhan-cig #  'jug-pa # r mngon no /
karmaNaH svaBAvasya ca kaH viSezaH
# las dang rang-gi #  ngo bo gnyis bye-brag #  ci yod ce na /
kriyamANa apekzam karma vyavasTApyate / taTA hi ADArya dravya sanDAraNA apekzayA pRTivI DAtoH DRtiH karma ucyate
# bya-ba #  la ltos nas las rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / 'di-ltar #  brten-par-bya-ba # 'i rdzas brten-pa #  la ltos nas sa'i-khams #  kyi las ni brten-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / bsdu-bar-bya-ba #  la ltos nas chu'i las ni sdud-pa # 'o / / smin-pa # r bya-ba #  la ltos nas /
saFgrAhya apekzayA apAMsaFgrahaH karma pAka apekzayA tejasaH paktiH karma varDanIya kalala aFkura apekzayA vyUhanam vAyoH karma / vyUhanam punar vRdDiH prasarpaNam ca
# me'i las ni smin-par-byed-pa # 'o / / 'phel-ba # r bya-ba #  nur-nur-po #  dang myu-gu #  la-sogs-pa #  la ltos nas rlung gi las ni skyod-pa # r byed-pa # 'o / / bskyod-pa #  ni 'phel-bar-byed-pa #  dang 'gyur-ba # r byed-pa # 'o /
svaBAvaH tusarva anya BAva nirapekzaH iti ayam karmaNaH svaBAvasya caviSezaH / uktAni BUtAni sAmAnya viSeza saQjQABiH svaBAvataH ca
# ngo-bo-nyid #  ni dngos-po #  gzhan thams-cad-la #  mi ltos-pa #  ste / / 'di ni las dang ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi bye-brag #  go / / 'byung-ba #  rnams kyi spyi dang khyad-par #  gyi ming dang rang-bzhin #  bshad-zin #  to /
BUta anantara uddizwam upAdAya rUpam praBedataH svarUpataH ca na vijQAyate iti atas pRcCati upAdAya rUpam kataH
# 'byung-ba #  rnams kyi 'og-tu #  bstan-pa #  rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  dang rang-gi #  ngo bo mi shes te / / de'i-phyir #  rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  gang zhe na zhes dris te /

# rnam-pa #  ni du zhig rang-gi #  ngo bo ni ci 'dra zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / mig-gi-dbang-po # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo ci 'dra zhe na /
varNa vizayaH / rUpa prasAdA eti tad svaBAva AvizkaraNam / catvAri mahABUtAni upAdAya iti prakRta tvAt sambaDyate
# yul kha-dog #  gzugs-dang-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba # s rang-gi #  ngo bor ston te / / skabs yin-pas #  'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  dag rgyur-byas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro /
varNaH nIla pIta AdikaH catur prakAraH / varNa AlocanAt varNa nirBAsa asADAraNa kAraNa tvAt vA varNaH vizayaH asya iti varNa vizayaH / ayaMcA atra prasAda arTaH tat yaTA prasannaH AdarSe udaka pAtre vA Alimbam pratItya tad pratiBAsam pratibimbam utpadyate tadvat paQcasu rUpa prasAda Atmakezu cakzuH Adizu rUpa ganDa AdIn pratItya tad pratiBAsA vijQaptayaH utpadyante
# kha-dog #  ni sngon-po-dang-ser-po #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi # 'o / / kha-dog #  la lta-ba #  dang kha-dog #  tu snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i thun-mong-ma-yin-pa # 'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir kha-dog #  ni de'i yul yin-pas #  yul kha-dog #  ces bya'o / / 'di ni 'dir dang-ba # 'i don te / / dper-na #  gzugs la brten-nas #  de-ltar #  snang-ba'i-gzugs #  brnyan me long ngam / / snod kyi chu dang-ba # 'i nang-du #  'byung-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  gzugs dang sgra la-sogs-pa #  la brten-nas #  / / de-ltar #  snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  mig la-sogs-pa #  gzugs-dang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  lnga po dag las 'byung ngo /
atra cakzuH AdIn AMpara sparataH vizaya rUpa AtmakAt prasAdAt manastaH SradDAtaH ca vyavacCedaH kAryaH / rUpa prasAda Atmaka tva aviSezAt varNa vizaya tva aviSezAt ca varNa vizaya UrUpa prasAdaH iti ca ca / tatra varNa vizaya tvena Srotra AdiByaH vizaya prasAdAt ca vyavacCinatti
# 'dir ni mig la-sogs-pa #  phan tshun dang yul gzugs kyi bdag-nyid #  dang-ba #  dang yid dang dad-pa #  las rnam-par-dbye-ba # r bya ste / / gzugs-dang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  du bye-brag-med-pa #  dang yul kha-dog #  yin par bye-brag-med-pa # 'i phyir yul kha-dog #  gzugs-dang-ba # 'o zhes gnyis-ka #  brjod do / / de-la #  yul kha-dog #  ces bya-ba # s ni rna-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang yul gyi gzugs-dang-ba #  las rnam-pa # r 'byed de /
na hi Srotra AdayaH vizaya prasAdaH vA varNa vizayaH asti
# rna-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang yul ni dang-ba #  yin yang kha-dog #  yul ma yin no /
rUpa prasAda Atmaka tvena manastaH vyavacCinatti
# gzugs-dang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid-kyis #  ni yid las rnam-pa # r 'byed de /
tat hi sati api varNa vizaya tve na rUpa prasAda Atmakam / rUpa grahaNam SradDA AtmakAt prasAdAt vyavacCedakam / SradDA api hi prasAda AtmikA rUpa Adi vizayA ca iti atas rUpa grahaNam / varNa vizayaH prasAdaH cakzuH indriyam iti ucyamAne SradDAyAH api prasaFgaH iti atas rUpa grahaNaMkriyate iti SradDAyAH arUpa Atmaka tvAt / cakzuH AdIni hiindanti iti indriyANi / ISantaH iti arTaH ADipatyam asmin saFGAtekurvanti iti arTaH / atas ca ADipatya arTaH indriya arTaH indanti iti indriyANi / evam indrANi iti prApnoti / nipAtanAt indriyam iha Bavizyati / evam api DAtvarTaH vaktavyaH / sa ca na uktaH iti ayam parihAraH / vijQAna vat eva kRt syAt / tat yaTA vijAnAti iti vijQAnam iti prApte lyuXarTam anAdRtya vijQAnam uktaMtat vyatirikta vijQAtR saFgraha vyudAsa arTam evam iha api indriya vyatirikta liFga kalpanA vyudAsa arTam evam uktaMsyAt iti / yaTA eva hi cakzuH AdInAm vizayiNAm paraspara tovizaya Bedena BedaH uktaH cakzuH indriyam katamat / varNa vizayaH rUpa prasAdaH / Srotra indriyam katamat / Sabda vizayaH rUpa prasAdaH iti evamAdi evam rUpa AdInAm api vizayANAm cakzuH AdiBiH vizayiBiH Beda Ocyate / cakzuzaH eva vizayaH rUpam na Srotra AdInAm tad vizayANAm Sabda Adi tvena vyavasTAnAt / atra ca manasaH naviDiH na pratizeDaH aprakRta tvAt / evam ca rUpa AdIn AMpara sparataH BedaH uktaH Bavati cakzuzaH vizayaH rUpam eva na arUpam iti / evam api nIla pIta AdInAm paraspara vilakzaNAn aMcakzuH indriya vizayANAm rUpa tvena aBedaH uktaH Bavati iti / yadi cakzuH vizaya tvena rUpam viSezitam eva iti evam sati varNa saMsTAnam vijQaptiH ca iti kimarTam / rUpa praBeda sandarSana arTam
# de'i yul kha-dog #  yin yang gzugs-dang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  ni ma yin no / / gzugs smos-pa # s ni dad-pa #  dang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  las rnam-pa # r 'byed de / / dad-pa #  ni dang-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  kyang yin la yul kha-dog #  kyang yin te / / de'i-phyir #  gzugs smos so / / mig-gi-dbang-po #  ni dang-ba #  yul kha-dog #  go zhes brjod na dad-pa #  la yang thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba # s de'i-phyir #  gzugs smos te / / dad-pa #  ni gzugs kyi bdag-nyid #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir / / mig la-sogs-pa #  ni dbang-byed-pa # 'i phyir dbang-po #  rnams te / / tshogs-pa #  'di-la #  bdag-po #  byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / de-bas-na #  bdag-po # 'i don ni dbang-po # 'i don te / / ji-ltar #  mig la-sogs-pa #  yul can rnams phan tshun yul tha-dad-pa # s tha-dad-pa # r brjod de / / mig-gi-dbang-po #  gang zhe na / / yul kha-dog #  gzugs-dang-ba # 'o / / rna-ba # 'i dbang-po #  gang zhe na / / yul sgra gzugs-dang-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s tha-dad-pa # r brjod-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  yul rnams kyang mig la-sogs-pa #  yul can rnams tha-dad-pa # s tha-dad-pa # r brjod de / / gzugs ni mig nyid-kyi-yul #  yin te / / rna-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i ma yin te / / de-dag #  gi yul rnams ni sgra la-sogs-pa # r rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'dir yid ni skabs ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir sgrub-pa #  yang med / / dgag-pa #  yang med do / / de-ltar-na #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  phan tshun tha-dad-pa # r brjod-pa #  yin no / / mig gi yul ni gzugs nyid yin gyi / / gzugs ma-yin-pa #  ni ma yin te de-ltar-na #  mig-gi-dbang-po # 'i yul sngon-po-dang-ser-po #  la-sogs-pa #  phan tshun mi-'dra-ba #  rnams kyang gzugs su tha-dad-pa #  med-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no / / gal-te #  gzugs mig gi yul nyid kyis bye-brag #  tu byas-pa #  yin na kha-dog #  dang dbyibs dang rnam-par-rig-byed #  do zhes-bya-ba #  ci'i-phyir #  smos she na /

# ring-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ma smras sam /
tat etat eva na jQAyate / yatra dIrGa Adi budDayaH Bavanti tat dIrGa Adi saMsTAnam
# de nyid mi shes so zhe na gang-la #  ring-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i blo 'byung-ba #  de ring-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbyibs so /
evaMtarhi na varNa Adi vyatiriktam saMsTAnam vidyate / kim kAraNam
# de-ltar-na # 'o na kha-dog #  la-sogs-pa #  las gud-na #  dbyibs med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
yasmAt eka diFmuKa pravRtte BUyasi varNa Adi saFGAteH Ga budDiH Bavati alpIyasi hrasva budDiH caturdiSaMsame vRtta budDiH sarvatas same parimaNXala budDiH eka diFmuKe sAtabudDiH nAnA Adi FmuKe visAtabudDiH iti
# 'di-ltar #  kha-dog #  la-sogs-pa #  'dus-pa #  mang-po #  phyogs-gcig #  na gnas-pa #  la ring-po # 'i blo 'byung / / chung-ngu #  la ni thung du'i blo 'byung / / phyogs-bzhi # r mnyam-pa #  la ni lham-pa # 'i blo 'byung / / kun nas mnyam-pa #  la ni zlum-po # 'i blo 'byung / / dbus su phal-che-ba #  la ni mtho-ba # 'i blo 'byung / / nyung-ba #  la ni dma'-ba # 'i blo 'byung / / phyogs-gcig #  gi ngos la ni phya le ba'i blo 'byung / / phyogs tha-dad-pa # 'i ngos la ni phya le ba ma-yin-pa # 'i blo 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
kaTam punar etat gamyate varNa Adi samudAye dIrGa budDiH Bavati na punar arTa antara BUte saMsTAne iti / sparSana dvAreNa api dIrGa Adi budDi utpatteH naBa indriya antara vizayaH indriya antara dvAreNa budDiH utpadyate na eka indriya vEyarTya prasaFgAt / na eva tat indriya jQAnam kim tarhi anumAna jQAna mganDAt puzpa varNa jQAna vat
# kha-dog #  la-sogs-pa #  'dus-pa #  la ring-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i blo 'byung-ba # r zad kyi / / dbyibs don-gzhan-du-gyur-pa #  med-pa # r de ji-ltar #  shes she na / / reg-pa # 'i sgo nas kyang ring-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i blo 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / dbang-po #  gzhan gyi yul la gzhan gyi sgo nas blo 'byung du mi rung ste / / dbang-po #  du-ma #  don-med-pa # r thal-ba # r 'gyur ro / / de ni dbang-po # 'i shes-pa #  ma yin gyi / / rjes-su-dpag-pa # 'i shes-pa #  ste / / dri las me-tog #  gi kha-dog #  shes-pa #  bzhin no /
yaTA ganDaH puzpa varNa niyataH na tu evam sparSaH saMsTAnaH iti vizamaH ayam upanyAsaH
# dri me-tog #  gi kha-dog #  la nges-pa #  ltar reg-pa #  ni dbyibs la de-ltar #  ma yin te / / bzhag-pa #  'di ni mthun-pa #  ma yin no /
tasmAt uBaya indriya dvAreNa Gawa Adi vat dIrGa Adi saMsTAna pravRtteH na tat varNa AdiByaH arTa antaram iti
# de-lta-bas-na #  dbang-po #  gnyis kyi sgo nas bum-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  / / ring-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbyibs la shes-pa #  'jug-pa # 'i phyir de kha-dog #  la-sogs-pa #  las don gzhan ma yin no /
na ca niravayava tvAt paramANUnAm dIrGa Adi rUpeNa parasparataH BedaH yuktaH / tasmAt nanIla Adi paramANu vat dIrGa Adi paramANavaH santi iti atas casaMsTAna paramANu samudAyaH api dIrGa Adi saMsTAnam iti ayuktam dIrGa Adi saMsTAna paramANu aBAvAt
# rdul-phra-rab #  rnams ni cha-shas #  med-pa # 'i phyir ring-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i ngo bor nang phan tshun tha-dad-pa # r yang mi rigs so; / / de-lta-bas-na #  sngon-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rdul-phra-rab #  ltar ring-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rdul-phra-rab #  rnams yod-pa #  ma yin no / / de'i-phyir #  dbyibs kyi rdul-phra-rab #  rnams 'dus-pa #  la ring-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbyibs shes-bya # r yang mi rung ste / / dbyibs kyi rdul-phra-rab #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na ca saMsTAna Atmakam dravyam arvAk maDya para BAga samBavAt / na ca tezAm aBedaH yugapad pratyakza apratyakza tvAt / sambanDi BedAt catasya avaSyam Bedena Bavitavyam aBede vAta tsambanDInAm api aBinna tva prasaFgaH iti
# dbyibs ni rdzas gcig pa ma yin te / / tshu-rol #  dang dbus dang pha rol gyi cha yod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-dag #  tha-dad-pa #  med-pa #  ma yin te / / cig-car-du #  mngon-sum #  dang mngon-sum-du #  ma-gyur-pa #  dang 'brel-pa #  can tha-dad-pa # 'i phyir de-dag #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  tha-dad-pa # r 'gyur ro / / ci ste tha mi dad na yang de dang 'brel-pa #  can rnams kyang phyogs tha-dad-pa #  med-pa # r thal-ba # r 'gyur ro /
tasmAt na asti eva dravyataH saMsTAna mkim tarhi varNa Adizu eva taTA taTA avyavasTitezu dIrGa Adi prajQapyate
# de-lta-bas-na #  dbyibs ni rdzas-su-yod-pa #  ma yin te / / 'on-kyang #  kha-dog #  la-sogs-pa #  de-lta-de-ltar #  gnas-pa #  rnams la ring-po #  la-sogs-pa # r 'dogs so /
aTa vijQaptiH nAma kaH eza DarmaH
# 'o na rnam-par-rig-byed #  ces bya-ba # 'i chos 'di gang zhig yin /
tad Alambana citta jaMkAya mahABUta ASrayeNa utpannaMkAyasya saMsTAnaMsva samutTApaka citta vijQapanAt vijQaptiH iti ucyate
# de-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i sems las skye-ba #  lus kyi 'byung-ba-chen-po #  la brten-nas-'byung-ba #  lus-kyi-dbyibs #  te / / rang kun-nas-slong-ba # 'i sems rnam-par-rig-pa # r byed-pa # s rnam-par-rig-byed #  ces bya-ba # 'o /
atra ca tad AlambanAt eva yat jAyate cittAt saMsTAnam tat eva vijQaptiH na punar anya AlambanAt
# 'dir ni de-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i sems las skyes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de nyid rnam-par-rig-byed #  de / / gzhan la dmigs-pa #  las ni ma yin no /
evam ca punar bruvataH ozWa Adi saMsTAnam atadAt Alambana citta jatvAn nirAkRtam pUrva praNiDAna jaMca
# de-ltar-na #  smra-ba # 'i mchu la-sogs-pa # 'i dbyibs ni de-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i sems las skyes-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  dang smon-lam #  las skyes-pa #  yang bkag-pa #  yin no /
tat hi praNiDAna cittAt anya vipAka hetu citta jam api iti na vijQaptiH izyate
# de ni smon-lam #  gyi sems dang gzhan rnam-par-smin-pa'i-rgyu # 'i sems las kyang skyes-pa #  yin te / / de'i-phyir #  rnam-par-rig-byed #  du mi 'dod do /
tatra yadi vijQapti AKyaMsaMsTAnam ekam kAya AKya samudAya vyApi tat ekatvAt vyApi tvAt ca pratyavayavam gRhyateH asmin= tad BAvAt / na vA tat ekam BAgataH vyavasTAnAt
# de-la #  gal-te #  rnam-par-rig-byed #  ces bya-ba # 'i dbyibs gcig-pu # s lus kyi spyir khyab-pa #  yin na ni gcig yin pa'i phyir dang khyab-pa #  yin pa'i phyir te thams-cad #  na yod-pa # s yan-lag #  so-so #  la yang gzung-ba # r 'gyur ro / / yang-na #  cha-shas #  su rnam-par-gnas-pa # 'i phyir gcig-tu #  mi rung ngo /
daSa ca AyatanAni paramANu saQcitAni iti sidDAntaH bADyeta
# skye-mched #  bcu ni rdul-phra-rab #  bsags-pa # 'o zhes 'byung-ba # 'i grub-pa # 'i mtha' la'ang gnod-pa # r 'gyur ro /
tasmAt na asti saMsTAnam nAma dravya antaram / atas ca na saMsTAnaMvijQaptiH
# de-lta-bas-na #  dbyibs zhes-bya-ba #  rdzas gzhan-du #  gyur-pa #  med de / / de'i-phyir #  dbyibs ni rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma yin no /
yadi kAyAt arTa antaram na saMsTAnam kA tarhi sA
# gal-te #  lus-las #  don-gzhan-du-gyur-pa # 'i dbyibs rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma yin na'o na de gang yin /
tad Alambana cetanA nimittA kAya santateH nErantaryeNa deSa antara utpattiH / cetanA nimitta tvam tu kAya santateH deSa antara utpatti hetu vAyu DAtu nirvartanAt
# de-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i sems-pa # 'i rgyu mtshan can lus kyi rgyud rgyun ma chad-pa # r yul gzhan-du #  'byung-ba # 'i rgyu yin no / / sems-pa #  rgyur-gyur-pa #  ni lus kyi rgyud yul gzhan-du #  'byung-ba # 'i rgyu rlung-gi-khams #  bsgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sA ca kAyasya deSa antara utpattiH sva nimittam cetanAm vijQApayati iti vijQaptiH / tasyAH tu kuSala akuSala tvam na svABAvikam
# lus yul gzhan-du #  'byung-ba #  de ni rang-gi #  rgyu sems-pa #  rnam-par-rig-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-rig-byed #  do / / de ni dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ma yin te /
kim tarhi kuSala akuSala cetanA pravartita tvAt kuSala akuSala tvam upacaryata Ikzaye kAraNa upacArAt
# 'on-kyang #  de dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-sems #  pas skyed-pa # 'i phyir 'bras-bu #  la rgyu btags te / / dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  nyid-du #  'dogs so; /
atra tu rUpa vyavasTAnam svaBAvataH sanniveSataH kriyA lakzaNataH ca
# 'dir gzugs rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  dang gnas-pa #  dang byed-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyis rnam-pa # r gzhag ste /
svaBAvataH nIla AdInAm caturNAm varNAnAm tad svaBAva tvAt
# ngo-bo-nyid #  ni sngon-po #  la-sogs-pa #  kha-dog #  bzhi-po #  rnams te / / de'i ngo bo yin pa'i phyir ro /
sanniveSataH daSa anAMdIra Adi saMsTAnAnAm taTA taTA varNa sanniveSAt
# gnas-pa #  ni ring-po #  la-sogs-pa #  dbyibs rnam-pa-brgyad #  de / / kha-dog #  de-lta-de-ltar #  gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kriyA lakzaNataH vijQapteH kAya praspanda Atmaka tvAt
# byed-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni rnam-par-rig-byed #  de / / lus g-yo-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
dravya sat vizaya tvAt cakzuH AdInAm saMsTAnasya vijQapteH caprajQapti sattvAt na cakzuzaH vizaya tvam asti
# rdzas-su-yod-pa #  ni mig la-sogs-pa # 'i yul yin la / / dbyibs dang rnam-par-rig-byed #  ni / / btags-pa #  yod-pa # 'i phyir mig gi yul-ma-yin-pa #  snyam na ji-ltar #  gzugs mig gi yul zhes brjod /
kaTaMca kzu vizaya tvena rUpam ucyate / atra hi loka anuvRttyA varNaH saMsTAna viSezaNaH cakzuH vizayatvena vivakzitaH
# 'dir 'jig-rten-dang-mthun-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir dbyibs kyi khyad-par #  dang bcas-pa # 'i kha-dog #  mig gi yul du 'dod de /
taTA hi saMsTAna viSizwaH cakzuzA varNaH gRhyate na kevalaMsaMsTAnam varNaH vAdIra Adi saMsTAna viSizwa varNa nirBAsa cakzuH vijQAna utpatteH
# 'di-ltar #  dbyibs kyi khyad-par-can #  du gyur-pa # 'i kha-dog #  la mig gis 'dzin gyi / / dbyibs sa ma kha-dog #  gcig-pu #  la ni ma yin te / / ring-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbyibs kyi khyad-par #  du gyur-pa # 'i kha-dog #  tu snang-ba # 'i mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  skye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
atas varNaH saMsTAnam cacakzuzaH vizayaH iti loke prasidDiH
# de'i-phyir #  kha-dog #  dang dbyibs ni mig gi yul lo zhes 'jig-rten #  na grags so /
taTA deSa antara utpatti viSizwa kAya santati grahaNAt vijQaptiH api cakzuzaH vizayaH iti prasidDiH
# de-bzhin-du #  yul gzhan-du #  'byung-ba # s khyad-par #  du gyur-pa # 'i lus kyi rgyud 'dzin-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-rig-byed #  kyang mig gi yul zhes grags so /
paramArTataH tu saMsTAna vat na varNaH api cakzuzaH vizayaH saMsTAna vat paramANoH anizpanna tvAt vijQAnasya bAhya arTa avizaya tvAt
# don-dam-pa # r ni dbyibs bzhin-du #  kha-dog #  kyang mig gi yul ma yin te / / dbyibs bzhin-du #  rdul-phra-rab #  ma-grub-pa # 'i phyir dang phyi-rol #  gyi don rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i yul-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tasmAt loka SAstra prasidDiH eva atra AcAryeNa anuvRttA iti gamyate
# de-lta-bas-na #  slob-dpon #  gyis 'dir 'jig-rten #  dang bstan-bcos #  las grags-pa #  dang mthun-par #  mdzad-pa # r shes so /
rUpa anantaram uddizwa tvAt tad nirdeSa anantaram eva Sabdasya nirdeSaH nyAyyaH iti praSnaH SabdaH katamaH
# gzugs kyi 'og-tu #  sgra bstan-pa # 'i phyir de bshad ma-thag-tu #  sgra bshad-pa # r rigs-pas #  na /
Srotrasya vizayaH iti Srotrasya eva vizaya Una anyasya indriyasya iti
# sgra gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang rna-ba # 'i yul de zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / rna-ba #  nyid-kyi-yul #  yin gyi / / dbang-po #  gzhan gyi ma yin no /
evam hi upAdAya rUpa tva aviSeze api anya indriya vizayeByaH rUpa AdiByaH asya viSezaH uktaH Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  yin par khyad-par #  med kyang dbang-po #  gzhan gyi yul gzugs la-sogs-pa #  las de bye-brag #  tu bstan-pa #  yin no /
Srotra vizayaH ca SabdaH eva iti paraspara BinnAnA aMSa bda BedAnAm Sabda Ayatana tvena aBedaH uktaH Bavati
# rna-ba # 'i yul ni sgra nyid do zhes-bya-ba # s kyang sgra'i bye-brag #  phan tshun tha-dad-pa #  rnams sgra'i skye-mched #  nyid-du #  bye-brag-med-par #  bstan-pa #  yin no /
tad Beda pradarSana arTam Aha upAtta anupAtta uBaya mahABUta hetuka eti
# de'i dbye-ba #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / zin-pa #  dang ma-zin-pa #  dang gnyi-ga # 'i ste / / 'byung-ba-chen-po # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tatra upAttAni Atma BAva paryApannAni citta cEttEH aDizWAna BAvena upagRhItAni / viparyayAt anupAttAni
# de-la #  zin-pa # 'i ni lus su gtogs-pa #  rnams te / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyis gnas-kyi-dngos-po # r gzung-ba #  rnams so / / bzlog-pa #  ni mi zin-pa #  rnams so /
tAni hetuH asya iti upAtta anupAtta uBaya mahABUta hetukaH
# de-dag #  ni 'di'i rgyu yin-pas #  'byung-ba-chen-po #  zin-pa #  dang ma-zin-pa #  dang gnyi-ga # 'i ste / / 'byung-ba-chen-po # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'o /
tatra upAtta mahABUta hetukaH hasta tvAt Sabda iti evamAdi
# de-la #  zin-pa # 'i 'byung-ba-chen-po # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba #  ni lag-pa #  dang ngag gi sgra la-sogs-pa # 'o /
anupAtta mahABUta hetukaH vAyu vanaspati nadI Sabda Eti evamAdi / uBaya mahABUta hetukaH mRdaFga SabdA eti evamAdi ganDaH katamaH / GrANasya eva vizayaH
# mi zin-pa # 'i 'byung-ba-chen-po # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba #  ni rlung dang nags-tshal #  dang 'bab-chu # 'i sgra la-sogs-pa # 'o / / gnyi-ga # 'i 'byung-ba-chen-po # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba #  ni rnga'i sgra la-sogs-pa # 'o / / dri gang zhe na /
GrANa vizayaH ca ganDaH eva iti pUrvavat
# sna nyid-kyi-yul #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang sna'i yul ni dri nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  yang snga-ma-bzhin #  no /
sama ganDaH tutena indriya mahABUtAnAm na anugrahaH na upaGAtaH / sa caganDaH sahajaH sAMyogikaH pAriNAmikaH ca
# dri-mnyam-pa #  ni dbang-po # 'i 'byung-ba-chen-po #  rnams la phan-pa #  yang mi 'dogs gnod-pa #  yang mi-byed-pa # 'o / / dri ni lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  dang sbyar-ba #  las byung-ba #  dang gyur-pa #  las byung-ba # 'o /
tatra sahajaH candana kuFkuma AdInAm
# de-la #  lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  ni tsandan dang gur gum la-sogs-pa # 'o /
sAMyogikaH DUpa varti ganDa AdInAm / pAriNAmikaH pakva Amra Pala AdInAm rasaH katamaH ityAdi
# sbyar-ba #  las byung-ba #  ni bdug spos ri lu la-sogs-pa # 'i dri'o / / gyur-pa #  las byung-ba #  ni aa mra smin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams kyi'o /
jihvAyAH eva vizayaH jihvA vizayaH ca rasaH eva iti pUrvad vistareNa vaktavyam
# ro gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  lce nyid-kyi-yul #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang lce'i yul ni ro nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  yang / / snga-ma-bzhin-du #  rgya-cher #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
prakRti BedAt zaX BedaH uktaH
# rang-bzhin-gyis #  tha-dad-pa # 'i phyir tha-dad-pa #  drug smos te /
anyaH tu BedaH tad saMyoga BedAt anantaH ca Bavati
# gzhan-du #  dbye-na #  ni de'i sbyar-ba #  tha-dad-pa #  mtha' yas bar 'gyur ro /
atra hi upAdAya rUpa nirdeSaH prastutaH rasa anantaraMtusprazwavya eka deSe upAdAya rUpatvena uddizwaH iti atorasa nirdeSa anantaram sprazwavya eka deSa nirdidikzayA praSnaH sprazwavya eka deSaH katamEti / sprazwavyam hi / dviviDam BUtAni tAni ca upAdAya rUpam / BUtAni ca pUrvam uddizwA ninirdizwAni ca
# 'dir ni rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  bstan-pa # 'i skabs yin-pas #  ro'i 'og-tu #  rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  reg-bya # 'i phyogs-gcig #  bstan-pa # s de'i-phyir #  ro bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  reg-bya # 'i phyogs-gcig #  bshad-pa # r 'dod nas / / reg-bya # 'i phyogs-gcig #  gang zhe na zhes dris so / / reg-bya #  ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / 'byung-ba #  rnams dang de-dag #  rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  so / / 'byung-ba #  rnams ni sngar bstan-pa-dang-bshad-pa #  rnams so /
iha tu upAdAya rUpam prakRtam iti / atas sprazwavya eka deSaH katamaH upAdAya rUpam iti sambaDyate
# 'dir ni rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  [?] kyi skabs yin-pas #  de'i-phyir #  reg-bya # 'i phyogs-gcig #  gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgur byas-pa # 'i gzugs zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro /
kAyasya vizayaH iti kAyasya eva vizayaH na cakzuH AdInAm iti rUpa Sabda AdiByaH asya BedaH uktaH Bavati
# lus kyi yul te zhes-bya-ba #  ni lus nyid-kyi-yul #  yin gyi / / mig la-sogs-pa # 'i ni ma yin no / / de-ltar-na #  gzugs dang sgra la-sogs-pa #  las de tha-dad-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
kAyasya ca vizayaH sparSaH eva iti BUta BOtikayoH paraspara vilakzaNa tve api sparSa tvena aBedaH uktaH Bavati
# lus nyid-kyi-yul #  reg-bya #  nyid ces bya-ba # s ni 'byung-ba #  dang 'byung-ba-las-gyur-pa #  gnyis phan tshun mi 'dra yang reg-bya #  nyid-du #  bye-brag-med-par #  bstan-pa #  yin no /
kAyasya vizayaH iti BUtAnAm api kAya vizaya tvAt upAdAya rUpa prasaFgaH iti atas Aha mahABUtAni sTApayitvA iti
# lus kyi yul te zhes-bya-ba #  'byung-ba #  rnams kyang lus kyi yul yin-pas #  rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  su thal-ba # r 'gyur ro / / de'i-phyir #  'byung-ba-chen-po #  rnams gzhag ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
sprazwavya eka deSa pradarSana arTam Aha SlakzNa tvaMkarka Sata tvam ityAdi
# reg-bya # 'i phyogs-gcig #  rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / 'jam-pa-nyid #  dang rtsub pa nyid dang zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  smos so /
nanu ca kAya indriyeNa spRSyate iti SlakzNa tva Adi sprazwavyam ucyate
# lus kyi dbang-po # r reg-par-bya-ba # s na 'jam-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  reg-bya #  zhes brjod na ni /
yat ca yena spRSyate niyogAt tat api tat spRSati iti kAya indriye api sparSa tva prasaFgaH / na hikenacid kiQcid spRSyate
# gang-gis #  gang-la #  reg-pa #  des kyang de-la #  reg-pa # r gdon-mi-za-bar #  'gyur-ba # s lus kyi dbang-po #  yang reg khyar thal-ba # r mi 'gyur ram /
sarva AtmanA sparSane hi sarva piNxaNa apara mANu pramANAH syuH
# gang-gis #  kyang ci la yang reg-pa #  med de / / bdag-nyid #  thams-cad-kyi # s reg na ni gong bu thams-cad #  rdul-phra-rab #  kyi tshad tsam du 'gyur ro /
pradeSena sparSane paramANUna aMsa avayava tva prasaFgAt paramANu tvam avahIyate
# phyogs kyis reg na ni rdul-phra-rab #  rnams cha-shas #  dang bcas-pa # r thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba # s rdul-phra-rab #  nyid nyams-pa # r 'gyur ro /
tasmAt vizaya indriyayoH nirantara utpattO yat ASritam vijQAnam vizayam upalaBate tena sa vizayaH spRzwaH iti upacaryate na tuvizayeNa vijQAna ASrayaH
# de-bas-na #  yul dang dbang-po #  gnyis bar-ma #  chad-pa # r skye-ba #  na gang-la #  brten-nas #  rnam-par-shes-pa # s yul dmigs-pa #  des yul la reg ces bya-ba # r gdags kyi yul gyis rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i gnas-pa #  ni ma yin no /
atas eva kAya indriyeNa BUtAni eva spRSyante iti upacaryate na tad ASritAH rUpa AdayaH kAya vijQAnena agrahaNAt
# de'i-phyir #  lus kyi dbang-po # s 'byung-ba #  rnams nyid la reg go zhes gdags kyi / / de-dag #  la gnas-pa # 'i gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la ni ma yin te /
puzpa Adizu ca varNa Adi upaGAtaH tad ASraya upaGAtAt na kAya saMsparSAt iti
# lus kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # s mi-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / me-tog #  la-sogs-pa # 'i kha-dog #  la-sogs-pa #  la gnod-pa #  ni de'i-gnas #  la gnod-pa # 'i phyir gyi lus-kyis #  reg-pa # 'i phyir ni ma yin no /
varNa Adi ASrayasya apikAyena aspRzwasya kaTam upaGAtaH iti / cintyam etat
# kha-dog #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnas la yang lus-kyis #  reg-pa #  ma yin na ji-ltar #  gnod-pa # r 'gyur zhe na / / 'di ni bsam-pa # r bya-ba #  ste /
tasmAt loka vyavahAraH eva atra anusartavyaH na paramArTaH
# de-lta-bas-na #  'dir 'jig-rten #  gyi tha-snyad #  du 'brang bar bya'i don-dam-pa # r ni ma yin no /
SlakzNa tvam mRdu aparUzam AliFgana kzamam iti arTaH
# 'jam-pa-nyid #  ni ma nyen-pa #  dang mi rtsub dang spyad du bzod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
SlakzNam eva SlakzNa tvam
# 'jam-pa #  kho-na #  'jam-pa-nyid #  do /
karkaSa tvam iti karkam asyAH tItika arka Sam lomaSa vat
# rtsub pa nyid ces bya-ba #  ni 'di-la #  rtsub pa yod-pa # s rtsub pa zhes bya ste / / spu can bzhin no /
karkam iti balasya AKyA
# rtsub pa zhes-bya-ba #  ni stobs zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
karkaSam eva karkaSa tvam
# rtsub pa kho-na #  rtsub pa nyid de /
rUkzam paruzam asukumAram iti arTaH / guruH sAndraH iti arTaH
# rud rud po dang hrud hrud po dang shin-tu #  'jam-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / lci-ba #  ni lcid gnon zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
guru eva guru tvam / yena BAvAH tulyanta izavantam anti
# lci-ba #  kho-na #  lci-ba-nyid #  de / / dngos-po #  rnam-pa #  'jam-pa #  na gang-gis #  dma'-ba # r byed-pa # 'o /
laGu tvanyena BAvAH na avanamanti / saMsTAna pRTu tve api yasya sadBAvAt suKam Ahriyate
# yang-ba-nyid #  ni gang-gis #  dngos-po #  rnams 'jam-pa #  na dma'-ba # r mi-'gyur-ba #  ste / / dbyibs cher zin-kyang #  gang yod-na #  gdeg bla ba ste /
tulAya AjaGana avanati kAraNam iti arTaH / yat aByAhatasya uzNa aBilAzoBavati tat SItam / nanu ca grIzme Saradi ca sati api SIta OzNa aBilAzaH na Bavati
# srang mda'i rtse mo dma'-ba # r 'gyur-ba'i-rgyu #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / gang-gis #  nyen na dro-ba #  'dod-pa #  de ni grang-ba #  nyid do / / dpyid dang ston grang-ba #  yod kyang dro-ba #  mi-'dod-pa #  ma yin nam /
uzNa aBilAzasya anyaTABAvAt SItam eva uzNa aBilAza kRt iti avaDAryate
# dro-ba #  'dod-pa #  ni gzhan-du #  mi-'byung-ba # s grang-ba #  nyid dro-ba #  'dod-par-byed-pa #  zhes nges-par #  gzung ngo /
evam ca tad kAryam apitajjAtIya tvAt lakzyate lAkzaNikEH
# de-ltar-na #  de'i 'bras-bu #  yang de dang rigs gcig pa'i phyir mtshan-nyid #  pa rnams kyis rtogs so /

pipAsA pAna aBilAza kRt
# skom-pa #  ni skom-'dod-pa # r byed-pa # 'o /
na hi cEta sikoDarmaH kAya indriya vizayaH asti iti
# sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  ni lus kyi dbang-po # 'i yul ma yin no zhe na /
atas kAraNe kArya upacAraMkRtvA iha nirdeSaH jiGatsA pipAsA iti
# de'i-phyir #  rgyu la 'bras-bu #  gdags-pa #  byas-na # s 'dir bkres-pa #  dang skom-pa #  bstan te /
vAyu DAtu BUyizWaH hi kaScid sprazwavya viSezaH jiGatsA hetuH kozWaH utpadyate / sa jiGatsA kAraNa tvAt jiGatsA iti uktaH
# rlung-gi-khams #  kyi shas-che-ba #  ni bkres-pa # 'i rgyu reg-bya # 'i bye-brag #  'ga' zhig 'byung-ba #  de ni bkres-pa # 'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir / / bkres-pa #  zhes brjod do /
evam tejaH DAtu BUyizWaH pipAsA kAraNa tvAt pipAsA iti uktaH

# gzhan nas brgyal-ba #  dang nyams yod-pa #  dang nyam-chung-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  reg-bya # 'i bye-brag #  smos-pa #  rnams kyang 'di dag gi nang-du #  'dus-pa # s logs-shig #  tu ma brjod do /
mUrCA SlakzNa tvAt na Bidyate / balam karkaSa guru tvAByAm
# brgyal-ba #  ni 'jam-pa-nyid #  las gud-na #  med do / / nyams yod-pa #  ni rtsub pa dang lci-ba-nyid #  las logs-shig #  na med de /

# de-ltar #  gzhan nas reg-bya # 'i bye-brag #  'byung-ba #  rnams kyang 'di dag gi nang-du #  mthun mthun du bsdu-ba # r bya'o / / 'jam-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yang gnas kyi bye-brag #  gis phan tshun tha dad de /
ap tejaH DAtu utsadatvAt SlakzNa tvam / pRTivI vAyu DAtu utsavAt karkaSa tvam / pRTivI abDAtu utsada tvAt guru tvam / tejaH vAyuDA tunda tvAt laGu tvam
# chu nyid las gud-na #  med do / / nyams yod-pa #  ni rtsub pa dang lci-ba #  rlung-gi-khams #  kyi shas-che-ba #  ni rtsub pa nyid do / / sa dang chu'i-khams #  kyi shas-che-ba #  ni lci-ba-nyid #  do / / me dang rlung-gi-khams #  kyi shas-che-ba #  ni yang-ba-nyid #  do /
atas eva mRta SarIrezu aDikam guru tvam
# de nyid kyi phyir shi-ba # 'i lus la lci-ba-nyid #  kyi shas-che-ba # 'o /

tejoDA tutsada tvAt pipAsA
# me'i-khams #  kyi shas-che-ba #  ni skom-pa # 'o /
evam anyasmin= api upAdAya rUpe yaTAsamBavam ASraya viSezAt paraspara viSezaH avagantavyaH iti / atra tu diS mAtram pradarSitaMgranTa gOrava parihAra arTam iti / rUpa skanDAt upAdAya rUpAt vA avijQaptiH eva avaSizyate iti praSnaH avijQaptiH katamA iti
# de-bzhin-du #  gnas kyi bye-brag #  gis phan tshun bye-brag #  tu gyur-pa # r rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  gzhan la yang ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du khong-du-chud-pa # r bya ste / / 'dir ni tshig mang-du #  'gyur-ba #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir phyogs tsam zhig bstan to / / gzugs-kyi-phung-po # 'am rgyur byes pa'i gzugs las rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  'ba'-zhig #  lus pas /
tad nirdeSaH / vijQapti samADi jaMkuSala akuSalaMrUpam anidarSanam apratiGam iti
# rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang rnam-par-rig-byed #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  las byung-ba # 'i gzugs te / / bstan-du-med-pa #  thogs-pa-med-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba # s de bstan to /
tatra vijQaptiH dviviDA
# de-la #  rnam-par-rig-byed #  ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  te /
kAya vijQaptiH vAc vijQaptiH ca
# lus kyi rnam-par-rig-byed #  dang ngag gi rnam-par-rig-byed #  do /
sA punar pratyekam triDA aBidyate kuSala akuSala avyAkRta BedAt
# de re-re #  la yang dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung du mi ston-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-gsum #  gsum du 'gyur ro /
avijQaptiH api triviDA eva kAma AptA rUpa Apta anAsravA ca
# rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  yang rnam-pa-gsum #  nyid do / / 'dod-pa # r gtogs-pa #  dang gzugs su gtogs-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa # 'o /
tatra kAmAvacari avijQaptiH kuSala akuSala vijQapti jA
# de-la #  'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  ni dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i rnam-par-rig-byed #  las byung-ba #  ste /
sA punar prAtimokza saMvaraH boDisattva saMvaraH asaMvaraH tad viyuktA ca
# de-yang #  so-sor-thar-pa # 'i sdom-pa #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i sdom-pa #  dang sdom-pa-ma-yin-pa #  dang de-dag #  ma-rtogs-pa # 'o /
tatra prAtimokza saMvaraH Bikzu SrAmaNeH upAsaka upavAsa sTa Beda adravyataH caturviDaH
# de-la #  so-sor-thar-pa # 'i sdom-pa #  ni dge slong dang dge-tshul #  dang dge-bsnyen #  dang bsnyen-gnas-la-gnas-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis rdzas su rnam-pa-bzhi # 'o /
nAmataH tu azwaviDaH BikzuBi kzuNya Adi BedAt
