# de-la #  so-sor-thar-pa # 'i sdom-pa #  ni gzhan la gnod-pa-byed-pa #  las gzhi-dang-bcas-pa # r rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  ldog-pa # 'o /
boDisattva saMvaraH kAya jIvita upAtta vastu nirapekzam kAya vAc cittEH sarva AkAra para upakAra pravRttiH
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i sdom-pa #  ni lus-dang-srog #  gis bsdus-pa # 'i dngos-po #  la mi-lta-ba # r / / lus dang ngag dang sems-kyis #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  gzhan-la-phan-'dogs-pa # r zhugs-pa # 'o /
asaMvaraH sarvaH AkAr apar opak hAta prav Rtti H
# sdom-pa-ma-yin-pa #  ni rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  gzhan la gnod-pa-byed-pa # r zhugs-pa # 'o /
deka deSena anugraha upaGAta pravRttiH na eva saMvaraH na asaMvaraH
# phyogs-gcig #  gis phan-'dogs-pa #  dang gnod-pa-byed-pa # r zhugs-pa #  ni sdom-pa #  yang ma yin sdom-pa-ma-yin-pa #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'o /
tatra rUpa Apta anAsravA ca esamADi jA / sA punar yaTAkramam DyAna saMvaraH anAsrava saMvaraH ca
# de-la #  gzugs su gtogs-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  ni ting-nge-'dzin #  las byung-ba #  ste / / de-yang #  bsam-gtan #  gyi sdom-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa # 'i sdom-pa #  go-rims #  bzhin no /
n etat haviH vavUH tatra caturzu DyAnezu anAgamye DyAna antare ca sa Asrava samADi jaH DyAna saMvaraH varaH
# de-la #  bsam-gtan-bzhi #  po dag dang mi lcogs-pa #  med-pa #  dang bsam-gtan #  khyad-par-can #  dag na zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  dang lhan-cig #  byung-ba #  ni bsam-gtan #  gyi sdom-pa # 'o /
anAsrava samADi jaH anAsrava saMvaraH / tasyAH tUpAt Aya rUpa tvam BUtAni ASritya pravRtteH anuvRtteH ca / idam iha amutra iti ayam eva vyapadeSaH nidarSanam / saH atra na asti iti anidarSanam
# zag-pa-med-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  dang lhan-cig #  byung-ba #  ni zag-pa-med-pa # 'i sdom-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  'byung-ba #  rnams la brten-nas-'byung-ba #  dang rjes-su-'jug-pa # 'i phyir rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  nyid do / / 'di ni 'di na'o / / pha bi ni pha bi na'o zhes brjod-pa #  'di ni bstan-pa # 'o / / de 'di-la #  med-pa # s bstan-du-med-pa # 'o /
sva pradeSe parasya utpatti pratibanDaH pratiGAtaH / sa ca avijQapteH adeSa tvAt na samBavati iti apratiGam / sarvam hi rUpam triviDam
# rang-gi #  phyogs su gzhan 'byung-ba # 'i gegs-byed-pa #  ni thogs-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  ni yul na mi-gnas-pa # 'i phyir de mi srid-pa # s thogs-pa-med-pa # 'o / / gzugs thams-cad #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / bstan du yod-la #  thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang bstan du med la thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang bstan du yang med la thogs-pa #  yang med-pa # 'o /
sa nidarSana saMsa pratiGam cakzuH indriya vizayaH
# de-la #  bstan du yod-la #  thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  ni mig-gi-dbang-po # 'i yul lo /
anidarSanam sa pratiGam cakzuH AdayaH paQca Sabda ganDa rasa sparSAH catvAraH anidarSanam apratiGam ca Darma Ayatanikam rUpam / tat punar paQca prakAram ABisaFkzepikam AByavakASi kaMsAma AdAnikam parikalpitam vEBUtvikaMca iti
# bstan du med la thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  ni mig la-sogs-pa #  lnga dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg-bya #  bzhi'o / / bstan du yang med la thogs-pa #  yang med-pa #  ni chos-kyi-skye-mched #  kyi gzugs so / / de-yang #  rnam-pa-lnga #  ste / / bsdus-pa #  las gyur-pa #  dang mngon-par-skabs-yod-pa #  dang yang-dag-par-blangs-pa #  las byung-ba #  dang kun-brtags-pa #  dang dbang 'byor-pa # 'o /
iha tu ekAdaSa dravye eva rUpa skanDaH vivakzitaH iti sAmAdAnikam eva rUpam anidarSanam apratiGam iti uktam na anyat / kimarTaMpunaH tat na uktam
# 'dir gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  ni / / rdzas bcu gcig kho-nar #  'dod-pa # s yang-dag-par-blangs-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i gzugs nyid-du #  bstan du yang med la thogs-pa #  yang med-pa # r bshad de / / gzhan ni ma yin no / / ci'i-phyir #  de-dag #  mi bstan zhe na /
ABisaFkzepikam paramANava iva nIla AdikAt varNAn na Bidyante
# bsdus-pa #  las gyur-pa #  ni rdul-phra-rab #  rnams nyid de / / de-dag #  ni sngon-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i kha-dog #  las gud-na #  med de /
na ca varNa niBAH anyAH nIla AdikAt varNAt
# sngon-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i kha-dog #  las kha-dog #  tu snang-ba #  gzhan rnams ni med do /
AByavakASikam paramANavaH eva tad anya pratiGAtika sprazwavya virahitAH
# mngon-par-skabs-yod-pa #  yang rdul-phra-rab #  rnams nyid de / / de-las-gzhan-pa #  thogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i reg-bya #  dang bral-ba #  rnams so /
te ca varNa Atmaka tvAt iha upAttAH eva iti punar na nirdizwAH
# de-dag #  kyang kha-dog #  gi bdag-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir 'dir 'dus-pa #  nyid pas yang ma bshad do /
parikalpitam pratibimba rUpam asTi saFkalikA Adikam
# kun-brtags-pa #  ni gzugs-brnyan #  gyi gzugs keng-rus #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
vEBUtvikaMvimokza DyAyi gocaram yat rUpa mtat vikalpa Atmaka tvAt iha na upAttam
# dbang 'byor-pa #  ni rnam-par-thar-pa #  la bsam-gtan-pa # 'i spyod yul gyi gzugs gang-yin-pa #  ste / / de ni rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  'dir ma 'dus te /
na hi tat tad AkAra vijQAna pratyavaBAsAt bahis vidyate
# de ni de'i rnam-pa #  can gyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la so-so # r snang-ba #  las phyi-rol #  na med do /
pratibimbam ca vizaya pratyavaBAsaH vijQAnasya eva itina vijQAnAt pratibimbam pratibimbAt vA vijQAnam pRTak asti / tasmAt sAma AdAnikam eva uktam na anyat
# gzugs-brnyan #  yang yul du snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid do / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  las gzugs-brnyan #  nam gzugs-brnyan #  las rnam-par-shes-pa #  gud-na #  med do / / de-lta-bas-na #  yang-dag-par #  blangs la-la # s byung-ba #  nyid 'dir bshad kyi /
kaH vA apraBAva mahatAm asmadviDaH budDi vispanditAni avagAhitum samarTaH
# gzhan ni ma yin no / / mthu stobs kyis che-ba # 'i blos bskyod-pa #  ni bdag lta-bu #  gang-gis #  kyang rtogs-pa # r ga la nus te /
tasmAt tad anaBiDAnaH AcArya aBiprAyaH anvezyaH
# de-lta-bas-na #  de-dag #  ma bshad-pa #  ni slob-dpon #  gyi dgongs-pa #  btsal bar bya'o /
etat uktam Bavati vijQapti samADi samBUtaMkuSala akuSalam upAdAya rUpam vikzipta avikzipta cittasya acittasya ca yat anubaDnAtitat parityAga kAraNa aBAve uktam Bavati avijQaptiH iti
# de ni 'di-skad-du #  rnam-par-rig-byed #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  las byung-ba #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  las byung-ba #  rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  ni sems g-yeng ba dang ma g-yeng ba dang sems med-pa #  na yang rjes-su-'brang-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  ste / / de stong-pa # 'i rgyu med na yod-pa #  ni rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa # 'o zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro /
rUpa kriyAsu aBAvA api satI sva samutTApakam cittaMvijQapti vat param na vijQapayati iti avijQaptiH
# gzugs dang byed-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin-du-zin #  kyang rang kun-nas-slong-ba # 'i sems rnam-par-rig-pa # r byed-pa #  bzhin-du #  gzhan la rnam-par-rig-pa # r mi-byed-pa # s rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa # 'o /
atra ca vEBAzika parikalpita vijQapti vat avijQaptiH api na eva asti pramANa avizaya tvAt / na caprAtimokza saMvara Adi aBAvaH / taTA hiyayA cetanaya akRta aByupagamaH upasampadAdi viDAna pUrvakam pratizidDAt karmaNaH kAya vAcO saMvRNotitayA cetanayA Alaya vijQAne anAgata tad jAtIya cetanA utpataye bIjam Ahitam yatas uttara kAlam aham prANa atipAta AdiByaH prativirataH iti samAdAna smRtiH utpadyate / rtasyAm samutpannAyAm yaH lajjI na sa SikzA aMBinnatti
# 'dir ni bye-brag #  tu smra-ba # s kun-brtags-pa # 'i rnam-par-rig-byed #  bzhin-du #  rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  yang med de / / tshad-ma # 'i yul du-ma #  gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / so-sor-thar-pa # 'i sdom-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni med-pa #  ma yin te / / 'di-ltar #  sems-pa # s bya-ba # r khas blangs-nas #  bsnyen-par-rdzogs-pa # r bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i cho-ga #  sngon-du-btang-ste #  / / sems-pa #  gang-gis #  lus-dang-ngag-gi-las #  bkag-pa #  las sdom-pa # 'i sems-pa #  des ma-'ongs-pa #  na de dang rigs gcig pa bskyed-pa # 'i phyir kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la sa-bon #  btab nas / / de'i-'og-tu #  bdag ni srog-gcod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  spangs-pa # 'o zhes yang-dag-par-blangs-pa #  dran-pa #  'byung ste / / de byung nas gang 'dzem-pa #  de bslab-pa #  mi 'dral lo /
evam ca sa anubanDA samAdAna cetanA saMvaraH iti uktam Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  yang-dag-par-blang-ba # 'i sems-pa #  rgyun-chags-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  ni sngom-pa #  zhes bstan-pa #  yin no /
taTA DyAnam mArgam vA samApannaH vinA api avijQaptyA tad rUpam mArgam ASrayam ca pratilaBate yasya pratilamBAt vyutTitaH api na punar miTyA vAc Adizu pravartateH saMyagva Adizu eva pravartate
# de-bzhin-du #  bsam-gtan #  nam lam la snyoms-pa # r zhugs na rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  med-pa # r yang gang thob na langs-nas #  log-pa # 'i ngag la-sogs-pa #  la mi-'jug-pa #  dang yang-dag-pa'i-ngag #  la-sogs-pa #  la 'jug-pa #  de-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  dang gnas thob ste /
atas nimitte nEmittika upacAraMkRtvA azwO mArga aFgAni DyAna saMvaraH ca vyavasTApyate
# de'i-phyir #  rgyu la rgyu can gdags-pa # r byas-na # s lam gyi yan-lag-brgyad #  rnams dang bsam-gtan #  gyi sdom-pa #  yang rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
asaMvaraH api vaDaka prayoga kriyA cetanA tad kulInAnAm tad karma aByupagama cetanAH anya kulInAnAm
# sdom-pa-ma-yin-pa #  yang de'i rigs su skyes-pa #  rnams kyi gsad-pa # r sbyor-ba # r bya-ba # 'i sems-pa #  dang gzhan gyi rigs su skyes-pa #  rnams kyi las de bya-ba # r khas-len-pa # 'i sems-pa #  ste /
na cataccetanA apagame asamvara tyAgaH sattva izu droha ASayasya avinivRtta tvAt
# sems-pa #  de med kyang sdom-pa-ma-yin-pa #  btang-ba #  ma yin te / / sems-can #  rnams la gnod-pa #  bya-ba # r bsam-pa #  las ma-log-pa # 'i phyir ro /
evam cakriya acetanA aByupagama cetanA ca sattva izu droha ASaya anugata asaMvaraH iti uktam Bavati
# de-ltar #  bya-ba # 'i sems-pa #  dang khas-len-pa # 'i sems-pa #  sems-can #  rnams la gnod-pa #  bya-ba # 'i bsam-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  ni sdom-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'o zhes bstan-pa #  yin no /
atra ca vijQapti samADi ja tvam su boDam eva iti na punar iha prapaQcitam
# 'dir rnam-par-rig-byed #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  las byung-ba #  nyid ni brda-phrad-pa # r sla-ba # s yang ma spros so /
kuSala akuSala tvam tu saMvara asaMvara cetanAnAMsvate eva tad anubanDasya kuSala akuSala cetanA Akzipta tvAt kuSala akuSala cetanA PalatvAt ca
# sdom-pa #  dang sdom-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i sems-pa #  rnams kyi dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  ni bdag-nyid #  kho-na # s so; / / de'i rgyun-chags-pa #  ni dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-sems #  pas 'phangs-pa #  dang dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-sems #  pa'i 'bras-bu #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
DyAna anAsrava saMvaraNayoH apiDyAnA nAsrava mArga nimitta tvAt saMyagvAgAdi PalatvAt cakuSala tvam / rUpa tvam punar kAya vAc vizaya tvAt vizayiNi vizaya upacArAt / anidarSana apratiGa tvam tu su boDam iti
# bsam-gtan #  dang zag-pa-med-pa # 'i sdom-pa #  yang bsam-gtan #  dang zag-pa-med-pa # 'i lam rgyu yin pa dang yang-dag-pa # 'i dag la-sogs-pa #  'bras-bu #  yin pa'i phyir dge-ba # 'o / / gzugs ni lus dang ngag yul yin pa'i phyir te / / yul can la yul btags-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bstan-du-med-pa #  thogs-pa-med-pa #  ni / / brda-phrad-pa # r sla-ba # s ma bshad do /
kasmAt punar ayam avijQapti paryantaH rUpa skanDaH rUpam iti ucyate
# de'i ci'i-phyir #  rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  la thug-pa # 'i gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  'di gzugs zhes bya zhe na /
uktam hi BagavatA t urUpyate rUpyate iti BikzavaH tasmAt rUpa upAdAna skanDEti ucyate / kena rUpyate
# bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis kyang dge slong dag gzugs su rung-ba # s de'i-phyir #  gzugs nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  zhes pa'o / / ci gzugs she na /
pANi saMsparSena api spRzwaH rUpyate iti vistaraH
# lag-pa # 'i 'dus-te-reg-pa # s reg na gzugs su rung-ba # 'o zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
sUtre hi vpANi Adi saMsparSena rUpaNAt rUpam iti uktam / kA punar iyam rUpasya rUpaNA
# mdo las kyang lag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'dus-te-reg-pa # s gzugs yod-pa # 'i phyir gzugs so zhes gsungs so / / gzugs kyi gzugs su yod-pa #  'di gang zhe na /
hasta Adi saMsparSana pUrva avasTAtaH anyaTA utpAdanA / iyam ca santAnam aDikRtya ucyate nakzaNa mkzaNasya utpAda vinASa kAlayoH aDikRta tvAt
# lag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'dus-te-reg-pa #  snga-ma # 'i gnas las gzhan-du #  skyed-pa #  ste / / 'di yang rgyun gyi dbang-du-byas-te #  brjod kyi / / skad-cig #  la ni ma yin te / / skad-cig #  ni skye-ba-dang-'jig-pa # 'i dus kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  dang gnas-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
rUpa skanDa anantaram vedanA skanDa nirdeSa avasaraH tad anantaram uddizwatvAt iti praSnaH vedanA katamA iti / triviDaH anuBava eti nirdeSaH
# gzugs-kyi-phung-po # 'i 'og-tu #  tshor-ba'i-phung-po #  bshad-pa # 'i skabs yin te / / de'i-'og-tu #  bstan-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / tshor-ba #  gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang myong-ba #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ste zhes-bya-ba # s bstan to /
anuBUtiH anuBavaH tu n ohlAda paritApa tad uBaya AkAra vinirmukta svarUpa sAkzAt karaNaH
# nyams-su-myong-ba #  ni myong-ba #  ste / / dngos-po # 'i sim-pa #  dang gdung-ba #  dang gnyi-ga # 'i rnam-pa # r ma-gtogs-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo mngon-sum-du-byed-pa # 'o /
aTa vA hlAda paritApa uBaya AkAra vinirmuktam vastu svarUpam anuBavati iti anuBavaH / sa ca svaBAva BedAt triviDaH suKaH duHKaH aduHKa asuKaH ca
# yang-na #  sim-pa #  dang gdung-ba #  dang gnyi-ga # 'i rnam-pa # r ma-gtogs-pa # 'i dngos-po # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo myong-bar-byed-pa # s myong-ba # 'o / / de-yang #  ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-gsum #  ste /
kaTam punar / suKa duHKa vyatiriktaH anyaH tRtIyaH anuBavaH asti iti vijQAyate / AgamAt yuktitaH ca
# bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  dang sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'o / / bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  ma-gtogs-par #  myong-ba #  gsum-pa #  yod-pa #  ji-ltar #  zhe na / / lung dang rigs-pas #  mngon te /
uktam hi sUtre tisraH vedanA iti / punar ca uktam suKasya ca prahANAt duHKasya ca prahANAt aduHKasya ca iti
# mdo las tshor-ba #  rnam-pa-gsum #  zhes gsungs so / / yang bde-ba #  yang spangs sdug-bsngal #  yang spangs-te #  / / bde-ba #  yang ma yin sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin zhes gsungs so /
yuktiH api vedanA virahita citta utpatti aBAvAt apeta suKa duHKa citta upalabDeH ca iti
# rigs-pa #  ni tshor-ba #  dang bral-ba # 'i sems-skye-ba #  med-pa #  dang bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  dang bral-ba # 'i sems kyang mi dmigs so /
vedanA anuBavaH sparSasya iti AcArya saFGa BadraH
# reg-pa #  myong-ba #  ni tshor-ba #  zhes slob-dpon #  'dus bzang gsungs te /
izwa anizwa uBaya viparItAnAm sparSAnAm anuBavaH sA vedanA / taTA ca uktam suKa vedanIyam sparSaMprati iti utpadyate suKAH vedanA iti vistaraH
# 'dod-pa #  dang mi-'dod-pa #  dang gnyi-ga #  las ldog-pa # 'i reg-pa #  rnams myong-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de tshor-ba # 'o / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  / / bde-ba-myong-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'i reg-pa #  la brten-nas #  bde-ba'i-tshor-ba #  'byung ngo zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
suKa vedanA Adi janaka tvena tad viBakta tvAt
# bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  bskyed-pa #  yin-pas #  de rnam-par-dbye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
yadi ca vizaya anuBavaH vedanA syAt eka AlambaneByaH asya kaH viSezaH syAt
# gal-te #  yul myong-ba #  tshor-ba #  yin-du-zin #  na dmigs-pa-gcig-pa #  rnams las 'di khyad-par #  ci yod de /
yena sparSa anuBavaH vedanA iti vyavasTApyate
# de'i-phyir #  reg-pa #  myong-ba #  ni tshor-ba # 'o zhes rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
evam tarhi saQjQA aDimokza smRti prajQA AdInAm Alambana dvArakaH vedanA vat svaBAvaH na vaktavyaH
# de lta na 'o na ni 'du-shes #  dang mos-pa #  dang dran-pa #  dang; shes-rab #  la-sogs-pa #  yang tshor-ba #  bzhin-du #  dmigs-pa # 'i sgo nas ngo-bo-nyid #  brjod-pa # r mi bya'o /
aTa eka AlambaneByaH nimitta udgrahaNa AdiBiH saQjQA AdInAm viSezaH ucyate vedanAyAH vizaya anuBavena kim na izyate
# ji ste 'du-shes #  la-sogs-pa #  mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s dmigs-pa-gcig-pa #  rnams las khyad-par #  du 'dod na ni tshor-ba #  yang yul myong-ba # r ci'i-phyir #  mi 'dod /
sparSa anuBavaH catatsamprayogaH kAraNa BAvaH vA parikalpyeta tad Alambana tva asamBavAt
# de-la #  dmigs-pa # r mi srid-pa # 'i phyir reg-pa #  myong-ba #  yang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'am / / rgyu'i-dngos-po # r yongs su brtag grang na /
tatra na Bavet samprayogaH sarva cEttAnAm sparSa samprayoga aviSezAt
# de-la #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ni ma yin te / / sems-las-byung-ba #  thams-cad #  reg-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # r bye-brag-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na api kAraNa BAvaH sarva cEttAnAm sparSasya kAraNa tva aviSezAt
# rgyu'i-dngos-po # r yang mi rung ste / / sems-las-byung-ba #  thams-cad-kyi #  rgyu reg-pa #  yin par bye-brag-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na ca loke SAstre vA anuBava SabdaH kArye kAraNe vA prasidDaH / prasidDaH tusAkzAt kAre
# 'jig-rten #  dang bstan-bcos #  las kyang myong-ba # 'i sgra ni 'bras-bu # 'am rgyur grags-pa #  med kyi mngon-sum-du-byed-pa # r grags so /
evaMtu manyante SuBa aSuBAnAm karmaNA aMPala vipAkam pratyanuBavanti anena iti anuBavaH
# 'di-snyam-du-sems #  te las dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  rnams kyi 'bras-bu #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  'dis myong-ba #  ste /
tatra SuBAnAm karmaNAm suKaH anuBavaH Pala vipAkaH / aSuBAnAm duHKaH / uBayezAm aduHKa asuKaH
# de-la #  bde-ba-myong-ba #  ni las dge-ba #  rnams kyi 'bras-bu #  rnam-par-smin-pa # 'o / / sdug-bsngal #  ni mi-dge-ba #  rnams kyi'o / / bde-ba #  yang ma yin sdug-bsngal #  yang ma-yin-pa #  ni gnyi-ga # 'i'o snyam mo /
atracAlaya vijQAnam eva SuBa aSuBa karma vipAkaH
# 'dir ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid las dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  ste /
tad samprayuktA eva upekzA paramArTataH SuBa aSuBa anAMkarmaNAm vipAkaH
# don-dam-pa # r na de dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i btang-snyoms #  nyid las dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa # 'o /
suKa duHKayoH tu vipAka ja tvAt vipAka upacAraH
# bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  ni rnam-par-smin-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i phyir rnam-par-smin-pa #  zhes btags-pa # 'o /
tatra suKaH anuBavoyasya niroDa ityAdi
# de-la #  bde-ba-myong-ba #  ni gang 'gags na zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  yin na /
yat tarhi uktam pratItyasamutpAde yasyAm utpannAyAm aviyoga icCA jAyatesA suKA vedanA iti tat kaTam
# 'o na rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  las gang 'byung na bral-ba # r mi-'dod-pa #  skye-ba #  de bde-ba'i-tshor-ba # 'o zhes 'byung-ba #  de ji-lta-bu #  /
na asti atra viroDaH arTataH itara upAdAnAt
# 'di-la #  'gal-ba #  med de / / don-du #  na cig shos kyang zin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yasyAm utpannAyAm aviyoga icCA jAyate iti arTataH uktam Bavati tasya aMnirudDAyAm punar saMyoga icCA api Bavati iti
# gang byung na 'bral-ba # r mi 'dod ba skye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni don-du #  na de 'gags na phrad-pa # r 'dod-pa # r yang 'gyur ro zhes bstan-pa #  yin no /
yasya niroDa saMyoga= CandoBavati iti atra api arTataH uktamBavati tasya utpAde aviyoga= CandaH Bavati
# gang 'gags na phrad-pa # r 'dod-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba #  yang 'dir don-du #  na de byung na 'bral-ba # r mi-'dod-pa # 'o zhes bstan-pa #  yin no /
yat tarhi anicCa upagata rAga paryavasTAnAnAm yatInAm rAga je suKe utpanne viyoga icCA jAyate niroDe ca asaMyoga= CandaH tat kaTam / na asO tatas eva jAyate tad vidUzaNAt
# 'o na dka'-thub #  can rnams mi-'dod-bzhin-du #  'dod-chags #  kyi kun-nas-dkris-pa #  dang phrad-pa #  rnams 'dod-chags #  las byung-ba # 'i bde-ba #  skyes-pa # 'i tshe 'bral-ba # r 'dod-pa #  skye zhing / / 'gags-pa-na #  phrad-pa # r mi-'dod-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ji-lta-bu #  zhe na / / de ni sun-'byin-pa # 'i phyir de-nyid-la # s skye-ba #  ma yin te /
SIla samADi paripanTi tvam tasya suKasya paSyatAm tad uBayaMBavati iti na asti viroDaH
# bde-ba #  de tshul-khrims #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi bar-du-gcod-pa # r mthong-ba #  rnams la gnyi-ga #  mi-'byung-ba # s 'gal-ba #  med do /
duHKoyasya utpAda iva yoga= CandaH iti niroDe ca punar / asaMyoga= CandaH
# sdug-bsngal #  ni gang byung na bral-ba # r 'dod-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang 'gags na yang phrad-pa # r mi-'dod-pa # 'o /
viyogaH tad ucCedaH / CandaH aBilAzaH prArTanA
# bral na ni de'i rgyun-chad-pa # 'o / / 'dod-pa #  ni mngon-par-'dod-pa #  dang smon-pa # 'o /
duHKa asuKaH yasya utpAda uBayam / na Bavati ityAdi
# sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa #  ni gang byung na gnyi-ga # r 'dod-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
tatra kAya citta upacaya pravRtta tvAt manojQa svaBAva tvAt ca suKaH anuBavaH iti niroDe punar tad saMyoga aBilAzaH pravartate
# de-la #  lus dang sems rgyas-par-byed-pa #  dang yid-du-'ong-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir / / bde-ba-myong-ba #  ni gang 'gags na de dang phrad-pa # r 'dod-pa # 'o /
kAya citta apacaya pravRtta tva asvaBAvataH ca pratikUlaH duHKaH anuBavaH iti tasya utpAdet viyoga= CandaH Bavati
# lus dang sems nyams dams [?] par byed-pa #  dang ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi mi-mthun-pa # 'i phyir / / sdug-bsngal #  myong-ba #  ni de byung na de dang bral-ba # r 'dod-pa #  yin no /
yaH tu na uBaya pravRttaH asti ca saH anuBavaH duHKa asuKaH akRzNa aSukla karma vat
# gnyi-ga #  ni mi-'byung-ba #  la yang myong-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de yod de / / bde-ba #  yang ma yin sdug-bsngal #  yang ma-yin-pa #  ste / / nag-po #  yang ma yin dkar-po #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'i las dang 'dra'o /
atas eva cAnugraha anupaGAta pravRtta tvAt tad aduHKa utpAda oGayA icCaBAvaH
# de'i-phyir #  phan-'dogs-pa #  yang med la gnod-pa-byed-pa #  yang med-pa # r zhugs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de byung na gnyi-ga # r 'dod-pa #  med do /
eza tu triviDaH anuBavaH pratyekam ASraya BedAt punar zaXviDaH Bavati cakzuH Srotra GrANa rasana kAya manaH saMsparSa ja tvAt / punar ADeya saFkalanataH dviDA Bidyata ekAyikaH ca etasikaH ca iti
# myong-ba #  rnam-pa-gsum #  po 'di ni re-re #  la yang gnas kyi bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-drug #  tu gyur te / / mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi 'dus-te-reg-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / yang brten-pa # r bsdu na ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  su 'gyur te /
tatra kAya avinirBAva varti tvAt sa pratiGa tvAt cakzuH Srotra GrANa rasanA indriyANi kAye antar BAvya kAya Sabdena uktAni iti atas cakzuH Srotra GrANa rasana kAya saMsparSa anuBavaH kAyikaH iti uktaH
# lus kyi dang sems kyi'o / / de-la #  mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang lce'i dbang-po #  rnams ni lus la tha dad du mi-'jug-pa #  dang thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang bsags-pa #  bzhin pa'i phyir lus kyi nang-du #  bsdus te lus kyi sgrar brjod do / / de'i-phyir #  mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi 'dus-te-reg-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i myong-ba #  ni lus kyi zhes bstan to /
manaH saMsparSa jaH tu cEtasikaH iti uktaMmanaH mAtra ASraya tvAt
# yid kyi 'dus-te-reg-pa #  las byung-ba #  ni yid tsam la gnas-pa #  yin pa'i phyir sems kyi zhes-bya'o #  /
punar vipakza pratipakza Bedena pratyekam anuBavasya dviDA vyavasTAnam sa AmizaH nirAmizaH iti greDA ASrita unEzkramya ASritaH ca iti
# yang mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po # 'i bye-brag #  gis myong-ba #  re-re #  la yang rnam-pa-gnyis #  gnyis su 'gyur te / / zang-zing-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zang-zing-med-pa #  dang zhen-pa #  brten-pa #  dang mngon-par-'byung-ba #  brten-pa # 'o /
Amiza rAtma BAva tRzNA / Atma BAvaH ADyAtmikAH upAdAna skanDAH
# zang-zing #  ni lus la sred-pa # 'o / / lus ni nang gi nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po # 'o /
tasmin= tRzNA priya eka putra upagUXa nyAyena aviyogam iva icCantI yA pravartatesA Amizam / tayA saha vartate iti sa AmizA / tayA tRzNayA avisaMyuktA viyoga anukUlA ca nirAmizA / paQca izwAH rUpa AdayaH kAma guNAH
# de-la #  sred-pa #  bu gcig pa phongs-pa #  la 'khyud-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  mi 'brel-ba # r 'dod-pa #  lta-bu # r 'jug-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni zang-zing #  ste / / de dang ldan-pa # s zang-zing-dang-bcas-pa # 'o / / sred-pa #  de dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  dang bral-ba # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa #  ni zang-zing-med-pa # 'o /
apekzABiH aFga prArTanA lakzaNena kAmena guNyante punar punar aByasyante iti kAma guNAH / tezu aBizvaFgaH prArTanA ca greDaH
# gzugs la-sogs-pa #  'dod-pa'i-yon-tan #  sdug-pa #  lnga la lta-ba #  dang mngon-pa # r chags-pa #  dang smon-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi 'dod-pa # s zlos shing yang-dang-yang #  goms-par-byed-pa # s 'dod-pa'i-yon-tan #  rnams te de-dag #  la mngon-pa # r chags-pa #  dang smon-pa #  ni zhen-pa # 'o /
tad ASritaH tena vA ASrita ugra eDa ASritaH
# de-la #  brten-pa # 'am zhen-pa #  de brten-pa # s na zhen-pa #  brten-pa # 'o /
nEzkramyam kAma vErAgyam tad mArgaH vA
# mngon-par-'byung-ba #  ni 'dod-pa'i-yon-tan #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'am de'i lam ste /
tad ASritaH tena vA ASritaH nEzkramya ASritaH
# de-la #  brten-pa # 'am de brten-pa # s mngon-par-'byung-ba #  la brten-pa # 'o /
tatra satkAya vErAgyam puroDAya vipakza pratipakza BAvena sAmiza nirAmizayoH vyavasTAnam
# de-la #  'jig-tshogs #  dang 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-te #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po # 'i dngos-po # r zang-zing-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zang-zing-med-pa #  gnyis rnam-pa # r gnas so /
lOkika vErAgyam aDikRtya greDanEH kramya ASrita vyavasTAnam
# 'jig-rten-pa #  dang 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-te #  zhen-pa #  brten-pa #  dang mngon-par-'byung-ba #  la brten-pa #  rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
kimarTam punar atrasva rUpataH eva BedaH uktaH na ASraya Adi Bedena yaTA anyatra
# ci'i-phyir #  'dir rang-gi #  ngo bo'i bye-brag #  bstan gyi ji-ltar #  gzhan nas 'byung-ba #  bzhin-du #  gnas la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis ma yin zhe na /
iha saFkzepasya vivakzita tvAt sarva BedAnAm ca svarUpAt apRTak ASraya Adi Bedena na uktaH iti
# 'dir ni mdor bsdu-ba # r bzhed-pa #  dang tha-dad-pa #  thams-cad #  kyang rang-gi #  ngo bo las gud-na #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'dir gnas la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  ma bshad do /
vedanA skanDa nirdeSa anantaram saQjQA skanDa nirdeSa avasara eti atas praSnaH saQjQA katameti iti / tvizaya nimitta udgrahaNam iti tad nirdeSaH / vizaya Alambanam
# tshor-ba'i-phung-po #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  'du-shes #  kyi phung bo bshad-pa # 'i skabs su bab ste / / de'i-phyir #  'du-shes #  gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang yul la mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  de bstan to /
nimittam vizaya viSezaH nIla pIta Adi Alambana vyavasTA kAraNam
# yul ni dmigs-pa # 'o / / mtshan-ma #  ni yul gyi bye-brag #  sngon-po-dang-ser-po #  la-sogs-pa #  dmigs-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i rgyu'o /
tasya udgrahaNam nIla nirUpaNaMnIlam etat pItam etat iti
# de-la #  mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa #  ni 'di ni sngon-po # 'o / / 'di ni ser-po # 'o zhes rtog-pa # 'o /
evam tarhi cakzuH Adi vijQAna samprayuktA saQjQA vizaya nimitta udgrahaNa AtmikA na syAt viSeza asaMlakzaNAt
# de lta na 'o na ni / / mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  bye-brag #  rtog-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir yul la mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  du mi 'gyur ro zhe na /
sa api nimitta udgrahaNa AtmikA eva na paricCedikA manda tvAt
# de ni mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  kho-na #  yin par shes-pa #  yin gyi / / zhan-pa # 'i phyir yongs su gcod-pa #  ni ma yin no /
anyaTA pUrvam agRhIte viSeze paScAt api nirUpaNam na syAt nIlam etat pItam etat iti
# gzhan-du-na #  sngar ma-zin-pa # 'i bye-brag #  las phyis kyang 'di ni sngon-po # 'o / / 'di ni ser-po # 'o zhes rtog-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
svarUpa aBede api BedaH saQjQAyAH ASraya tAla mbanataH ca veditavyaH
# rang-gi #  ngo bo tha-dad-pa #  med kyang gnas dang dmigs-pa # s 'du-shes #  tha-dad-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
ASrayataH zaw saQjQAkAyAH cakzuH saMsparSa jA saQjQA evam yAvat manaH saMsparSa ja Asan jQA
# gnas las 'du-shes #  kyi tshogs drug ste / / mig gi 'dus-te-reg-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  dang de-bzhin-du #  yid kyi bar-du #  'dus-te-reg-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  so /
Alambanam punar nisanimittam animittam parIttammahadgatam apramANam AkiQca nyAyatanaMca
# dmigs-pa #  ni mtshan-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang mtshan-ma-med-pa #  dang chung du dang rgya-chen-por-gyur-pa #  dang tshad-med-pa #  dang ci-yang-med-pa # 'i skye-mched #  do /
tatra Sabda dvAreNa yat arTa rUpam aDyAropitam tena nimittena vastu svarUpam sa nimittam
# de-la #  sgra'i sgo nas gang don gyi ngo bor sgro-btags-pa #  de ni mtshan-ma #  ste / / mtshan-ma #  de dang lhan-cig #  pa'i dngos-po # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo ni mtshan-ma #  dang bcas-pa # 'o /
tasmin vastuni aDyAropitaMrUpam etat SabdaH asO= iti yA saQjQA sA sa nimitta AlambanA
# dngos-po #  de-la #  sgro-btags-pa # 'i ngo bo de-dang-de #  ni sgra'o snyam pa'i 'du-shes #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni mtshan-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  la dmigs-pa # 'o /
animittam punar anaDyAropita AkAram vastu svarUpam nirvANam Bava agram ca
# mtshan-ma-med-pa #  ni sgro-btags-pa # 'i mtshan-ma-med-pa #  ste / / dngos-po # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang srid-pa # 'i rtse mo'o /
tatra aDyAropita nimitta aBAvAt rUpa vedanA nimitta aBAvAt apawutvAt ca etat trayam animittam ucyate
# de-la #  sgro-btags-pa # 'i mtshan-ma-med-pa #  dang gzugs dang tshor-ba # 'i mtshan-ma-med-pa #  dang gsal-ba #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir / / 'di gsum ni mtshan-ma-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
avyutpanna Sabda arTa sambanDasya hi rUpa svarUpaH eva saQjQA Bavati na tu rUpam iti
# sgra dang don-du #  'brel-ba #  mi-shes-pa #  ni ngo bo la rang-gi #  ngo bo kho-na # 'i 'du-shes #  'byung mod kyi / / gzugs yin no zhes-bya-ba # r ni ma yin te /
atas tad vizaya saQjQAa nimitta AlambanA
# de'i-phyir #  yul de-la #  'du-shes #  pa ni mtshan-ma-med-pa #  la dmigs-pa # 'o /
nirvANa DAtuH api sarva saMskRta nimitta prati astamita svarUpaH iti tad Alambanena api samADinA samprayuktA saQjQA animitta AlambanA
# mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i dbyings kyang 'dus byas thams-cad-kyi #  mtshan-ma # r rab tu nub-pa # 'i ngo bo yin-pas #  de-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  ni mtshan-ma-med-pa #  la dmigs-pa # 'o /
Bava agram apawu tvAt animittam
# srid-pa # 'i rtse mo ni gsal-ba #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir mtshan-ma-med-pa #  ste /
tad samApannasya saQjQA Alambanam na nimittIkaroti iti animitta AlambanA / Bava agrasya atra asPuwa nimitta tvAt tad Alambanam animittam ucyate anudarAkanyAnyAyena na punar tatra nimittaMnA eva asti iti animittam / anyaTA saQjQA BAva prasaFgaH iti nimitta aBAve nimitta udgrahaNa aBAvAt
# de-la #  snyoms-par-zhugs-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  ni / / dmigs-pa #  la mtshan-ma # r mi-byed-pa # s mtshan-ma #  la dmigs-pa # 'o / / 'dir ni mtshan-ma #  gsal-ba #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir / / de-la #  dmigs-pa #  yang bu-mo #  lto med ces bya-ba # 'i tshul du mtshan-ma-med-pa #  zhes bya'i de ni mtshan-ma-med-pa-nyid #  kyi phyir mtshan-ma-med-pa #  zhes ni mi bya'o / / gzhan-du-na #  ni 'du-shes #  par thal-ba # r 'gyur te / / mtshan-ma-med-pa # s mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa #  yang med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
parIttam kAmaDAtuH nikRzwa tvAt / mahat gataH rUpaDAtuH utkRzwa tvAt
# chung-ngu #  ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  te ngan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rgya-chen-por-gyur-pa #  ni gzugs-kyi-khams #  te / / mchog-tu-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
apramANa AkASa vijQAna anantya Ayatane aparyanta tvAt
# tshad-med-pa #  ni nam-mkha' #  mtha' yas dang rnam shes mtha' yas skye-mched #  dag ste / / mu thug-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
parigraha kiQcanA aBAvAt AkiQca nyAyatanam AkiQcanyam
# yongs-su-gzung-ba #  ci-yang-med-pa # 'i phyir ci-yang-med-pa #  ni ci-yang-med-pa # 'i skye-mched #  do /
tasmAt kAmaDAtu Adi AlambanA saQjQA parItta Adi saQjQA iti ucyate / saQjQA skanDa nirdeSa anantaram saMskAra skanDa nirdeSa unyAyyaH tad anantaram uddizwa tvAt iti atas praSnaH saMskArAH katame iti / vedanA saQjQAByAm / anye ca etasikAH DarmAH citta viprayuktAH ca iti
# de-lta-bas-na #  'dod-pa'i-khams #  la-sogs-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  ni chung-ngu #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  zhes-bya'o #  / / 'du-shes-kyi-phung-po #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  'du-byed-kyi-phung-po #  bshad-pa # r rigs te / / de'i-'og-tu #  bstan-pa # s na de'i-phyir #  / / 'du-byed-rnams #  gang zhen zhes dris-pa #  dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  las gzhan-pa #  sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  rnams dang sems dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba # s de bstan to /
tad nirdeSaH / sametya samBUya pratyayEH kRtatvAt sarve eva rUpa Adi skanDa saFgRhItAH DarmAH saMskArAH iti ucyante
# rkyen rnams 'dus-shing-tshogs-nas #  byas-pa # 'i phyir gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i phung-po # r bsdus-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  ni 'du-byed-rnams #  zhes-bya'o #  /
iha tusaMskAra skanDa saFgRhItAH eva saMskArAH aBipretAH
# 'dir ni 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po # r bsdus-pa #  nyid 'du-byed-rnams #  su 'dod de /
rUpa vedanA saQjQA saFgRhItAnAm ukta tvAt vijQAna skanDa saFgRhItAnAm ca vakzyamANa tvAt / atas eva vedanA saQjQayoH sparSamanaskAra AdiBiH cEtasika tva aviSeze api Aha vedanA saQjQAByAm anye cEtasikAH iti
# gzugs dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes-kyi-phung-po # r bsdus-pa #  rnams ni bshad-zin #  la / / rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i phung-po # r bsdus-pa #  rnams ni 'og nas 'byung-ba #  de'i tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  gnyis reg-pa #  dang yid-la-byed-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams dang sems-las-byung-ba #  nyid-du #  bye-brag #  med kyang / / tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  pa las gzhan-pa # 'i sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams zhes smos-pa #  ni /
vedanA saQjQayoH cEtasika tve sati api vedanA saQjQA skanDa saFgRhIta tvAt na saMskAra skanDe asti saFgrahaH iti pradarSana arTam
# tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  gnyis sems-las-byung-ba #  nyid yin-du-zin #  kyang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  gnyis phung-po # r bsdus-pa # s 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po # r ma bsdus-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vedanA hi upaBoga vastu
# tshor-ba #  ni nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i dngos-po #  ste /
taTA hi vedanayA SuBa aSuBAnAm karmaNA aMPala vipAkam anuBavati / saQjQA vyavahAra vastu
# 'di-ltar #  tshor-ba # s ni las dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  rnams kyi 'bras-bu #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  myong-ba # r byed / / 'du-shes #  ni tha-snyad-'dogs-pa # 'i gzhi ste /
saQjQayA ahi dRzwa Sruta mata vijQAtezu arTezu nimittam udgRhya dRzwa Adizu dRzwa Sruta mata vijQAtAH iti lokaH saMvyavahAre pravartate iti atovedana asaQjQe pRTak skanDIkRte na anye cEtasikAH iti
# 'du-shes #  kyis mthong-ba #  dang thos-pa #  dang bye-brag-phyed-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i don rnams la mtshan-ma # r bzung nas mthong-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la mthong ngo / / thos so / / bye-brag #  phyed do / / rnam-pa # r shes so zhes 'jig-rten-pa'i-tha-snyad #  pa 'jug ste / / de'i-phyir #  tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  nyid so-so # r phung-po # r byas kyi / / sems-las-byung-ba #  gzhan rnams ni ma yin no; /
yat iva edana asaQjQAByAm anye sparSa AdayaH vicAra antAH cEtasika aDarmAH citta viprayuktAH ca prApti AdayaH saMskAra skanDa saFgRhItAH evam sati sUtra viroDaH
# gal-te #  tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  las gzhan-pa #  reg-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  spyod-pa #  la thug-pa #  rnams dang sems dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  thob-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  'du-byed-kyi-phung-po # r bsdu na / / de lta na 'o na ni mdo dang 'gal-te #  /
uktam hi sUtre saMskAra skanDaH katamaH
# mdo las ni 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po #  gang zhe na /
zaz cetanAkAya iti / nAstiviroDaH prADAnyena tad nirdeSAt
# sems-pa # 'i tshogs drug go zhes gsungs so zhe na / / de ni gtso bo bstan-pa # 'i phyir 'gal-ba #  med de /
cetanA hicitta aBisaMskaraNe praDAnaManuvartante manaskAra AdayaH iti cetanA eva saMskAra skanDa tvena uktAH
# sems-pa #  ni sems mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  ni gtso bo yin la / / yid-la-byed-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni de'i rjes-su-'brang-ba #  yin-pas #  sems-pa #  nyid 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po # r gsungs te /
taTA hi kuSale cittaMprerayati akuSale api avyAkRte api suKa duHKa Adi avasTAsu api cittam prerayati iti
# 'di-ltar #  gang dge-ba #  la yang sems-'jug-pa # r byed / / mi-dge-ba #  dang lung ma bstan-pa #  dang bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  gyi gnas rnams la yang sems-'jug-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
saMskAra vat cEtasikAH api DarmAH na vijQAyante iti praSnaH / ye DarmAH cittena / samprayuktAH iti vyAkaraNam
# 'du-byed #  bzhin-du #  sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  rnams kyang mi-shes-pa # 'i phyir dris-pa #  dang chos gang dag sems dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba # s bstan to /
te tu na vijQAyante iti atas pRcCati / vyAkaraNam sparSaH manaskAraH iti vistaraH
# de-dag #  kyang mi-shes-pa # s de'i-phyir #  dris-pa #  dang reg-pa #  dang yid-la-byed-pa #  dang zhes rgya-cher #  smos so /
ete / api sparSa AdayaH vicAra antAH paQcaBiH ASraya Alambana AkAra kAla dravya sama tA prakArEH citta anuvartanAt samam prayuktAH iti samprayuktAH
# reg-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dpyod-pa #  la thug-pa #  de-dag #  kyang gnas dang dmigs-pa #  dang rnam-pa #  dang dus dang rdzas mtshungs-pa #  nyid rnam-pa-lnga # s sems kyi rjes-su-'brang-ba # 'i phyir mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # s mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  rnams so /
cittena samprayuktAH iti aviSeza aBiDAnAt sarvezAm sarva citta samprayogaH prasaktaH iti tad nirDAraNa arTam Aha ezAMpaQca sarvatragAH / jpaQca pratiniyata vizayAH / ekAdaSa kuSalAH / zaw kleSAH
# sems dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  bye-brag-med-pa # 'i phyir thams-cad #  kyang sems thams-cad #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # r thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  de bsal-ba # 'i phyir / / de rnams las lnga ni kun du 'gro-ba # 'o / / lnga ni yul so-sor-nges-pa # 'o / / bcu gcig ni dge-ba # 'o / / drug ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'o /
avaSizwAH upakleSAH
# lhag-ma #  rnams ni nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # 'o /
kOkRtya AdyAH catvAraH anyaTA api iti
# 'gyod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhi ni gzhan-du #  yang ngo zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
ezAm yaH AdyAH sparSaH manaskAraH / vedanA saQjQA cetanA ca ete sarvatragAH
# 'di dag gi nang nas dang-po # 'i reg-pa #  dang yid-la-byed-pa #  dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang sems-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni kun du 'gro-ba #  ste /
ete hi paQca DarmAH sarvam cittam anugacCanti iti sarvatragaH
# chos lnga po 'di dag ni sems thams-cad-kyi #  rjes-su-'gro-ba # s kun du 'gro-ba # 'o /
taTA hi eteka Salena trEDAtukena anAsraveNa ca samprayujyante / akuSalena kAma Aptena klizwA vyAkRtAByAm catrEDAtuka aByAMsam prayujyante / avaSyam hi sarva citta pravRttizu trika sannipAtena Bavitavyam trika sannipAtaH casparSAvI aBicArI iti atas sparSasya sarvatra ga tvam
# 'di-ltar #  'di dag ni khams-gsum-pa # 'i dge-ba #  dang zag-pa-med-pa # 'i sems dang yang mtshungs-pa # r ldan la / / 'dod-pa # r gtogs-pa # 'i mi-dge-ba #  dang khams-gsum-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-can #  dang lung du mi ston-pa #  dang yang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no / / sems-kyi-'jug-pa #  thams-cad-la #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  gsum-'dus-pa #  'byung ste / / gsum-'dus-pa #  yang reg-pa #  las 'khrul-pa-med-pa # s / / de'i-phyir #  reg-pa #  ni kun du 'gro-ba #  nyid do /
nirABogasya cittasya Alambane pravRtti aBAvAt manaskAraH api sarvatragaH
# sems-kyi-'jug-pa #  med-pa # r dmigs-pa #  la 'jug-pa #  mi srid-pa # s yid-la-byed-pa #  yang kun du 'gro-ba #  nyid do /
niranuBavasya nimitta udgrahaNa nirapekzasya cacittasya aBAvAt vedanA saQjQayoH api sarvatra ga tvam
# myong-ba #  med-pa #  dang mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa #  la mi ltos-pa # 'i sems med-pa # s na tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  kyang kun du 'gro-ba #  nyid do /
cetanA tumanaskarmA eva iti tayA api avaSyam sarvatra cetasi Bavitavyam iti atas ete paQca DarmAH sarvatra gAH
# sems-pa #  ni yid-kyi-las #  nyid yin-pas #  de-yang #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  sems thams-cad-la #  'byung-ba # s de'i-phyir #  chos lnga po 'di dag ni kun du 'gro-ba # 'o /
paQca pratiniyata vizayAH iti pratiniyataH vizayaH ezAm na sarvaH iti pratiniyata vizayAH
# lnga ni yul so-sor-nges-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di dag yul so-sor-nges-pa #  yin gyi thams-cad-la #  ma-yin-pa # s yul so-sor-nges-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
te punar CandaH aDimokzaH smRtiH samADiH prajQA / ekAdaSa kuSalAH
# de-dag #  kyang 'dun-pa #  dang mos-pa #  dang dran-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  bo / / bcu gcig ni dge-ba #  ste /
te punar SradDA AdayaH avihiMsA avasAnAH
# de-dag #  kyang dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nas rnam-par-mi-'tshe-ba #  la thug-pa-yan-chad #  do /
ete hi ASradDya Adi vipakza tvAt kuSala mUla samprayogAt ca kuSalAH / etEH eva ca samprayuktam cittam kuSalam
# de-dag #  ni ma-dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  yin pa dang dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i phyir dge-ba #  rnams te / / de dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i sems kyang dge-ba # 'o /
zax kleSAH rAgaH pratiGomAnaH avidyA dRzwiH vicikitsA ca
# nyon-mongs-pa #  drug ni 'dod-chags #  dang khong-khro-ba #  dang nga-rgyal #  dang ma-rig-pa #  dang lta-ba #  dang the-tshom #  ste /
ete hi cittam kliSnanti iti kleSAH
# de-dag #  ni sems nyon-mongs-pa # r byed-pa # s nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams so /
avaSizwAH upakleSAH / te punar kroDa AdyAH asamprajanyAntAH
# lhag-ma #  rnams ni nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-dag #  kyang khro-ba #  nas shes-bzhin #  ma-yin-pa #  la thug-pa-yan-chad #  do /
kOkRtya AdyAH catvAraH anyaTA iti vacanAt upakleSAH avaSizwAH iti aviSeza aBiDAne api asamprajanya avasAnAH eva iti gamyate
# 'gyod-pa #  la sogs bzhi ni gzhan-du #  yang ngo zhes 'byung-ba #  de'i-phyir #  lhag-ma #  rnams ni nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # 'o zhes khyad med-pa # r brjod kyang shes-bzhin #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mthar-thug-pa #  kho-na #  yin par mngon no /
kleSa aFgika tvAt citta kleSa kara tvAt ca kleSa samIpe vartante iti upakleSAH
# nyon-mongs-pa # 'i char gtogs-pa #  dang sems nyon-mongs-pa # r byed-pa #  dang nyon mongs dang nye-ba # 'i phyir nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams so /
kOkRtya AdyAH catvAraH iti kOkRtyam midDam vitarkaH vicAraH ca
# 'gyod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin ni zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'gyod-pa #  dang gnyid dang rtog-pa-dang-dpyod-pa # 'o /
anyaTA api iti na kevalam ete upakleSAH eva kim tarhi kuSalAH api avyAkRtAH api iti / saH eza cEtasikAnAm piNXaH samAsatas ekapaQcASat Bavati / ezAm tu pratyekam svarUpam na prajQAyate iti praSnaH sparSaH katamaH / manaskAraH katamaH ityAdi / iha / cEtasikAnAm lakzaNataH eva nirdeSaH na karmataH yaTA anyatra saFkzepasya vivakzita tvAt
# gzhan-du #  yang ngo zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di dag nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  'ba'-zhig #  yin par ma zad kyi / / dge-ba #  yin pa dang lung du mi ston-pa #  yang yin pa'i phyir ro / / sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyi sdom 'di ni bsdu na lnga bcu rtsa gcig go / / 'di dag gi so-so # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo mi-shes-pa # s / / reg-pa #  gang zhe na / / yid-la-byed-pa #  gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dris so / / 'dir ni mtshan-nyid #  kho-na #  bstan gyi mdor bsdu-ba # r 'dod-pa # s gzhan nas 'byung-ba #  bzhin-du #  las ni ma yin no /
vayam tu karma api ezAm nirdekzyAmaH suKa avaboDa arTam / tatra pUrvam svarUpam eva nirdizwam prAc uddizwa tvAt / evam anyatra api yaTAsamBavam vAcyam
# bdag-gis #  ni bde blag tu rtogs-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro / / las kyang bshad-par-bya # 'o / / de-la #  rang-gi #  ngo bo ni sngar bstan-pa # 'i phyir sngar bshad de / / de-bzhin-du #  gzhan-yang #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du brjod-pa # r bya'o /
trika samavAya paricCeda eti prakRta indriya vizaya vijQAnAni trINi eva trikam / tasya kArya kAraNa BAvena samavasTAnam samavAyaH
# gsum 'dus nas yongs su gcod-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni skabs yin-pas #  dbang-po #  dang yul dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  gsum nyid gsum mo / / de rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # 'i dngos-po # s gnas-pa #  ni 'dus-pa #  ste /
tasmin satitatkAlam eva indriyasya suKa Adi vedanA utpatti anukUlaH yaH vikAraH tena sadRSaH vizayasya suKa Adi vedanIya AkAra paricCedaH yaH sa sparSaH / indriyam punar yena viSezeNa suKa duHKa Adi hetu tvam pratipadyate sa tasya vikAra Endriya vikAraH
# de yod-na #  de'i dus nyid na bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i tshor pa 'byung-ba #  dang mthun-pa #  dbang-po # 'i 'gyur-ba #  'di gang-yin-pa #  de-dang-'dra-ba #  bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  myong-ba # r 'gyur-pa # 'i yul gyi rnam-pa #  yongs su gcod-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de reg-pa # 'o / / dbang-po #  yang bye-brag #  gang-gis #  bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  ba la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyur-gyur-pa #  de ni de'i 'gyur-ba #  ste /
sAdRSyena indriyam spRSati indriyeNa vA spRSyata eti sparSaH
# dbang-po #  'gyur-ba #  dang 'dra-ba # s dbang-po #  la reg-pa # 'am dbang-po # s reg-pa # s reg-pa # 'o /
vedanA Asan niSraya tvam asya karma
# 'di'i las ni tshor-ba # 'i rten byed-pa # 'o /
evam hi uktaMsUtre suKa vedanIyam sparSam pratItya utpadyate suKa Avedana iti
# de-skad #  du mdo las kyang bde-ba-myong-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'i reg-pa #  la brten-nas #  bde-ba'i-tshor-ba #  'byung ngo zhes gsungs so /
manaskAraH katamaH / u vcetasaH ABoga eti / ABujanam ABoga
# yid-la-byed-pa #  gang zhe na / / sems-kyi-'jug-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'jug-par-byed-pa # s 'jug-pa #  ste /
Alambane yena cittam aBimuKIkriya tesacittasya ABogaH
# dmigs-pa #  la gang-gis #  sems mngon-du-phyogs-pa # r byed-pa #  de sems-kyi-'jug-pa # 'o /
sa punar Alambane citta DAraNa karmakaH / citta DAraNam punar tatra eva Alambane punar punar cittasya Avarjanam
# de ni dmigs-pa #  la sems 'dzin-pa # 'i las can te / / sems 'dzin-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  de-nyid-la #  yang-dang-yang #  gtod-pa # 'o /
etat ca karma citta santateH Alambana niyamena viSizwam manaskAram aDikRtya uktam na tuyaH praticitta kzaNam
# las de-yang #  sems-kyi-rgyun #  gyi dmigs-pa #  nges-pa # s yid-la-byed-pa #  bye-brag #  can gyi dbang-du-byas-te #  bshad kyi / / de sems-kyi-skad-cig #  re-re #  la ni ma yin te /
yat api atra nidarSanam ucyate samADi lABI manaskAra lABI iti ucyata eti tatra viSizwa manaskAra lABAt eva manaskAra lABI iti ucyate
# yid-la-byed-pa #  thob-pa #  ni ting-nge-'dzin #  thob-pa # 'o zhes gang smos-pa #  ni 'dir dper brjod-pa #  ste / / der yang yid-la-byed-pa #  khyad-par-can #  thob-pa # s yid-la-byed-pa #  thob-pa # 'o zhes brjod do; /
anyaTA hi sarva sattvAH eva manaskAra lABinaH syuH sarvezAMprati citta kzaNam manaskAra BAvAt / cetanA katamA
# gzhan-du-na #  ni thams-cad-kyi #  sems-kyi-skad-cig #  re-re #  la yid-la-byed-pa #  thob-pa # 'i phyir sems-can-thams-cad #  kyis yid-la-byed-pa #  thob-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur ro / / sems-pa #  gang zhe na /
guNataH dozataH na uBayatas / bcitta aBisaMskAra umana skarma iti guNataH / dkuSalezu Darmezu dozataH akuSalezu anuBayataH avyAkRtezu / aTa vA guNataH iti upakarizu dozataH iti apakArizu anuBayate iti maDyasTezu / citta aBisaMskAraH iti manaH cezwA / yasya aMsatyAm Alambanam prati cetasaH praspandaH Bavati ayaskAnta vaSAt ayaspraspanda vat
# yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa #  dang gnyi-ga #  ma-yin-pa #  la sems mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  yid-kyi-las #  so zhes-bya-ba #  la / / yon-tan #  ni dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams so / / nyes-pa #  ni mi-dge-ba #  rnams so / / gnyi-ga #  ma-yin-pa #  ni lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  rnams so / / yang-na #  yon-tan #  ni phan-'dogs-pa #  rnams so / / nyes-pa #  ni gnod-par-byed-pa #  rnams so / / gnyi-ga #  ma-yin-pa #  ni bar-ma-do #  rnams so / / sems mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni yid g-yo-ba # r byed-pa #  ste / / gang yod-na #  khab len gyi dbang gis lcags g-yo-ba #  bzhin-du #  dmigs-pa #  la sems g-yo-ba # r byed-pa # 'o /
Aha ca kzaNa antarAna avasTAnam nirvyApAram yayA manaH
# skad-cig #  gzhan-du #  mi gnas shing / / byed med yid kyang gang-gis #  ni /
savyApAram iva AKyAti sA manaskarma cetanA iti

citta aBisaMskAraH iti ukte manaskarma iti kimarTam / sarvEH eva ca etasikEH cittam aBisaMskriyate
# zhes gsungs so / / sems mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  zhes de-skad #  ces bstan na / / yid-kyi-las #  zhes ci'i-phyir #  bya zhe na /
teByaH vyavacCeda arTam manaskarma iti Aha vijQAnasya parispandA eva yaH DarmaH saH eva cetanA na anyaH iti jQApana arTam
# sems-las-byung-ba #  thams-cad-kyi # s kyang sems mngon-par-'du-byed-pa # s de'i-phyir #  gzhan dag las rnam-par-dbye-ba # 'i don-du #  yid-kyi-las #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  kun du g-yo-ba #  ltar byed-pa # 'i chos gang-yin-pa #  de ni sems-pa #  yin gyi / / gzhan ni ma yin no zhes shes-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
guNatodozataH anuBayataH citta aBisaMskAraH iti karma nirdeSaH
# yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa #  dang gnyi-ga #  ma-yin-pa #  la sems mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni las bstan-pa # 'o /
manaskarma iti cetanAyAH svarUpa nirdeSaH

aBilAzya eti aBipreta grahaNam anaBipreta inda aBAva jQApana arTam / evam ca cCandasya pratiniyata vizaya tvam jQApitam Bavati
# bsams-pa #  smos-pa #  ni ma bsams-pa #  la 'dun-pa #  med do zhes shes-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir te / / de-ltar-na #  'dun-pa #  yul so-sor-nges-pa #  nyid-du #  bstan-pa #  yin no /
darSana SravaNa Adi kriyA vizaya tvena yat aBimatam vastu tat aBipretam
# lta-ba #  dang mnyan-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bya-ba # 'i yul du gyur-pa #  la bsam-pa # 'i dngos-po #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni bsam-pa # 'o /

# de-la #  lta-ba #  dang mnyan-pa # r 'dod-pa #  ni don-du-gnyer-ba # 'o /
yadi aBilAzAtmakaH CandaH tRzNA CandayoH kaH prativiSezaH
# gal-te #  'dun-pa #  'dod-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin na de'i tshe sred-pa #  dang 'dun-pa #  gnyis bye-brag #  ci yod ce na /
tRzNA aBizvaFga lakzaNA
# sred-pa #  ni mngon-pa # r chags-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yin la /
CandaH aBilAza lakzaNaH iti asti viSezaH / sa cavIrya AramBa sanniSraya dAna karmakaH / aDimokzaH katamaH / niScite vastuni
# 'dun-pa #  ni 'dod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yin-pas #  bye-brag #  yod de / / 'di ni brtson 'grus rtsom pa'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / mos-pa #  gang zhe na /
taTA eva avaDAraNam iti niScita grahaNam / aDimokzasya sarva vizaya asattva prajQApana arTam
# nges-pa'i-dngos-po #  la de-bzhin-du #  nges-par-'dzin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la nges-pa #  smos-pa #  ni mos-pa # 'i yul yang thams-cad #  ma-yin-pa # r shes-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir te /
na hi aniScite vastuni taTA eva avaDAraNa samBavaH asti iti
# nges-pa-med-pa # 'i dngos-po #  la de-bzhin-du #  nges-par #  'dzin mi srid do /
yuktita Apta upadeSAt vA yat vastu niHsandigDam tat niScitam
# rigs-pa # 'am yid-ches-pa'i-lung #  gi dngos-po #  de-la #  the-tshom-med-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de nges-pa #  ste /
yena eva AkAreNa tat niScitam anitya duHKa Adi AkAreNa tena eva AkAreNa tad vastunaH cetasi niveSanam evam eva etat nAni aTa iti avaDAraNam aDimokzaH / sa siMha Arya tA karmakaH
# mi-rtag-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  gang-gis #  de rnam-par-nges-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  de nyid kyis dngos-po #  de-la #  sems 'jog-pa #  ste / / 'di ni de-bzhin #  te /
aDimukti praDAnaH hi sva sidDAntAt para pravAdiBiH apahartum na Sakyate / smRtiH katamA / saMstute vastuni / asampramozaH cetasaH aBilapanatti saMstutaH iti
# gzhan-du #  ma yin no zhes nges-par-'dzin-pa #  ni mos-pa # 'o / / 'di ni mi-'phrogs-pa #  nyid-kyi-las #  can te / / mos-pa #  gces su byed-pa #  ni phas-kyi-rgol-ba #  rnams kyis rang-gi #  grub-pa # 'i mtha' las 'phrog-pa # r mi nus so / / dran-pa #  gang zhe na / / 'dris-pa'i-dngos-po #  ma brjed-pa #  ste / / sems kyi mngon-par-brjod-pa #  nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  la /
asaMstute smRti aBAva pradarSana arTam
# 'dris-pa #  ni ma-'dris-pa #  la dran-pa #  med do zhes bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aMstutam ca vastu pUrva anuBUtam
# 'dris-pa'i-dngos-po #  ni sngon myong-ba # 'o /
asampramoza Alambana grahaNa avipUrNa aSakAraNam / tat pUrva gRhItasya vastunaH punar punar Alambana AkAra smaraNam aBilapana tA / aBilapanam iva aBilapanam aBilapanam eva aBilapana tA
# ma brjed-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  la 'dzin-pa #  chud-mi-za-ba # r byed-pa'i-rgyu #  ste / / de ni sngon bzung-ba # 'i dngos-po #  la dmigs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  yang-dang-yang #  dran-pa # 'o / / mngon-par-brjod-pa #  nyid ni mngon-par-brjod-pa #  dang 'dra-ba # s mngon-par-brjod-pa # 'o /
sA punar Alambana aBilapane sati na cittasya Alambana antarepa AkAra antare vA vikzepaH Bavati iti atas avikzepa karmikA / samADiH katamaH / upaparIkzye vastuni / cittasya ekAgrati upaparIkzyaH iti na anyatra
# mngon-par-brjod-pa #  kho-na #  mngon-par-brjod-pa #  nyid do / / de ni dmigs-pa #  mngon-par-brjod-pa #  yod-na #  dmigs-pa #  gzhan nam rnam-pa #  gzhan la sems g-yeng ba med-pa # s de'i-phyir #  mi g-yeng ba'i las can no / / ting-nge-'dzin #  gang zhe na / / brtag-pa'i-dngos-po #  la sems rtse gcig pa nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  la / / brtag-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzhan-du #  ma yin te /
evam ca / samADeH pratiniyata vizaya tvam uktam Bavati / upaparIkzya iva tuni guNataH dozataH vA / cittasya ekAgra tA iti ekAlambana tA
# de-ltar-na #  ting-nge-'dzin #  kyang yul so-sor-nges-pa #  nyid-du #  bstan-pa #  yin no / / brtag-pa'i-dngos-po #  ni yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa # 'o / / sems rtse gcig pa ni dmigs-pa-gcig-pa #  nyid de /
agram hi atra Alambanam ucyate / QAna sanniSraya dAna karma kaHsamAhite citte yaTA BUta parijQAnAt / upaparIkzyam vastu satya catuzwayam / guNataH niroDa satyaMmArga satyam ca
# 'dir rtse gcig ni dmigs-pa #  la bya'o / / sems-mnyam-pa # r bzhag na yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  / / yongs-su-shes-pa # 'i phyir shes-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / de-la #  rtag-pa # 'i dngos-po #  ni bden-pa #  bzhi ste /
niroDa sati aMSAnta Adya AkArEH upaparIkzyam / mArga satyaMnEryANika Adi AkArEH
# 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  la zhi-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  dang lam gyi bden-pa #  la nges-par-'byin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-brtags-pa # s 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  dang lam gyi bden-pa #  ni yon-tan #  no /
duHKa samudaya satye dozataH / duHKam anitya Adi AkArEH hetu Adi AkArEH samudayaH
# sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  dang kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa #  la ni rgyu la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-brtags-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa #  ni nyes-pa # 'o /
taTA nava anAMBUmInAm aDarAm dozataH UrDva aMguNataH
# de-bzhin-du # s dgu la 'og ma la ni nyes-pa # r lta gong-ma #  la ni yon-tan #  du'o /
evam anyezu api sAmAnya Alambanezu yaTAsamBavam vaktavyam / prajQA katamA / tatra eva pravicayaH
# de-bzhin-du #  rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  kyi dmigs-pa #  gzhan rnams la yang ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du brjod-pa # r bya'o / / shes-rab #  gang zhe na / / de-dag-nyid #  la rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa #  ste /
yoga ayoga vihitaH anyaTA ca iti tatra eva iti upaparIkzya / eva vastuni
# rigs-pa #  dang rigs-pa-ma-yin-pa # s bskyed-pa #  dang gzhan-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / de-dag-nyid #  la zhes-bya-ba #  ni brtag-pa'i-dngos-po #  nyid la ste /
evam ca samADi vat prajQA api pratiniyata vizaya iti uktam Bavati / pravicinoti iti pravicayaH / saMyat miTyA vAsaFkIrNa sva sAmAnya lakzaNezu iva Darmezu viveka avaboDaH
# de-ltar-na #  ting-nge-'dzin #  bzhin-du #  shes-rab #  kyang yul so-sor-nges-pa #  nyid-du #  bstan-pa #  yin no / / rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa # s kyang rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa #  ste / / rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  'dres-pa #  lta-bu # 'i chos-rnams #  la yang-dag-pa # 'am / / log-pa # r so-sor-rtog-pa # 'o /
yuktiH yogaH Apta upadeSaH anumAnam pratyakzam ca
# rigs-pa #  ni bshad ba ste / / yid-ches-pa'i-lung #  dang; rjes-su-dpag-pa #  dang mngon-sum #  mo /

# rnam-pa #  de gsum gyis bskyed-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni rigs-pas-bskyed-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  thos-pa-las-byung-ba #  dang bsams-pa-las-byung-ba #  dang bsgoms-pa-las-byung-ba #  ste /

# rigs-pa #  nges-par #  bsam-pa #  las skyes-pa #  ni bsams-pa-las-byung-ba # 'o / / ting-nge-'dzin #  las skyes-pa #  ni bsgoms-pa-las-byung-ba # 'o /
ayogaH punar anApta upadeSaH anumAna ABA soma miTyA praNihitaH ca samADiH
# rigs ba ma-yin-pa #  ni yid-ches-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i lung dang rjes su dpag ba ltar snang-ba #  dang log-pa # r bsam-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  te /
tena yaH janitaH saH ayoga vihitaH
# rigs-pa-ma-yin-pa #  des bskyed-pa #  ni rigs-pa-ma-yin-pa # s bskyed-pa # 'o /
tatra sAFKya vESezikA AdInAm Sruta mayaH cintA mayaH ca anApta upadeSa janita tvAt kutarka janita tva Adi yoga vihitaH
# de-la #  grangs can dang bye-brag #  pa la-sogs-pa # 'i thos-pa-las-byung-ba #  dang bsams-pa-las-byung-ba #  ni yid-ches-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i lung gis bskyed-pa #  dang rtog gi ngan-pa # s bskyed-pa # 'i phyir rigs-pa-ma-yin-pa # s bskyed-pa # 'o /
vIta rAgAnAm tu SASvata ucCeda vAdinAm ekatyaSASvatikA AdInAm camiTya apraNihita samADi janita tvAt ayoga vihitaH
# 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  rnams kyi rtag-pa #  dang chad-par-smra-ba #  rnams kyi dang kha-cig #  rtag-pa #  rnams kyi yang log bar bsam-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  las skyes-pa # 'i phyir rigs-pa-ma-yin-pa # s bskyed-pa # 'o /
upapatti pratilamBi kola ekika vyavahAra avaboDaH cana eva yoga vihitaH na ayoga vihitaH
# skye-ba # s thob-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-pa'i-tha-snyad #  shes-pa #  ni rigs-pas #  bskyed ba yang ma yin / / mi-rigs-pas-bskyed-pa #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'o /
eza casaMSaya vyAvartana karmakaH
# 'di ni som nyi bzlog-pa # 'i las can te /

# som nyi bzlog-pa #  ni shes-rab #  kyis chos rab tu rnam-par-phye-nas #  nges-par #  thob-pa # 'i phyir ro / / phung-po #  lnga'i rab tu byed-pa # 'i bye-brag #  tu bshad-pa #  / / ba ma po gnyis-pa #  / / dad-pa #  gang zhe na /
karma Pala satya ratnezu / maBi sampratyayaH aBilAzaH cetasaH prasAd / iti karma triviDam puNyam apuNyam AniQjyam ca
# las dang 'bras-bu #  dang bden-pa #  dang dkon-mchog #  la mngon-par-yid-ches-pa #  dang 'dod-pa #  dang sems-dang-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-la # s ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / bsod nams dang bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  dang mi g-yo-ba # 'o /
tatra apuNyam kAma Aptam eva akuSala mUla samprayogAt
# de-la #  bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  ni mi-dge-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i phyir 'dod-pa # r gtogs-pa #  nyid do /
puNyam api vipAka niyamAt kAma Aptam eva / karma vipAkam pratyaniQjanAda aniQjyam / apuNyasya kAmaDAtO= anizwaH vipAkaH puNyasya izwaH / aniQjasya rUpa arUpa DAtvoH izwaH eva vipAkaH / tatra karma PalayoH asti iti aBisampratyaya AkArA SradDA
# bsod nams ni rnam-par-smin-pa #  nges ba med-pa # 'i phyir 'dod-pa # r gtogs-pa #  nyid do / / rnam-par-smin-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  la g-yo-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir mi g-yo-ba # 'o / / bsod nams ma-yin-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  na mi-'dod-pa # 'o / / bsod nams kyi ni 'dod-pa # 'o / / mi g-yo-ba # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  na 'dod-pa #  nyid do / / de-la #  las dang 'bras-bu #  gnyis yod-pa # r mngon-par-yid-ches-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'i dad-pa #  ni las dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  yod-pa #  dang de-yang #  'bras-bu #  'dod-pa #  dang mi-'dod-pa #  dang go-rims #  bzhin no /
astikuSalam akuSalam ca karma tat ca yaTAkramam izwa anizwa Palam tat api kuSala akuSala karma hetukam na ISvara Adi nirmitam iti yaH evam karma Pala svarUpe aviparIte cakarma Pala vipAkayoH hetu Pala sambanDe aBisampratyayoH iyam karma PalayoH astitva sampratyaya AkArA SradDA
# de-yang #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-las #  kyi rgyu-las-byung-ba #  ste / / dbang-phyug #  la-sogs-pa # s sbrul pa ni ma yin no zhes de-ltar #  las dang 'bras-bu # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo phyin-ci-ma-log-pa #  las dang 'bras-bu # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  gnyis rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # r 'brel-ba # r mngon-pa # r yid ches ba gang-yin-pa #  de ni las dang 'bras-bu #  gnyis yod-pa-nyid #  du yid-ches-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'i dad-pa # 'o /
duHKa samudaya niroDa mArgAH satyAni
# bden-pa #  ni sdug-bsngal-ba #  dang kun-'byung-ba #  dang 'gog-pa #  dang lam rnams te /
AryANa aMpratikUla tvAt anitya tvAt tvena avitaTa tvAt ca Pala BUtAH paQca upAdAna skanDA duHKa satyam
# 'phags-pa #  rnams dang mi-mthun-pa #  dang mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nyid-du #  ma nor-ba # 'i phyir 'bras-bu # r gyur-pa #  nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po dag ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # 'o /
duHKa hetu tvAt pratyaya Adi AkArEH ca aviparIta tvAt Detu BUtAH te eva paQca upAdAna skanDAH samudaya satyam
# sdug-bsngal-gyi-rgyu # r gyur-pa #  dang rkyen la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i phyir rgyur-gyur-pa # 'i nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po de-dag-nyid #  kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa # 'o /
sa hetuka duHKa upaSama Atmaka tvAt SAnta Adi AkAra aviparIta tvAt ca duHKa niroDaH niroDa satyam
# sdug-bsngal #  rgyu-dang-bcas-pa #  nye-bar-zhi-ba # 'i bdag dang zhi-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i phyir sdug-bsngal #  'gog-pa #  ni 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa # 'o /
duHKa niroDa prApaka tvAt nEryANika tva AdinA avitaTa tvAt ca Arya azwa aFga mArgaH mArga satyam
# sdug-bsngal #  'gog-pa #  thob-par-byed-pa #  dang nges-par-'byin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i phyir / / 'phags-pa'i-lam #  yan-lag-brgyad-pa #  ni 'phags-pa'i-bden-pa # 'o /
tatra duHKa samudaya satyayoH asti duHKam asti samudayaH iti aBisampratyaya AkArA eva SradDA
# de-la #  sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba # 'i bden-pa #  gnyis la sdug-bsngal #  yod do / / kun-'byung-ba #  yod do zhes yod-pa # r mngon-par-yid-ches-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  nyid dang-ba # 'o /

ratnAni trINi budDa Darma saFGAH
# dkon-mchog #  ni gsum ste / / sangs-rgyas #  dang chos dang dge-'dun #  rnams so /
durlaBa tvAt mahArGa tvAt prIti kara tvAt upakAra kara tvAt amAnuza Adi upaGAta pratipakza tvAt ca ratnAni iva ratnAni
# dkon pa nyid dang rin che-ba #  nyid dang dga'-bar-byed-pa #  dang phan-'dogs-pa #  dang mi-ma-yin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gnod-pa-byed-pa # 'i gnyen-por-gyur-pa # 'i phyir rin-po-che #  dang 'dra-ba # s na dkon-mchog #  go /
tatra durlaBa tvam Bava Bogezu asaktEH kAya jIvita nirapekzEH boDisattvEH nErantaryeNa boDi samBArezu pravartamAnEH triBiH kalpa asaFKyeyEH budDa tvam prApyate iti durlaBam
# de-la #  dkon pa nyid ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  la ma-chags-pa # s lus-dang-srog #  la mi-lta-ba #  rgyun mi chad-pa # r byang-chub-kyi-tshogs #  la zhugs-pa #  rnams kyis kyang sangs-rgyas #  nyid bskal-pa-grangs-med-pa #  gsum gyis thob-par-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  na dkon pa nyid do /
atas eva udumbara puzpa prAdurBAva vat durlaBaH budDa utpAda Ocyate / budDa utpAdasya ca durlaBa tvAt Darma saFGa ratnayoH api durlaBa tvaMbudDa utpAda pratibadDa tvAt
# de'i-phyir #  sangs-rgyas-'byung-ba #  nyid ni au dum b'a ra'i me-tog #  'byung-ba #  dang 'dra-bar #  dkon pa zhes-bya'o #  / / sangs-rgyas-'byung-ba #  la rag-las-pa # 'i phyir chos dang dge-'dun #  dkon-mchog #  kyang dkon pa nyid do /

# rin che-ba #  nyid ni 'dod dgu mthar-phyin-pa # 'i gnas thob-pa #  rnams kyis bsod nams dang ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  gnyis-ka # s thob-par-bya-ba #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
tatra puNya samBAraH dAna SIla kzAnti pAramitAH tisraH

jQAna samBAraH prajQA DyAna pAramite

# bsod nams dang ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  kyi yan-lag #  gi dngos-po # r gyur-pa # s brtson 'grus kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ni tshogs gnyi-ga # r gtogs-pa # 'o /
Darma ratnam api sarva saMskRta parityAgena prApya tvAt mahA arGam
# chos dkon-mchog #  ni 'dus byas thams-cad #  yongs-su-btang-ba # s thob-par-bya-ba #  yin pa'i phyir rin che-ba # 'o /

# dge-'dun #  dkon-mchog #  ni 'khor-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  'grub-pa #  las khyad-par #  du gyur-pa # 'i phyir / / bsod nams dang ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  gnyis kyis thob-par-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  rin che-ba # 'o /
ratnatrayam hi darSana SravaNa anusmaranEH prIti hetu tvAt prIti karam
# dkon-mchog-gsum #  ni mthong-ba #  dang thos-pa #  dang rjes su dran na dga'-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir dga'-ba # 'i rgyur-'gyur-ba # s dga'-bar-byed-pa # 'o /
taTA aBigamana aDyupAsana anvezaNa parijQAnEH sattvAnAm upakAra karam
# 'di-ltar #  bsu ba dang bsnyen-bkur-bya-ba #  dang brtsal ba dang yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba #  rnams kyis sems-can #  rnams la phan-'dogs-pa #  yin-pas #  phan-'dogs-pa #  ste /

# ji-skad-du #  / / khyod-la #  bsu bas dpal du byed / / bsnyen-bkur #  byas-na #  bde-ba # r byed / / kun du tshol-ba # s blo-gros #  byed / / yongs su shes byed rnam-pa # r sbyong / / zhes-bya-ba #  brjod-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /

evam Darma ratna anusmaraNesaFGa ratna anusmaraNe ca vaktavyam
# de-bzhin-du #  chos dkon-mchog #  rjes-su-dran-pa #  dang dge-'dun #  dkon-mchog #  rjes-su-dran-pa #  la yang brjod bar bya'o /
tatra sarvasmin jQeye asakta apratihata jQAna Sakti lABAt ASraya parAvRttiH budDaH
# de-la #  shes-bya-thams-cad #  la chags-pa #  med cing thogs-pa-med-pa # r mkhyen-pa # 'i mthu brnyes-pa # s gnas-gyur-pa #  ni sangs-rgyas #  te /
sA punar sarva BAskara Darma bIja apagatA sarvAn Asrava Darma bIja pracitA ananta praBAva parigrahA cintAmaNi ratna vat anABogena aSeza sattva arTa karaNa samarTA iti
# de ni zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  kyi sa-bon #  dang bral-ba #  zag-pa-med-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  kyi sa-bon #  rgyas-pa #  / / mthu stobs mtha'-yas-pa # s yongs-su-bzung-ba # 'i phyir yid bzhin gyi nor-bu-rin-po-che #  ltar lhun-gyis-grub-pa # r sems-can #  ma-lus-pa # 'i don-mdzad-pa # r spyod-pa # 'o /
DarmaH triviDaH
# chos ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste /
deSanA DarmaH sUtra geya AdikaH / pratipatti DarmaH Arya azwa aFgaH mArgaH sa upacAraH / paramArTa DarmaH nirvANam / sa ca dvi prakAraH sa upaDi Seza UniH upaDi SezaH ca
# bstan-pa # 'i chos mdo'i-sde #  dang dbyangs-kyis-bsnyad-pa'i-sde #  la-sogs-pa #  dang sgrub-pa # 'i chos 'phags-pa'i-lam #  yan-lag-brgyad-pa #  'khor dang bcas-pa #  dang don-dam-pa # 'i chos mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'o /
tatra kleSa visaMyoga AKyaH sa upaDi SezaH
# de-la #  nyon-mongs-pa #  dang bral-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  dang bcas-pa # 'o /
vartamAna janma niroDe anAgata janma anutpAdaH nirUpaDi SezaH

azwO puruza pudgalAH saFGaH catvAraH pratipannAH catvAraH ca Pala sTAH
# dge-'dun #  ni skyes-bu #  gang-zag #  brgyad de / / 'jug-pa #  bzhi dang 'bras-bu-la-gnas-pa #  bzhi'o /
parasparataH SAstRtaH ca aBedya arTena saFGaH
# phan tshun mi-phyed-pa #  dang ston-pa #  mi-phyed-pa # 'i phyir dge-'dun #  no /
sarva guNa doza prakarza apakarza nizWA gata tvAt budDeH Bagavati romAQca aSru pAta Adi sUcitA prasAda lakzaNA SradDA
# yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa #  thams-cad #  mchog-tu #  phyin pa dang bsal-ba # 'i mthar-phyin-pa # 'i gnas-pa #  yin pa'i phyir / / sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  de-la #  spu-zing-zhes-byed-pa #  dang mchi-ma #  'byung-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s mtshon pa'i dang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni dad-pa # 'o /
sarva sa hetuka duHKa upaSama Atmaka tvAt prApaka tvAt tad dyotaka tvAt ca Darme prasAda lakzanA eva SradDA
# rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal-thams-cad #  zhi-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  dang thob-par-byed-pa #  dang gsal-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir dang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni chos la dad-pa # 'o /
