# dad-pa #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  du 'gyur te /
sati vastuni guNavati aguNavati vA sampratyaya AkArA sati guNavati ca prasAda AkArA sa tiguNavati ca prAptum utpAdayitum Sakye aBilAza AkArA
# dngos-po-yod-pa #  yon-tan-can #  nam yon-tan-can #  ma-yin-pa #  la yid-ches-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  dang yod-pa # 'i yon-tan-can #  la dang-ba # 'i rnam-pa #  dang yod-pa #  yon-tan-can #  thob-pa # 'am / / skyed nus-pa #  la 'dod-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'o /
nanu evam aBilAza AkAra tvAt tRzNA AcCandayoH anyatarA Bavati / na etat evam
# de-ltar-na #  'dod-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  yin pa'i phyir sred-pa # 'am / / 'dun-pa #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig tu mi 'gyur ram / / de ni de lta ma yin te /
kuSala vizaya tvAt na tRzNA SradDA pUrvaka tvAt Candasya na cCandaH
# dge-ba #  yul yin pa'i phyir sred-pa #  ma yin no / / 'dun-pa #  ni dad-pa #  sngon-du-'gro-ba #  yin-pas #  'dun-pa #  ma yin no /
cetasaH prasAdaH iti SradDA hicitta kAluzya vEroDikI iti atas tad samprayoga ekleSa upakleSa mala kAluzya vigamAt cittam SradDAm Agamya prasIdati iti cetasaH prasAdaH ucyate / udaka prasAdaka maNi sTAnIyam Darma antaram ca etasi kaMSradDA na rUpa prasAda AtmikA iti pradarSana arTam Aha cetasaH prasAdaH iti / cetasaH prasAdaH na rUpasya iti / sA punar Canda sanniSraya dAna karmikA / hrIH katamA / AtmAnam Darmam / vA aDipatim kRtvA avadyena lajjA / yat pratibadDA / yasya kriyAsu pravRttiH nivRttiH vA sa tasya aDipatiH svAmI iti arTaH
# sems-dang-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  la dad-pa #  ni sems kyi rnyog-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  de dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan na nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnyog-pa #  mi 'byung ste / / dad-pa #  la brten-nas #  sems-dang-ba # r 'gyur-ba # s sems-dang-ba #  zhes bya ste / / chu dang-bar-byed-pa # 'i nor-bu #  dang 'dra-ba # 'i chos gzhan sems-las-byung-ba #  la dang-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  / / gzugs dang pa'i bdag-nyid #  ni ma yin no zhes bstan-pa # 'i phyir sems-dang-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / gzugs ni ma yin no / / de ni 'dun-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / ngo-tsha-shes-pa #  gang zhe na / / bdag gam chos kyi dbang-du-byas-te #  / / kha na mtho-ba # s 'dzem-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang-la #  brten-nas #  su zhig bya-ba #  rnams la 'jug-pa-dang-ldog-pa #  de ni de'i dbang-du-byed-pa #  ste / / bdag-po # r byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
AtmAnam Darmam vA aDipatim svAminam kRtvA AsadBiH vigarhita tvAt anizwa vipAka tvAt ca pApam eva avadyam tena avadyena kRtena AkRtena vA cittasya avalIna tA lajjA
# dam-pa #  rnams kyis smad-pa #  dang rnam-par-smin-pa #  mi-'dod-pa #  yin-pas #  sdig-pa #  nyid kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  ste / / byas kyang rung ma byas kyang rung bdag gam chos kyi dbang-bdag #  por byas-na # s / / kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  des sems bag 'khums pa ni 'dzem-pa # 'o /
kula jQAna AdiBiH guNEH pApa kriyAyAm AtmAnam ayogyam matvA kaTam hi sA mama yA evaMviDena evam pApam kRtaMkriyate karizyate vA Darme api etat anizwa vipAka tvAt para upaGAta pravRtta tvAt ca garhitam iti evam yAtmAnam Darmam ca avekzamANasya Adyena lajjAsA hrIH / iyam caduH carita saMyamana sanniSraya dAna karmikA / apatrApyam katamat / lokam aDipatim / kRtvA avadyena lajjA / loke hi etat garhitam mAm
# rigs dang shes rgya la-sogs-pa # 'i yon-tan #  rnams kyis sdig-pa #  bya-ba # r mi-rigs-pa # r shes-pa # s bdag 'di-lta-bu # r gyur-pa # s sdig-pa #  'di-lta-bu #  ga la bya zhe'am / / byed-par-'gyur-ba #  lta-ga-la #  rung snyam pa dang mi-'dod-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  dang gzhan la gnod-par-byed-pa # r zhugs-pa # 'i phyir / / chos las kyang smad-pa # 'o / / zhes de-ltar #  ji tsam du bdag gam chos la lta zhing kha-na-ma-tho-ba # s 'dzem-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ngo-tsha-shes-pa # 'o / / 'di ni nyes-par-spyod-pa #  yang-dag-par-sdom-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / khrel-yod-pa #  gang zhe na / / 'jig-rten #  gyi dbang-du-byas-te #  kha-na-ma-tho-ba # s 'dzem-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'jig-rten #  na 'di ni smad-pa #  ste /
ca eva aFkarmANam viditvA vigarhizyanti iti aSloka Adi BayAt avadyena lajjate
# bdag la-la # s 'di-lta-bu #  rigs na smod-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'jigs-pa # s kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  la 'dzem-pa # 'o /
idam api duScarita saMyamana sanniSraya dAna karmakam eva / duScaritAt virati saMyamanam / lajjamAnasya apatrapamANasya vA kRte api duScarite avaSyam tat viramaNAt anayoH tad sanniSraya dAna karmaka tvam / aloBEti ayam akAraH trizu arTezu vartate / aBAve
# 'di yang nyes-par-spyod-pa #  yang-dag-par-sdom-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can nyid do / / ngo-tsha-shes-pa #  de ni nyes-par-spyod-pa # r byas-na #  yang gdon mi-za-ba #  spong-ba # s yang-dag-par #  sngom-pa #  yin no / / ngo-tsha-shes-pa #  dang khrel-yod-pa #  ni nyes-par-spyod-pa #  byas-na #  yang gdon-mi-za-bar #  de spong-ba # s yang-dag-par-sdom-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / khrel-yod-pa #  ni nyes-par-spyod-pa # r ma byas-na #  yang-dag-par-sdom-pa # s 'di gnyis ni de'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can te / / sngon-du #  'dren-pa #  nyid do / / ma-chags-pa #  gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  la ma chags zhes-bya-ba #  ni don rnam-pa-gsum #  la 'jug ste /
anyasmin pratipakze ca
# med-pa #  dang gzhan-pa #  dang gnyen-po #  la'o /
atra pratipakzaH eva vartate na anyasmin= aBAvaH iti pradarSana arTam Aha loBa pratipakzaH iti / evam adveze amohe ca vaktavyam / nirvid anAgrahaH iti tad svarUpa nirUpaNam
# 'dir ni gnyen-po #  nyid la 'jug gi med-pa #  dang gzhan la ni ma yin no zhes bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / chags-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos so; / / zhe-sdang #  med-pa #  dang gti-mug #  med-pa #  la yang de-bzhin-du #  brjod-pa # r bya'o / / yid 'byung zhing mi len-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i rang-gi #  ngo bo la rtog-pa #  mdzad-pa # 'o /
loBaH nAma Bave Bava upakaraNezu caAsaktiH prArTanA ca
# chags-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  rnams la kun du chags-pa #  dang smon-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
tad pratipakzaH aloBa veBavA upakaraNezu ca anAsaktiH vEmuKyam ca
# de'i gnyen-po #  ni ma-chags-pa #  ste / / srid-pa #  dang srid-pa # 'i yo-byad #  rnams la chags-pa #  dang mi-phyogs-pa # 'o /
nirvidBava Boga AdInAm parijQAnAt Bave Bava upakaraNezu cavEmuKyam
# yid-byung-ba #  ni sred-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  kyi nyes-dmigs #  yongs-su-shes-pa # 'i phyir srid-pa #  dang srid-pa # 'i yo-byad #  rnams la mi-phyogs-pa # 'o /
anAgrahaH Bava Bava BogayoH asaktiH
# mi len-pa #  ni srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  gnyi-ga #  la ma-chags-pa # 'o /
aTavA anAgraha viSezaNa arTam nirvidgrahaNam BaveBava upakaraNezu ca vEmuKya AkAraH yaH anAgrahaH ayam aloBEti / ayam caduScarita apravRtti sanniSraya dAna karmakiti / advezaH katamaH
# yang-na #  mi len-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gi phyir yid-byung-ba #  smos te / / srid-pa #  dang srid-pa # 'i yo-byad #  rnams la mi-phyogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'i mi len-pa #  de ma-chags-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / 'di ni nyes-par-spyod-pa #  la mi-'jug-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / zhe-sdang #  med ba gang zhe na /
dveza pratipakzaH mEtrI
# zhe-sdang #  gi gnyen-po #  ste /
dvezaH hi sattvezu duHKe duHKa sTAnIyezu ca Darmezu AGAtaH
# byams-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la zhe-sdang #  ni sems-can #  rnams dang sdug-bsngal #  dang sdug-bsngal #  gyi gnas kyi chos-rnams #  la kun-nas-mnar-sems #  pa ste /
tad pratipakzaH anAGAtaH
# de'i gnyen-po #  ni kun-nas-mnar-sems #  pa med-pa # 'o /
dvezasya anye api pratipakzAH santi iti atas Aha mEtrI
# zhe-sdang #  gi gnyen-po #  ni gzhan dag kyang yod-pa # s de'i-phyir #  byams-pa #  smos te /
mEtra AtmakaH dvezasya yaH pratipakzaH saH advezaH na anyaH iti
# zhe-sdang #  gi gnyen-po #  byams-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni zhe-sdang #  med-pa #  ste /
ayam api duScarita apravRtti sanniSraya dAna karmaka eti
# gzhan ni ma yin no / / nyes-par-spyod-pa #  la mi-'jug-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no /
amohaH katamaH / moha pratipakzaH / BUta sampratipattiH
# gti-mug #  med-pa #  gang zhe na gti-mug #  gi gnyen-po #  ste / / yang-dag-pa #  la yang-dag-par-rtogs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
sarve eva hi kuSalAH DarmAH klizwAnAm DarmANAm samudAcAra viroDAt pratipakzaH iti atas Aha BUta sampratipattiH iti / saMyaga viparIta pratipatti BedAt / sA punar dviviDA jQAnam pratisaFKyA ca
# dge-ba'i-chos #  thams-cad #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi chos-rnams #  kun du 'byung-ba #  dang mi-mthun-pa #  yin-pas #  gnyen-po #  yin te / / de'i-phyir #  yang-dag-pa #  la yang-dag-par-rtogs-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / yang-dag-par #  phyin ci ma logs par rtogs-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / shes-pa #  dang so-sor-rtog-pa # 'o /
punar caturviDA vipAka Agama cintA aDigamani mittA
# shes-pa #  yang rnam-par-smin-pa #  dang lung dang bsam-pa #  dang rtogs-pa # 'i rgyu'i bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-bzhi # 'o /
pratisaFKyA tu prajQA eva DErya sahitA
# so-sor-rtog-pa #  ni shes-rab #  bstan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  nyid do /
DEryam iti prajQA vIrya samADayaH ucyante
# bstan-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni shes-rab #  dang brtson 'grus dang ting-nge-'dzin #  rnams la bya'o /
tatra dvayoH prajQA dravyayoH samavaDAna asamBavAt vIryeNa samADinA vA samprayuktA prajQA pratisaFKyA iti ucyatA iyat balena anudDRtAn upahata kleSa bIjaH api kleSAnAm avakASat nadadati / ayam atra vAkya arTaH
# de-la #  shes-rab #  kyi rdzas gnyis 'grogs mi srid-pa # s brtson 'grus sam / / ting-nge-'dzin #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i shes-rab #  la so-sor-rtog-pa #  zhes bya ste / / gang-gi #  stobs kyis nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  ma bton ma bcom yang nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams kyi skabs mi 'byed-pa # 'o / / 'dir tshig gi don ni 'di yin te /
yaTA BUta jQAna AtmakaH pratisaFKyA AtmakaH ca jQAna viSezaH amohaH iti ucyate
# yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  shes-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  dang so-sor-rtog-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  shes-pa #  khyad-par-can #  ni gti-mug #  med-pa #  zhes bya ste /
ataeva amohoduH carita apravRtti sanniSraya dAna karmakaH / vIryam katamat / kOsIdya pratipakzaH / jkuSa lecetasaH aByutsAhaH vat k i / kutsitam sIdati iti / kusIdaH / tad BAvaH kOsIdyam / Alasyam iti arTaH / tat cakuSalA kuSalayoH cittasya anusAhaH
# de'i-phyir #  gti-mug #  med-pa #  ni nyes-par-spyod-pa #  la mi-'jug-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / brtson 'grus gang zhe na / / le-lo # 'i gnyen-po #  ste / / dge-ba #  la sems-mngon-par-spro-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la sbyor-ba #  dman-pa #  ni le-lo #  ste / / snyom-las #  byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go de ni dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  la sems mi spro-ba # 'o / / de'i gnyen-po #  ni brtson 'grus yin-pas #  /
tad pratipakzaH ca vIryam iti atas kOsIdya vat uBaya prasaFge vyavacCeda arTam Aha kuSale cetasaH aByutsAhaH vIryamna tu klizwaH iti / klizwe tu utsAhaH kutsita tvAt kOsIdyam eva
# de'i-phyir #  le-lo #  bzhin-du #  gnyi-ga # r thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  rnam-pa # r gcad-pa # 'i phyir / / brtson 'grus ni dge-ba #  la sems-mngon-par-spro-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / nyon-mongs-pa-can #  la spro-ba #  ni ma yin no / / nyon-mongs-pa-can #  la spro-ba #  ni smad-pa #  yin pa'i phyir le-lo #  nyid do /
nanu ca klizwam svaByaH tattvAt sva rasena eva pravartatekim tatra utsAhena / prAyeNa evam
# nyon-mongs-pa-can #  la shin-tu #  goms-pa # 'i phyir / / rang-gi-ngang-gis #  'jug bzhin-du #  de-la #  spro-ba # r bya ci dgos she na phal-cher #  ni de lta mod kyi /
asti tukiQcid yatra utsAhaH api apekzyate
# gang-du #  spro-ba #  la ltos-pa #  yang cung-zad #  yod do /
tat punar yat samprayogAt sannAhe prayoge vA alamIna tve vA avyAvRttO vAsantuzwO vA akuSalezu Darmezu cetasaH aByutsAhaH tat vIryam
# de-yang #  gang dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan na go-cha #  dang sbyor-ba #  dang; mi 'god-pa #  dang mi-ldog-pa #  dang chog-par-mi-'dzin-pa #  dang dge-ba'i-chos #  gzhan rnams la yang sems-mngon-par-spro-ba #  de ni brtson 'grus te /
kuSala pakza paripUraNa parinizpAdana karmakam
# dge-ba'i-phyogs #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa #  dang yongs su sgrub-pa # 'i las can no /
paripUraNaMyaTA mOla praveSaH
# yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa #  ni ji-ltar #  dngos-gzhi #  la 'jug-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
parinizpAdanam tasya eva parikarma kRta tvam / prasrabDiH katamA / OzWulya pratipakzaH
# yongs su sgrub-pa #  ni de nyid legs-par #  yongs-su-sbyang-ba # r byas-pa # 'o / / shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  gang zhe na / / gnas-ngan-len #  gyi gnyen-po #  ste /
kAya citta karmaNya tA
# lus dang sems-las-su-rung-ba #  nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  la /
dOzWulyam kAya cittayoH akarmaNya tA sa aFklezika Darma bIjAni ca
# lus dang sems-kyi-gnas-ngan-len #  ni las-su-mi-rung-ba #  nyid dang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i chos kyi sa-bon #  rnams ti go-rims #  bzhin no /
tad apagameprasrabDi sadBAvAt dOzWulya pratipakzaH
# de med na ni shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  yod-pa # 'i phyir gnyen-po # 'o /
lakzaNam tuprasrabDeH kAya citta karmaNya tA
# shin-tu-sbyangs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni lus dang sems-las-su-rung-ba #  nyid do /
tatra kAya karmaNi atAkAyasya sva kAryezu laGu samutTAna tA yatas Bavati
# de-la #  lus-las #  su rung-ba #  ni lus kyi rang-gi #  bya-ba #  rnams la ldang-ba #  yang-ba #  gang-la # s byung-ba # 'o /
citta karmaNya tA samyak manasikAra prayuktasya hlAda lAGava nimittam yat cEtasikam Darma antaram
# sems-las-su-rung-ba #  ni yang-dag-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  la zhugs-pa # 'i sems kyi sim-pa #  dang yang-ba # r 'gyur-ba'i-rgyu #  sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  gzhan-du #  gyur-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  ste /
tad yogAt cittam asaktam Alambane pravartate iti atas tad citta karmaNi atra iti ucyate
# de dang ldan na dmigs-pa #  la sems thogs-pa-med-pa # r 'jug-pa # s de'i-phyir #  sems-las-su-rung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
kAyasya punar sprazwavya viSezaH eva prIti AhRtaH kAya prasrabDiH veditavyA
# lus kyi reg-bya # 'i khyad-par #  dga'-ba # s zin-pa #  la lus shin-tu #  sbyang-ba # r rig-par-bya #  ste /
prIta manasaH kAyaH prasraByata eti sUtre vacanAt
# yid-dga' #  na lus-shin-tu-sbyangs-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes mdo las gsungs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
atra cEtasika aDikArAt acEtasikI api kAya prasrabDiH prasrabDi samboDi aFgatvena uktA kAya karmaNya tA vAcitta karmaNi tAm AvAhayati iti atas cEtasikI api kAya karmaNi atra uktA
# 'dir lus-shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  sems-las-byung-ba #  ma yin-du-zin #  kyang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i skabs yin-pas #  shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  yang dag byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  tu bshad do / / yang-na #  lus-las #  su rung-ba # n yid ni sems-las-su-rung-ba #  sgrub-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir te / / de'i-phyir #  sems-las-byung-ba #  ma yin-du-zin #  kyang /
iyam catadbalena ASraya parAvRttitaH aSeza kleSa Adi AvaraNa nizkarzaNa karmikA apramAdaH katamaH / pramAda pratipakzaH aloBaH yAvat vIryam / yAn niSrityA akuSalAn / DarmAn prajahAti / tad pratipakzAn= cakuSalAn DarmAn BAvayati iti / pramAdaH hi yena
# 'dir lus-las #  su rung-ba #  nyid-du #  brjod do / / 'di ni de'i dbang gis gnas-'gyur-ba # s nyon-mongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgrib ba ma-lus-pa #  sel-ba # 'i las can no / / bag-yod-pa #  gang zhe na / / bag-med-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  ste / / ma-chags-pa #  nas brtson 'grus kyi bar de-dag #  la gnas nas mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  spong zhing de'i gnyen-po #  dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams kyang bsgom-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la bag-med-pa #  ni /
kleSeByaH cittam na rakzati kuSalam ca hApayati
# gang-gis #  nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams las sems mi srung zhing dge-ba #  rnams 'bri-bar-byed-pa # 'o /
apramAdena punar kleSAn prajahAti pratipakzAn= ca DarmAn BAvayati iti atas apramAdaH pramAda pratipakzaH uktaH / aloBaH yAvat vIryam iti aloBAt veza amohAH saha vIryeNa gRhyante
# bag-yod-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams spong zhing de'i gnyen-po # 'i chos-rnams #  kyang bsgom-pa #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  bag-yod-pa #  ni bag-med-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r bstan-pa # 'o / / ma-chags-pa #  nas brtson 'grus kyi bar zhes-bya-ba #  ni ma-chags-pa #  dang zhe-sdang #  med-pa #  dang gti-mug #  med-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang bcas-pa # r gzung /
yAn aloBa AdIn vIrya paryantAn niSritya Agamya prApya akuSalAn DarmAn prajahAti iti anena sarve aloBa AdayaH apramAdaH iti uktam Bavati
# ma-chags-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nas brtson 'grus la thug-pa # 'i bar de-dag #  la gnas-pa #  ni brten-pa #  dang gnas bcas nas mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams spong-ba #  ste / / 'dis ni ma-chags-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  thams-cad #  bag-yod-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
akuSalAH DarmAH AsravAH AsravasTAnIyAH ca vizayAH veditavyAH
# mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams ni zag-pa #  dang zag-pa # 'i gnas yul rnams su rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra AsravANAm vinodana vizkamBaNa bIja samudDAra Atmakam prahANam
# de-la #  zag-pa #  rnams sel-ba #  dang rnam-pa # r gnon-pa #  dang sa-bon #  yang-dag-pa #  'don-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  ni spong-ba # 'o /
vizayANAm punar parivarjanena prahANam
# yul rnams ni yongs su spangs-pa # s spong ngo /
tad pratipakzAH iti akuSala Darma pratipakzAH
# de'i gnyen-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  kyi gnyen-po #  rnams te /
te punar kuSala sa AsravAH anAsravAH ca
# de-dag #  kyang dge-ba #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  rnams so /
tezAm aByAsaH BAvanA pOnaHpunyena sammuKIkaraNam
# sgom-pa #  ni de-dag #  goms-par-byed-pa #  ste / / yang-dang-yang #  mngon-du-byed-pa # 'o /
yasmAt vIrya sahItAn aloBa AdIn niSrityA kuSalAn DarmAn prajahAti tad pratipakzAn= ca DarmAn BAvayati tasmAt sa vIryezu aloBa Adizu apramAdaH prajQapyate iti anena sa aDizWAnA sa kAraNA ca apramAdasya prajQaptiH uktA
# 'di-ltar #  brtson 'grus dang bcas-pa # 'i ma-chags-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la brten-nas #  mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams spong zhing de'i gnyen-po #  dge-ba'i-chos #  kyang sgom-pa # 'i phyir / / brtson 'grus yan-chad #  dang bcas-pa # 'i ma-chags-pa #  la bag-yod-pa #  gdags te / / 'dis ni gnas-dang-bcas-pa # 'am / / rgyu-dang-bcas-pa #  la bag-yod-pa #  gdags-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
sa punar sarva lOkika lokottara sampatti paripUraNa karmakaH
# 'di ni 'jig-rten-pa #  dang; 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  thams-cad #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i las can no /
tatra lOkika sampattiH Bava Boga viSeza lABaH loka uttara aSrAvaka Adi boDi aDigamaH
# de-la #  'jig-rten-pa # 'i phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  ni srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  kyi khyad-par #  rnyed-pa # 'o / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  ni nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # 'i byang-chub #  thob-pa # 'o /
upekzA katamA
# btang-snyoms #  gang zhe na /
saH eva aloBaH yAvat vIryam / ityAdi apramAdaH iva atra api vyAKyAnam
# ma-chags-pa #  nas brtson 'grus kyi bar de-dag-nyid #  la gnas shing zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  bag-yod-pa #  bzhin-du #  'dir yang bshad-par-bya # 'o /
citta samatA AdiBiH triBiH padEH upekzAyAH Adi maDya avasAna avasTA Adi otitA
# sems-mnyam-pa-nyid #  dang zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  tshig gsum gyis ni btang-snyoms #  kyi thog-ma #  dang-ba # r dang tha-ma # 'i dus bstan to /
tatra laya OdDatyam cetasaH vEzamyam / tasya aBAvAt AdOcittasya sama tA
# de-la #  bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  ni sems mi-mnyam-pa #  ste / / de med-pa # s thog-mar #  sems-mnyam-pa-nyid #  do /

# rnam-par-mi-'tshe-ba #  gang zhe na / / rnam-par-'tshe-ba # 'i gnyen-po #  ste /
karuNA iti / vaDa banDa AdiBiH aviheWanam adrohaNa MsattvAnAm avihiMsA iti vihiMsA apratipkzaH / kam ruNadDi iti karuNA / kam iti suKasya AKyA / suKam ruNadDi iti arTaH / kAruNikaH hi para duHKa duHKI Bavati iti / iyam ca apramAda vat prajQaptitaH eva na dravya satI adveza aMSa eva prajQapanAt / viheWana karmikA / uktAH ekAdaSa kuSalAH / zaw kleSAH vaktavyAH / te ucyante rAgaH katamaH / paQca sUpa AdAna skanDezu snehaH aDyavasAnam / sa AsravANi

# nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga la zhen-pa #  dang lhag-par-chags-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i gzugs dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  lnga ni gzugs dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams so /

# de-la #  gzugs nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  ni khams gnyis kyi gzugs tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  bzhi ni khams-gsum-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / 'dis srid-pa #  gsum du srid-pa #  skye-ba # 'am / / yang-srid-pa # 'i las len-pa # s na /
upAdAna samBUta tvAt upAdAna viDeya tvAt upAdAnAni vA teByaH samBavanti iti upAdAna skanDAH / snehaH iva snehaH / yaTA hi tEla AdikaH snehaH vastra Adikam ASrayam anupraviSya vyApnoti mahatA api cayatnena sva ASrayAt durvivecyaH evam rAgaH api sva Alambanam anupraviSya eva vyApnoti mahatA api ca prayAsena tasmAt AlambanAt durvivecyaH iti snehaH ucyate / aDyavasAnaMtanmayatA
# sred-pa #  la nye-bar-len-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / nye-bar-len-pa #  las byung-ba #  dang nye-bar-len-pa #  la rag lus pa dang de-dag #  las nye-bar-len-pa #  rnams 'byung-ba # s nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams so / / 'jen pa dang 'dra-ba # s zhen-pa #  ste / / ji-ltar #  'bru-mar #  la-sogs-pa # 'i snum ras la-sogs-pa # 'i gnas la zhugs te mched pa shin-tu #  bsgrims kyang rang-gi #  gnas nas dbyung-ba # r dka'-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  / / 'dod-chags #  kyang rang-gi #  dmigs-pa #  la zhugs nas mched pa ni 'bad-pa #  chen-po # s kyang dmigs-pa #  de dang dbral-ba # r dka'-bas #  zhen-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /

# lhag-pa # r chags ba ni de'i-rang-bzhin #  nyid do / / yang-na #  reg-bya # 'i khyad-par #  la yang snum-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  yod-pa #  de dang rnam-par-dbye-ba # 'i phyir lhag-par-chags-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /

# cung-zad #  snyam pa'i nga-rgyal #  ni rigs dang shes rgya dang nor la-sogs-pa #  khyad ches 'phags-pa #  bas rigs la-sogs-pa # s bdag cung-zad-cig #  gis chung ngo snyam-du #  sems khengs-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /

# re-zhig #  mtshungs-pa #  dang mtshungs so snyam pa dang mtshungs-pa #  bas khyad-par #  du 'phags so snyam pa'am / / khyad-par-can #  bas kyang 'phags so snyam pa ni khengs-pa # 'i gnas yin-pas #  nga-rgyal #  du rigs na / / bdag chung-ba # r mthong-ba #  khengs-pa # 'i gnas su ci'i-phyir #  'gyur na 'di-ltar #  de-la #  nga-rgyal #  zhes bya zhe na /

# de-lta-bas-na #  yon-tan #  ma-yin-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  la bdag yon-tan #  dang ldan no snyam pa'o /
aguNavataH iti anena hidAna SIla Adi aBAve guNavat tvam aByupagatam Bavati iti atonirvastuka tvAt miTyAmAnaH ucyate / avidyA katamA / karma Pala satya ratnezu / ajQAnam / sA punar sahajA parikalpitA ca / tatra / sahaja anya kleSa asamprayogAt AveNikI / parikalpita avicikitsA miTyA dRzwi SIla vrata parAmarza Adi kleSa samprayuktA
# yon-tan #  ma-yin-pa #  dang ldan zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni sbyin-pa #  dang tshul-khrims #  la-sogs-pa #  med-pa # r yon-tan-dang-ldan-pa #  nyid-du #  khas-blangs-pa #  yin te / / de'i-phyir #  dngos-po-med-pa # s na log-pa # 'i nga-rgyal #  zhes-bya'o #  / / ma-rig-pa #  gang zhe na / / las dang 'bras-bu #  dang bden-pa #  dang dkon-mchog #  rnams mi-shes-pa #  ste / / de-yang #  lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  dang kun du brtags-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  gzhan dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma yin gyi ma-'dres-pa # 'o / / kun-brtags-pa #  ni the-tshom #  dang log-pa # r lta-ba #  dang tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'o / / las-mi-shes-pa #  ni bsod nams dang bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  dang me g-yo-ba # 'i las yod-pa # r mi-shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  ste / / mi rtogs-pa #  dang khong du mi chud-pa # 'o /
karmaNi ajQAnam puNya apuNya niQjya karma astitve yat ajQAnam apratipattiH anavaboDaH iyam sahajA avidyA
# 'di ni lhan-cig-skyes-pa # 'i ma-rig-pa # 'o / / bsod nams dang bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  dang mi g-yo-ba # 'i las yod-pa-nyid #  la the-tshom-za-ba # 'am /
puNya apuNya aniQjya karmA astitve vicikitsataH vA apavadataH vA na asti puNyam apuNyam AniQjyam ca iti paSu banDa agni praveSa Adi nivartane puNye apuNya saQjQinA vA apuNye puNya saQjQinAm yA vicikitsAmiTya adRzwi samprayuktA avidyA sA parikalpitA / sADarmezu SumiTyA niScaya vicikitsA saFkleSa utpatti sanniSraya dAna karmikA
# bsod nams dang bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  dang mi g-yo-ba # 'i las med do zhes skur-pa-'debs-pa #  dang bsod nams la bsod nams ma-yin-pa # r 'du-shes #  pa rnams / / phyugs gsod cing mer-'jug-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  byed-pa #  dang bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  la bsod nams su 'du-shes #  pa rnams phyugs gsod cing mer-'jug-pa # r byed-pa #  dang the-tshom-za-ba #  dang log-pa # r lta-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i ma-rig-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni / / kun du brtags-pa # 'o / / 'di ni chos-rnams #  la log-pa # r nges-pa #  dang the-tshom #  dang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / rtog-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  shes-rab #  ni lta-ba #  zhes bya ste /
prajQA nitIrikA AtmikA dRzwiH ucyate iti atolOkikI saMyagdRzwi Adi prasaFge dRzwiH iti satkAya dRzwi Adi kAH paQca dRzwayaH iha aBipretAH iti pradarSan= Aha paQca / dRzwayaH iti
# de'i-phyir #  'jig-rten-pa # 'i yang-dag-par-lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang lta-ba #  thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba # s / / 'dir ni 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  lta-ba #  lnga la bya-ba # r bzhed-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / lta-ba #  lnga ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tAsAMklizwa tva aviSeze api Alambana AkAra BedAt Beda pradarSana arTam punar api Aha satkAyadRzwiH anta grAha dRzwiH iti vistaraH / nsIdati iti sat / cayaH kAyaH
# de-dag #  kyang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  nyid-du #  bye-brag #  med kyang dmigs-pa #  dang rnam-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis tha-dad-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  smos so /
vinaSvare saFGAtA iyam dRzwiH / na Atmani na AtmIye ca iti jQApitam Bavati
# 'jig-par-'gyur-ba # s 'jig-pa # 'o / / bsags-pa # s tshogs te / / 'jig-pa'i-ngang-can #  mang-po #  la lta-ba #  'di ni bdag dang bdag-gi #  ba med-pa # r ming nyid kyis bstan-pa #  yin te /
AtmA hi nityaH ca ekaH ca Atma vAdiniH aByupagamyate / iyam ca anitya aneka vizaya tvAt na Atma vizaya iti uktam Bavati
# bdag ni rtag-pa #  dang; gcig-pu #  yin par bdag-tu-smra-ba #  rnams khas len la / / 'di ni mi-rtag-pa #  dang du-ma # 'i yul du gyur-pa # 'i phyir bdag yul-ma-yin-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
paQca upAdAna skanDAn ityAdi ye kecid SramaNAH vA brAhmaNAH vE AtmAnam AtmIyaMvA iti samanupaSyantaH samanupaSyanti te imAn eva paQca upAdAna skanDAn iti sUtre uktam / te hi svarUpataH kAryataH vE AtmAnam prajQapayeyuH / sAFKyAH cEtanya svarUpam AtmAnam manyante
# nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams la zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni dge-sbyong #  ngam bram-ze #  gang-la #  la dag bdag dang bdag-gis #  rjes su lta-ba # s rjes su lta-ba #  dag ni nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po 'di dag la'o zhes mdo las gsungs so / / de-dag #  gis kyang rang-gi #  ngo bor ram / / 'bras-bu # 'i sgo nas bdag tu 'dogs grang na / / grangs can rnams ni bdag shes-pa #  yod-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo yin par sems te /
te ca citta cEtasika praBede avidvAMsaH sakalam citta cEtasika kalApam eva cEtanyam iti AhuH / atas tecaturaH skanDAn AtmA iti pratipannAH rUpa skanDam AtmIya tvena
# de-dag #  kyang sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  la mi-mkhas-pa # s sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i tshogs nyid kyi spyir shes-pa #  yod-pa #  zhes zer te / / de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  gi phung-po #  bzhi la ni bdag yin pa dang gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  la ni bdag-gi #  yin par rtogs so /
na ca budDi vRttitaH anyat cEtanyam svasTa cittena aSakyate vaktum pratipattum vA
# blo'i 'jug-pa #  ma-gtogs-par #  shes-pa #  yod-pa #  gzhan zhig yod-pa # r ni sems kyi nyams tha-mal-pa # s brjod-pa # 'am rtogs-pa # r mi nus so /
evam vedanA AdInAm
# tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  yang de-bzhin #  no /
ekezAMca nirgranTAnAm jQAna svarUpaH AtmA iti tezAm AtmA AtmIya grAhaH anantara ukta eva drazwavyaH / vESezika AdayaH tu kAryataH Atma anaMvyapadiSanti / yaH paSyati yAvat manyate taTA yaH vedayateAnAti smarati cetayate vijAnAti ca saH AtmA iti
# gcar bu pa kha-cig #  ni shes-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo bdag yin no zhes zer te / / de-dag #  gi bdag dang bdag-gi # r 'dzin-pa #  yang gong-du #  bshad-pa #  bzhin-du #  blta-bar-bya # 'o / / bye-brag #  pa la-sogs-pa #  ni lta-ba #  nas sems-pa # 'i bar gang-yin-pa #  dang de-bzhin-du #  tshor-bar-byed-pa #  dang 'dus te shes-par-byed-pa #  dang dran-par-byed-pa #  dang sems-par-byed-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa # r byed-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  yin no zhes 'bras-bu # 'i sgo nas bdag tu ston to /
tezAm api cakzuH Adizu eva Atma aBimAnaH
# de-dag #  kyang mig la-sogs-pa #  nyid la bdag tu mngon-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  byed de /
yasmAt cakzuH vyatiriktaH yaH paSyati tasya aBAvaH
# ji-ltar-de #  med-pa # 'i phyir mig ma-gtogs-par #  lta-ba #  gzhan ni med do /
cakzuH vijQAne hi darSana samAKyA
# mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la mthong-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  zhes bya ste /
tasya asADaraNa kAraNa tvAt cakzuH paSyati iti vyapadiSyate
# de'i thun-mong-ma-yin-pa # 'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir mig gis mthong ngo zhes ston to /
tat yaTA nAdasya asADAraNa kAraNatvAt GaNwA rOti iti ucyate
# dper-na #  sgra'i thun-mong-ma-yin-pa # 'i rgyu yin-pas #  dril-bu #  'khrol lo zhes-bya-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
yatra tarhi cakzuzA rUpANi dRzwvA na eva sumanAH Bavati na eva durmanAH iti tatra kaTam / tatra api yatra Atma prajQaptiH samUhA santAne vA saH eva cakzuzA rUpANi dRzwvA iti ucyate
# 'o na gang-la # s mig gis gzugs mthong yang yid-dga'-ba # r yang mi 'gyur / / yid-mi-dga'-ba # r yang mi 'gyur zhes 'byung-ba #  de-la #  ji-skad #  bya / / der yang 'dus-pa # 'am rgyud gang-la #  bdag gdags-pa #  de-nyid-la #  mig gis gzugs rnams mthong ngo zhes-bya'o #  /
rUpa nirBAsatA eva hi rUpa darSanam yasmAt tad BAva aBAva rUpasya darSana AdarSane vyavasTApyete
# gzugs su snang-ba #  nyid la gzugs mthong ngo zhes bya ste / / 'di-ltar #  de yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  la gzugs mthong-ba #  dang mi mthong-ba # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
evam SravaNa Adizu api vaktavyam
# thos-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang de-bzhin-du #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
yatra tu uktam vedayate iti vedanA evam yAvat vijAnAti iti vijQAnam / tatra BAva mAtre kartR vyapadeSaH vijQAna vyatirikta vijQAtR pratizeDa arTam
# gang nas tshor-bar-byed-pa # s tshor-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  nas / / de-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-shes-pa # r byed-pa # s rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes 'byung-ba #  der yang rnam-par-shes-pa #  ma-gtogs-par #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  po dgag-pa # 'i phyir dngos-po #  tsam la byed-pa-po # r bstan to /
evam vedanA Adizu api vaktavyam
# tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang de-bzhin-du #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
aTa vA vizaya nirBAsa tAm upAdAya kartR vyapadeSaH yaToktam prAk
# yang-na #  ji-ltar #  gong-du #  bstan-pa #  bzhin-du #  yul du snang-ba # 'i phyir-byed-pa #  por bstan to /
na ca Atma lABa vyatirikta akriyA vidyate kzaNika tvAt sarva BAvAnAm kriyA kAle anavasTAnAt
# dngos-po-thams-cad #  ni skad-cig-ma #  yin-pas #  byed-pa # 'i dus na mi-gnas-pa # 'i phyir bdag thob-pa #  ma-gtogs-par #  byed-pa #  gzhan med do /
na ca akartRkA kriyA asti
# byed-pa-po #  med-pa # r ni bya-ba #  med do /
Atma lABa anantaram caBAvAnAm nirhetuka tvAt yadi vinASaH na syAt paScAt api nasyAt vinazwuH vinASasya ca paScAt AtmA atiSaya aBAvAt
# dngos-po #  rnams bdag thob ma-thag-tu #  gal-te #  'jig-pa # r mi 'gyur na ni rgyu-med-pa # 'i phyir phyis kyang 'jig-pa # r mi 'gyur te / / 'jig-pa #  po dang 'jig-pa #  ni phyis kyang rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu gyur-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sa hetuka vinASa parikalpe ca vinazwA eva tad vyatiriktaH vA avinASa hetuH parikalpyeta
# 'jig-pa #  rgyu-dang-bcas-pa # s yongs su rtog na yang 'jig-pa #  po nyid dam / / de-las-gzhan-pa #  zhig 'jig-pa'i-rgyu # r yongs su brtag grang na /
pUrvasmin pakza Atma lABa anantara MBAvAnAm vinASaH na eva vA asti vinASaH iti prasajyate / yaH anya nirapekzaH pUrvam yasya na kAraNam sa paScAt api tasya na eva kAraNam Atma atiSaya aBAvAt / itarasmin= api pakze vinASAnAm kAraNa niyamaH na syAt / kAryANAm iva tad vinASAnAm api kAraNa niyamaH Bavizyati
# phyogs snga-ma #  ltar na ni dngos-po #  rnams bdag thob ma-thag-tu #  'jig-pa # 'am / / 'jig-pa #  med-pa # r thal-ba # r 'gyur te / / gang gzhan la mi ltos-pa #  de ni sngar gang-gi #  rgyur ma-gyur-pa #  de rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu gyur-pa #  med-pa # s phyis kyang de'i rgyur mi-'gyur-ba #  nyid do / / phyogs cig shos ltar na yang 'jig-pa'i-rgyu #  nges-pa-med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / 'bras-bu #  bzhin-du #  'jig-pa #  rnams kyi rgyu la yang nges-pa #  yod do zhe na /
na etat evam kAryANAm hiparasparataH Binna svarUpa tvAt tad kAraNAnAm api Sakti BedAt niyamaH na viruDyate
# de ni de lta ma yin te / / 'bras-bu #  rnams ni phan tshun tha-dad-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo yin-pas #  de-dag #  gi rgyu rnams kyi nus-pa #  yang tha-dad-pa #  nges-pa #  yod-pa # r 'gal-ba #  med kyi /
vinASAnAm tu nirupAKya tvAt Atma atiSaya aBAve kiFkRtaH ayam niyamaH
# 'jig-pa #  ni dngos-po # r brjod-pa-med-pa # s rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu gyur ba med na nges-pa #  'di sus byas /
tasmAt sarvam vA avinASaNam sarva vinASasya na eva vA vinASa kAraNam asti iti pratipattavyam
# de-lta-bas-na #  'jig-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  rgyu thams-cad #  yin pa'am / / 'jig-pa #  la rgyu-med-pa #  zhig tu shes-pa # r bya'o /
vinASaH ca yadi vinASa kAraNAt pUrvam api astievam sati vinASa kAraNa vEyarTyam prasajyeta / BAvAnAm cavinASe sati utpattiH iti vinazwAnAm api utpatti prasaFgaH
# yang gal-te #  'jig-pa #  'jig-pa'i-rgyu # 'i snga-rol #  na yod-pa #  de-ltar-na #  ni 'jig-pa'i-rgyu #  don-med-pa #  dang dngos-po #  rnams kyang zhig bzhin-du #  skye-ba # s zhig zin-pa #  rnams skye-ba # r thal-ba # r 'gyur ro /
aTa vinASa kAraNeByaH pUrvam na vidyate evam sati BAvavat aBAvasya api prAgaBAvaH prajyate / yasya ca prAgaBAvaH tasya cAvaSyam BAva tvAt praDvaMsa aBAvena api Bavitavyam
# ji ste 'jig-pa #  'jig-pa'i-rgyu #  rnams kyi snga-rol #  na med na de-lta-na-yang #  dngos-po #  bzhin-du #  dngos-po-med-pa #  yang snga na med-pa # r thal-ba # r 'gyur ro / / gang-la #  snga na med-pa #  yod-pa #  de ni gdon-mi-za-bar #  dngos-po #  yin pa'i phyir zhig-nas #  med-pa # r yang 'gyur ro /
evam BAva aBAvayoH aviSezAt sarvam BAva Atmakam aBAva Atmakam vA prasajyeta / yadi ca praDvaMsa aBAvasya api praDvaMsa aBAvaH evam praDvaMsa aBAvAnAm anavasTAnAt tad kAraNAnAm api na izyata evam satiBAva praDvaMsa aBAvasya api na eva izwavyA dvayoH api Atma atiSaya tva aBAvAt / kriyA ca BAveByaH anyA ananyA vA aparikalpyeta / yadi ananyAH AtmA eva AtmanaH kartA karma ca iti nayujyate
# de-ltar-na #  dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  gnyis khyad-par-med-pa # 'i phyir thams-cad #  dngos-po # 'i bdag-nyid #  dam dngos-po #  med ba'i bdag-nyid #  du thal-ba # r 'gyur ro / / ji ste zhig-nas #  med-pa #  yang zhig-nas #  med-pa # r 'gyur na / / de lta na ni zhig-nas #  med-pa #  rnams thug-pa #  med-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir de'i rgyu rnams kyang 'gyur ro / / de-ltar #  mi 'dod na ni gnyi-ga #  yang rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu gyur-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir dngos-po #  zhig-nas #  med-pa # r yang 'dod-pa # r mi bya'o / / bya-ba #  yang dngos-po #  las gzhan nam gzhan ma-yin-pa # r brtag grang na / / gal-te #  gzhan ma yin na ni bdag-nyid-kyi #  byed-pa #  bo dang las su mi rigs so /
yadi ca labDa AtmakaH kriyAm karoti na asOtasya Atma BUtA / yaH hi yena vinA api Bavati na sa tasya Atma BUtoH yujyate / kriyA SUnye ca kartR tvam na yujyate / kriyA rahitAt cakri vyADi asitaH anyaH eva iti kaTam kartuH karmaNaH vA Atma BUta akriyA
# gal-te #  bdag thob-nas #  bya-ba #  byed na de ni de'i-bdag-nyid #  du gyur-pa #  ma yin te / / gang zhig gang med-pa # r 'byung-ba #  de ni de'i-bdag-nyid #  du gyur-pa # r mi rung ngo / / bya-ba # s stong na yang byed-pa-po # r mi rung ngo / / bya-ba #  dang bral-ba #  ni bya-ba #  dang ldan-pa #  las gzhan nyid yin na bya-ba-byed-pa #  po'am /
kriyA rahita tad aDyAsitayoH ca yOgapadyAt arSanAt pUrva vinASaH uttarasya utpAdaH aByupagantavyaH
# las kyi bdag-nyid #  du ji-ltar #  'gyur / / bya-ba #  dang bral-ba #  dang de dang ldan-pa #  gnyis cig-car-du #  ma-mthong-ba # 'i phyir snga-ma #  'jig la phyi-ma #  skye-ba # r khas-blang-ba # r bya'o /
aTa alabDa AtmakaH evam api tasya kartR tvam kriyAyAH catat Atma BUta tvam na yujyate dvayoH api asattvAt
# ji ste bdag ma thob na de-ltar-na #  yang byed-pa-po #  dang bya-ba #  yang de'i-bdag-nyid #  du 'gyur-ba # r mi rung ste /
kiMca ekasya kriyA rahita tvAt dvitIyasya kriyA aDyAsita tvAt kartR tva aBAvaH kartuH aBAvAt ca kriyAyAH api aBAvaH iti evam ca sva rasa vinASAt kzaNika tvam eva aByupagatam Bavati
# gnyi-ga #  med-pa # 'i phyir ci-yang #  ma yin no / / gzhan-yang #  gcig ni bya-ba #  dang bral-ba #  yin la cig shos ni bya-ba #  dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir-byed-pa #  po med do / / byed-pa-po #  med na bya-ba #  yang med do / / de-ltar-na #  rang-gi-ngang-gis #  'jig-pa # 'i phyir skad-cig-pa #  nyid-du #  khas-blang-ba #  yin no /
kartR karmaNoH anyA api kriyA na eva asti / kArakEH hi kriyA janyate / janya tvAt ca karma eva Bavati / na ca niHkriyam karma kartA vAyujyate iti avaSyam tatra anyayA kriyayA Bavitavyam / tatra api anyayA iti anavasTA kriyANAm kartLNAm ca
# byed-pa-po #  dang las gnyis las bya-ba #  gud-na #  yang med de / / byed-pa-po #  rnams kyis bya-ba #  skyed la / / bskyed-par-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  na las nyid yin no / / bya-ba #  med-pa # r yang las-dang-byed-pa #  bor mi rung ste / / gdon-mi-za-bar #  der bya-ba #  gzhan yong par 'gyur ro / / de-la #  yang gzhan yod-par-'gyur-ba # s bya-ba #  dang byed-pa-po #  rnams thug-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
aTa kriyA kriyA antarAm anapekzA janyate / evam tarhi dravyam eva kriyA antara rahitam janya tvena kim na izyate / kimarTa antara BUtayA adRzwa svarUpa sAmarTyayA kriyayA parikalpitayA
# ji ste bya-ba #  gzhan la mi ltos-pa # r bya-ba #  skyed do zhe na / / de lta na ni bya-ba #  gzhan dang bral-ba # 'i rdzas nyid skyed-pa # r ci'i-phyir #  mi 'dod la / / don-gzhan-du-gyur-pa #  rang-gi #  ngo bo dang nus-pa #  yang ma-mthong-ba # 'i bya-ba #  yongs su brtags-pa # s ci-zhig #  bya /
yadi ca kriyA kArakEH janyate na dravyam
# gal-te #  yang byed-pa-po #  rnams kyis bya-ba #  bskyed kyi rdzas ni ma yin na /
evam prAk praDvaMsa aBAvO kriyAyAH eva na dravyasya iti sarva dravyANi nityAni na eva vA santi iti aByupeyam
# de lta na ni snga na med-pa #  dang zhig-nas #  med-pa #  gnyis bya-ba #  la yod kyi rdzas la med-pa # r 'gyur te / / rdzas thams-cad #  ni rtag-pa # 'am med-pa #  nyid-du #  khas-blang-ba # r bya'o /
yadi cakArakeByaH anyA kriyA kriyA rahitam ca sADanam evaMkriyANAm anavasTAnam sADana aBAvaH vA / sADana aBAvAt cakri BAvaH api
# gal-te #  yang byed-pa-po #  rnams las bya-ba #  gzhan zhig yin na sgrub-pa #  bya-ba #  dang bral-ba # r 'gyur te / / de lta na ni bya-ba #  la thug-pa #  med-pa #  dang sgrub-pa #  yang med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / sgrub-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir bya-ba #  yang med-pa # r 'gyur te /
na hi asADanA kriyA asti
# sgrub ba med na bya-ba #  med do /
yadi ca gantuH anyAgatiH taNXuleByaH anyA paciH evam sati gantuH nadeSa antara prAptiH taNXulAnAm vA apacanaMpUrva avasTAtaH avikRta tvAt / aTa kriyA eva sva ASrayasya vikAra hetuH iti pUrva avasTAtaH vikRta tvam apratizidDam / vikAraH hi pUrvasmAt Atma atiSayaH / sa ca anya tva avinABAvI
# yang gal-te #  'gro-ba #  po las 'gro-ba-gzhan #  pa dang 'bras rnams las tshos-pa #  gzhan-du #  gyur na / / de lta na ni sngon-gyi-gnas #  las 'gyur-ba-med-pa # 'i phyir 'gro-ba #  po yul gzhan-du #  phyin pa med-pa #  dang 'bras kyang gnas-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / ji ste yang bya-ba #  nyid rang-gi #  gzhir 'gyur-ba'i-rgyu #  yin-pas #  sngon-gyi-gnas #  las 'gyur-ba #  ma bkag go zhe na / / 'gyur-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sngon-las #  rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu 'gyur-ba #  yin la / / de-yang #  gzhan-du-'gyur-ba #  med-pa # r mi 'byung ste /
tasmAt avaSyaMpUrva uttarayoH yOgapadya aBAvAt pUrva vinASena aBinnakAlaMuttarasya utpAdaH aByupagantavyaH
# de-lta-bas-na #  snga-ma-dang-phyi-ma #  gnyis cig-car #  yod-pa-ma-yin-pa # s gdon-mi-za-bar #  sngar zhig la dus-tha-dad-pa #  med-pa # r phyi-ma #  skye-ba # r khas-blang-ba # r bya'o /
evam kriyAyAH ASraya aBAvAt anavasTita tvAt kutas vikAra hetu tvam
# de-ltar-na #  bya gzhi-med-pa #  dang mi-gnas-pa # 'i phyir 'gyur-ba'i-rgyu # r ga la 'gyur /
tasmAt AtmalABa anantara vinASezu nirIhezu antar vyApAra puruza rahitezu upaQcasUpa AdAna skanDezu eva sadBAva mAtreNa prAgaBUtAnAm anyezAm skanDAnAm hetu BAvena vyavasTitezu nitya kartR BoktR grAha pUrvakaH ayam Atma AtmIya grAhaH na Atmani AtmIye ca iti
# de-lta-bas-na #  bdag thob ma-thag-tu #  'jig-pa #  can g-yo-ba #  med-pa #  nang na byed-pa # 'i skyes-bu #  med-pa # r nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po nyid yod-pa #  tsam gyis snga-ma #  med-pa # 'i phung-po #  gzhan rnams la rtag-pa #  dang byed-pa-po #  dang za-ba-po # r 'dzin-pa #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # 'i bdag dang bdag-gi # r 'dzin gyi /
Atma taAtmIya toca iti anta grAha dRzwitaH vyavacCinatti
# 'di bdag dang bdag-gi #  la ni ma yin no / / bdag dang bdag-gi # r zhes-bya-ba #  ni mthar 'dzin-pa # 'i lta-ba #  rnam-pa # r gcod-pa # 'o /
tsam anupaSyata eti niScinvataH / yA klizwA prajQA iti / na hi amUXasya anAtmani AtmA iti jQAnam Bavati
# yang-dag-par #  rjes su lta-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'o / / shes-rab #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni rmongs-pa # r ma gyur na / / bdag-med-pa #  la bdag-tu-'du-shes #  par mi 'gyur te /
atomoha samprayogAt viparyasta tvAt ca klizwA / tatra svasantati patitAn Atma tvena samanupaSyati parasantati patita anupAttAn= ca AtmIya tvena / yadA api svasantati patitAnAm eka deSam Atma tvena tadA itarAn api AtmIya tvena
# de'i-phyir #  gti-mug #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang phyin-ci-log #  tu gyur ba'i phyir nyon-mongs-pa-can #  no / / de-la #  rang-gi-rgyud #  du gyur-pa #  rnams la ni bdag tu yang-dag-par #  rjes su lta / / gzhan-gyi-rgyud #  du gyur-pa #  dang ma-zin-pa #  rnams la ni bdag-gi # r yang-dag-par #  rjes su lta'o / / gang-gi-tshe #  bdag-gi #  rgyun-du #  gyur-pa #  rnams kyi phyogs-gcig #  la bdag-tu-lta-ba # 'i tshe-gzhan #  la ni bdag-gi # r lta'o /
iyam casarva dRzwi gata sanniSraya dAna karmikA
# 'di ni lta-ba #  thams-cad-kyi #  rten byed-pa # 'i las can no /
tAm eva aDipatim kRtvA iti satkAya dRzwim
# de nyid kyi dbang-du-byas-nas #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  ste /
satkAya dRzwi balena tad utpatteH satkAya dRzwiH tasyAH aDipatiH
# 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba # 'i stobs kyis de'i 'byung-ba # 'i phyir 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  ni de-la #  dbang byed do /
SASvatataH ucCedataH vA iti / yat satkAyadRzwi Atma tvena / vastu Alambitam tat eva SASvatataH iti nityatas ucCedataH iti ucCedaH atra apratisanDikaH vinASaH
# rtag-pa # 'am chad-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba # s dngos-po #  gang-la #  bdag tu dmigs-pa #  de-nyid-la #  ste / / rtag-pa #  ni ther zug go / / chad-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la chad-pa #  ni 'dir nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba #  med-pa # r 'jig-pa # 'o /
samanupaSyataH yA aklizwA prajQA iti pUrvavat vAcyam
# yang-dag-par #  rjes su lta-ba # 'i shes-rab #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni snga-ma-bzhin-du #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
iyam ca maDyamA pratipad niryANa paripanTa karmikA / maDyamA pratipat SASvata ucCeda grAha varjita Mprati iti asamutpAda jQAnam / hetum vA apavadataH Palam vA kriyAm vA
# 'di ni dbu-ma'i-lam #  gyi nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i las can no / / dbu-ma'i-lam #  ni rtag-pa #  dang chad-pa # r 'dzin-pa #  spangs-nas #  rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  shes-pa # 'o /
sat vA vastu nASayata ityAdi / su carita Adi kamsugati durgatI mAtA Adi kriyAm arhat Adikam ca yaTAkramaMhetu Adik a m / kuSala mUla samucCeda karmikA kuSala mUla dRXa tA sanniSraya dAna karmikA ceyam / sA tu viSizwA eva na sarvA
# rgyu'am 'bras-bu # 'am byed-pa #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa #  dang yod-pa'i-dngos-po #  'jig-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  de-yang #  khyad-par-can #  la bya'i / / thams-cad-la #  ni ma yin no / / 'di ni dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba gcod-pa # 'i las can dang mi dge / / ba'i rtsa ba dam du 'dzin-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no /
dRzwi parAmarSaH katamA eti dRzwi AdIn / paratvena amRSati iti dRzwi parAmarSaH
# lta-ba #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la dam-pa # r 'dzin-pa # s lta-ba #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'o /
tAm eva catriviDAm dRzwim itisatkAya dRzwim anta grAha dRzwi miTyA dRzwim ca / tad ASrayAn= ca skanDAn iti
# lta-ba #  rnam-pa-gsum #  po de-dag-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  ni 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  dang mthar-'dzin-par-lta-ba #  dang; log-pa # r lta-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni lta-ba-po # 'i lus zhes-bya-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  dag ste /
ye / drazwuH Atma BAva saMSabditAH yAn ASritya dRzwayaH pravartantete tad ASraya agratas SrezWatas viSizwataH parama tA eti ete agra AdayaH SabdAH tulya arTAH / api uttara uttara vyAKyAna tvena upAttAH / ayaMAsat dRzwvA yaBi nive Sasa nniSrayadAn akar maka H
# gang dag la brten-nas #  lta-ba #  rnams 'byung-ba # 'o / / de'i-gnas #  la mchog dang gtso bo dang khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  dang dam-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mchog la-sogs-pa # 'i sgra de-dag #  don mtshungs mod kyi / / gcig-gis-gcig #  bshad-pa # 'i phyir smos so / / 'di ni lta-ba-ngan-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can te /
dRzwi lakzaNasya aBiniveSasya guNa rUpeNa grahaNAt tad aparityAga muKena sarva dRzwInAm ayam sanniSrayaH iti uktam Bavati
# lta-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  yon-tan #  gyi ngo bor 'dzin-pa # s de yongs-su-mi-gtong-ba # 'i sgro nas 'di ni lta-ba #  thams-cad-kyi #  rten byed-pa # r bshad-pa #  yin no; /
SIlam vratam tad ASrayAn= ca skanDAn iti
# tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  dang de'i-gnas #  phung-po #  rnams la zhes-bya-ba #  la /
dOHSIlya viratiH SIlam veSa vRtta kAya vAc pravRttiH niyamaH vratam
# 'chal-ba'i-tshul-khrims #  spong-ba #  ni tshul-khrims #  so / / cha byad dang tshul dang lus dang ngag gi 'jug-pa #  nges-par-byed-pa #  ni brtul-zhugs #  so /
yAn ASritya skanDAn SIlam vratam vA pravartate te SIla vrata ASrayAH skanDAH
# phung-po #  gang dag la brten-nas #  tshul-khrims #  sam brtul-zhugs #  'byung-ba # 'i phung-po #  de-dag #  tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  kyi gnas so /
kutsitAm dRzwim guNataH gRhItvA atatpUrvakam SIlam vratam vA paratvena AmRSati iti SIla vrata parAmarSaH
# lta-ba-ngan-pa #  la yon-tan #  du bzung nas de mngon du 'gro-ba # 'i tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  la dam-pa # r 'dzin-pa #  ni tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'o /
atas eva SIla vrata parAmarSAt dRzwi parAmarSaH pUrvaH uktaH
# de'i-phyir #  tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # s mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  sngar bshad do /
SuDyate anena vA pApa AcayanAt SIlena vratena ca iti SudDiH
# tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  'dis sdig-pa # 'i dri-ma #  sel zhing dag-pa # r byed-pa # s dag-pa # 'o /
mucyate anena kleSa banDAt iti muktiH
# 'dis nyon-mongs-pa # 'i 'ching-ba #  las grol bar byed-pa # s grol ba'o /
niryAti anena saMsArAt iti niryANam
# 'dis 'khor-ba #  las nges-par-'byin-pa # r byed-pa # s nges-par-'byung-ba # 'o /
niryANam eva anEryANikaH mokza mArgaH iti arTaH / samanupaSyata / iti nirUpayataH
# nges-par-'byin-pa #  ni thar-pa # 'i lam zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / yang-dag-par #  rjes su lta-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rtog-pa # 'o /
SIle vrate vA SudDi Adi AkArEH aBiniveSa AtmikA prajQA SIla vrata parAmarSaH
# tshul-khrims #  sam brtul-zhugs #  bdag-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  shes-rab #  ni tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'o /
klizwA tu viparIta Alambana tvAt
# nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ni phyin-ci-log #  tu dmigs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ayam caSrama vEPalya sanniSraya dAna karmakaH / vicikitsA katamA
# 'di ni ngal-ba #  'bras-bu-med-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / the-tshom #  gang zhe na /
satya Adizu yA vimatiH iti / Adi Sabdena karma Pala ratnAni gRhyante / dviDA matiH vimatiH syAt na syAt iti
# bden-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la gang yin gnyis za-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # s ni las dang 'bras-bu #  dang dkon-mchog #  rnams bsdu'o / / yin nam ma yin zhes som nyi yod-pa #  ni yid-gnyis-za-ba # 'o /
prajQAtaH ca iyam jAti antaram eva drazwavyA / sA akuSala pakza apravRtti sanniSraya dAna karmikA
# 'di shes-rab #  las rang-bzhin #  tha-dad-pa # r blta-bar-bya #  ste / / 'di ni dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la mi-'jug-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no /
kleSAnAm ca rAga AdInAm kati parikalpitAH eva kati sahajAH parikalpitAH ca iti Aha tisraH dRzwayaH parikalpitAH iti
# 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams la du zhig ni kun du brtags-pa #  kho-na #  yin / / du zhig lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  dang kun du brtags-pa #  yin zhe na /
eva iti / tAH tu pUrvAH api santi iti atas Aha paScimAH iti
# lta-ba #  gsum po de-dag #  ni gong-ma #  la yang 'gol bas de'i-phyir #  'og ma zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tAH punar miTyA dRzwiH dRzwi parAmarSaH SIla vrata parAmarSaH ca
# de-dag #  kyang log-pa # r lta-ba #  dang lta-ba #  la mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  dang tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'o /
nakevalam etAH eva parikalpitAH kim tarhi vicikitsA caparikalpitA
# 'di dag nyi tshe kun du brtags-pa #  yin par ma zad kyi / / the-tshom #  yang kun du brtags-pa # 'o /
SezAH saha jAH parikalpitAH ca iti uBayaTA / ke punar SezAH / rAga pratiGamAna avidyAH satkAya dRzwiH anta grAha dRzwiH ca / uktAH kleSAH upakleSAH vaktavyAH / te ucyante / vartamAnaMpratyutpannam nAnAgatam atItam vA / naH deva vyabinO= apakAram Agamya iti apakAram gRhItvA iti anena kroDasya vizayam nirUpayati / kroDaH hi apakAra vastuni eva vartamAnena eva pravartate na anyatra iti / cetasa AGAtA eti
# lhag-ma #  ni lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  dang kun du brtags-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnyi-ga # 'o / / lhag-ma #  rnams gang zhe na / / 'dod-chags #  dang khong-khro-ba #  dang gti-mug #  dang nga-rgyal #  rnams dang 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  dang mthar-'dzin-par-lta-ba # 'o / / nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams bshad-zin #  to / / nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams brjod dgos-pa # s de-dag #  bshad-par-bya # 'o / / 'phral du zhes-bya-ba #  ni da-ltar-byung-ba #  la bya ste / / ma-'ongs-pa #  dang 'das-pa #  la ni ma yin no / / gnod-par-byed-pa #  la gnas te zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnod-par-byed-pa #  gzung ste / / 'dis ni khro bo'i yul bstan to / / khro bo ni de-ltar #  nyid gnod-par-byed-pa # 'i dngos-po #  la 'jug gi / / gzhan-du #  ni ma yin no /
atra api vijQAna sambanDi tvam sva rUpam ca nirUpitam
# sems kyi kun-nas-mnar-sems #  pa'o zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang 'brel-ba #  can dang rang-gi #  ngo bo yang bstan to /
ayam ca AGAta sva rUpa tvAt pratiGAn na Bidyate kim tarhi pratiGAMSikaH eva pratiGasya aMSe viSeze prajQapta tvAt
# 'di ni kun-nas-mnar-sems #  pa'i rang-bzhin #  yin-pas #  khong-khro-ba #  dang tha-dad-pa #  ma yin mod kyi / / 'di ni khong-khro-ba # 'i cha'i khyad-par #  la btags-pa # 'i phyir khong-khro-ba # 'i char gtogs-pa #  nyid de /
vartamAnam apakAram aDikRtya yaH cetasaH AGAtaH sattva asattva vizaya udaNXa AdAna Adi sanniSraya dAna karmakaH ca sa kroDaH iti prajQapyate
# 'phral du gnod-par-byed-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  sems-can #  dang sems-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i yul la sems kyi kun-nas-mnar-sems #  pa'o / / dbyug-pa #  len-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can gang-yin-pa #  de khro-ba #  zhes gdags so /
kroDAt UrDvam mama anena idam apakRtam iti etasya vEra Atmakasya ASayasya anubanDaH anutsargaH / prabanDena pravartanam upanAhaH / akzAnti sanniSraya dAna karmakaH / akzAntiH apakAra amarzaNaMprati apakAra cikIrzA iti arTaH
# khros-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  'dis bdag-la-gnod-pa #  'di byas so zhes shar gnyer ba'i bdag-nyid #  de'i mdud-pa # r 'dzin-pa #  mi-gtong-ba # r rgyun-du #  'byung pa ni kho-na #  du 'dzin-pa #  ste / / mi-bzod-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / mi-bzod-pa #  ni gnod-par-byed-pa #  la ji-mi-snyam-pa # r mi byed kyi / / phyir gnod-pa #  byed 'dod ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
ayam ca kroDa vat pradveza avasTA viSeze prajQapyate iti prajQapti san veditavyaH
# 'di yang khro-ba #  bzhin-du #  zhe-sdang #  gi gnas kyi khyad-par #  la btags-pa #  yin-pas #  btags-pa'i-yod-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
Canda dveza Baya AdIn= tiraskRtya kAle tat hita eziNA ca udakena tvam eva aFkArI iti anuyuktasya moha aMSikya vat yava pracCAdana AmrakzaH / moha aMSika tvam tu / mrak zasi Avac CAd anAk Arat vAt
# 'chags-pa #  ni 'dun-pa #  dang zhe-sdang #  dang 'jigs ba la sog pa bsal te / / de-la #  phan-pa # r 'dod-pa # 'i gleng-bar-byed-pa # s dus-su #  khyod 'di-lta-bu #  byed-pa # 'o zhes bsnyad-pa #  la gti-mug #  gi char gtogs-pa # s kha na ma thob ma khyud pa'o / / 'chab-pa #  ni kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  mkhyud pa'i rnam-pa #  yin-pas #  gti-mug #  gi char gtogs-pa #  nyid de /
kOkRtyA sparSa vihAra sanniSraya dAna karmakaH / Darma tEzAyat avadyam pracCAdayataH kOkRtyam
# 'di ni 'gyod-pa #  dang reg-pa # r mi-gnas-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / 'di ni chos-nyid #  yin te / / 'di-ltar #  kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  mkhyud na 'gyod-pa # r 'gyur ro /
kOkRtyAt ca avaSyaMdOH manasyena samprayogAt asparSa vihAraH iti / caNXam vacaH pragAXam pAruzyam marma Gawwana yogena / daSana SIlaH dASI / tad BAvaH dASitA / ayam ca BAva pratyayaH svArTikaH / caNXena vacasA pradaSati iti caNXa vacA udASitA
# 'gyod-na #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # r 'gyur-ba # s reg-pa # r mi gnas so / / tshig-brlang-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mtshang-'bru-ba # 'i tshul-gyis #  zhe-gcod-pa #  dang tshig rtsub po zher-'debs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i ngang tshul ni zher-'debs-pa #  ste / / de'i dngos-po #  ni zher-'debs-pa #  nyid do / / tshig-brlang-po # s za-ba #  dang 'dra-bar #  tshig-brlang-po # r zher-'debs-pa #  nyid ni 'tshig-pa # 'o /
pradASaH / ayam cakroDa upanAha pUrvaFgamaH cetasa AGAta svaBAvaH iti pratiGAMSika eva iti na dravyataH vidyate
# 'di yang khro-ba #  dang kho-na #  du 'dzin-pa #  sngon-du-'gro-ba #  sems kyi kun-nas-mnar-sems #  pa'i rang-bzhin #  yin-pas #  khong-khro-ba # 'i char gtogs-pa #  nyid de / / rdzas-su-yod-pa #  ni ma yin no /
ayam cavAgduH carita prasavana karmakaH asparSa vihAra karmakaH ca / tat vataH pudgalasya duHsaMvAsa tvAt
# 'di ni ngag-gi-nyes-pa # r sbyong-ba #  skyed-pa # 'i las can dang reg-pa # r mi-gnas-pa # 'i las can te de dang ldan-pa # 'i gang-zag #  dang 'grogs-pa # r dka'-ba # 'i phyir ro /
ABasatkAra kula SIla Sruta AdIn guNAn upalaBya dveza aMSikaH hcetasaH vyArozaH IrzyA / svam ASayam vyApya rozaH
# phrag-dog #  ni rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  dang tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  dang rigs dang tshul-khrims #  dang thos-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i yon-tan #  mthong-nas #  zhe-sdang #  gi char mngon-pa # r gtogs-pa # 'i sems khong nas 'khrugs-pa #  ste /
vyArozaH / dOrmanasya samprayogAt tad pUrvakaH ca asparSa vihAra iti dOrmanasya asparSa vihAra karmikA
# rang-gi #  bsam-pa #  la khyab-pa # r 'khrugs-pa # s khong nas 'khrugs-pa # 'o / / 'di ni yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang reg-pa # r mi-gnas-pa # 'i las can no /
upAttam vastu Darma Amiza kOSala Atmakam yena pUjA anugraha kAmyayA arTine anarTine vA dIyate tat dAnam / tasmin sati dAna aBAvAt tad viroDi iti ucyate
# zin-pa # 'i dngos-po #  chos dang zang-zing #  dang mkhas-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  rnams gang-gi-phyir #  mchod-pa #  dang phan-'dogs-pa # r 'dod-pa # s 'dod-pa # 'am / / mi-'dod-pa #  la yang rung ste sbyin-par-byed-pa #  de ni sbyin-pa # 'o / / de yod-na #  sbyin-pa #  med-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir de dang mi-mthun-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
lABa satkAra aDyavasitasya jIvita upakaraNezu rAga aMSikaH cetasaH AgrahaH aparityAga icCA mAtsaryam
# rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  la zhen nas 'tsho-ba'i-yo-byad #  rnams la 'dod-chags #  kyi shas kyis sems-kyis #  kun-tu-'dzin-pa #  dang yongs-su-mi-gtong-ba # r 'dod-pa #  ni ser-sna # 'o /
idaMA saMleKa sanniSraya dAna karmakam
# 'di ni yo-byad #  ma bsnyungs-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no /
asaMleKaH punar mAtsaryeNa anupayujyamAnAnAm api upakaraNAnAm sannicayAt veditavyaH pad
# yo-byad #  ma bsnyungs-pa #  ni ser-sna # s yo-byad #  mi mkho ba rnams kyang sogs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rgyu gang zhe na /
mAyA para vaQcanAya aBUta arTa sandarSanA / lABa satkAra aDyavasitasya para vaQcana aBiprAyeNa anyaTA vyavasTitasya SIla AdeH arTasya anyaTA prakASanA
# gzhan la slu-ba # 'i yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i don ston-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  la lhag-par-chags-pa # s gzhan la slu-ba # 'i bsam-pa # s tshul-khrims #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don gzhan-du #  gnas la gnas gzhan-du #  ston-pa #  ste /
iyam cayAByAm rAga mohAByAm aBUtAn guNAn prakASayate tayoH samuditayoH prajQapyate iti kroDa Adi vat prajQaptitaH eva na dravyataH / miTyAjIva sanniSraya dAna karmikA
# 'di ni 'dod-chags #  dang gti-mug #  gnyis kyis yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i yon-tan #  ston-pa # s na de gnyis 'dus-pa #  la gdags te / / khro bo la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  btags-pa #  nyid yin gyi / / rdzas su ni med do / / log-pa # s 'tsho-ba # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can te /
kAya vAc kuhana upAttAH SayyA Asana AdayaH upajIvyante na cavyAyAma labDAH iti miTyAjIvaH ucyate / SAWyam katamat / sva doza pracCAdana upAya saFgRhItaMcetasaH kOwilyam
# lus dang ngag gi tshul-'chos-pa # s zin-pa # 'i mal-cha #  la-sogs-pa #  nye-bar #  'tsho'i / / yang-dag-pa # 'i rtsol bas rnyed-pa # s ni ma-yin-pa #  ni log-pa # s 'tsho-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  / / g-yo gang zhe na / / bdag-gi-nyes-pa #  bcab pa'i thabs bzung-ba #  ste /
sva doza pracCAdana upAyaH / para vyAmohanam / tat punar anyena anyat pratisarati kzipati aparisaPuwam vA pratipadyate / atas eva SAWyam mrakzAt Bidyate / sa hi parisPuwam eva pracCAdayati / sva doza pracCAdana upAya saFgrahaH tad nimitta tvAt
# sems gya-gyu #  ba'o zhes-bya-ba #  la bdag-gi-nyes-pa #  bcab pa'i thabs ni gzhan mgo rmongs-pa # r byed-pa #  ste / / de-yang #  gzhan nas gzhan-du #  bsgyur zhing gtam rlung skur ba dang bsal-ba # r mi-byed-pa # 'o / / de'i-phyir #  g-yo dang 'chab-pa #  gnyis tha dad de / / de ni dngos su mkhyud par byed-pa # 'o / / 'di ni bdag-gi-nyes-pa #  bcab pa'i thabs bzung-ba #  ste / / de'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
cetasaH kOwilyam vaFkatA yasya yogAt cittam Rju mArgam na pratipadyate
# sems gya-gyu #  ba ni mi drang-ba #  ste / / de dang ldan na sems lam drang-po # r mi 'jug go /
idam cala ABa satkAra aDyavasitaH yAByAMrAga moha aByaMsu adoza pracCAdana arTam paramohanAya pravartate tayoH eva sahitayoH tat prajQapyate
# 'di ni rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  la lhag-pa # r chags-na # s 'dod-chags #  dang gti-mug #  de gnyis kyi bdag-gi-nyes-pa #  bcab pa'i phyir mgo rmongs-pa # r byed-pa # s de gnyis 'dus-pa #  la de gdags so /
idam ca zsaMyaga vavAda lABa paripanTa karmakam
# 'di ni yang-dag-pa # 'i gdams-ngag #  rnyed-pa # 'i bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i las can no /
saMyaga vavAde yolABaH yoniSas manaskAraH tasya antarAyam karoti iti
# yang-dag-pa # 'i gdams-ngag #  ni gang rnyed na tshul-bzhin #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ste / / de'i bar-chad-byed-pa # 'o /
madaH sva sampattO raktasya udDarzaH
# rgyags pa gang zhe na / / bdag-gi #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  la chags-pa # 'i bar-du #  dga'-ba #  ste /
cetasaH paryAdAnam / kula Arogya rUpa yOvana bala ESvarya budDimeDa Adi prakarzaH sva sampattiH
# sems yongs-su-'dzin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni rigs dang nad-med-pa #  dang gzugs dang lang-tsho-la-bab-pa #  dang stobs dang phyug-pa #  dang blo dang yid-gzhungs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mchog-tu-gyur-pa #  ni rang-gi #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa # 'o /
udDarzaH harza viSezaH
# rab-tu-dga'-ba #  ni dga'-ba # 'i bye-brag #  go /
harza viSezam eva vyAcazwe cetasaH paryAdAnam iti
# sems yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # s ni dga'-ba # 'i bye-brag #  nyid ston te /
yena harza viSezeNa cittam asvatantrIkRtam tena tat Atma tantrI karaNAt paryAttam Bavati iti atas uktam cetasaH paryAdAnam iti
# dga'-ba # 'i bye-brag #  gang-gis #  sems rang-dbang-med-pa # r byed-pa #  des de bdag-gi #  dbang du bya-ba-byed-pa # s yongs-su-'dzin-pa # r 'gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  sems yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  zhes bshad do /
eza saFkzepaH harza viSeza sahitaH tRzNA prakAraH madaH iti
# 'dir ni mdor-na #  dga'-ba # 'i bye-brag #  dang ldan-pa # 'i sred-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  la rgyags pa zhes-bya'o #  /
ayam ca esarva kleSa upakleSa sanniSraya dAna karmakaH
# 'di ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  rten byed-pa # 'i las can no /
viviDEH vaDa banDana tA AXana tarjana AdiBiH sattvAnAm hiMsA vihiMsA
# rnam-par-'tshe-ba #  ni / / gsad-pa #  dang bcing-ba #  dang brdeg-pa #  dang bsdigs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gnod-pa #  sna-tshogs #  kyis / / sems-can #  rnams la 'tshe-ba # s rnam-par-'tshe-ba #  ste /
viheWyante anayA sattvAH vaDa banDana AdiBiH / duHKa dOrmanasya utpAdanAt iti viheWanA
# 'dis gsad-pa #  dang bcing-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s sems-can #  rnams la rnam-par-tho-'tshams-pa # s sdug-bsngal #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  skyed-pa # 'i phyir / / rnam-par-tho-'tshams-pa # 'o /
sA punar pratiGA aMSikA nirGRNatA nizkaruNa tA nirdaya tA Aca
# de ni khong-khro-ba # 'i char gtogs-pa #  ste / / snying brtse ba med-pa #  dang snying-rje-med-pa #  dang brtse ba med-pa # 'o /
etAH ca nirGRNata AdayaH svayam vaDa Adim kurvataH kArayataH parEH ca kriyamANAn dRzwvA SrutvA vA anumodataH ca yaTA kramaMbodDavyAH uttarottara vyAKyAnataH vA
# snying brtse ba med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  'di dag kyang gsod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bdag-nyid-kyis-byed-pa #  dang byed-du-'jug-pa #  dang gzhan dag byed-pa #  mthong ngam; thos-na #  rjes-su-yi-rang-ba #  rnams dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  sbyar-ba # r shes-pa # r bya'o / / yang-na #  gcig-gis-gcig #  bshad do /
eza tu saFkzepaH pratiGAMSikA sattvezu citta rUkza tA sattva viheWana karmikA vihiMsA iti ucyate / na asya hrIH asti iti ahrIH / sa yat yogAt evam ucya dehrI vipakza BUtam tat AhrIkyam / tasmin karmaNi / Atmanam ayogyam avekzyamANasya apivAdyena alajjA sArIkyam / apatrapate anayA iti apatrApyam / tat viparItam anapatrApyam / loka SAstra virudDam etat mayA kriyata / iti evam avagacCataH api yAnayA pApa kriyayA alajjA Asana patra Apyam / etat ca dvayam apisarvaH akle Sopa kleS asAh Ayya karm akam / rAga dveza moha prakArezu sarva satkAya prasava hetuzu rAga dvezayoH ayOgapadyAt yaTAsamBavam prajQapyate na svatantre staH iti / styAnaMcittA karmaNya tA / paryAya antareNa vyAcazwe / rstEmityam iti
# 'di ni mdor-na #  khong-khro-ba # 'i char gtogs-pa #  ste / / sems-can #  rnams la sems rtsub pa dang sems-can #  rnams la rnam-pa # r tho 'tshams ba'i las can ni rnam-par-'tshe-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  / / ngo-tsha-med-pa #  ni 'di-la #  ngo-tsha-med-pa #  ste / / de gang dang ldan na de-skad #  ces bya-ba #  de ngo-tsha-shes-pa # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  su gyur-pa #  ni ngo-tsha-med-pa #  ste / / las de bdag-gi #  cha ma yi na shes kyang gang kha na mtho pas mi 'dzem-pa #  de ngo-tsha-med-pa # 'o / / 'dis khrel ltas byed-pa # s khrel-yod-pa # s te / / de-las-bzlog-pa #  ni khred med-pa # 'o / / 'di gnyis ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  grogs-byed-pa # 'i las can no / / bya-ba #  ngan-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  rgyu 'dod-chags #  dang zhe-sdang #  dang gti-mug #  gi rnam-pa #  rnams ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du gdags te / / 'dod-chags #  dang zhe-sdang #  gnyis cig-car #  mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / 'di gnyis ni rang-gi-rgyud #  ni med do / / rmugs pa gang zhe na / / sems las-su-mi-rung-ba #  ste /
stimita BAvaH stEmityam yat yogAt cittaMjaXIBAvAt stimitam iva Bavati na Alambanam pratipattum utsahate
# blong-ba #  nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  la blong-ba #  nyid ni rnam-grangs #  gzhan gyis bstan-pa # 'o / / blong-ba # 'i dngos-po #  ni blong-ba #  nyid de / / de dang ldan na sems blun-pa # r gyur nas mi g-yo-ba #  bzhin-du #  dmigs-pa #  rtogs-pa # r mi-nus-pa # 'o /
etat ca sarva kleSa upakleSa sAhAyya karmakam
# 'di yang nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  grogs-byed-pa # 'i las can no /
Atma Uha aMSa ijQapta tvAt caprajQaptitaH eva na dravyataH / OdDatyaMcittasya avyaupaSamaH / vyupaSamaH hi / SamaTaH / tad virudDaH avyaupaSamaH / sa punar ArAga anukUlaH pUrva hasita ramita kriXita Adi anusmara torAga aMSikaH cetasaH avi upaSama hetuH / ySamaTa paripanTa karma kaMSradDA vipakzaH iti SradDA astitva guNavat tu aSakyatvezu / aBisampratyayaH prasAdaH aBilAzaH cayaTa Akramam / aSradDAta dvi paryayeNa astitva guNavat tu aSakya tvezu asampratyayaH aprasAdaH anaBilAzaH ca / kOSIdya sanniSraya dAna karmakam / aSradDa DAnasya prayoga= Canda aBAvAt kOsIdya sanniSraya dAna karmaka tvam
# gti-mug #  gi cha la gdags-pa # s btags-pa #  nyid yin gyi rdzas su ni ma yin no / / rgod-pa #  gang zhe na / / sems ma-zhi-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la zhi-ba #  ni zhi-gnas #  te / / de dang mi-mthun-pa #  ni ma-zhi-ba # 'o / / de-yang #  'dod-chags #  dang mthun-pa #  sngon dgod dgod-pa #  dang rtse rtse ba la-sogs-pa #  dran-pa # 'i 'dod-chags #  kyi char gtogs-pa #  sems ma-zhi-ba # 'i rgyu ste / / zhi-gnas #  kyi bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i las can no / / dad-pa # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / dad-pa #  ni yod-pa #  dang yon-tan-can #  dang nus-pa #  rnams la mngon-par-yid-ches-pa #  dang dang-ba #  dang 'dod-pa # 'o / / de-las-bzlog-pa #  ni ma dang pa ste / / dad-pa-med-pa #  ni sbyor-ba #  la 'dun-pa #  med-pa # s le-lo # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no /
kuSale kAya vAc manaH karmaNi nidrA pArSva Sayana suKam / Agamya yaH moha aMSikaH cetasaH anaByutsAhaH sakOsIdyam / kutsitam sIdati iti kusIdaH / tad BAvaH kOsIdyam vIrya vipakzaH / vIrya vipakzA eti vIryam hi
# nyal-ba #  dang gnyid pa dang 'phres-pa # 'i bde-ba #  la brten-nas #  gti-mug #  gi char gtogs-pa # s lus dang ngag dang yid-kyi-las #  dge-ba #  la sems mi spro-ba #  de ni le-lo #  ste / / ngan-pa #  la sbyor-ba # s ni le-lo # 'o / / brtson 'grus kyi mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  zhes-bya-ba #  la brtson 'grus ni dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la sbyor-ba #  la sems-mngon-par-spro-ba # 'o /
kuSala pakza prayoge cetasaH aByutsAhaH tad vipakza tvAt kOsIdyam / etat cakuSala pakza prayoga paripanTa karmakam / loBa dveza moha kOsIdyezu pramAdaH prajQapyate / yaTAvyAKyAtezu / ayaMcA kuSala vRdDi kuSala parihANi saMniSraya dAna karmakaH / muzita smRtitA klizwA smRtiH / klizwA iti / lkleSa samprayuktA / kuSalasya anaBilapanatA iti na hi / kleSa samprayuktA smRtiH kleSena aBinna vizaya tvAt kuSalam aBilapitum samarTA / iyam cavikzepa sanniSraya dAna karmikA / viviDam kzipyate anena cittam iti vikzepaH
# de'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  yin-pas #  le-lo #  ste / / dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la sbyor-ba # 'i bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i las can no / / bag-med-pa #  ni chags-pa #  dang zhe-sdang #  dang gti-mug #  ji-skad-du #  bshad-pa #  rnams la btags te mi-dge-ba #  'phel-ba #  dang dge-ba #  'grib-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / brjed-ngas-pa #  gang zhe na / / dran-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  de zhes-bya-ba #  la nyon-mongs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'o / / dge-ba #  la mi-gsal-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / nyon-mongs-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i dran-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang yul tha-dad-pa #  ma-yin-pa # s dge-ba #  la sems gsal-ba # r byed mi nus te / / g-yeng ba'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / rnam-pa # r g-yeng ba ni 'dis sems sna-tshogs #  su g-yeng bar byed-pa # 'o / / 'dod-chags #  dang zhe-sdang #  dang gti-mug #  de-dag #  gis sems ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi dmigs-pa #  las phyi-rol #  tu 'phro bar byed-pa #  ste /
yE / prAgadveza mohEH cittaMsam ADyAtambanAt bahis visAryate tezu yaTAsamBavam upakleSa AtmakaH vikzepaH prajQapyate / eza cavEH Agya paripanTa karmakaH
# de-dag #  la ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  g-yeng ba gdags so / / 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'i bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i las can no / / shes-bzhin #  ma-yin-pa #  gang zhe na /
samprajanI aMkleSa samprayuktA prajQA
# nyon-mongs-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i shes-rab #  ste /
yayAsam vidita akAya vAc citta caryA vikrama pratikrama Adizu pravartate
# des lus dang ngag dang yid kyi spyod-pa #  'gro-ba-dang-ldog-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la mi shes-bzhin #  du 'jug-pa #  ste /
karaNIyAkaraNIya ajQAnAt Apatti sanniSraya dAna karmakam / kOkRtyaMcetasaH vipratisAraH / kutsitam kRtam iti / kukRtam / tad BAvaH kOkRtyam
# bya-ba #  dang bya-ba-ma-yin-pa #  mi-shes-pa # s ltung-ba # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no / / phung-po #  lnga'i rab tu byed-pa #  bye-brag #  tu bshad-pa #  / / bam po gsum-pa #  / / 'gyod-pa #  gang zhe na / / yid la gcags pa'o zhes-bya-ba #  la ngan-pa #  byas-pa # s 'gyod de de'i dngos-po #  ni 'gyod-pa #  nyid do /
kukRta vizayaH cetasaH vileKaH kOkRtyam ucyate cEtasika aDikArAt
# ngan-pa #  byas-pa # 'i yul la sems mi-dga'-ba #  ste / / sems-las-byung-ba # 'i skabs yin-pas #  'gyod-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
aBipretam anaBipretaMkuSalam akuSalam avyAkRtam kAle akAle yuktam ayuktam cakRtvA akRtvA vA moha aMSikaH cetasaH vipratisAraH kOkRtyam
# 'dod-pa #  dang mi-'dod-pa #  dang dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  dang dus dang dus-ma-yin-pa #  dang rang mi-rigs-pa #  byas sam ma byas kyang rung ste / / gti-mug #  gi char gtogs-pa # 'i sems kyi yid la gcags pa ni 'gyod-pa #  ste /
yat tat cit sTiti paripanTa karmakam / n baBirati pUrvakam yat kriyat etat aBipretam
# 'di ni sems-gnas-pa # 'i bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i las can no / / mngon-par-dga'-ba #  sngon-du-'gro-ba # 'i byed-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni 'dod-pa # 'o /
anaBipretam punar parEH balAt avazwaByayat kAryate kleSa aBiBavAt vAyat karoti
# mi-'dod-pa #  ni gzhan dag gis nan-gyis #  byed-du-bcug-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i zil gyis non nas byed-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
kAlaH yAvat naviram ati kAlaH tad UrDvam / yuktam sTAne ayuktam asTAne
# dus ni ji-srid #  du-ma #  spangs-pa # 'o / / dus-ma-yin-pa #  ni de-la # s thal-ba # 'o / / rigs-pa #  ni gnas yin pa'o / / mi-rigs-pa #  ni gnas-ma-yin-pa # 'o /
tat ca api triviDam kuSalam akuSalam avyAkRtam ca
# de-la #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'o /
moha aMSikam iti upakleSa saFgRhItam atra gRhyate / e iH haviH vyabUH midDam asvatantra vRttiH cetasaH / aBisaFkzepaH / vRttiH Alambane pravRttiH / sa asvatantra acetasaH yatas Bavati tat midDam
# 'dir ni gti-mug #  gi char gtogs-pa # 'i nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # s bsdus-pa #  kho-na #  gzung ngo / / gnyid gang zhe na / / 'jug-pa #  rang-dbang-med-pa # r sems sdud-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la 'jug-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  la 'jug-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  sems kyi rang-dbang-med-pa #  gang-la # s 'byung-ba #  nyid ces bya'o /
kAya sanDAraNA samarTA avAvRttiH cetasaH asvatantrA sA yatas Bavati tat midDam / anyatas api asvatantrA vRttiH cetasaH Bavati iti atas Aha cetasaH aBisaFkzepaH iti / anyatas api aBisaFkzepaH cetasaH iti asvatantra vRttiH cetasaH iti Aha
# yang-na #  lus 'dzin mi-nus-pa # 'i sems-kyi-'jug-pa #  rang-dbang-med-pa #  de gang-la # s byung-ba #  de gnyid ces bya'o / / gzhan gyis kyang sems-kyi-'jug-pa #  rang-dbang-med-pa # r 'gyur-ba # s de'i-phyir #  sems sdud-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / gzhan gyis kyang sems sdud-pa # r 'gyur-ba # s sems-kyi-'jug-pa #  rang-dbang-med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
aBisaFkzepaH cetasaH cakzuH Adi indriya dvAreNa apravRttiH / sa punar kuSalaH akuSalaH akuSalaH avyAkRtaH ca
# sems sdud-pa #  ni mig la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang-po # 'i sgo nas mi-'jug-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'o /
midDa nimittaMdOH balya Srama kAya gOrava anDakAra nimitta manasikaraNa Adika mA Agamya moha aMSikoBavati / kRtya atipatti sanniSraya dAna karmakam
# gnyid kyi rgyu nyi nyams chung-ba #  dang ngal-ba #  dang lus lci-ba #  dang mun-pa'i-mtshan-ma #  yid-la-byed-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la brten-nas #  gti-mug #  gi char gtogs-pa #  'byung ste / / bya-ba #  shor ba'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no /
atra ca akuSalaH evam Uha aMSikaH na anyaH / vitarkaH paryAzakaH manaH jalpaH
# 'dir ni mi-dge-ba #  nyid gti-mug #  gi char gtogs-pa #  yin gyi gzhan ni ma yin no / / rtog-pa #  gang zhe na / / kun du tshol-ba # 'i yid kyi brjod-pa #  ste /
cetanA prajQA viSezaH / paryezakaH kim etat iti nirUpaNa AkAra pravRttaH
# sems-pa #  dang shes-rab #  kyi bye-brag #  ces bya-ba #  la kun du tshol-ba #  ni 'di ci yin zhes kun du rtog-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r zhugs-pa # 'o /
manaH svaBAvaH jalpaH manaH jalpaH
# yid kyi rang-bzhin #  gyi brjod-pa #  ni yid kyi brjod-pa # 'o /
jalpaH iva jalpaH arTa kaTanA / cetanA prajQA viSezaH iti cetanAyAH citta parispanda Atmaka tvAt prajQAyAH caguNa doza viveka AkAra tvAt
# brjod-pa #  dang 'dra-ba # s brjod-pa #  ste don brjod-pa # 'o / / sems-pa #  dang shes-rab #  kyi bye-brag #  ces bya-ba #  la sems-pa #  ni gang-gis #  sems kun du g-yo-ba # r byed-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin la /
tad vaSena citta pravRtteH kadAcid citta cetanayoH vitarka prajQaptiH kadAcid prajQAcetasoH yaTAkramam aByUhAna BrU hA avasTAyoH
# shes-rab #  ni yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa #  'byed-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  yin-pas #  de'i dbang gis kyang sems-'jug-pa # s na-ba # r 'ga' sems dang sems-pa #  la rtog-pa #  gdags / / 'ga' ni shes-rab #  dang sems la ste /
aTavA acetana aprajQayoH eva vitarka prajQaptiH tad vaSena cittasya taTA apravRtta tvAt
# mngon-par-mi-rtog-pa #  dang mngon-par-rtogs-pa # 'i dus dang go-rims #  bzhin no / / yang-na #  sems-pa #  dang shes-rab #  nyid la gdags te / / de'i dbang gis de-ltar #  'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
eza ca nayaH vicAre api drazwavyaH
# tshul 'di ni dpyod-pa #  la yang blta-bar-bya # 'o /
ittasya OdArika tA iti sTUla tA vastu mAtra paryezaNa AkAra tvAt
# sems rtsing ba'o zhes-bya-ba #  la che long ste / / dngos-po #  tsam kun du tshol-ba # 'i rnam-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
vicAraH pratyavekzakaH manaH jalpaH idam tat iti / pUrva aDigata nirUpaNAt
# dpyod-pa #  gang zhe na / / so-sor-rtog-pa #  yid kyi dpyod-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni sngar khong-du-chud-pa #  la 'di ni 'di'o zhes dpyod-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
taTA eva cittasya / sUkzmatA iti / taTA eva iti cetanA prajQA viSezaH
# de-bzhin-du #  gang sems-zhi-ba #  ba'o zhes-bya-ba #  la de-bzhin-du #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / sems-pa #  dang shes-rab #  kyi bye-brag #  go /
paryezaNa tovaH tu pratyavekzaNa AkAra tvAt sUkzmaH ucyate
# dngos-po #  la so-sor-rtog-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  yin-pas #  zhi-ba #  pa zhes-bya'o #  /
etO casparSa asparSa vihAra sanniSraya dAna karmakO
# 'di gnyis ni reg-par-gnas-pa #  dang reg-pa # r mi-gnas-pa # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can no /
anayoH ca OdArika sUkzma vyavasTAnAt pRTakkaraNam
# 'di gnyis ni sems rtsing ba dang zhib par rnam-par-gnas-pa #  tha dad du dbye'o /
saMskAra skanDaH vedanA saQjQA vyatirikta cEtasika AtmakaH citta viprayukta saMskAra AtmakaH ca iti uktam / tatra cEtasika uktAH
# 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po #  ni tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  las gzhan-pa #  sems-las-byung-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  dang sems dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  kyi bdag-nyid #  do zhes bshad-pa #  de-la #  sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams bshad-zin #  to /
citta viprayuktAH saMskArAH idAnIm vaktavyAH iti atas Aha citta viprayuktAH saMskArAH katamaH iti
# da-ni #  sems dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  brjod dgos-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / sems dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
praSna vat sAmAnyatas tad nirdeSaH yA rUpa citta cEtasika avasTAsu prajQapyante
# dris-pa #  bzhin-du #  gang dag gzugs dang sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  la gdags-pa #  ste /
tattva anyatvataH ca na prajQapyante teviprayuktAH saMskArAH iti prakaraNAt sambaDyate
# de nyid dang gzhan-du #  mi gdags so zhes de-dag #  spyir bstan te / / de-dag #  ni mi-ldan-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  yin par skabs kyis sbyar ro /
rUpa Adi avasTA vyatirikta svarUpa aBAvAt te rUpa Adi avasTAsu saMvyavahAra arTam prajQapyante / atas eva sva upAdAnAt tattva anyatvena avasTAvat na prajQapyante avasTA avasTAvatoH ekAneka tva prasaFgAt avasTAvataH ca akArya nitya tva prasaFgAt / sAmAnya nirdeSAt viSezAn avagamAt viSeza buButsayA praSnaH te punar katamaH iti / prAptiH / asaQjQi samApattiH iti vistareNa tad viSeza nidarSanam / evam BAgIyAH eva QjAtIyAH
# gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  pas rang-gi #  ngo bo gud-na #  med-pa # s / / de-dag #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  la tha-snyad #  gdags-pa # 'i phyir btags-pa # 'o / / de'i-phyir #  rten-dang-bcas-pa #  yin-pas #  gnas-skabs #  bzhin-du #  de nyid dang gzhan-du #  mi gdags te / / gnas-skabs #  dang gnas-skabs #  can gcig dang du-ma #  nyid-du #  thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir dang gnas-skabs #  can la 'bras-bu #  rtag-par #  thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro; / / de-ltar #  spyir bstan nas khyad-par #  khong-du-chud-pa # r 'dod nas / / de-dag #  kyang gang zhe na zhes dris-pa #  dang thob-pa #  dang 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dang zhes-bya-ba #  de-dag #  gi khyad-par #  rgya-cher #  bstan to / / de-lta-bu # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  dag go zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-lta-bu # 'i rang-bzhin-can #  dag ste /
ye anye api / rUpa citta cEtta avasTAsu prajQapyante teviprayuktAH saMskAra AveditavyAH / te punar katame
# gzhan gang dag gzugs dang sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  la gdags-pa #  ste / / de-dag #  kyang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  su rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-dag #  kyang gang zhe na /
pravRttiH pratiniyamaH yogaH javaH anukramaH kAlaH deSaH saFKyA sAmagrI ca iti evamAdayaH
# 'jug-pa #  dang so-sor-nges-pa #  dang 'byor-pa #  dang mgyogs-pa #  dang go-rims #  dang rus dang yul dang grangs dang tshogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
idAnIm sAmagri AdInAm pratyekam svarUpa nirDAraNa arTa MpraSnaH prAptiH katamA iti evamAdiH / pratilamBaH samanvAgamEti Adi / tat kila ayam aprApta pUrvasya praTamatas prAptiH pratilamBaH
# da-ni #  tshogs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo so-so # r dmigs kyis dbye-ba # 'i phyir / / thob-pa #  gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dris-pa #  dang rnyed-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  smos so / / sngon-ma-thob-pa #  thog-ma #  nyid-du #  thob-pa #  ni rnyed-pa # 'o /
prApta anAMdvitIya Adizu kzaNezu prAptiH samanvAgamaH samanugamaH samanvAgamaH iti kRtvA
# rnyed-pa #  rnams skad-cig-gnyis-pa-la #  sogs-pa # r yod-pa #  ni ldan-pa #  ste / / yang-dag-par #  rjes-su-'gro-ba #  ni ldan-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
evam caprApti SabdaH pratilamBe samanvAgame ca vartata eti jQApitam Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  thob-pa # 'i sgra ni rnyed-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  la yang snyegs-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
sA punar / bIjam vaSitA sammuKIBAvaH ca iti triDA aBidyate yaTAyogam iti
# de-yang #  sa-bon #  dang dbang dang mngon-du-gyur-pa #  dang rnam-pa-gsum #  du dbye'o / / ci-rigs-su #  sbyar ro zhes-bya-ba #  de-la #  rigs-pa #  ni 'di yin te /
tatra ayam yogaH praTama ati kzaNAt AraBya prAptiH yAvat vaSitA avasTam bIjam ucyate iti pratilamBa samanvAgamO bIja AKyO BavataH vaSitA sammuKIBAvaH ca samanvAgamaH eva / kim punar bIjam
# skad-cig #  dang-po #  thob-pa #  nas brtsams te dbang gi dus kyi bar-du #  sa-bon #  zhes bya ste / / de-ltar-na #  sa-bon #  ni rnyed-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  gnyi-ga # r brjod-pa #  yin no / / dbang dang mngon-du-gyur-pa #  ni ldan-pa #  yin no / / sa-bon #  ci la bya zhe na /
kuSala akuSala avyAkRtEH DarmEH AhitaH vijQAne anAgata tad jAtIya Darma hetuH sAmarTya viSezaH bIjam
# dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la ma-'ongs-pa #  na de dang rigs gcig pa'i chos kyi rgyu bskyed-pa # 'i nus-pa # 'i bye-brag #  ni sa-bon #  no /
bIje hi labDe tad AyattatvAt asammuKIBUtam api yasya tat bIjam tat prAptam ucyate
# sa-bon #  rnyed nas de-la #  rag-las-pa # 'i phyir mngon du-ma #  gyur kyang de'i sa-bon #  gang-yin-pa #  de thob-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
vaSitA punar tasya pratyaya anapekzya apratibanDena sva kArya nirvartana avasTA / sammuKIBAvaH tad kArya nirvRtti avasTA / asaQjQA vA samApattiH asaQjQi samApattiH asaQjQAnAm vAsam ApattiH iti asaQjQi samApattiH / eSuBa kRtsna vIra rAgasya iti tRtIya DyAna vIta rAgasya iti / tRtIyaMDyAnam parItta SuBAH apramANa SuBAH SuBa kRtsnAH ca
# dbang ni de'i rkyen la ltos nas rgyun gyi 'bras-bu #  bsgrub-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  so / / mngon du gyur ba ni de'i 'bras-bu #  grub-pa # 'i dus so / / 'du-shes-med-pa # 'am 'du-shes-med-pa #  rnams kyi ste / / 'du-shes-med-pa # r snyoms bar 'jug-pa # 'am / / 'du-shes-med-pa #  rnams kyi snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  ni / / 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'o / / dge-rgyas #  kyi 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  ni bsam-gtan #  gsum-pa # 'i 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'o / / bsam-gtan #  gsum-pa #  ni dge-chung #  dang tshad-med-dge #  dang dge-rgyas #  so /
tatra yaH SuBa kRtsneByaH vIta rAgaH sa tRtIyAt DyAnAt vIta rAgaH
# de-la #  gang dge-rgyas #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  de ni bsam-gtan #  gsum-pa #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'o /
na UrDvam= tRtIyAt DyAnAt / UrDvaMcaturTaMDyAnam caturTAt DyAnAt avIta rAgasya iti arTaH
