# gong-ma #  ma-yin-pa #  ni bsam-gtan #  gsum-pa #  las gong-du #  gyur-pa #  bsam-gtan-bzhi-pa #  ste / / bsam-gtan-bzhi-pa #  la 'dod-chags #  dang ma bral zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
niHsaraNa saQjQA pUrvakeNa iti niHsaraNa saQjQA pUrvam yasya manasikArasya sa niHsaraNa saQjQA pUrvakaH
# 'byung-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  sngon-du #  btang-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'byung-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  su la yod-pa #  de 'byung-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  sngon-du #  btang-ba #  ste /
AsaQjQike mokza saQjQinaH samApattO vA tad mArga saQjQinaH asaQjQi samApattiMsamApadyante
# 'du-shes-med-pa #  la thar bar 'du-shes #  pa'am / / snyoms bar 'jug-pa #  la de'i lam-du #  'du-shes #  pa rnams 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  la snyoms-pa # r 'jug go /
atas niHsaraNa saQjQA mokza saQjQA tad mArga saQjQA vA
# de'i-phyir #  'byung-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  ni thar-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  sam / / de'i lam-du #  'du-shes #  pa'o /
vidUzaNa AkAraH atra niHsaraNa saQjQA pUrva komanasikAraH aBipretaH
# 'dir ni sun-'byin-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  la 'byung-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # r 'dod de /
atas eva sarva citta cEtta niroDe api saQjQA BAvaH eva nirdiSyate asaQjQi samApattiH iti
# de nyid kyi phyir sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  'gags su zin-kyang #  'du-shes-med-pa #  nyid la 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  zhes bstan te /
taTA hi saQjQAm eva vidUzayan niravaSeza citta cEtta niroDam prApnoti / sTAvarANAm citta cEtasikAnAm yaH niroDa / iti / sTAvarAH pravRtti vijQAna saFgRhIta aHsasam prayoga aHzaX vijQAnakAyAH / sarvAsu acittikAsu avasTAsu aBAvAt sa cittikAsu api avasTAsu ye na sarvadA Bavanti te asTAvarAH
# 'di-ltar #  'du-shes #  nyid la sun-'byin-pa # s sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  ma-lus-par #  'gag-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  su 'gyur ro / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  brten-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  rnams gang 'gog-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la brten-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  rnams ni 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # r bsdus-pa #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug-po #  dag ste / / gang-gi-phyir #  sems med-pa # 'i dus-thams-cad #  na med-pa #  dang sems dang bcas-pa # 'i dus rnams na yang gang-gi-phyir #  ni rtag-tu #  yod-pa-ma-yin-pa #  de-dag #  brtan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  rnams so / / brtan-pa #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  ste / / gtan-du #  yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sTAvaram Alaya vijQAnam sa samprayogam sarvadA BAvAt klizwam camanaH anAsrava mArga satya samApatti avasTA aMniroDa samApatti avasTAm tAm aSEkzAva sTAm ca hitvA anyA anusarvAsu avasTAsu BAvAt iti asTAvarANAm iti viSezaNam
# zag-pa-med-pa # 'i lam gyi bden-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i dus dang 'gog-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i dus dang mi-slob-pa # 'i dus ma-gtogs-par #  dus gzhan kun na yod-pa # 'i phyir brtan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  rnams zhes bye-brag #  smos so / / gang 'gog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sems-kyis #  byas-pa #  ste /
yoniroDaH iti samApatti cittakRtaH kAla antaram sTAvara citta cEtta samudAcAra viroDi ASrayasya avasTA viSezaH / niruDyate anena iti niroDaH
# 'dis 'gag-par-byed-pa # s na 'gog-pa # 'o / / dus-gzhan-na #  sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  brtan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  kun du 'byung-ba #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i lus kyi gnas-skabs #  kyi bye-brag #  la bya ste /
evam ca ASraya avasTA viSezeasaQjQi samApattiH prajQapyate iti uktam Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  lus kyi gnas-skabs #  kyi bye-brag #  la 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  la gdags-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
samApatti cittena anantaram citta antara utpatti virudDaH ASrayaH yaH sa samApatti cittena kRtaH iti ucyate / niraH DasamA pattiH / mAkiQca nyAyatana vIta rAga syaBava agrAt / uccalitasya iti / Bava agrAt anuccalitaH api asti AkiQca nyAyatana vIta rAgaH pRTagjanaH iti atas Aha Bava agrAt uccalitasya iti
# snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sems-kyis #  de-ma-thag-pa # 'i sems gzhan skye-ba #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i lus skyed-pa # 'i phyir snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sems-kyis #  byas-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  gang zhe na / / ci-yang-med-pa # 'i skye-mched #  kyi 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  srid-pa # 'i rtse mo las gyen-du #  bskyod-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
Bava agrAt uccalitaH AkiQca nyAyatana vIta rAgaH api asti kaScid Pala sTaH pratipannakaH ca Bava agrAt uccalita AkiQca nyAyatanAt avIta rAgaH api asti kaScid Pala sTaH pratipannakaH ca iti atas Aha AkiQca nyAyatana vIta rAgasya iti
# srid-pa # 'i rtse mo las gyen-du #  ma bskyod kyang ci-yang-med-pa # 'i skye-mched #  kyi 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'i so-so #  skye-bo # 'i yang yod-pa # s de'i-phyir #  srid-pa # 'i rtse mo las gyen-du #  bskyod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / srid-pa # 'i rtse mo las gyen-du #  bskyod-pa #  ci-yang-med-pa # 'i skye-mched #  kyi 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  kha-cig #  / / 'bras-bu-la-gnas-pa #  dang 'jug-pa #  yang yod-pa # s / / de'i-phyir #  ci-yang-med-pa # 'i skye-mched #  kyi 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
upari avIta rAgasya iti avacanam Bava agra vIta rAgasya arhataH api niroDa samApatti samBavAt
# gong-ma # 'i 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  zhes ma brjod-pa #  ni srid-pa # 'i rtse mo'i 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  dgra-bcom-pa #  yang 'gog-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
AkiQca nyAyatana vIta rAgasya Bava agrAt uccalitasya iti uBaya aBiDAnena Aryasya eva iyam anAgAminaH arhataH vA samApattiH na pRTagjanasya iti jQApitaMBavati / na hi pRTagjanaH Bava agrAt uccalati Bava agra pratipakzasya mArgasya aBAvAt
# ci-yang-med-pa # 'i skye-mched #  kyi 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  dang srid-pa # 'i rtse mo las gyen-du #  bskyod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  gnyi-ga #  smos-pa # s ni 'di 'phags-pa #  phyir-mi-'ong-ba # 'am / / dgra-bcom-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  yin gyi / / so-so'i-skye-bo #  ni ma-yin-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no / / so-so'i-skye-bo #  ni srid-pa # 'i rtse mo las gyen-du #  mi bskyod do / / srid-pa # 'i rtse mo las gnyen-po #  'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
darSana mArgaH tuBava agra pratipakzaH BAvanA mArgaH ca anAsravaH / atas AryaH eva Bava agrAt uccalitaH darSana prahAtavya kleSa prahANAt cavirajya
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  zag-pa-med-pa #  ni srid-pa # 'i rtse mo'i gnyen-po #  yin te / / de'i-phyir #  'phags-pa #  nyid mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-spangs-pa #  dang bsgom bas spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i phyir ma-chags-pa # s srid ba'i rtse mo las bskyod-pa # 'o /
vihAra saQjQA pUrvakeNa manasikAreNa iti na hi niroDa samApattim / asaQjQA samApattim iva niHsaraNa saQjQA pUrva keNa manasikAreNa samApadyante kim tarhi vihAra saQjQA pUrvakeNa
# gnas-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # 'i yid-la-byed-pa # s zhes-bya-ba #  la 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  ni 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  bzhin-du #  'byung-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # 'i yid-la-byed-pa # s snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  ma yin gyi gnas-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # s so /
niroDa samApattiH Bava agrakI na ca AryANAm Bavet niHsaraNa saQjQA pravartate
# 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  ni srid-pa # 'i rtse mo ba ste / / 'phags-pa #  rnams ni srid-pa #  las 'byung-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  mi 'jug gi /
saQjQA vedita pariKinnaH tad aBAvAt niroDa samApattO SAnta vihAra saQjQI Bavati / vihAraH iti saQjQA vihAra saQjQA viharati anena iti vA vihAraH / kAla antaram yApayati iti arTaH
# 'du-shes-dang-tshor-ba # s yongs su skyo nas de med-pa # 'i phyir 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  la zhi-ba # r gnas-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  su 'gyur ro / / gnas su mnyam-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  ni gnas-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  so / / 'dis gnas-par-byed-pa # s gnas-pa #  ste / / dus gzhan-du #  sdod ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
nirvANa sadRSena samApatti viSezeNa viharizyAmaH iti anayA saQjQayA saMskRta umana sikAraH vihAra saQjQA pUrvakaH manasikAraH ucyate
# snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i khyad-par #  mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang 'dra-ba # s gnas-pa # r bya'o snyam pa'i 'du-shes #  mngon-par-'du-byed-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  ni gnas-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
sa punarBava agrikaH SUkzmaH tad anantaram niroDa samApatti sammuKIBAvAt
# srid-pa # 'i rtse mo pa de ni phra-ba # 'i phra-ba #  ste / / de ma-thag-tu #  'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  mngon-du-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sTAvarANAm iti zaNNAm pravRtti vijQAnAnAm caturNAm ekasya kAma rUpa ArUpya DAtuzu yaTAkramam niroDaMsam ApadyamAnAnAm
# brtan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  rnams zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'gog-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  rnams kyi 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  drug dang bzhi dang gcig 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  rnams su go-rims #  bzhin no /
ekatIyAnAm ca sTAvarANAm iti / sTAvarAH iti vipAka vijQAna saFgRhItAH api santi iti atas Aha ekatIyAnAm iti
# brtan-pa #  rnams las kyang kha-cig #  ces bya-ba #  la brtan-pa #  ni rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # r bsdus-pa #  dag kyang yod-pa # s de'i-phyir #  kha-cig #  ces bya-ba #  smos so /
klizwasya ca manasaH sarvasmin sa Asrave cAresTAna SIla tvAt sTAvara tvam anyatra niroDa samApatti aSEkza avasTayoH / niroDa eti
# nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid ni 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dang mi-slob-pa # 'i dus ma-gtogs-par #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i spyod-pa #  thams-cad #  na gnas-pa'i-tshul #  can yin-pas #  brtan-pa # 'o / / 'gog-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # s byas-pa #  ste /
samApatti vijQAna kRtaH vipAka vijQAne pravRtti vijQAnAnAm klizwasya ca manasaH bIja upaGAtaH
# rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i sa-bon #  la gnod-pa-byed-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  ste /
niruDyate anena pravRtti vijQAnam klizwam ca manaH kAla antaram apravRttitaH iti niroDaH ucyate
# 'dis 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid dus-gzhan-na #  mi-'byung-ba # r 'gog-pa # s 'gog-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
evam cAlaya vijQAnasya samApatti cittena upahata bIja avasTAyAm niroDa samApattiH prajQapyate
# de-ltar-na #  snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sems-kyis #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la sa-bon #  nyams-par-byas-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  la 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  gdags so /
AsaQjQikam asaQjQi samApatteH Palam / tasan jQi sattvezu
# 'du-shes-med-pa #  gang zhe na / / 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ste /
deve zUpa pan= asyAH sTA varANAMcitta cEtasikAnAm DarmANAm yaH niroDaH / ubRhatPalAH nAma devAH caturTe DyAne tRtIyam sTAna antaram
# 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i sems-can #  lha rnams kyi nang-du #  skyes-pa # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  brtan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  rnams gang 'gog-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la lha de-dag #  ni 'bras-bu-che-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  rnams te / / bsam-gtan-bzhi-pa # 'i gnas gzhan gsum-pa # 'o /
tezAm parigaNAH iva upari asaQjQi sattvAnAm devAnAm sTAnaMtatra upannasya Asan jiQi samApatti vipAka Palam
# de-dag #  gi gong-na #  khang-khyim #  lta-bu # r 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i sems-can #  lha rnams kyi gnas yod-pa #  der skyes-pa # 'i 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'o /
asTAvarANAMcitta cEttAnAm yaH niroDaH iti tad svarUpa avaDAraNam
# sems dang sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  brtan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  rnams gang 'gog-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di'i rang-bzhin #  nges-par #  bzung-ba #  ste /
tatra hi upapannasya AsTAvarAH citta cEttAH svASrayesva jAtIya citta cEtta bIja upaGAte vartamAnAH kzAma kzAma tara utpadyante yAvat ante atikzAmatAm gatAH citta antara MsambanDum na Saknuvanti sva ASrayasya upahata bIja tvAt
# der skyes-pa # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  chos-bstan-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  rnams rang-gi #  gnas la rang-gi-rigs #  kyi sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i sa-bon #  la gnod-par-byed-pa #  ni srab-pa #  bas kyang ches srab bar 'gyur zhing tha-ma # r shin-tu #  srab-pa # 'i bar-du #  gyur nas rang-gi #  gnas la sa-bon #  nyams-par-byas-pa # 'i phyir sems gzhan dang sbyor mi nus so /
atas ca AsTAvarANAm citta cEttAnAm tad kAla ASrayeNa apravRttiH / tasyAMca upahata bIja avasTAyAm ASrayasya AsaQjQikam prajQapyate
# de'i-phyir #  sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i brtan ba ma-yin-pa #  rnams de'i tshe gnas las mi 'byung ste / / sa-bon #  nyams-pa # r gyur ba'i dus de na gnas la 'du-shes-med-pa #  gdags so /
evam ASrayasya avasTA viSezaH eva niruDyate anena iti niroDaH / jIvita indriyaMnikAya saBAgezu
# de-ltar-na #  gnas kyi dus nyid la bya ste / / 'dis 'gog-par-byed-pa # s na 'gog-pa # 'o / / srog-gi-dbang-po #  gang zhe na /
pUrva karma AvidDaH yaH saMskArANAm sTiti kAla niyama eti / jIvyate anena iti jIvitam
# ris-mthun-pa #  rnams su sngon-gyi-las #  kyis 'phangs-pa # s gang 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi gnas ba'i dus-nges-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dis 'tsho-bar-byed-pa # s srog go /
tat eva nikAya saBAga sTiti ADipatyAt indriyam / nikAyaH sattva samUhaH
# ris-mthun-pa #  de nyid-du #  gnas bar dbang-byed-pa # 'i phyir dbang-po #  zhes-bya'o #  / / ris ni sems-can-gyi-tshogs #  so /
samAnaH BAgaH iti sa BAgaH sadRSaH iti arTaH / nikAyasya saBAgAH
# skal-ba #  mtshungs-pa #  ni mthun-pa #  ste / / 'dra zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / ris-mthun-pa # s ris-mthun-pa #  ste /
tezu ca nikAya saBAgezu gati Bedena karma Bedena ca Binnezu pratyekam eka jAnmikaH yaH skanDa santAnaHsa nikAya saBAga AKyaH
# 'gro-ba #  tha-dad-pa #  dang las tha-dad-pa # s tha-dad-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i ris-mthun-pa #  de-dag #  tu so-so # 'i tshe gcig gi phung-po # 'i rgyun gang-yin-pa #  de ris-mthun-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tasya pUrva upacita kuSala akuSala aniQjya karma AvidDaH karma janitaH / yaH sTiti kAla niyamaH iti aBinna nikAya BAga saFgRhIta anAMsaMskArANAm pravRttiH sTiti niyamaH ucyate / tasyAH sTiteH kAla niyamaH iyantam kAlam anena asmin nikAya saBA gesTAtavyam varza Satam varza sahasram vA iti asaMsTiti kAla niyamaH / evam ca sTiti kAla niyama svaBAvam AyuH iti uktam Bavati
# de-yang #  sngon bsags-pa # 'i dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang mi g-yo-ba # 'i las kyis 'phangs-pa #  ni las kyis bskyed-pa # 'o / / gang gnas-pa # 'i dus-nges-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni tha-dad-pa #  ma yin ba'i ris-mthun-pa # s bsdus-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi 'jug-pa #  la gnas-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / gnas-pa #  de'i dus-nges-pa #  ni 'dis ris-mthun-pa #  der lo brgya'am / / lo stong ngam / / dus-ji-srid-du #  gnas-par-'gyur-ba #  de gnas-pa # 'i dus-nges-pa # 'o /
aDizWAnam tu tasya sTAvarAH saMskAra Alaya vijQAna pUrvakAH pUrva janma upacitena karmaNa Akzipta sAmarTya viSezAH iti / nikAya saBA goyA sattvAnAm
# de-ltar-na #  gnas-pa # 'i dus-nges-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  la tshe zhes bstan-pa #  yin no / / de'i-gnas #  ni sngon bsags-pa'i-las #  kyis 'phangs-pa # s nus-pa # 'i khyad-par-can #  gyi 'du-byed #  brtan-pa #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  sngon-du-'gro-ba #  rnams so /
Atma BAva saBA gatA / sattvAH deva manuzya AdayaH paQca gati paryApannAH / tezAm AtmA iti BAvaH yatra sa sattvAnAm Atma BAvaH
# ris-mthun-pa #  gang zhe na gang sems-can-rnams-kyi-lus #  'dra-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la sems-can #  ni lha-dang-mi #  la-sogs-pa #  'gro-ba-lnga # r gtogs-pa #  rnams so / / de-dag #  gi bdag-gi #  dngos-po # r gang-la #  'dzin-pa #  de / / sems-can-rnams-kyi-lus #  yin te /
sa punar paQca upAdAna skanDa AtmakaH catur skanDa AtmakaH vA / saBA gatA sAdRSyam
# de-yang #  nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po nyid dam / / phung-po #  bzhi'i bdag-nyid #  do / / 'dra zhes-bya-ba #  ni mtshungs-pa # 'o /
etat uktaMBavati gati sTAna Atma BAva Adi Bedena BinnAnAm sattva anAMgati sTAna Atma BAva Beda nibanDanam sattvAnAm yapa raspareNa Atma BAva sAdRSyam tatra nikAya saBAgaH iti prajQaptiH / jAtiH nikAya saBA ge yaH saMskArANAm / aBUtvA BAvaH / nikAya saBAga grahaNam na / saMskAra mAtrasya utpAdaH jAtiH kim tarhi nikAya saBAga vartinaH ye saMskArAH / tezAm eva aBUtvA BAvaH jAtiH na sarvezAm iti jQApana arTam
# de ni 'di-skad-du #  'gro-ba #  dang gnas dang lus la-sogs-pa #  tha-dad-pa # s tha-dad-pa #  ni sems-can #  rnams kyi 'gro-ba #  dang gnas dang lus tha-dad-pa # 'i gzhi sems-can-rnams-kyi-lus #  phan tshun 'dra-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de-la #  ris-mthun-pa #  gdags so zhes bstan-pa #  yin no / / skye pa gang zhe na / / ris-mthun-pa # r gang 'du-byed-rnams #  ma-byung-ba #  las byung-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la / / ris-mthun-pa #  smos-pa #  ni 'du-byed #  tsam gyi 'byung-ba #  la skye-ba #  zhes mi bya'i / / ris-mthun-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag-nyid #  ma-byung-ba #  las byung-ba #  la skye-ba #  zhes bya ste / / thams-cad #  ni ma yin no zhes bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ye BAvAnAm anutpanna avinazwAnAm arTa antara BUtAm jAtim kAritrataH ca aDva vyavasTA saMpratipannAH tad mata nirAsa arTam Aha aBUtvA BAvaH iti
# gang dag dngos-po #  la skyes-pa #  med-pa #  dang zhig-pa #  med-pa #  rnams kyi skye-ba #  don gzhan-du #  'gyur-pa #  dang byed-pa #  las dus rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r 'dzin-pa #  rnams kyi 'dod-pa #  de bsal-ba # 'i phyir / / ma-byung-ba #  las byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
svarUpasya eva hi saMskArANAm aBUtvA BAvaH jAtiH na arTa antara BUtA na ca kAritrataH aDva vyavasTA iti / jarA taTA eva tezAm prabanDAni aTa tvam
# 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi rang-bzhin #  ma-byung-ba #  las byung-ba #  ni skye-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  / / don gzhan gyur-pa #  yang med / / byed-pa #  las dus rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  yang ma yin no / / rga-ba #  gang zhe na /
taTA eva tezAm iti nikAya saBAga patitAnAm eva saMskArANAm
# de-ltar #  de-dag #  gi rgyun gzhan-du-'gyur-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la de-ltar #  de-dag #  gi zhes-bya-ba #  ni ris-mthun-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  nyid kyi'o /
prabanDAni aTa tvam iti upapatti BavAt yAvat maraNa BavaH
# rgyun gzhan-du-'gyur-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni skye-ba'i-srid-pa #  nas 'chi-ba'i-srid-pa # 'i bar-du #  ste /
tatra antare hetu Pala BAvena avasTitAnAm saMskArANAm nErantaryeNa utpAdaH prabanDaH ucyate
# bar der rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # 'i dngos-po # r gnas-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  'byung-ba #  la rgyun ces bya'o /
tasya anyaTA ca anyaTA ca BAvaH anyaTA tvam / taTA hikalala avasTAtaH arbuda avasTA iti evam yAvat vRdDa avasTA
# de'i gzhan-dang-gzhan-du #  gyur-pa # 'i dngos-po #  ni gzhan-du-'gyur-ba #  ste; 'di-ltar #  nur-nur-po # 'i dus las mer-mer-po # r 'gyur-ba # 'i dus dang de-bzhin-du #  dar-la-bab-pa'i-dus #  las rgas-pa # 'i dus kyi bar-du # 'o /
kalala Adi avasTAsu api pUrvasmAt uttarasya pratikzaNam anyaTABAvaH vAcyaH / evam ca prabanDAni aTa atvejara aprajQaptiH na ekasya kzaNasya na api arTa antara BUta iti
# nur-nur-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dus rnams la yang snga-ma #  las phyi-ma # r 'gyur-ba # 'i skad-cig-re-re-la #  gzhan-du-'gyur-ba #  zhes brjod do / / de-ltar-na #  rgyun gzhan-du-'gyur-ba #  la rga-ba #  gdags te / / skad-cig-gcig #  la yang ma-yin-pa #  don gzhan-du-'gyur-ba #  yang med do /
sTitiH taTA eva tezAm prabanDa anuvRttiH iti
# gnas-pa #  gang zhe na / / de-ltar #  de-dag #  gi rgyun rgyud chags-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la /
taTA eva iti ekasmin nikAya saBAge
# de-ltar #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni ris-mthun-pa #  gcig na'o /
A maraNAt saMskArANAm prabanDa vRttO sTitiH iti prajQaptiH na ekasya kzaNasya na api arTa antara BUtA iti jQApitam Bavati / nityatA taTA eva tezAm prabanDa uparamaH
# shi-ba #  la thug gi bar-du #  'du-byed-rnams #  kyi rgyun rgyud chags-pa #  la gnas-pa #  gdags te / / skad-cig-gcig #  la yang mi bya zhing don-gzhan-du-gyur-pa #  yang med-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
taTA eva tezAm iti ekasmin nikAya saBAge saMskArANAm prabanDa uparame anitya tA prajQapyate / na pratikzaNam na api arTa antara BUte tat Bavati
# mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  gang zhe na / / de-ltar #  de-dag #  ni rgyun 'chad-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  la de-ltar #  de-dag #  gi zhes-bya-ba #  ni ris-mthun-pa #  gcig-tu #  'du-byed-rnams #  kyi rgyun-chad-pa #  la mi-rtag-pa #  gdags te / / skad-cig-re-re-la #  yang ma yin zhing don-gzhan-du-gyur-pa #  yang med-pa # r bstan-pa #  yin no /
prabanDa uparamaH tu atramaraNam veditavyam
# rgyun-chad-pa #  ni 'dir 'chi-ba #  la bya-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
nanu ca bAhyasya api rUpasya jAti jarA sTiti anitya tAH santi
# phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs la yang skye-ba #  dang rga-ba #  dang gnas-pa #  dang mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  yod-pa # r nges na /
tat kimarTam nikAya saBAgaH eva saMskAra santAnasya jAti AdayaH uktAH na bAhyasya rUpasya iti
# ci'i-phyir #  ris-mthun-pa #  nyid-kyi-'du-byed #  kyi rgyun la skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r bshad kyi / / phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs kyi ni ma yin zhe na /
yAni imAni BagavatA saMskRta lakzaNAni iti uktAni jAtiH jarA sTitiH anitya tA ca tAni sattva AKyAn eva saMskArAn ADikRtya na bAhyAn iti jQApana arTam
# bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis 'du byas kyi mtshan-nyid #  skye-ba #  dang rga-ba #  dang gnas-pa #  dang mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  gang dag bshad-pa #  de-dag #  ni sems-can #  du brjod-pa #  nyid-kyi-'du-byed #  kyi dbang du mdzad-pa #  yin gyi /
kasmAt punar BagavatA uBayezAm api tulye jAti sattva izu pAttAn eva saMskArAn aDikRtya saMskRta lakzaNAni uktAni
# phyi-rol #  gyi ma-yin-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gnyi-ga #  la yang skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  yod-pa # r mtshungs na zin-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  kyi dbang du mdzad de / / bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis 'du-byed-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  bshad-pa #  ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
bAhyam hi rUpam saMvarta vivarta praBAvitam ADyAtmikAH tu saMskAra ajAti jarA Adi praBAvitAH
# phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs ni 'jig-pa #  dang chags bas rab-tu-phye-ba #  yin la / / nang gi 'du-byed-rnams #  ni skye-ba #  dang rga-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
etat uktam Bavati vinASa utpAda oGasya rUpasya saMvarta vivarta Sabdena loke prasidDO= iti BagavatA api lokam anuvartamAnena taTA eva uktO na jAti Adi Sabdena
# de ni 'di-skad-du #  'jig-rten #  na phyi'i gzugs kyi 'jig-pa-dang-skye-ba #  la 'jig-pa #  dang chags-pa # 'i sgrar grags-pa # s bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis kyang 'jig-rten-dang-mthun-pa # r de-skad #  du bshad de / / skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgrar ni ma yin no / / nang gi 'du-byed-rnams #  ni skyes so / / rgas so /
ADyAtmikAH tu saMskArAH jAti jarA Adi praBAvitAH jAtAH jIrNAH sTitAH vinazwAH iti tezAm BagavatA apiloka anuvRttyA utpAda AdayaH jAti Adi Sabdena nirdizwAH iti / nAmakAya aDarmANAm
# gnas so / / zhig go zhes skye-ba #  dang rga-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba #  yin te / / bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis kyang 'jig-rten-dang-mthun-pa # r de-dag #  gi 'byung-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgrar bstan to zhes bshad-pa #  yin no / / ming-gi-tshogs #  gang zhe na /
svaBAva aDivacanAni / aBiDeyam aBiDeyam pratijQAnam nAmayati iti nAma / tat punar arTezu kRta avaDi varNa samudAyaH
# chos-rnams #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi tshig bla dags so zhes-bya-ba #  ni brjod-par-bya-ba #  dang brjod-pa #  la rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzhol-bar-byed-pa # s ming ngo / / de-yang #  don rnams la brda sprod ba'i yi-ge #  'dus-pa #  ste /
nAmnAm varNAnAm vA samudAya unmakAyaH / DarmANAm svarUpasya anAKyeya tvAt aDyAropya vacanam aDivacanam / svaBAvaH sva lakzaNam
# ming ngam yi-ge #  rnams 'dus-pa #  la ming-gi-tshogs #  zhes-bya'o #  / / chos-rnams #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  brjod-du-med-pa # 'i phyir sgro-btags-pa # 'i tshig la tshig bla dags zhes-bya'o #  /
yena anaBilapya svarUpANAm DarmANAm svarUpam dyotyati etat aBiDAnam nAma iti ucyate tat yaTA cakzuH SrotraMrUpam SabdaH iti
# ngo-bo-nyid #  ni rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  do / / chos-rnams #  kyi rang-gi #  ngo bo brjod du med kyang gang-gis #  rang-gi #  ngo bo gsal-bar-byed-pa # 'i brjod-pa #  de ming zhes bya ste / / dper-na #  mig rna-ba #  gzugs sgra zhes-bya-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
pada kAya aDarmANAm viSeza aDivacanAni / padyate anena sa viSezaH arTaH iti padam
# tshig gi tshogs gang zhe na / / chos-rnams #  kyi khyad-par #  gyi tshig bla dags so zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dis khyad-par #  gyi don shes-par-byed-pa # s tshig ste /
evam nAmnaH lOkikAt ca padAt padam viSezitam Bavati
# de lta na ming dang 'jig-rten-pa # 'i tshig las tshig bye-brag #  tu byas-pa #  yin no /
nAma padayoH varNa samudAya Atmaka tva aviSeze api arTa viSezAt viSezaH / DarmANAm svaBAva aDivacanam nAma viSeza aDivacanaMpadam / svaBAva aDizWAna tvAt viSezasya pUrvaMsu aBAva aDivacanam / viSezaH punar anitya tA AdikaH anuvRtti vyAvRtti AtmakaH / anyatra AvartamAnam svaBAvaMviSinazwi iti viSezaH tat yaTA anityAH sarva saMskArAH sarva DarmAH anAtmAnaH SAntam nirvANam
# ming dang tshig gnyis yi-ge #  'dus-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin par bye-brag #  med kyang don gyi bye-brag #  gis bye-brag #  tu dbye ste / / chos-rnams #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi tshig bla dags ni ming yin la / / khyad-par #  gyi gzhi ni ngo-bo-nyid #  yin-pas #  sngar ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi tshig bla dags smos so / / khyad-par #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / 'jug-pa-dang-ldog-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  dang gzhan-du #  mi snyegs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  las bye-brag #  tu byed-pa #  ni khyad-par #  te / / dper-na #  'du-byed-thams-cad #  ni mi-rtag-pa # 'o / / cho thams-cad #  ni bdag-med-pa # 'o / / ya ngan las 'das-pa #  ni zhi-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
etat uktam Bavati vastu svaBAva aBiDAna mAtram nAma viSizwa vastu svaBAva aBiDAnam padam iti / Sezam tunAma vyAKyAnataH vijQeyam / vyaQjana kAyAH akzarANi / tad uBaya aBivyaQjana tAm upAdAya / vyajyate anena iti vyaQjanam
# de ni 'di-skad-du #  dngos-po # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  brjod-pa #  tsam ni ming yin la / / dngos-po # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi khyad-par #  brjod-pa #  ni tshig yin no zhes bstan-pa #  yin no / / lhag-ma #  ni ming bshad-pa #  bzhin-du #  shes-pa # r bya'o / / yi-ge # 'i tshogs gang zhe na / / yi-ge #  rnams te de-gnyi-ga #  gsal-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dis gsal-bar-byed-pa # s yi-ge # 'o /
vyaQjanAnAm kAyaH vyaQjana kAyaH kAya grahaNam sarva vyaQjana upAdAna arTam / tad SabdAt kevalAt anantarasya eva sambanDaH ASaFkyeta / uBaya SabdAt api kevalAt katamasya uBayasya iti na vijQAyate / atOBaya aBiDAnam tat uBayam iti
# yi-ge #  rnams kyi tshogs ni yi-ge # 'i tshogs so / / tshogs smos-pa #  ni yi-ge #  thams-cad #  bsdu-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra 'ba'-zhig #  smos na ni gong-ma #  nyid la sbyor du dgos la / / gnyi-ga #  zhes-bya-ba #  nyi tshe smos na yang gnyi-ga #  gang-la #  bya-ba # r gtol med de / / de'i-phyir #  de-gnyi-ga #  zhes gnyi-ga #  smos so /
evam anantarasya eva nAmnaH padasya ca aBivyaQjaka tvAt vyaQjanam iti uktaMBavati
# de-ltar-na #  bshad ma-thag #  pa'i ming dang tshig gsal-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir yi-ge #  zhes bshad-pa #  yin no /
kaTam punar akzarEH nAma padayoH aBivyaQjanam
# ji-ltar #  na yi-ge #  rnams kyis ming dang tshig gsal-ba # r byed ce na /
akzarezu samuditezu svaBAva viSeza aDivacana avasTAm gatezu nAma pada prajQapanAt
# ngo-bo-nyid #  dang khyad-par #  gyi tshig bla dags kyi gnas-skabs #  su gyur-pa # 'i yi-ge #  'dus-pa #  rnams la ming dang tshig gdags-pa # 'i phyir te /
evam akzarEH nAma pada aBivyaQjana akzarANi na vAc vijQapti svaBAvAni
# de-ltar-na #  yi-ge #  rnams kyis ming dang tshig gsal-ba # r byed do / / yi-ge #  rnams kyi ngag gi rnam-par-rig-byed #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  ma yin te /
akAra AdayaH varNAH iti prasidDam loke
# yi-ge #  la-sogs-pa #  ni brjod-pa # 'o zhes 'jig-rten #  na grags so; /
te punar nAma pada ASraya tvena arTa saMvarNanAt varNA / ucyante / yad avasTezu arTezu vyutpAdyante tad avasTAezu eva nAma padayoH prajQaptiH iti te tad ASraya tvena ucyante
# de-dag #  ni ming dang tshig gnas kyis don-yang-dag-pa # r brjod-pa # 'i phyir brjod-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / don gyi gnas gang dag la bstan-pa # 'i gnas de-dag #  la ming dang tshig gdags-pa # s de-dag #  ni de'i-gnas #  zhes-bya'o #  /
akzara tvam punar tezAm paryAya akzaraNa tAm
# yi-ge #  yang de-dag #  gi rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa #  gzhan-du-mi-'gyur-ba # r byed-pa # 'i phyir te /
upAdAya / taTA hi cakzuH netra Adi paryAya antara izu kzarati / aBiDeya tvena paryAya antarEH gamyate iti arTaH / na punar evam akArasya paryAya antaram asti yena AkAra aBiDAnam uktvA AkAraH gamyeta
# 'di-ltar #  mig dang 'dren byed ces bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa #  gzhan dag tu 'gyur-ba #  ste / / brjod-par-bya-ba #  nyid rnam gangs su gtogs-pa #  gzhan rnams kyis shes so zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / gang-gis #  aa zhes brjod-pa #  ma-gtogs-par #  aa zhes-bya-ba #  shes-par-'gyur-ba #  aa zhes-bya-ba # 'i rnam-grangs #  de-lta-bu #  gzhan med do /
etAvat ca sarvam yat uta svaBAvaH viSezaH tad uBaya vyavahAraH ca
# thams-cad #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / ngo-bo-nyid #  dang khyad-par #  dang de-gnyi-ga # 'i tha-snyad #  tsam du zad de /
tat sarvam eBiH anuvyavahriyate iti atas ete nAmapada vyaQjana kAya avyavasTApitAH iti
# de-dag #  thams-cad #  ni 'di dag gis rjes su tha-snyad #  gdags-pa #  yin-pas #  de'i-phyir #  ming dang tshig-dang-yi-ge # 'i tshogs de-dag #  rnam-pa # r gzhag go; /
evam anyezAm api viprayuktAn aMnAma pada vyaQjana kAya vat prayojana apekzayA vyavasTAnaMveditavyam
# de-bzhin-du #  ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  gzhan dag kyang tshig-dang-yi-ge # 'i tshogs bzhin-du #  dgos-pa #  la ltos nas rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
pRTagjana tvam Arya DarmANAm alABa iti / yasya Darmasya yogAt pRTagjanaH iti AKyAyate tad pRTagjana tvam / ArAt yAtAH pApakeByaH akuSala iBoDarmeByaH iti AryAH / te punar SEkzAH aSEkzAH / tezAm Darma adarSana BAvanA SEkza mArgAH
# so-so'i-skye-bo #  nyid gang zhe na / / 'phags-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  ma-thob-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni chos gang dang ldan na so-so'i-skye-bo #  zhes brjod-pa #  de so-so'i-skye-bo #  nyid do / / sdig-pa #  mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams las ring-du-song-ba # s 'phags-pa #  rnams so / / de-dag #  kyang slob-pa #  dang mi-slob-pa #  rnams te / / de-dag #  gi chos-rnams #  ni mthong-ba #  dang bsgom-pa #  dang mi-slob-pa # 'i lam rnams te /
tezAm alABaH pRTagjana tvam
# de-dag #  ma-thob-pa #  ni so-so'i-skye-bo #  nyid do /
alABaH punar atra Arya DarmANAm anutpAdaH
# ma-thob-pa #  ni 'dir 'phags-pa # 'i chos ma-skyes-pa #  ste /
taTA hi anutpanna Arya DarmaH sattva santAnaH pRTagjanaH iti ucyate
# 'di-ltar #  'phags-pa # 'i chos ma-skyes-pa # 'i sems-can #  gyi rgyud la so-so'i-skye-bo #  zhes-bya'o #  /
Arya Darma utpAdAt tu AryaH iti / pravRttiH katamA / hetu Pala prabanDa anupacCedaH pravRttiH iti ucyate / na ekasmin kzaNe prabanDa uparame vA apravRtti upacAraH / pratiniyamaH katamaH / hetu Pala nAnAtve pratiniyama vyavasTA
# 'phags-pa # 'i chos skyes-pa #  la ni 'phags-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / 'jug-pa #  gang zhe na / / rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  rgyun-mi-'chad-pa #  la 'jug-pa #  zhes bya ste / / skad-cig-gcig #  la'am / / rgyun-chad-pa #  la ni 'jug-pa #  gdags-pa #  ma yin no / / so-so # r nge pa gang zhe na / / rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  tha-dad-pa #  nyid la so-sor-nges-pa #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ste /
hetu Pala nAnAtvam punar izwasya vizayasya su caritam anizwasya duScaritam ityAdi Pala anAMpRTak anyonya hetutA / yogaH katamaH / hetu Pala anurUpye yogaH iti prajQaptiH
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  tha-dad-pa #  yang 'dod-pa # 'i yul gyi ni legs-par-spyad-pa # 'o / / mi-'dod-pa #  ni nyes-pa # r spyad ba'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i ni 'bras-bu #  so-so-ba #  rnams kyi rgyu tha-dad-pa # 'o / / 'byor-ba #  gang zhe na / / rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  'tsham-pa #  la 'byor-pa #  gdags te /
tat yaTA dAnasya Boga sampad anurUpa iti yujyate dAnasya Boga sampad Palam / sjavaH katamaH
# dper-na #  sbyin-pa #  ni longs-spyod #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  dang 'tsham-pa # r rigs-pa # r sbyin-pa'i-'bras-bu #  ni longs-spyod #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o / / mgyogs-pa #  gang zhe na /
hetu Pala ASu pravRttO javaH iti prajQaptiH
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  myur-du #  'byung-ba #  la mgyogs-pa #  zhes gdags so /
anukramaH katamaH
# go-rims #  gang zhe na /
hetu Pala ekEka pravRttO= anukramaH iti prajQaptiH
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  re-re-nas #  'byung-ba #  la go-rims #  zhes gdags te /
kEkatvena pravRttiH ayugapad pravRttiH kAlaH katamaH
# re-re-nas #  'byung gi cig-car-du #  'byung-ba #  ni ma yin no / / dus gang zhe na /
hetu Pala prabanDa pravRttO kAlaH iti prajQaptiH / hetu PalayoH prabanDena pravRttO satyAm yat tatra hetu Palam utpanna nirudDam saH atItaH kAlaH iti prajQapyate
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  rgyun-du #  'byung-ba #  la dus zhes gdags te / / rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  'byung-ba #  la de-la # s rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  byung nas 'gags-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de 'das-pa'i-dus #  zhes gdags so /
yat anutpannam saH anAgataH
# gang ma-byung-ba #  de ma-'ongs-pa # 'i dus so /
yat utpanna anirudDam sa pratyutpannaH kAlaH / deSaH katamaH
# gang byung-ba #  ma 'gags-pa #  de da-ltar-byung-ba # 'i dus so / / yul gang zhe na /
pUrva dakziNa paScima uttara aDara UrDva asusarvataH daSasu dikzu hetu PalaH eva deSaH iti prajQaptiH
# shar dang lho dang nub dang byang dang 'og dang steng dang phyogs-bcu #  thams-cad-la #  rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  yod-pa-nyid #  la yul zhes gdags te /
hetu Palasya diS vyAptO deSa upacAraH
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # s phyogs khyab-pa #  la yul zhes gdags so /
rUpa saFgRhItam cahetu Palam veditavyam arUpiNAm diS vyApanAsAm arTyAt
# gzugs su bsdus-pa #  ni rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / gzugs-med-pa #  rnams ni phyogs la khyab-par-byed-pa # r mi-nus-pa # 'i phyir ro /
saFKyA katamA
# grangs gang zhe na /
saMskArANAm pratyekaSaH Bede saFKyA iti prajQaptiH
# 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi so-so #  tha-dad-pa #  la grangs zhes gdags te /
BedaH iti aBinna eka Atmaka tvedvitIya saFKyA anupapatteH
# tha-dad-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni tha-dad-pa #  ma yin zhing gcig pa'i bdag-nyid #  la gnyis zhes-bya-ba #  grangs mi 'thad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sAmagrI katamA / hetu pratyaya sama vaDAne sAmagrI iti prajQaptiH
# tshogs-pa #  gang zhe na / / rgyu-dang-rkyen #  'dus-pa #  la tshogs-pa #  zhes gdags so /
evam ete citta viprayuktAH saMskArAH DarmANAm avasTA viSezezu prajQapyante iti prajQaptisantaH veditavyAH / uktaH saMskAra skanDaH
# de-ltar-na #  sems dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  'di dag ni chos-rnams #  kyi gnas-skabs #  kyi khyad-par #  la gdags-pa # s rtags yod-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po #  bshad-zin #  to /
saMskAra skanDa antar aMvijQAna skanDaH veditavyaH iti atas Aha vijQAna skanDaH
# 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po # 'i 'og-tu #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i phung-po #  bshad-par-bya #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gang zhe na /
katamaH iti / Alambana vijQaptiH iti Alambanam citta cEtta vizayaH
# dmigs-pa #  rnam-par-rig-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smras so / / dmigs-pa #  ni sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i yul te /
sa punar zaz prakAraH rUpam yAvat DarmAH
# de-yang #  gzugs nas chos kyi bar-du #  rnam-pa-drug #  go /
tasya vijQaptiH grahaNam avaboDaH pratipattiH iti arTaH
# de-yang #  rnam-par-rig-pa #  ni 'dzin-pa #  dang rtog-pa #  dang khong-du-chud-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
sA punar zax pravRtti vijQAnAni cakzuH vijQAnam yAvat manaH vijQAnam
# de ni 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  drug ste mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  nas yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
tatra cakzuH vijQAnam cakzuH indriya ASraya arUpa prativijQaptiH
# de-la #  mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mig-gi-dbang-po #  la brten-nas #  yul so-so # r rnam-par-rig-pa # 'o /
evam yAvat manaH vijQAnaMmanA Endriya ASrayA sarva Darma prativijQaptiH
# de-bzhin-du #  yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du #  yang yid-kyi-dbang-po #  la brten-nas #  chos-thams-cad #  so-so # r rnam-par-rig-pa # 'o /
vijQAna svarUpam uktvA tad paryAya pradarSana arTam Aha cittam manaH apitat iti / tat vijQAnam cittam api ucyate / manaH iti api iti / paryAya arTa pradarSana arTam Aha citra tAm manaH sanniSrayatAm ca upAdAya iti / citra tAm upAdAya cittam iti ucyate / samanantara citta sanniSrayatAm upAdAya manaH iti
# rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo bshad nas / / de'i rnam-grangs #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / sems dang yid kyang de yin te / / zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  de ni sems zhes kyang bya / / yid ces kyang bya'o / / rnam-grangs #  kyi don bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / sna-tshogs-pa #  dang yid rten byed-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / sna-tshogs-pa # 'i phyir sems zhes-bya'o #  / / de-ma-thag-pa # 'i sems kyi rten byed-pa # s yid ces bya'o /
tatra pravRtti vijQAnasya Alambana prativijQapti svarUpa tvAt Alambanasya ca prativijQAnam aneka AkAra tva cakzuH Adi vijQAnam citram utpadyate
# de-la #  'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  so-sor-rig-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  yin pa dang dmigs-pa #  so-so # r rnam-par-rig-pa #  yang rnam-pa-du-ma #  yin pa'i phyir / / mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni sna-tshogs #  zhes-bya'o #  /
atas eva tad indriya ASrayeNa api utpadyamAnam vizayam vijAnAti iti ucyatena indriyam
# de'i-phyir #  de'i dbang-po #  la brten-nas-'byung-ba #  na yul rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes bya'i / / dbang-po #  rnams ni ma yin no /
taTA zaNNAm cakzuH Adi vijQAnAnAm yat yat niruDyatetat tat anantarasya vijQAnasya utpadyamAnasya ASraya BAvena vyavatizWataH iti atas samanantara citta sanniSrayatAm upAdAya manaH iti ucyate
# 'di-ltar #  mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  drug-po #  gang-dang-gang #  'gags-pa #  de-dang-de #  ni de-ma-thag-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i rten gyi dngos-po # r gnas te / / de'i-phyir #  de-ma-thag-pa # 'i sems kyi rten byed-pa # s yid ces bya'o /
yat etat citra tvAt cittam iti uktam tat jAtim aDikRtya nalakzaNam
# sna-tshogs-pa # 'i phyir sems zhes-bya'o #  zhes gang bshad-pa #  de ni rigs kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  yin gyi skad-cig #  la ni ma yin no /
lakzaNam tu pratiniyata Alambana AkAra tvAt na citram iti na tat prADAnyena cittam / prADAnyena punar / cittam AlayavijQAnam
# skad-cig #  ni dmigs-pa #  so-sor-nges-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  yin-pas #  sna-tshogs #  zhes mi bya ste / / de ni dngos su sems ma yin no / / dngos su na sems ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste /
atra eva kAraNam Aha taTA ahitat citam sarva saMskAra bIjEH iti
# 'dir rgyu bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / 'di-ltar #  de'i 'du-byed-thams-cad #  kyi sa-bon #  bsags-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
pratikzaNam / lsarva saMskAra bIjEH cita tvAt cittam iti prADAnyena tat eva cittam
# skad-cig-re-re-la #  'du-byed-thams-cad #  kyi sa-bon #  bsags-pa # s sems zhes bya ste / / dngos su na de nyid sems so /
cayaH tu pOnaHpunyena bIja paripozaH saMskAra bIja anusyUtiH vA
# bsags-pa #  ni yang-dang-yang #  sa-bon #  yongs su gsos pa'am / / 'du-byed #  kyi sa-bon #  rjes-su-'brel-ba # 'o /
saMskAraH atra sa AsravAH Darma aBipretAH / tezAm punar utpattiH caturByaH pratyayeByaH
# 'du-byed-rnams #  ni 'dir zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  su 'dod de / / de-dag #  kyang rkyen bzhi las 'byung ngo /
tatra hetu pratyayaH AlayavijQAna sannivizwAH vAsanA
# de-la #  rgyu'i-rkyen #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gnas-pa # 'i bag-chags #  te /
pOnaHpunyena saMskArANAm samudAcArAt bIja puzwiH vAsanA iti ucyate
# yang-dang-yang #  'du-byed-rnams #  kun du 'byung-ba # s sa-bon #  brtas-pa #  la bag-chags #  zhes-bya'o #  /
aDipati pratyayaH cakzuH AdIni indriyANi / samanantara pratyayaH samanantara nirudDam vijQAnam
# bdag-po'i-rkyen #  ni mig la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang-po #  rnams so / / de-ma-thag-pa # 'i rkyen ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  'gags-ma-thag-pa # 'o /
Alambana pratyayaH rUpa AdikaH
# dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'o /
taTA hi sUtre api uktam cakzuH apariBnam Bavati rUpANi ABAsa gatAni tad jaH camanasikAraH pratyupasTitaH Bavati evam tad jasya cakzuH vijQAnasya prAdurBAvaH Bavati iti
# 'di-ltar #  mdo las kyang mig nyams-pa # r ma gyur la gzugs rnams kyang snang-bar-gyur-pa #  dang de skyed-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  yang nye-bar-gnas-pa # r gyur na de-la # s byung-ba # 'i mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba # r 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so /
evaMSrotra Adi vijQAnezu api yaTAsamBavam vAcyam
# de-bzhin-du #  rna-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la yang ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du brjod-pa # r bya'o /
hetu pratyayaH tu sadA sannihita tvAt durvijQeya tvAt ca na uktaH
# rgyu'i-rkyen #  rtag-tu #  gnas-pa #  dang shes-par-dka'-ba # 'i phyir ma smos so / / de'i-'og-tu #  kun du tshol-ba # 'i yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o /
tad anantaram paryezakam manaH vijQAnam paryAyezakAt anantaraMvyavasTApakam evam vyavasTApaka anantaram vikalpakam manaH vijQAnam utpadyate / tatra ca vizayAt saFkliSyatA iva avadAyate vA / tad avasTaH ca puNya apuNyAn iQjyAn saMskArAn= cetanA AtmakAn aBisaMskaroti
# kun du tshol-ba # 'i 'og-tu #  rnam-par-'jog-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-'jog-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung ste; de'i tshe yul las kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # r 'gyur ro / / de'i tshe bsod nams dang bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  dang mi g-yo-ba # 'i 'du-byed #  sems-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-can #  rnams mngon-pa # r 'du-byed #  do /
te aBisaMskRta aniDyamAna Alaya vijQAne vipAka vAsanAm vA puzNanti nizyanda vAsanAm vA
# mngon-par-'du-byas-pa #  de-dag #  'gag-pa #  na kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i bag-chags #  so / / rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i bag-chags #  gso-ba # r byed do /
tatra nizyanda vAsanAm Agamya Alaya vijQAnAt puNya apuNya aniQjyAH saMskArAH pravartante
# de-la #  rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i bag-chags #  la brten-nas #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las bsod nams dang bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  dang mi g-yo-ba # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  'byung ngo /
vipAka vAsanAm Agamya Alaya vijQAnAt nikAya saBAga antarezu AlayavijQAnam eva vipAka Atmaka nirvartate
# rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i bag-chags #  la brten-nas #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las ris-mthun-pa #  gzhan dag tu kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  du 'grub bo /
tatra ye api anye akuSalAH kuSala sa AsravAH ca DarmAH tezAm api ayam eva nayaH
# de-la #  mi-dge-ba #  dang dge-ba #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos gzhan gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  la yang tshul 'di nyid do /
avyAkRtAH tu nizyanda vAsanAm eva puzNanti na vipAka vAsanAm tezAm avipAkatvAt
# lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  ni rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i bag-chags #  nyid gso-ba # r byed kyi / / rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i bag-chags #  ni ma yin te / / de-dag #  la rnam-par-smin-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tat evam AlayavijQAnam dvi prakAram
# de-ltar-na #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  de rnam-pa-gnyis #  te /
nizyanda vAsanAm upAdAya kAryam kAraNam ca
# rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i bag-chags #  la brten-nas #  rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  ste /
taTA hi sarva saMskArAH sva bIja ADAna vartamAnAH AlayavijQAna Atma atiSaya hetu BAvena vyavatizWanta eti sarva saMskArANAm tat kAryam
# 'di-ltar #  'du-byed-thams-cad #  rang-gi-sa-bon #  bskyed-pa #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu 'gyur-ba'i-rgyu # 'i dngos-po # r gnas-pa # s de ni 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi 'bras-bu # 'o /
sarva saMskArAH catat bIja upAdAnAt AlayavijQAnAt utpadyante iti sarva saMskArANAm AlayavijQAnam kAraNam
# 'du-byed-thams-cad #  de-dag #  gi sa-bon #  nye-bar-len-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las 'byung-ba # 'i phyir kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni 'du-byed-thams-cad #  kyi rgyu yin no /
vipAka vAsanAm tu aDikRtya kuSala akuSalAnAm saMskArANAm kAryam eva tad na kAraNam
# rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i bag-chags #  kyi dbang-du-byas-te #  / / dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi 'bras-bu #  yin gyi rgyu ni ma yin no /
kAraNam tu tat vipAka vAsanAm upAdAya nikAya saBA antarezu vipAka vijQAnasya eva iti
# rgyu ni rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i bag-chags #  la brten-nas #  ris-mthun-pa #  gzhan dag tu rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rgyu'o /
pravRtti vijQAnam hi rUpa Sabda Adi Alambana tvAt sva sAmAnya lakzaNa AkAra tvAt caparicCinna Alambanam paricCinna AkAram ca
# 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni gzugs dang sgra la-sogs-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  dang rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  kyi rnam-pa #  yin pa'i phyir dmigs-pa #  yongs su chad-pa #  dang rnam shes yongs su chad-pa # 'o /
AlayavijQAnam punar aparicCinna Alambana AkAram
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  dang rnam-pa #  yongs su ma chad-pa #  ste /
na hi asya Alambanam paricCettum Sakyatena AkAraH / kim kAraNam
# 'di'i dmigs-pa #  dang rnam-pa #  yongs su gcad-pa # r mi nus so / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
yasmAt Alaya vijQAnam dvAByAm AlambanAByAm pravartate
# 'di-ltar #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  gnyis la 'jug-pa #  ste /
aDyAtmam upAdAna vijQaptitaH bahirDA paricCinna AkAra BAjana vijQaptitaH ca
# nang gi nye-bar-len-pa # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  dang phyi-rol #  gyi snod la rnam-par-rig-pa #  rnam-pa #  yongs su ma chad-pa # 'o /
tatra aDyAtmam upAdAnam parikalpita svaBAva aBiniveSa vAsanA sa aDizWAnam ca indriya rUpam
# de-la #  nang gi nye-bar-len-pa #  ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i bag-chags #  dang gnas-dang-bcas-pa # 'i dbang-po # 'i gzugs so /
etat ca Alambanam sUkzma tvAt loka paNXitEH apidura vaDAram iti atas aparicCinna Alambana AkAram iti ucyate napunaH anAlambanam eva
# dmigs-pa #  'di gnyis ni phra-ba # 'i phyir 'jig-rten #  gyi mkhas-pa #  rnams kyis kyang rtogs-par-dka'-ba # s de'i-phyir #  dmigs-pa #  dang rnam-pa #  yongs su ma chad-pa #  zhes bya'i /
pravRtti vijQAnam kuSala klizwa avyAkRta jAtIyam AlayavijQAnam tu eka jAtIyam
# dmigs-pa-med-pa #  nyid ni ma yin no / / 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni dge-ba #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  no / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni rigs gcig pa yin no /
tatra na tAvat kuSala akuSala jAtIyam / kuSala akuSalEH asamprayogAt
# de-la #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i rang-bzhin #  ni ma yin te / / de dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  rnams dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tat hi paQcaBiH eva sarva tragEH cEtasEH samprayujyata imam anaskAra sparSa vedanA saQjQA cetanABiH
# de ni sems-las-byung-ba #  kun du 'gro-ba #  yid-la-byed-pa #  dang reg-pa #  dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang sems-pa #  lnga po kho-na #  dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no /
AlayavijQAna aMsa samprayogam pUrva karma saMskAra hetuka tvAt ekAntena vipAkaH eva iti avyAkRta jAtIyam eva / santAna anuvRtti ca
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa # r sngon-gyi-las #  kyi 'du-byed #  kyi rgyu-las-byung-ba # s gcig-tu #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  nyid yin pa'i phyir lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'i rigs so /
atra hi Alaya vijQAna aMnikAya saBA antarezu pratisanDim upAdAya yAvat cyutiMtAvat kzaNa prabanDa pravAhena vartate na tu antara antarA avicCidyate pravRtti vijQAna vat
# rgyun-chags-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'o / / de-la #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni ris-mthun-pa #  gzhan dag tu nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba #  nas-bzung-ste #  / / ji tsam na 'chi-'pho-ba #  de'i bar-du #  skad-cig #  rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  'jug gi / / 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  bzhin-du #  bar-skabs #  bar-skabs #  su chad-pa #  ni ma yin te /
taTA hi cakzuH vijQAna anantaraMSrotra Adi vijQAnAni utpadyante Srotra vijQAna anantaraMcakzuH Adi vijQAnAni / evam GrANa Adi vijQAna anantaram iti vistareNa vAcyam
# 'di-ltar #  mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  rna-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams 'byung-ba #  dang rna-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams 'byung-ba #  dang de-bzhin-du #  sna la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
taTA kuSala anantaram akuSalam utpadyate akuSala anantaram kuSalam tat uBaya anantaram avyAkRta mhIna DAtuka anantaram maDya DAtukam maDya DAtuka anantaram praNIta DAtu kampraNIta DAtuka anantaram apraNIta DAtukam apraNIta DAtuka anantaram maDya DAtukam iti vistareNa vAcyam
# de-bzhin-du #  dge-ba # 'i 'og-tu #  mi-dge-ba #  'byung-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i 'og-tu #  dge-ba #  dang de gnyis-ka # 'i 'og-tu #  lung du mi ston-pa #  dang khams dman-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  khams bar-ma #  dang khams bar-ma # 'i 'og-tu #  khams gya-nom-pa #  dang khams gya-nom-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  gya-nom-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  dang khams gya-nom-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  khams bar-ma #  zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  brjod-pa # r bya ste /
na api ekam dravyam A maraNAt anuvartate iti
# shi-ba #  la thug gi bar-du #  rdzas gcig-tu #  'jug-pa #  ni ma yin no /
zaz prakAra pravRtti vijQAna vyatiriktam anyat AlayavijQAnam asti iti kaTam vijQAyate / AgamataH yuktitaH ca
# 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  drug-po #  ma-gtogs-par #  gzhan kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  yod-pa # r ci mngon zhe na / / lung dang rigs-pas #  mngon no /
tatra AgamaH uktaMBagavata aBiDarma sUtre anAdi kAlikaH DAtuH sarva Darma samASrayaH
# de-la #  ni 'di ni lung yin te / / bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis chos-mngon-pa # 'i mdo las / / thog-ma-med-pa # 'i dus kyi dbyings / / chos-rnams #  kun gyi gnas yin te /
tasmin sati gatiH sarvAH nirvANa aDigamaH api ca
# de yod-pa # s na 'gro kun dang / / mya-ngan #  'das-pa # 'ang thob-pa # r 'gyur / / zhes gsungs so /
punar ca sanDi nirmocane api uktam AdAna vijQAna gamBIra sUkzmaH oGaH yaTA vartati sarva bIjaH / bAlAnaH ezaH mayi na prakASitaH mA ha eva AtmA parikalpayeyuH
# yang dgongs ba nges-par-'grel-ba # 'i mdo las kyang / / len-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  zab cing phra / / sa-bon #  thams-cad #  chu-bo # 'i rgyun bzhin 'bab / / bdag tu rtog-pa # r gyur na mi rung zhes / / 'di ni byis-pa #  rnams la ngas ma bstan / / zhes gsungs so /
yuktim api aDikRtya Aha yatas niroDa samApatti asaQjQi samApattyA saQjQij / eByaH vyutTitasya punar vizaya vijQapti AKyam pravRtti vijQAnam / utpadyate
# rigs-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-te #  / / 'di-ltar #  'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dang 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dang 'du-shes-med-pa #  po rnams las langs-nas #  yang yul rnam-par-rig-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung /
tat AlayavijQAnam pravRtti vijQAneByaH arTa antaram iti vAkyaSezaH
# zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams las don-gzhan-du-gyur-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  tshig gi lhag-ma # 'o /
niroDa asaQjQi samApatti samApannasya asaQjQike ca prAdurBUteniravaSezezu pravRtti vijQAnezu nirudDezu punar vyutTAna kAla Alaya vijQAnam antareNa pravRtti vijQAna utpattiH na yujyate / na hi samApatti cittAt tasya utpattiH yuktA tasya cira nirudDa tvAt nirudDasya ca asattvAt asat ca na kAryam na kAraNaMpraDAna Atma Adi vat / yaH api manyate anapAya upAdAna vikAra aMBAva svarUpam / anAgata vartamAna atIta tvam tu BAva anAMkAritra dvArakam / taTA hi akurvad kAritraH anAgataH kurvat kAritraH vartamAnaH uparata kAritraH atItaH iti ucyate / evaMtarhi kAritram BAvAt anyat iti aByupagantavyam atIta anAgata avasTayoH kAritre asatI api BAva aByupagamAt / evam ca kAritrasya eva utpAdaH vyayaH ca na BAvAnAm aBUtvA aBAvAt BUtvA ca aBAvAt na ca rUpa vedanA saQjQA saMskAra vijQAnAnAm sarvadA svarUpa aDyAsita tvAt
# 'gog-pa #  dang 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dang 'du-shes-med-pa #  par gyur-pa #  na 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams ma-lus-par #  'gag-pa #  las yang ldang-ba # 'i tshe kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  med na 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung du mi rung ngo / / snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sems las de 'byung du mi rung ste / / de 'gags nas ring du lon pa dang 'gags-pa #  de med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / med-pa #  ni rgyur yang mi rung 'bras-bu # r yang mi rung ste / / gtso bo dang bdag la-sogs-pa #  bzhin no / / gang yang 'di snyam-du #  dngos-po # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo la skye-ba-dang-'jig-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i dngos-po #  med kyi ma-'ongs-pa #  dang da-ltar #  dang 'das-pa #  ni dngos-po #  rnams kyi byed-pa # 'i sgo nas yin te / / 'di-ltar #  bya-ba #  mi-byed-pa #  ni ma-'ongs-pa # 'o / / bya-ba-byed-pa #  ni da-ltar #  ro / / byed ba rgyun-chad-pa #  ni 'das-pa # 'o zhes-bya'o #  snyam-du #  sems-pa #  de-lta-bu #  yin na ni byed-pa #  las dngos-po #  gzhan yin par khas-blang-ba # r bya ste / / 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  gnyis kyi dus na byed-pa #  med kyang dngos-po #  khas-len-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar-na #  med-pa #  las byung-ba #  dang byung nas kyang med-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir-'byung-ba #  dang 'jig-pa #  ni byed-pa #  yin gyi / / dngos-po #  rnams kyis ni ma yin no / / gzugs dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams kyis ma-yin-pa #  nyid de /
tatas ca utpAda vyaya aBAvAt niroDa vat na anityAH rUpa AdayaH skanDAH syuH
# rtag-tu #  rang-gi #  ngo bo dang ldan-pa #  dang de-yang #  'byung-ba #  dang 'jig-pa #  med ba'i phyir te / / gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams ni 'gog-pa #  bzhin-du #  mi-rtag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # r 'gyur ro /
tatas ca duHKAH api na syuH
# de'i-phyir #  sdug-bsngal-bar #  yang mi 'gyur te /
uktam hi sUtre yat anityam tat duHKam iti
# mdo las ni mi-rtag-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de sdug-bsngal-ba # 'o zhes gsungs so /
evam caskanDAn anityataH duHKataH ca cintayataH viparyAsaH eva syAt
# de lta na ni phung-po #  rnams la ni mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  nyid-du #  sems-pa #  phyin-ci-log #  nyid-du #  'gyur ro /
na ca viparyAsAt kleSa prahANam yuktam anitye duHKe ca nitya suKa viparyAsa vat
# phyin-ci-log #  gis ni nyon-mongs-pa #  spang-ba # r mi rigs te / / mi-rtag-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  la rtag-pa #  dang bde-ba # r phyin-ci-log-pa #  bzhin no /
kAritrasya ca utpAda vyaya samBavAt saMskRta tvam rUpa Adizu ca skanDezu saFgraha aBAvAt zazWaH skanDaH aByupagantavyaH kanDaH
# byed-pa #  la ni 'byung-ba #  dang 'jig-pa #  yod-pa # s 'dus byas nyid yin te / / gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams su ni ma 'dus-pa # s phung-po #  drug-pa # r khas-blang-ba # r bya'o /
na ca sa AsravAH Darma upAdAna skanDEH sarve vA saMskRtAH skanDEH saFgRhItAH iti vaktavyam
# yang nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams kyis zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  dang phung-po #  rnams kyis 'dus byas thams-cad #  bsdus so zhes ma zer cig /
anyaH punar Aha kAritram nAma Pala parigrahaH
# yang gzhan na re byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'bras-bu #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa # 'o /
DarmaH hi yasya Darmasya hetu BAvena vyavatizWatesa DarmaH taMDarmam Pala tvena gRhNAti iti atas hetu BAva vyavasTAna saMBAvAnAm Pala parigrahaH / hetu BAvena ca saH eva DarmaH vyavatizWataH iti DarmeByaH kAritram ananyat
# chos gang zhig chos gang-gi #  rgyu dngos-po # r gnas-pa #  ste / / chos dang chos de 'bras-bu # r 'dzin-pa #  de'i-phyir #  rgyu'i-dngos-po # r gnas-pa #  ni dngos-po #  rnams kyi 'bras-bu #  yongs su 'dzin te / / chos de nyid rgyu'i-dngos-po # r gnas-pa # s na chos-rnams #  las-byed-pa #  gzhan ma yin no /
atas cana anantara ukta doza prasaFgaH / ananyaH hi nAma saH eva / etat uktam Bavati na anyat kAritram DarmAt kim tarhi DarmaH eva kAritram / taTA kAritrAt na anyaH DarmaH / kAritram eva DarmaH iti / evam ca atIta anAgatayoH aDvanoH kAritra vat Darma aBAvaH
# de-bas-na #  gong-du #  smos-pa # 'i skyon du mi 'gyur ro zhes zer ro / / gzhan ma yin zhes-bya-ba #  ni de nyid de / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  chos las-byed-pa #  gzhan ma yin te / / chos-nyid #  byed-pa # 'o / / de-bzhin-du #  byed-pa #  las kyang chos gzhan ma yin te / / byed-pa #  nyid chos yin no zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / de lta na ni 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  gnyis kyis chos-rnams #  byed-pa #  bzhin-du #  med-pa # r 'gyur te /
tatas ca atIta anAgatAH titvavAdaH parityakta uBayavati
# de'i-phyir #  'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  yod do zhes smras-pa #  btang-ba #  yin no /
kAritrasya vA Darma svarUpa vat DarmAt ananyatvAt trEyaDvaka tvam aByupagantavyam
# yang-na #  byed-pa #  yang chos kyi rang-gi #  ngo bo bzhin-du #  chos las gzhan ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir dus-gsum #  par khas blang dgos te /
evam apikAritreNa aDvAnaH vyavasTitAH iti vAda hAniH / kAritram ca kurvan vartamAnaH izyate / anyat ca anyena kriyate na sva AtmanA eva tasya kRta tvAt / akRtam ca kriyate na kRtam
# de-lta-na-yang #  byed-pa #  las dus rnams rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r smra-ba #  nyams-pa # r 'gyur ro / / bya-ba-byed-pa #  ni da-ltar #  du 'dod de / / gzhan ni gzhan gyis byed-pa #  la / / de byas-zin-pa # 'i phyir bdag-nyid-kyis #  ni ma yin no / / ma-byas-pa #  ni byed dgos kyi byas-zin-pa #  la ni ma yin no /
atas caDarma kAri trayoH kRta akRta tvAt spazwam anya tvam / tasmAt pUrva ukta dozaH tad avasTaH eva
# de'i-phyir #  byed-pa #  dang chos gnyis ni byas-pa #  dang ma-byas-pa #  ma-yin-pa # s tha-dad-pa # r mngon no; / / de-lta-bas-na #  gong-du #  smos-pa # 'i skyon de yod do /
Darma kAri trayaH ca ananya tvena aBAva prasaFgaH
# chos dang byed-pa #  gnyis kyang tha-dad-pa #  ma yin na ni rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  med-pa # r 'gyur te /
taTA hi Palasya kAraNa vat pUrvam eva parinizpanna tvAt Palasya kim kurvat kAraNam Bavati akurvat vA kaTam kAraNam / Palam api tena akriyamANaMkaTam tasya kAryam Bavati
# 'di-ltar #  'bras-bu #  yang rgyu bzhin-du #  thog-ma-nyid-nas #  yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i phyir 'bras-bu #  la ji zhig byed na rgyur 'gyur / / mi byed na yang rgyu zhes ji-skad-du #  bya 'bras-bu #  yang des ma byas-na #  de'i 'bras-bu # r ji-ltar #  'gyur /
kAritrANAm eva ca paraspara tA hetu Pala BAvaH na DarmANAm
# byed-pa #  rnams nyid phan tshun rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # 'i dngos-po # r 'gyur gyi / / chos-rnams #  kyi ni ma yin te /
taTA hi kAritre satikArita antaram BavatinA asati
# 'di-ltar #  byed-pa #  yod-na #  byed-pa #  gzhan 'byung gi med na ni ma yin te /
na tu Darma svarUpam na api Darma svarUpAt Darma svarUpam sarva dAH tattvAt / taTA cayasmin sati yat Bavati asati ca na Bavatitat tasya kAraNa mita rac ca kAryam
# chos kyi rang-bzhin #  la ni ma yin no / / chos kyi rang-bzhin #  las kyang chos kyi rang-bzhin #  ma yin te / / rtag-tu #  yod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar-na #  gang yod-na #  gang 'byung gi med na ni mi-'byung-ba #  de ni de'i rgyu yin no /
loka prasidDam etat / evam ca na Darma svarUpam kAraNam na kAryam iti loka SAstra viroDaH / kAritram Darmasya tattva anyatvena avAcyam iti anye / kimarTam tattvena avAcyam / Darma svaBAvam na Bavati iti
# cig shos ni 'bras-bu #  yin no zhes-bya-ba #  'di ni 'jig-rten #  gyi grags-pa # 'o / / de-ltar-na #  chos kyi rang-bzhin #  ni rgyu yang ma yin 'bras-bu #  yang ma-yin-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-pa #  dang bstan-bcos #  dang 'gal lo / / gzhan dag na re chos-rnams #  las-byed-pa #  de nyid dang gzhan-du #  brjod-par-bya-ba #  ma yin no zhes zer te / / ci'i-phyir #  de nyid ces mi brjod ce na / / chos kyi rang-bzhin-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro; /
kimarTam anyatvena na ucyate / anya svaBAvam api tat na eva iti antvena api na ucyate
# ci'i-phyir #  gzhan zhes mi brjod ce na / / chos kyi rang-bzhin #  de'i-ngo-bo-nyid #  yang ma-yin-pa # s gzhan zhes mi bya'o /
evam tarhi yat na tad svaBAvam na anya svaBAvam tat SaSavizANa vat niHsvaBAva tvAt na asti eva iti / kaTam avidyamAnam aDva vyavasTA nimittam Bavizyati
# de lta na ni gang de'i-ngo-bo-nyid #  kyang ma yin la gzhan gyi ngo-bo-nyid #  kyang ma-yin-pa #  de ni ri-bong-gi-rva #  bzhin-du #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # 'i phyir med-pa #  nyid yin te / / med-pa #  ni dus rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i rgyur ji-ltar #  'gyur /
evam kAritrAt sarvaTA api aDva vyavasTA na siDyati / tasmAt anutpannaH BAvaH anAgataH nirudDaH atItaH utpanna anirudDaH vartamAnaH iti aByupeyam
# de-ltar-na #  byed-pa #  las dus rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  mi 'grub bo / / de-lta-bas-na #  dngos-po #  ma-byung-ba #  ni ma-'ongs-pa #  yin / / 'gags-pa #  ni 'das-pa #  yin / / byung lam 'gags-pa #  ni de-ltar #  yin par khas-blang-ba # r bya'o /
na punar akurvad kAritraH anAgataH kurvat kAritraH vartamAnaH uparata kAritraH atItaH iti
# bya-ba #  mi-byed-pa #  ni ma-'ongs-pa #  / / bya-ba-byed-pa #  ni da-ltar #  / / byed-pa #  rgyun-chad-pa #  ni 'das-pa # 'o zhes khas-blang-ba # r mi bya'o /
anyaH punar Aha sa indriyam rUpam cittam ca anyonya bIjakam iti atas niroDa saQjQi samApattiByAm asaQjQikAt cavyuttizWataH sa indriyAt rUpAt cittam utpadyate
# yang gzhan dag na re dbang-po-dang-bcas-pa # 'i gzugs dang sems ni gcig gi sa-bon #  gcig yin te / / de'i-phyir #  'gog-pa #  dang 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dang 'du-shes-med-pa #  las ldang-ba #  na dbang-po #  dang bcas ba'i gzugs las sems 'byung ste /
yaTArUpya DAtoH cyavamAnasya cittAt eva cira nirudDam api sa indriyam rUpam utpadyate iti / tasmAt na atra kiQcid AlayavijQAnena prayojanam iti
# dper-na #  gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  nas 'chi-'pho-ba # 'i sems las kyang 'gags nas ring du lon ba dbang-po-dang-bcas-pa # 'i gzugs 'byung-ba #  lta-bu # 'o / / de-lta-bas-na #  'di-la #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ca dgos zhes zer te /
evam tarhi ekEkasya sattvasya dvO citta santAnO syAtAm / ekaH sa indriyAt rUpAt aparaH cittAt
# de-ltar-na #  sems-can #  re-re # 'i sems-kyi-rgyud #  kyang gnyis gnyis su 'gyur te / / gcig ni dbang-po-dang-bcas-pa # 'i gzugs las byung / / cig shos ni sems las 'byung-ba # r 'gyur ro /
ArUpyezu ca niroDa samApannasya rUpa aBAvAt vyutTAna aBAvaH
# gzugs-med-pa # 'i sems su 'gog-pa #  la snyoms-par-zhugs-pa #  ni gzugs-med-pa # s ldang-ba #  yang med do /
tatas ca asya parinirvANam eva syAt iti akalpanA iyam
# de'i-phyir #  'di ni yongs su mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur-ba # s rtog-pa #  'di ni mi rung ngo /
ekam ca kAraNam sva sattA aDyAsitam nirIham anityam Saktam ca izyate na viparyAsAt
# rgyu ni bdag-yod-pa #  dang ldan zhing g-yo-ba #  med la mi rtag cing nus-pa #  yod-pa #  gcig-pu # r 'dod kyi / / bzlog-pa #  ni ma yin no /
taTA hi uktaMBagavatA asmin sati idam Bavati asya utpAdAt idam utpadyate / yat uta avidyA pratyayAH saMskArAH iti / tasmAt na nitya ahetuH na api asat na sat vyApAraH na api aSaktA eti / AlayavijQAnaMhi sarva saMskRta Darma bIja anugatam A maraNAt santAna vRtti ca iti AlayavijQAnAt eva acittaka avasTAtaH vyuttizWataH pravRtti vijQAnam utpadyate iti
# de-skad #  du bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis kyang 'di yod-pa # 'i phyir 'di 'byung / / 'di skye-ba # 'i phyir 'di skye ste / / 'di-ltar #  ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'du-byed-rnams #  zhes gsungs te / / de-lta-bas-na #  rgyu rtag-pa #  ma yin zhing med-pa #  yang ma yin la / / byed-pa #  yod-pa #  yang ma yin zhing nus-pa-med-pa #  yang ma yin no / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni 'dus byas kyi chos-thams-cad #  kyi sa-bon-dang-ldan-pa #  ste / / shi-ba #  la thug gi bar-du #  rgyun-chags-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'o / / sems med-pa # 'i gnas las ldang-ba #  na kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid las 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung ste /
sUtre ca niroDa samApannasya vijQAnam kAyAt anapakrAntam iti uktam / na cAlaya vijQAnAt anyasya niroDa samApatti avasTAyAm vijQAnasya kAyAt anapakramaH yujyate / kim kAraNam
# mdo las kyang 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  lus-las #  mi 'da'o zhes gsungs so / / snyoms-par-zhugs-pa # 'i dus na rnam-par-shes-pa #  lus-las #  mi 'da' ba ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las gzhan mi rung ngo / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
niroDa samApannasya Alaya vijQAnAt yadi anya vijQAna samudAcAraH izyate tatas catrayANAm sannipAtaH sparSaH sparSa sahajAH vedanA saQjQA cetanA iti sUtre vacanAt saQjQA vedanayoH api samudAcAraH aByupagantavyaH
# gal-te #  'gog-pa #  la snyoms-par-zhugs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las gzhan zhig kun du 'byung-ba # r 'dod na / / de lta na ni gsum-'dus-pa # 'i rig-pa #  dang reg-pa #  dang lhan-cig-skyes-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang sems-pa #  zhes mdo las gsungs-pa # 'i phyir 'du-shes-dang-tshor-ba #  gnyis kyang kun du 'byung-ba # r khas blang dgos so /
tatas cavedanA saQjQA sadBAvAt saQjQA vedita niroDaH eva na syAt
# de'i-phyir #  'du-shes-dang-tshor-ba #  yod-pa # s 'du-shes-dang-tshor-ba #  'gog-pa #  nyid-du #  mi 'gyur ro /
yaH api manyate sUtra iva idam apratyayA tRzNA uktA na ca sarvA vedanA tRzNAyAH pratyayaH
# gang yang mdo las tshor-ba # 'i rkyen gyis sred-pa #  zhes gsungs-pa #  yang tshor-ba #  thams-cad #  sred-pa # 'i rkyen ma yin te /
evam sparSaH api na sarvaH saQjQA vedanA pratyayaH iti na ayam dozaH / na etat evam
# de-bzhin-du #  reg-pa #  thams-cad #  kyang 'du-shes-dang-tshor-ba # 'i rkyen ma-yin-pa # s nyes-pa #  med do snyam-du #  sems-pa #  de-yang #  de lta ma yin te /
viSezitA hi vedanA sUtra antare avidyA saMsparSa jam veditaMprati iti utpannA tRzNA iti / na tu evam kvacid sparSaH viSezitaH iti asamAnam etat
# mdo gzhan-las #  ma-rig-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i reg-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i tshor-ba #  la brten-nas #  sred-pa #  'byung zhes bye-brag #  tu mdzad kyi reg-pa #  ni gang-du #  yang de-ltar #  bye-brag #  mi mdzad-pa #  'di mtshungs-pa #  ma yin no /
tasmAt avaSyam AlayavijQAnAt eva sarva bIjakAt sarvAsu avasTAsu santAnena vartamAnAt niroDa asaQjQi samApattyA saQjQikeByaH vyutTAna cittam utpadyate iti aByupeyam
# de-lta-bas-na #  'gog-pa #  dang 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dang 'du-shes-med-pa #  pa rnams las ldang-ba #  na gdon-mi-za-bar #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # s sa-bon #  thams-cad #  gnas-skabs #  kun du 'byung-ba #  las skye-ba # r khas-blang-ba # r bya'o /
punar ca Alambana pratyaya apekzAm prakAra antara vRtti tAm upAdAya pravRtti vijQAnAt / AlayavijQAnam anyat iti pratipattavyam / upAdAya iti ante apadizwam iha api sambaDyate
# dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  la ltos nas rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  nyid kyi phyir 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  las kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzhan yod-pa # r khong-du-chud-pa # r bya'o / / phyir ro zhes tha-ma # r bstan-pa #  ni 'dir yang sbyar ro /
Alambana pratyayaH paQcAnAMcakzuH Adi vijQAnAnAm rUpa AdayaH paQca vizayAH manaH vijQAnasya sarva DarmAH
# dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  ni mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  lnga dang yul gzugs la-sogs-pa #  lnga'i yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  do /
rUpa Adi AkArAt Sabda Adi AkAraH prakAra antaram
# gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  las sgra la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  ni rnam-pa #  gzhan no /
evam Sabda Adi AkArAt rUpa Adi AkAraH / pIta Adi AkArAn nIla Adi AkAraH prakAra antaram
# de-bzhin-du #  sgra la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  las gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  dang ser-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  las sngon-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  ni rnam-pa #  gzhan no /
evam sarvatra vistareNa vAcyam
# de-ltar #  kun du yang rgya-cher #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
prakAra antareNa vRttiH Atma lABaH asya avijQAnasya iti tat vijQAnam prakAra antara vRtti / tad BAvaH prakAra antara vRtti tA
# rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  bdag thob-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  'di'i yin-pas #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  de ni rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  ste de yod-pa # s rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  nyid do /
Alambana pratyaya apekzA kAraNam yasyAH prakAra antara vRttitAyAH sa Alambana pratyaya apekzA tAdRSIMprakAra antara vRtti tAm upAdAya gRhItvA pravRtti vijQAnAt anyat Alaya vijQAnam pravRtti vijQAna bIja BUtam asti iti vijQAyate
# de dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  la ltos-pa'i-rgyu # s rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  gang-gi #  yin pad de dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  la ltos nas rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  nyid do / / nyid kyi phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni bzung nas 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  las kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzhan yod-pa # r shes so /
atrahi vijQAnam pratyavaBAsa BedAt parasparataH Bidyate na samanantara aDipati pratyaya BedAt / atas etat evam uktam Alambana pratyaya apekzAm prakAra antara vRtti tAm upAdAya
# 'dir ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams dmigs-pa #  so-so # r snang-ba #  tha-dad-pa # s phan tshun tha dad kyi de-ma-thag-pa #  dang bdag-po'i-rkyen #  tha-dad-pa # s ni ma yin no / / de'i-phyir #  'di-skad-du #  dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  la ltas nas rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bshad do /
sAca prakAra antara vRttitA yaTA na Alambana nirapekzA yujyate taTA hetu pratyaya nirapekzA api na eva yujyate yate
# rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  nyid de-yang #  ji-ltar #  dmigs-pa #  la mi ltos-pa # r mi-rung-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  rgyu'i-rkyen #  la mi ltos-pa # r mi-rung-ba #  nyid do /
yaH ca yezAm bIjEH anugataH sa tezAm hetu pratyayaH
# gang dag gi sa-bon #  rnams dang ldan-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni de-dag #  gi spyi'i rkyen te /
na ca pravRtti vijQAna anAMpara spara bIja tvam yujyate kuSala akuSala avyAkRta anAMhIna maDya praNIta DAtUnAm lOkika lokottarANi aMsa Asrava anAsravANAm vijQAnAnAm paryAyeNa BAvAt
# 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams ni gcig gi sa-bon #  du gcig mi rung ngo / / dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  rnams dang dman-pa #  dang 'bring dang gya-nom-pa # 'i khams pa rnams dang 'jig-rten-pa #  rnams dang 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  rnams dang zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams la rim-pa #  yod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de nyid kyi bag-chags #  bsgo-ba #  yang ma mthong la /
na hitena eva tasya vAsanA dRzwA na api anyena Binna kAlena asambadDena vA kim tarhi saha utpAda vinASEH eva puzpa AdiBiH tila AdInAm vAsanA dRzwA
# gzhan gyi dus-gzhan-na #  yang ma yin zhing 'brel-pa-med-pa # r yang ma yin no / / 'on-kyang #  lhan-cig-'byung-ba #  dang 'jig-pa #  nyid kyi me-tog #  la-sogs-pa # s 'bru-mar #  rnams la bsgo-ba # r mthong-ste #  /
atas vipAka vAsanA vijQAnena sama kAlam tatas eva utpadyamAnAni niruDyamAnAni ca pravRtti vijQAnAni sva anurUpa kArya utpAdana samarTaMvipAka vijQAnam kurvanti
# de'i-phyir #  rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i bag-chags #  kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang dus mtshungs-pa #  de-nyid-la # s 'byung-ba #  dang 'gag-pa #  ni 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams rang dang mthun-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  skyed nus ba rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la byed do /
tasya sAmarTyam vAsanA iti ucyate
# de'i nus-pa #  ni bag-chags #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tEH ca prakAra antara vRttiBiH pravRtti vijQAnEH vAsita Adi pAka vijQAnAt punar api Alambana apekzANi kuSala akuSala Adi prakAra antara vRttIni pravRtti vijQAnAni utpadyanta eti avaSyam aByupagantavyam / tatas ca vipAka vijQAna saMsarva saMskRta Darma bIja anugatam pravRtti vijQAneByaH anyat iti sidDam
# 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang dus rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  de-dag #  gis bsras [?] pa rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  las yang dmigs-pa #  la ltos-pa #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  'jug-pa #  'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams 'byung-ba # r gdon-mi-za-bar #  khas-blang-ba # r bya'o / / de'i-phyir #  'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams las rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'dus byas kyi chos-thams-cad #  kyi sa-bon-dang-ldan-pa #  gzhan yin par grub-pa # 'o /
Cinna punarvRtti tAm ca upAdAya Alaya vijQAnam pravRtti vijQAneByaH anyat asti iti pratipattavyam
# chad nas 'byung-ba # 'i phyir 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams las kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzhan yin par khong-du-chud-pa # r bya'o /
acittaka vidDa mUrCA Adi avasTAsu cCinnepravRtti vijQAna santAne punar acittakam idDa mUrCA apagata Alaya vijQAnam antareNa pravRtti vijQAna utpattiH na yujyate / niroDa samApatti Adi vyutTAna citta vat iha api vicAraH kartavyaH
# sems med-pa # 'i gnyid-kyis-log-pa #  dang brgyal-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rgyun-chad-pa #  las yang sems med-pa # 'i nyid kyis log-pa #  dang brgyal-ba #  las sangs pa na kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  med-pa # 'i 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba # r mi rung ngo / / 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  las ldang-ba # 'i sems dang 'dra-bar #  'dir yang dpyad-pa # r bya'o /
saMsAra pravRtti nivRttitAn= ca upAdAya / pravRtti vijQAnAt anyat AlayavijQAnam yat nimitta asaMsAra pravRttiH nivRttiH ca gamyate
# 'khor-ba # r 'jug-pa-dang-ldog-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang-gi #  rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i 'khor-ba # r 'jug-pa-dang-ldog-pa #  yod-pa # s 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  las kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzhan yin par shes so /
kzaNa avasTA nikAya BAganEH antar yapra banDena upAdAna skanDa utpAdaH saMsAraH iti ucyate
# skad-cig #  kyang mi-gnas-pa # r ris-mthun-pa #  rgyun mi 'chad ba'i rgyun gyi nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  'byung-ba #  ni 'khor-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tasya punar pravRttiH nikAya saBA antarezu pratisanDiH
# de'i 'jug-pa #  ni ris-mthun-pa #  gzhan dag tu nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'o /
nivRttiH sa upaDi Seza yoniH upaDi SezaH ca nirvANa DAtuH
# ldog-pa #  ni phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i dbyings so /
tatra Alay avij QAnAH naB yupa gamesaMskAra pratyaya vijQAna aBAvAt saMsAra pravRttiH na yujyate
# de-la #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  khas mi len na 'du-byed #  kyi rgyu rkyen gyis rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir 'khor-ba # r 'jug bar mi rung ngo / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  khas mi len na /
AlayavijQAna anaByupagame hi pratisanDi vijQAnam vAsaMskAra pratyayam parikalpyeta saMskAra pariBAvitAH vA zaXni vijQAna kAyAH saMskAra pratyayam vijQAnam
# 'du-byed #  kyi rkyen gyis rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes 'byung-ba #  nyid mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'am / / 'du-byed #  kyis yongs-su-bsgos-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug 'du-byed #  kyi rkyen las byung-ba # r brtag grang na /
tatra na pratisanDi vijQAnam pUrva janma upacita saMskAra pratyayam pUrva janma upacita saMskArANAm acira nirudDa tvAt nirudDasya ca asattvAt asataH ca pratyaya aBAvAt
# de'i tshe nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni tshe snga-ma #  la bsags-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  kyi rkyen las byung-ba #  ma yin te / / tshe snga-ma #  la bsags-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  ni 'gags nas ring du lon pa'i phyir ro / / 'gags-pa #  ni med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yadi nirudDasya pratyaya tvam na izyate evam ca sati aPalam eva karma syAt na hi vartamAnAt karmaNaH vipAkaH nirvartate / na etat evam tad ja BAvanA avasTAnAt / karma ahitAyAH citta santAne vAsanAya apari pAka viSezam gatAyAH vipAkaH nirvartate
# med-pa #  ni rkyen du mi-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gal-te #  'gags-pa #  rkyen du mi 'dod na de-ltar-na #  / / da-ltar-gyi-las #  las ni rnam-par-smin-pa #  mngon-par-mi-'grub-pa #  las-kyi-'bras-bu #  med-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur ro / / de ni de lta ma yin te / / de-la # s byung-ba # 'i bsgos-pa #  gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gang-la # s 'gyur-ba #  bye-brag #  tu gyur nas rnam-par-smin-pa #  'grub-pa # 'i bag-chags #  las kyis bskyed-pa #  sems-kyi-rgyud #  la yod do /
tasmAt na viPalaMkarma na ca nirudDAt karmaNaH vipAkaH iti / pratisanDO cana Ama rUpam eva na kevalam vijQAnam
# de-lta-bas-na #  las-kyi-'bras-bu #  med-pa #  ma yin la / / las 'gags-pa #  las rnam-par-smin-pa #  'byung-ba #  yang ma yin no / / nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba'i-tshe #  ni ming-dang-gzugs #  kyi yin te /
tatra vijQAnam eva saMskAra pratyayam na ca nAma rUpam iti kAtra yuktiH
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  'ba'-zhig #  ni ma yin na / / de-la #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid 'du-byed #  kyi rkyen gyis byung gi / / ming-dang-gzugs #  ni ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  'di-la #  rigs-pa #  ci yod /
tasmAt saMskAra pratyayam nAma rUpam iti vaktayam na tu vijQAnam iti / katamat vA anyat vijQAna pratyayam nAma rUpam
# de-lta-bas-na #  'du-byed #  kyi rkyen gyis ming-dang-gzugs #  zhes brjod-pa # r bya'i / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  ma yin no zhes brjod-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rkyen gyis ming-dang-gzugs #  zhes-bya-ba #  gzhan gang zhe na /
yad pratisanDi kzaNAt uttara kAlam / tasya prAtisanDikAt nAma rUpAt kaH Atma atiSayaH yatas tat eva vijQAna pratyayam na pUrvam ca saMskAra pratyayam na uttaram iti atas ca saMskAra pratyayam nAma rUpam eva astu / kiMpratisanDi vijQAnena aFga antareNa parikalpitena / tasmAt na pratisanDi vijQAnam saMskAra pratyayam yujyate / gsaMskArAH tu avidyA pratyayAH / tad aDivAsitam ca vijQAna MsaMskAra pratyayam / tad pratyayam pratisanDO ca nAma rUpam eva iti ezA eva nItiH niravadyA
# nyid mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i skad-cig #  las dus phyi-ma #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhe na / / de nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i ming-dang-gzugs #  las rang-bzhin #  bye-brag #  tu gyur-pa #  ci yod-na #  / / 'di-ltar #  de nyid rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rkyen gyis byung-ba #  yin la / / snga-ma #  ni 'du-byed #  kyi rkyen gyis byung-ba #  yin la / / phyi-ma #  ni ma yin te de'i-phyir #  'du-byed #  kyi rkyen gyis ming-dang-gzugs #  nyid-du #  'gyur gyi / / nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i rnam-pa # r shes ba'i yan-lag #  gzhan kun du brtags-pa # s ci-zhig #  bya / / de-lta-bas-na #  nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni 'du-byed #  kyi rkyen gyis byung-ba # r mi rung ngo / / 'du-byed-rnams #  ni ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis byung-ba #  yin la des bsgos-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni 'du-byed #  kyi rkyen gyis byung-ba #  dang de'i rkyen gyis byung-ba #  nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba #  ni ming-dang-gzugs #  nyid do zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshul 'di-la #  ni nyes-pa #  med do /
zaXu vijQAna kAya aHsaMskAra pariBAvitAH saMskAra pratyayam vijQAnam iti ayam api pakzaH durGawitaH eva / kim kAraNam
# rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug-po #  'du-byed #  kyis yongs-su-bsgos-pa #  dag 'du-byed #  kyi rkyen gyis rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i phyogs 'di yang sbyar ma legs-pa #  nyid de / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
na hi vijQAnaMvipAka vAsanAm nizyanda vAsanAm vA Atmani ADAtuMsam arTam Atmani kAritra viroDAt
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i bag-chags #  dang rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i bag-chags #  bdag la skyed-pa # r mi nus te / / bdag la byed-pa #  'gal-ba # 'i phyir ro /
na api anantare tasya tadA anutpanna tvAt anutpannasya ca asattvAt / na api utpannepUrvasya tadA nirudDa tvAt
# de ma theg-pa #  la yang ma yin te / / de ni de'i tshe ma-byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / ma-byung-ba #  ni med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / byung-ba #  la yang ma yin te / / de ni de'i tshe sngar 'gags-pa # 'i phyir ro /
acittakAsu ca midDa Adi avasTAsu punar saMskAra pariBAvita citta utpatti asamBavAt vijQAna pratyayam nAma rUpam na syAt
# sems med-pa # 'i gnyid-kyis-log-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dus na ni 'du-byed #  kyis yongs-su-bsgos-pa # 'i sems 'byung mi srid-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i rkyen gyis ming-dang-gzugs #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
tad aBAvAt zaXa AyatanaMna syAt
# de med-pa # r skye-mched-drug #  kyang med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
evam yAvat jarA maraNam na syAt / tatas casaMsAra pravRttiH eva viruDyate
# de-bzhin-du #  rga shi'i bar-du #  yang med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
saMsAra nivRttiH api Alaya vijQAne asatinA upapadyate
# de'i-phyir #  'khor-ba # r 'jug-pa #  nyid dang 'gal lo / / 'khor-ba #  las ldog-pa #  yang kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  med na mi 'thad de /
saMsArasya hi karma kleSAH kAraNam
# 'khor-ba # 'i rgyu ni las dang nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams so /
tayoH kleSAH praDAnam
# de gnyis las kyang nyon-mongs-pa #  ni gtso bo ste /
taTA hi kleSa ADipatyAt karma punar Bava Akzepa samarTam BavatinA anyaTA
# 'di-ltar #  nyon-mongs-pa # 'i dbang gis na las kyis yang-srid-pa #  'phen nus-pa # r 'gyur gyi gzhan-du #  ni ma yin no /
atas eva na dRzwa satyAnAm karmANi punarBavam Akzipanti darSana prahAta vyakleSa aBAvAt
# de'i-phyir #  bden-pa-mthong-ba #  rnams kyi las las yang-srid-pa #  mi 'phen te / / mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Akzipta punarBavam api karma kleSa aBAvAt na punarBavIBavati iti
# de-bzhin-du #  yang-srid-pa #  'phangs-pa # 'i las kyang nyon-mongs-pa #  med na yang-srid-pa #  'byung-ba # r mi 'gyur te /
taTA hita eDAtuka vIta rAgANAm Akzipta punarBavam api karma kleSa aBAvAt BavIBavitum na utsahate
# 'di-ltar #  khams-gsum #  gyi 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  rnams kyi yang-srid-pa #  'phangs-pa # 'i las kyang nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  srid-pa #  'byung-ba # r byed mi nus so /
atas ca tezAm punarBavaH nABi nirvartate
# de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  gi yang-srid-pa #  mngon-pa # r mi 'grub bo /
evam ca praDAna tvAt kleSAH eva saMsAra pravRtteH mUlam
# de-ltar-na #  gtso bo yin pa'i phyir nyon-mongs-pa #  nyid 'khor-ba # r 'jug-pa # 'i rtsa ba ste /
atas tezu prahINezu saMsAraH nivartatena anyaTA
# de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  spangs na 'khor-ba #  las ldog-pa # r 'gyur gyi gzhan-du #  ni ma yin no /
na cAlaya vijQAnam antareNa tad prahANam yujyate
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  med-pa # r de-dag #  spang du mi rung ste /
sammuKIBUtaH vA kleSaH prahIyeta bIja avasTaH vA
# nyon-mongs-pa #  mngon-du-gyur-pa # 'am / / sa-bon #  gyi tshe spang grang na /
tatrasammuKIBUtaH prahIyate iti anizwiH eva iyam tadA tad prahANa mArga aBAvAt
# de-la #  mngon-du-gyur-pa #  spang ngo zhe na ni / / de mi-'dod-pa #  nyid de / / de'i tshe de-dag #  spong-ba # 'i lam med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
bIja avasTaH api na eva prahIyate na hi pratipakzAt tadAnIm kiQcid anyat aByupagamyate yatra kleSa bIjam vyavasTitaMtatprati pakzeNa prahIyeta / aTa pratipakza cittam eva kleSa bIja anuzaktam izyate na hi kleSa bIja anuzaktam eva tad pratipakzaH yujyate
