# sa-bon #  gyi tshe yang spang du mi rung ste / / gang-la #  nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  gnas-pa #  de gnyen-po # s spong na / / de'i tshe ni gnyen-po #  las ci-yang #  khas ma blangs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / ji ste gnyen-po'i-sems #  nyid nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  dang 'dres na ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  dang 'dres-pa #  nyid pas gnyen-po # r mi rung ste /
naca aprahINa kleSa bIjAnAm saMsAra vinivRttiH samBavati iti tasmAt avaSyam AlayavijQAnam tad anya vijQAna sahaBUtEH kleSa upakleSEH BAvya teja bIja puzwi ADAnataH iti upeyam
# nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  ma-spangs-pa #  rnams ni 'khor-ba #  las ldog mi srid do / / de-lta-bas-na #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang lhan-cig-'byung-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams kyis rang-gi-sa-bon #  gso-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir bag-chags #  bsgo-ba # r khas blangs so /
punar ca tatas eva santati pariNAma viSezAt yaTAbalaMBAvanA vRtti lABe sati kleSa upakleSAH pravartante
# rgyun 'gyur-ba # 'i bye-brag #  gi stobs ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  bsgos-pa #  'jug-pa #  rnyed nas / / yang de-nyid-la # s nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams 'byung ste /
tezAm AcAlaya vijQAna vyavasTitam bIjaMtat sahaBuvA kleSa pratipakza mArgeNa apanIyate
# de-dag #  gi sa-bon #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gnas-pa #  ni de dang lhan-cig-'byung-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  lam gyis sel to /
tasmin= ca apanIte punar tena ASrayeNa kleSAnAm anutpattiH iti sa upaDi SezaH nirvANa DAtuH prApyate
# de bsal-nas #  gnas de nas nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams mi-'byung-ba # s phung-po #  lhag-ma #  dang bcas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i dbyings thob bo /
pUrva karma Akzipta janma niroDe ca tatas anya janma asaMsanDAnAt nirupaDi SezaH nirvANa DAtuH
# sngon-gyi-las #  kyis 'phangs-pa # 'i skye-ba #  ni 'gags la / / de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i skye-ba #  dang nying mtshams mi sbyor-ba #  ni lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i dbyings te /
na hikarma vidyamAnam api kleSezu prahINezu sahakAri kAraNa aBAvAt punarBavam aBinirvartayituMsam arTam
# las yod-du-zin-kyang #  nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams spangs na lhan-cig-byed-pa'i-rgyu #  med-pa # 'i phyir / / yang-srid-pa #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # r byed mi nus so /
atas eva Alaya vijQAne sati saMsAra pravRttiH nivRttiH cana anyaTA iti avaSyam AlayavijQAnam aByupagantavyam
# de-ltar-na #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  yod-na #  'khor-ba # r 'jug-pa-dang-ldog-pa # r rung gi gzhan-du #  ni ma yin te / / gdon-mi-za-bar #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  khas-blang-ba # r bya'o /
kim kAraNaMtat AlayavijQAnam iti ucyate
# ci'i-phyir #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes bya zhe na /
AlayavijQAna tvam punar tasya sarva bIja AlayatAm
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  'di ni sa-bon #  thams-cad-kyi #  gzhi nyid do /
upAdAya iti ante apadizwa Msarvatra aBisambaDyate / AlayavijQAna BAvaH AlayavijQAna tvam / tat punar AlayavijQAna Sabda pravRtti nimittam
# phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  tha-ma # r gang bstan-pa #  de ni thams-cad-du #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i dngos-po #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid do / / de ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'jug-pa'i-rgyu # 'o /
tatra vijQAna atIti vijQAnam
# de-la #  rnam-par-shes-pa # r byed-pa # s rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste /
tad vyatirikta vijQAta BAva pradarSana arTaMBAva mAtre kartR vyapadeSaH
# de-la # s ma-gtogs-par #  shes-par-byed-pa #  po med-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir dngos-po #  tsam la byed-pa # r bstan to /
sarva bIja AlayatA sarva sAFkleSika Darma bIja sTAna tA / Alayam sTAnam iti paryAyaH
# sa-bon #  thams-cad-kyi #  gzhi nyid ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i chos kyi sa-bon #  thams-cad-kyi #  gnas nyid do; / / gzhi ni gnas kyi rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa # 'o /
aTavA AlIyantaH upanibaDyante asmin sarva Darma HkArya BAvena tat vAlIyate upanibaDyate kAraNa BAvena sarva Darmezu iti AlayaH / Atma BAva Alaya nimitta tAm ca upAdAya / Atma BAvaH / nAma rUpam / AlIyate asmin= Atma BAvaH tad balena anuvRttitaH iti AlayaH
# yang-na #  'dir chos-thams-cad #  'bras-bu'i-dngos-po # r sbyor zhing nye-bar #  'brel-ba # 'am / / de chos-thams-cad #  la rgyu'i-dngos-po # r sbyor zhing nye-bar #  'brel-ba # s kun-gzhi # 'o / / lus kyi kun-gzhi #  nyid dang rgyu nyid kyi phyir zhes-bya-ba #  la lus ni ming-dang-gzugs #  so / / der lus sbyor te / / de'i stobs kyis 'byung-ba # s kun-gzhi #  nyid do /
tad BAvaH AlayatA / Atma BAva nimittam tad bIja paripozAt pratisanDO= Atma BAva nirvartanAt
# de'i dngos-po #  ni kun-gzhi #  nyid do / / lus kyi rgyu ni de'i sa-bon #  yongs su gsos pas nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba #  ni lus-mngon-par-'grub-pa # 'i phyir te /
Atma BAva AlayatAm Atma BAva nimitta tAm ca upAdAya Alaya vijQAna tvam aByupagantavyam / anye punar anyaTA paWanti Atma mAna Alaya nimitta tAm ca upAdAya iti
# lus kyi gzhi nyid dang lus kyi rgyu nyid yin-pas #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid khas-blang-ba # r bya'o gzhan nas de-bzhin-du #  'byung ste / / bdag tu nga-rgyal #  gyi gzhi dang rgyu nyid kyi phyir ro zhes 'byung ngo /
AlayavijQAnam Atma tvena AlambamAnasya yaH mAnaHsaH Atma mAna
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la bdag tu dmigs-pa # 'i nga-rgyal #  gang-yin-pa #  de bdag tu nga-rgyal #  lo /
AlIyata etasmin vizayi BAvena Atma mAnaH iti Alaya vijQAnam Atma nAlayaH
# bdag tu nga-rgyal #  ni 'di-la #  yul can gyi dngos-po # r sbyor-ba # s kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni bdag tu nga-rgyal #  gyi kun-gzhi # 'o /
AlIyate vA tad nimitta BAvena Atma mAnaH iti AlayA ucyate / Sezam pUrvavat / kAya AlIna tAm ca upAdAya iti / caSabdaH samuccaya arTaH
# yang-na #  de-dag #  tu nga-rgyal #  la rgyu'i-dngos-po # r sbyor-ba # s kun-gzhi #  zhes-bya'o #  / / lhag-ma #  ni snga-ma-bzhin #  no / / lus-la-gnas #  pa nyid kyi yang phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la yang zhes-bya-ba #  ni bsdu-ba # 'i don to /
kAyaH atra sa indriyam SarIram / samantam hi SarIraMvyApya Alaya vijQAnam vartate
# lus ni 'dir dbang-po-dang-bcas-pa # 'i khog-pa # 'o / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni khog-pa #  thams-cad-la #  khyab-pa # 'o /
atas kAya pratibadDa vRtti tvAt tad kAye AlInam iti kAya AlInam / tad BAvaH kAya AlIna tA
# de'i-phyir #  lus dang 'brel-ba # r 'jug-pa # s lus-la-gnas #  pa'i phyir lus-la-gnas #  pa'o / / de'i dngos-po #  ni lus-la-gnas #  pa nyid de /
tAMkAya AlInatAm upAdAya gRhItvA Alaya vijQAna tvam asi apratipattavyam
# lus-la-gnas #  pa nyid kyi phyir bzung nas 'di kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid-du #  khong-du-chud-pa # r bya'o /
na kevalam AlayavijQAnam etat ucyate kim tarhi AdAna vijQAnam api iti / kim kAraNam tat AdAna vijQAnam / iti ucyate / atas kAraNam Aha kAya upAdAna tAm upAdAya iti / AdIyate kAyaH anena iti AdAna vijQAnam iti ucyate
# de ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'ba'-zhig-tu #  ma zad kyi / / len-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  yang de yin te / / ci'i-phyir #  de len-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes bya zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  lus len-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes rgyu smos so / / 'dis lus len bas len-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes bya ste /
cittena kAyasya upAdAnam na anyena iti prasidDam
# sems-kyis #  lus len gyi bdag-gis #  ni ma yin no zhes-bya-ba # r rab tu grub bo /
tat ca yat pUrva saMskAra hetu kaMSukra SoNita sammUrCita avasTAyAm Bavam upAdatte
# de-yang #  sngon gyi 'du-byed #  kyi rgyu las 'byung-ba #  ste / / khu-ba-dang-khrag #  gi nang-du #  brgyal-ba # 'i dus na srid-pa #  len te /
tat eva amaraNAt kAya upAdAtR tvena izyate
# de nyid shi-ba #  la thug gi bar lus-len-par-byed-pa # r 'dod kyi /
na cakzuH Adi vijQAna anitat pRzWa labDam vA manaH vijQAnam tezAm tatas UrDvaMvartamAna cakzuH Adi pratyaya nimitta tvAt
# mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams dang de'i-rjes-la # s byung-ba #  yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # s ni ma yin te / / de-dag #  ni de'i-'og-tu #  mig la-sogs-pa #  rkyen rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
na ca tatra anyat manaH vijQAnam saMskAra hetukam tasya kuSala akuSala tvAt
# de-la #  yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzhan 'du-byed #  kyi rgyu-las-byung-ba #  ni ma yin te / / de-dag #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i phyir ro /
saMskAra hetukam hi ekAntena avyAkRtam vipAka tvAt
# 'du-byed #  kyi rgyu-las-byung-ba #  ni rnam-par-smin-pa #  yin pa'i phyir gcig-tu #  lung ma bstan-pa # 'o /
vipAkaH ca na vicCinnaH sanDIyate cakzuH Adi vat
# rnam-par-smin-pa #  la yang mig la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  rgyun chad nas yang nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba #  ma yin no /
na cAlaya vijQAna anyat ekAntena avyAkRta jAtIyam upalaByata iyat vipAka vijQAna tvena parikalpyeta
# gang rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid kun du rtag-pa #  gcig-tu #  lung ma bstan-pa # 'i rang-bzhin-can #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las gzhan ma mthong ngo /
api capratiniyata ASraya pravRtta tvAt zaNNAm vijQAna kAyAnAm vicCeda pravRtta tvAt ca na sarvasya ASrayasya upAdAna saMprasa jyate
# yang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug-po #  dag ni gnas so-sor-nges-pa #  las 'byung-ba #  dang rgyun chad nas 'byung-ba # 'i phyir gnas-thams-cad #  len-pa # r mi rung ste /
taTA hiyena yena ASrayeNa yat vijQAnam pravartatesaH eva tena upAttaH syAt avaSizwasya anupAtta tvaMvijQAna virahita tvAt
# 'di-ltar #  gnas gang-dang-gang-las #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gang 'byung-ba #  des de nyid zin-pa # r 'gyur gyi / / lhag-ma #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyir zin-pa #  ma yin no /
taTA cakzuH Adi vijQAnam vicCedena punar punar pravartate iti tad ASrayasya punar punar upAdAna doza prasaFgaH
# de-ltar #  mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rgyun chad nas yang-dang-yang #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir gnas de-yang #  dang yang nye-bar-len-pa # 'i skyon du 'gyur ro /
tasmAt AlayavijQAnam eva pratisanDO kAyam upAdatte A maraNAt ca samasta kAya ASrayeNa pravartate iti tat eva rpratisanDibanDAt praBRti A maraNAt kAyam upAdAttaH iti AdAna vijQAnam iti ucyate / prADAnyena manaH AlayavijQAna Alambanam / iti / klizwam hi manaH AlayavijQAnam Atma tvena nityam Alambata AtmA AlambanEH moha dRzwimAn asnehEH samprayukta tvAt / tat caniti akAlaMmanyana Atmaka tvAt manaH / prADAnyena tat eva manaH ucyate
# de lta-ba # s kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyid nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i dus nas lus bzung nas shi-ba #  la thug gi bar-du #  lus-mtha'-dag #  la brten-te #  'byung-ba # s de nyid nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba #  nas shi-ba #  la thug gi bar-du #  lus 'dzin-pa # s na len-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / dngos su na yid kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la dmigs zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la rtag-par #  bdag tu dmigs te / / bdag tu rmongs-pa #  dang lta-ba #  dang nga-rgyal #  dang chags-pa # r dmigs-pa #  rnams dang mtshungs bar ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-yang #  rtag-par #  rlom sems-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  yin-pas #  yod do / / dngos su na de yid ces bya'o /
yat zaNNAm cakzuH Adi vijQAna kAyAnAm samanantara nirudDam vijQAnam manaH iti uktam tat zazWasya manaH vijQAnasya ASraya prasidDi arTam na tumanya nAkAra tvAt / atas na tasya prADAnyena manaH tvam
# mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug-po #  dag 'gags-ma-thag-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la yid ces brjod-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni drug-pa #  yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i gnas sgrub-pa # 'i phyir yin gyi ngar sems-pa # 'i rna-ba # 'i phyir ni ma yin no / / de'i-phyir #  dngos su na de ni yid nyid ma yin no /
tat caturBiH kleSEH nityam samprayuktam / vA Atma moha Atma dRzwyA Atma nAnA Atma snehEH
# de-yang #  bdag tu rmongs-pa #  dang bdag-tu-lta-ba #  dang bdag tu nga-rgyal #  dang bdag-la-chags-pa #  ste / / nyon-mongs-pa #  bzhi dang rtag-par #  mtshungs-pa # r ldan te /
atra tu Atma grahaNam na moha mAtreNa samprayujyate kiMtarhi Atmani yaH mohaH / evam yAvat Atma snehe vaktavyam
# de-la #  bdag tu rmongs-pa #  ni gti-mug #  tsam dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma yin gyi / / bdag tu rmongs-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o / / de-bzhin-du #  bdag-la-chags-pa # 'i bar dag la yang brjod-pa # r bya'o /
Adi grahaNAt paQcaBiH sarva tragEH casparSa manaskAra AdiBiH sadA samprayuktam
# sogs-pa #  ni reg-pa #  dang yid-la-byed-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  kun du 'gro-ba-lnga-po #  dag dang yang rab tu mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'o /
tasya apratIta tvAt ca etAnAm api ca etEH samprayogAt catatsu rUpa nirDAraNa arTam Aha vijQAnam iti
# de-yang #  ma grags-pa #  dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # s na de'i rang-gi #  ngo bo dmigs kyis dbye-ba # 'i phyir / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
eka jAtIyam iti klizwa jAtIyam na kuSalam avyAkRtam vA anityam Atma moha AdiBiH caturBiH kleSEH samprayukta tvAt
# rigs gcig pa zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi rigs yin gyi / / dge-ba # 'am / / lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  ni ma yin te / / bdag tu rmongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa #  bzhi dang rtag-tu #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
santAna anuvRtti ca iti avicCedena vartate iti arTaH
# rgyun-chags-pa # r 'jug-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  rjes su 'byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
asya utsargasya apavAdam AraBateH arhat tu Arya mArga niroDa samApatti avasTAm sTApayitvA / arhat tva avasTAyAm na pravartate arhataH / niraH vaSe zatr ED Atuk akli zwad harm apra hINa tvAt
# spyir btang-ba #  'di'i dmigs kyis bsal-ba #  rtsom ste / / dgra-bcom-pa #  dang 'phags-pa'i-lam #  dang 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i dus ma gtogs so / / dgra-bcom-pa #  ni khams-gsum-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi chos spangs-pa # 'i phyir dgra-bcom-pa # 'i dus ni mi 'byung ngo /
Arya mArga avasTAyAm api na pravartate paramArTa jQAnasya Atma dRzwi samudAcAreNa atyanta viroDAt
# 'phags-pa'i-lam #  gyi dus na yang mi 'byung ste / / de na dam-pa #  shes-pa #  ni bdag-tu-lta-ba #  kun du 'byung-ba #  dang shin-tu #  mi-mthun-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatas UrDvam asya Alaya vijQAnAt pravRttiH SEkzasya aprahINa tvAt / niroDa samApatti avasTAyAm api na pravartate
# de'i-'og-tu #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las 'byung ste / / slob-pa # 'i dus na ma-spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i dus na yang mi 'byung ste /
asaQjQi samApattitaH niroDa samApatteH SAntatara tvam tad asamcAra tvAt eva veditavyam
# 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  bas [?] 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-zhugs-pa #  ches zhe ba'i phyir / / de kun du mi-'byung-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
atra ca manaH nirvacana tAlambanataH samprayogataH pravRtti kAlatas ca nirdizwaMveditavyam / kena arTena rUpa Adi skanDAH iti ucyante
# 'dir ni nges-pa'i-tshig #  dang dmigs-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang 'byung pa'i dus kyi yid bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / ci'i-phyir #  phung-po #  zhes bya zhe na /
rASi arTena / rASiH skanDaH iti paryAyaH / etat uktam Bavati rUpa rASI rUpa skanDaH
# spungs pa'i phyir te zhes-bya-ba #  la spungs pa ni phung-po #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i grangs-su-gtogs-pa # 'o / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  gzugs spungs pa ni gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  ste /
evam yAvat vijQAna rASiH vijQAna skanDaH iti / yasmAt sUtre aDva santAna prakAra gati deSa Beda BinnAn / Am rUpa AdInAm saFkzepa saFgraha tAm upAdAya rUpa AdayaH skanDAH uktAH / iti zyat kiQcid rUpam aatIta anAgata pratyutpannam ADyAtmikam vA bAhyam vA Odarikam vA sUkzmam vA hInam vA praNItam vA yat vA dUre yat vA antikesarvam EkaDyam aBisaFkzipya rUpa skanDa Eti saFKyAm gacCati iti evam yAvat vijQAnam
# de-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du #  sbungs pa la rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i phung-po #  zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / 'di-ltar #  mdo las dus dang rgyu dang rnam-pa #  dang 'gro-ba #  dang yul tha-dad-pa # 'i gzugs la-sogs-pa #  mdor-bsdus-pa # 'i phyir / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  phung-po # r bstan te / / gzugs gang-yin-pa #  ci-yang #  rung 'das-pa # 'am ma-'ongs-pa # 'am da-ltar #  byung pa'am / / nang gi'am phyi'i'am / / rags-pa # 'am / / phra-ba # 'am / / ngan-pa # 'am / / gya-nom-pa # 'am / / thag-nye-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'am / / rgyang ring-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  thams-cad #  gcig-tu-bsdus-na # s gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i grangs su 'gro'o / / de-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o zhes 'byung ste /
atIta anAgata pratyutpannAH iti aDva Bedena BinnAH
# 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  dang da-ltar-byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bye-brag #  gis dus-tha-dad-pa # 'o /
ADyAtmikAH vA bAhyAH vA iti santAna Bedena yasmAt ADyAtmikAH sva asAntAnikAH bAhyAH tatas anye
# nang ngam phyi zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu tha-dad-pa # s so / / 'di-ltar #  nang gi rnams ni rang-gi-rgyud #  du gtogs-pa #  dag go / / phyi'i rnams ni de-las-gzhan-pa #  dag go /
OdArikA vA asUkzmA vA iti prakAra Bedena
# rags-pa # 'am / / phra-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis so /
tatra rUpasya apekzikam OdArika sUkzma tvam
# de-la #  gzugs kyi rags-pa #  dang phra-ba #  nyid ni ltos ba can no /
sa pratiGam OdArikam apratiGaMsu Uzmam
# yang-na #  thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  ni rags-pa # 'o / / thogs-pa-med-pa #  ni phra-ba # 'o /
vedanA saQjQA saMskAra vijQAnAni tupaQca indriya ASraya utpannAni OdArikANi mAnasAni sUkzmANi
# tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams kyang dbang-po-lnga #  la brten-te #  / / byung-ba #  dag ni rags-pa # 'o / / yid la brten-te #  byung-ba #  dag ni phra-ba # 'o; /
hInA vA praNItA vA iti gati Bedena BinnAH
# ngan-pa # 'am gya-nom-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'gro-ba # 'i bye-brag #  gis tha-dad-pa #  rnams te /
taTA hi hIna gati saFgRhItAH hInAH praNIta gati saFgRhItAH praNItAH
# 'di-ltar #  'gro-ba #  ngan-pa # s zin-pa #  dag ni ngan-pa #  rnams so / / 'gro-ba #  gya-nom-pa # s zin-pa #  dag ni gya-nom-pa #  rnams so /
yat vA adUre yat vAntikaH iti deSa Bedena BinnAH
# thag-nye-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'am / / rgyang-ring-po #  gang-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni yul gyi bye-brag #  gis tha-dad-pa #  rnams so /
vedanA AdInAm tudUra antika tvam ASraya vaSena
# tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni gnas kyi dbang gis nye-ba #  dang ring-ba # 'o /
rUpa AdInAm iti rUpa vedanA saQjQA saMskAra vijQAnAnAm
# gzugs la-sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams so /
saFkzepa saFgraha tAm upAdAya iti aDva sant Anap rakAH raga tide SaB edab hin= AnAMrUpa vedanA saQjQA saMskAra vijQAnAnAm pratyekam saFkzepeNa saFgrahaH saFkzepa saFgrahaH / tad BAvaH saFkzepa saFgraha tA
# mdor-bsdus-pa #  nyid kyi phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni dus dang rgyu dang rnam-pa #  dang 'gro-ba #  dang yul tha-dad-pa #  rnams kyi gzugs dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams so-so # r mdor-bsdus-pa #  ni mdor-bsdus-pa # 'o / / de'i dngos-po #  ni mdor-bsdus-pa #  nyid do /
tAm saFkzepa saFgraha tAm upAdAya sUtre rASi arTaH skanDa arTaH vijQAyate
# de-dag #  mdor-bsdus-pa # 'i phyir mdo las sbungs pa'i don zhes 'byung-ba #  ni phung-po # 'i don ni zhes-bya-ba # r shes te /
taTA hi uktam / tat sarvam atIta Adi karma rUpam ekaDyam aBisaFkzipya rUpa skanDaH iti saFKyAm gacCati iti / evam yAvat vijQAnam / uktAH paQca skanDAH skanDa arTaH ca
# 'di-ltar #  'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gzugs de-dag #  thams-cad #  ni gcig-tu-bsdus-na # s gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i grangs-su-'gro-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  nas / / de-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  bstan to / / phung-po #  lnga po rnams dang phung-po # 'i don bshad-zin #  to / / phung-po #  lnga'i rab tu byed-pa #  bye-brag #  tu bshad-pa #  / / bam po bzhi-pa #  ste tha-ma # 'o /
sarva saMskArAH paQca skanDa saFgraheNa uktAH sarva DarmAH saMskRtAH asaMskRtAH ca Ayatana DAtu saFgraheNa / tatra skanDa nirdeSa anantaram AyatanAni vaktavyAni / kaH ca Ayatana arTaH iti atas Aha dvAdaSAyatanAni iti / tAni punar
# 'dus byas thams-cad #  ni phung-po #  lngas bsdus la / / 'dus byas dang; 'dus-ma-byas #  kyi chos-thams-cad #  ni skye-mched #  dang khams su bsdus-pa # r bstan-pa #  de-la #  phung-po #  bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  skye-mched #  rnams brjod dgos-pa # s du zhig gang-dang-gang #  skye-mched #  kyi don ni ci zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / skye-mched #  bcu gnyis zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
katamAni / cakzuH Ayatanam rUpa Ayatanam yAvat mana Ayatanam Darma Ayatanam ca eti / cakzuH AdInAm pUrvavat nirdeSaH iti
# de-dag #  kyang gang zhe na; mig-gi-skye-mched #  dang gzugs kyi skye-mched #  dang zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  nas / / yid kyi skye-mched #  dang chos-kyi-skye-mched #  do zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o /
rUpa skanDa viBAge yaTA cakzuH AdayaH svarUpataH nirdizwAH taTA iha api svarUpatonirdezwavyAH iti
# mig la-sogs-pa #  ni snga-ma-bzhin-du #  bshad do zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  rnam-par-phye-ba #  ni ji-ltar #  mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo bstan-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  'dir yang rang-gi #  ngo bo bstan-pa # r bya'o /
tatra hi uktam catvAri mahABUtAni upAdAya varNa vizayaH rUpa prasAdaH cakzuH indriyam iti
# de-la #  mig-gi-dbang-po #  ni 'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  rgyur-byas-pa #  ste / / yul kha-dog #  gzugs-dang-ba # 'o zhes bstan to /
evam Sabda ganDa rasa sprazwavya vizayAyaTa Akramam rUpa AtmakAH prasAdAH Srotra AdayaH
# de-bzhin-du #  sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg-bya #  yang yul te; go-rims #  bzhin no / / rna-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  yang gzugs kyi bdag-nyid #  dang-ba # 'o /
rUpa Sabda ganDa rasa AyatanAnAm ca pUrvavan / nirdeSaH iti sambaDyate
# gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro'i skye-mched #  rnams kyang snga-ma-bzhin-du #  bshad do zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
pUrvam hi nirdizwaH cakzuzaH vizayaH varNaH saMsTAnam vijQaptiH ca rUpam
# sngar ni mig gi yul ni / / kha-dog #  dang dbyibs dang rnam-par-rig-byed #  kyi gzugs so /
upAtta anupAtta uBaya mahABUta hetukaH Srotrasya vizayaH Sabda ityAdi
# rna-ba # 'i yul ni sgra ste / / zin-pa #  dang ma-zin-pa #  dang gnyi-ga # 'i ste 'byung-ba-chen-po # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  bstan to /
mahABUtAni yaH ca / sprazwavyasya eka deSaH uktaH tat saha mahABUtEH prazwavya Ayatanam
# 'byung-ba-chen-po #  dag dang gang reg-bya # 'i phyogs-gcig #  bshad-pa #  ste / / de 'byung-ba-chen-po #  rnams dang bcas-pa #  ni reg-bya # 'i skye-mched #  do /
tat punar SlakzNa tvam ityAdi
# de-yang #  'jam-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
manaya Ayatanam yaH vijQAna skanDa eti / azwO / vijQAnAni vijQAna skanDaH zaX pravRtti vijQAna aniAlaya vijQAnam klizwam ca manaH
# yid kyi skye-mched #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i phung-po #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la rnam-par-shes-pa #  brgyad ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i phung-po #  ste / / 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  drug dang kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yod do /
Ayatana vyavasTAyAm tuvijQAna skanDaH eva mana Ayatanam ucyate / Darma Ayatanam punar azwa prakAram
# skye-mched #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  la ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i phung-po #  nyid la yid kyi skye-mched #  ces bya'o / / chos-kyi-skye-mched #  ni rnam-pa-brgyad #  de /
vedanA saQjQA saMskAra skanDAH avijQaptiH ca asaMskRtAni cacatvAri
# tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po #  dang rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  dang 'dus-ma-byas #  bzhi'o /
tatra / vedanA saQjQA saMskAra skanDAH avijQaptiH ca skanDa viBaFga eva uktAH / asaMskRtam tu na uktam iti atas tad praBeda buButsayA pRcCati asaMskRtam katamat iti
# de-la #  tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po #  dang rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  ni phung-po #  rnam-par-phye-ba # s bshad-pa #  yin no / / 'dus-ma-byas #  ni ma bshad de / / de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  rab-tu-dbye-ba # r 'dod nas / / 'dus-ma-byas #  gang zhe na zhes dris so /
yat na / hetu pratyaya pratibadDa svarUpam tat asaMskRtam ucyate / AkASam apratisaFKyA niroDaH pratisaFKyA niroDaH taTatA ca iti
# gang rgyu-dang-rkyen #  la rag-las-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  rang-gi #  ngo bo ni 'dus-ma-byas #  zhes bya ste / / nam-mkha' #  dang so-so # r brtags ba ma-yin-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  dang so-so #  brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  dang de-bzhin-nyid #  do /
asaMskRta praBeda pradarSanam
# 'dus-ma-byas #  kyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ston te /
AkASam katamat iti / AkASa svarUpa avaboDa arTam praSnaH / yaH rUpa avakASa eti tad svarUpa nirdeSaH
# nam-mkha' #  gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni nam-mkha' # i rang-gi #  ngo bo khong-du-chud-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir 'dri-ba # 'o / / gang gzugs kyi go 'byed-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i rang-gi #  ngo bo bshad-pa # 'o /
evam apratisaFKya aniroDa Adizu api pratyekam vAcyam / sa pratiGam rUpam yatra pradeSe na pratihanya tejaH tasya avakASaH
# de-bzhin-du #  so-sor-brtags-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  so-so # r brjod-pa # r bya'o / / phyogs gang-du #  thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i gzugs la thogs-pa # r mi-byed-pa #  ni go 'byed-pa # 'o /
atas rUpiNAm BAvAnAm avakASa dAnAt AkASam iti ucyate
# de'i-phyir #  dngos-po-gzugs-can #  rnams la skabs-'byed-pa #  nam-mkha' #  zhes-bya'o #  /
AkASa anantaram uddizwa tvAt tat irde Anant aram eva apratisaFKyA niroDa svarUpa avaboDa arTam praSnaH apratisaFKyA niroDaH katamaH iti
# nam-mkha' # i 'og-tu #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir de bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  so-sor-brtags-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i 'gog-pa # 'i rang-gi #  ngo bo khong-du-chud-pa # r 'dod nas / / so-sor-brtags-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  gang zhe na zhes dris so /
saFKyAnam / tulanam vicayaH prajQA iti anarTa antaram / pratiH vIpsA arTaH
# brtags-pa #  dang gzhal-ba #  dang rnam-par-'byed-pa #  dang shes-rab #  ces bya-ba #  ni don gcig go / / so-so # r zhes-bya-ba #  ni spyir bsnyag pa'i don te /
tat uktam Bavati duHKa AdInAm Arya satya AnAMprati pratisaFKyAnam pratisaFKyA
# de ni 'di-ltar #  sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa #  'phags-pa'i-bden-pa #  rnams la so-sor-rtog-pa #  ni so-sor-brtags-pa #  ste /
prajQA viSezaH iti arTaH / na pratisaFKyA apratisaFKyA / kA punar asO / pratyaya vEkalyam
# shes-rab #  kyi khyad-par #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / so-so # r ma-brtags-pa #  ni so-sor-brtags-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  ste / / de-yang #  gang zhe na /
etat uktam Bavati pratyaya vEkalyAt anAgatAnAm DarmANAm yaH atyantam anutpAdaH saH apratisaFKyA niroDEti
# rkyen ma-tshang-ba # 'o / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  rkyen ma-tshang-ba # 'i phyir ma-'ongs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  gtan-du #  mi-skye-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de so-sor-brtags-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i 'gog-pa # 'o zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro /
yaH niroDaH na ca visaMyoga etya Adi praSna vyAkaraNam
# gang 'gog-pa #  la 'bral-ba #  ma-yin-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni 'dri-ba # 'i lan no /
niroDa SabdaH hi atra / pratisaFKya aniroDa samApatti upapatti anitya tA niroDezu api vartate iti pratisaFKyA niroDa vyavacCeda arTam Aha na cavisaMyogaH iti
# 'gog-pa #  zhes byas-na #  ni so-sor-brtags-pa #  ma-yin-pa # s 'gog-pa #  bzhin-du #  so-sor-brtags-pa #  dang; snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dang skye-ba #  dang mi-rtag-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  rnams la yang snyegs-pa # s 'dir so-sor-brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  rnam-par-dbye-ba # 'i phyir 'bral-ba #  ma-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /
saMyogaH hi anAgatEH DarmEH bIje sati tezAm utpatti Darma tAm upAdAya vyavasTApyate / tad pratipakzeNa svASrayAt tezAm bIje apa udDRte yaH atyantam anutpAdaH pratilabDaH itisaH api apratisaFKyA niroDaH prApnoti iti atas Aha sa punar yaH kleSa pratipakzeNa vinA skanDAnAm atyantam anutpAdaH iti / etat uktam
# 'bral-ba #  ma yin zhes-bya-ba #  ni sa-bon #  yod-na #  de-dag #  'byung-ba # 'i chos-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ma-'ongs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  dang phrad-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / de'i gnyen-po # s rang-gi #  gnas nas de-dag #  gi sa-bon #  bton bzhin gtan mi-skye-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de 'gog-pa # 'o / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  sa-bon #  bton la blo sngon-du #  ma btang yang rkyen ma-tshang-ba # s ma-'ongs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  gtan mi-skye-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de so-sor-brtags-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i 'gog-pa # 'o zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / dgra-bcom-pa #  la ni ris gzhan dang 'brel-ba # 'i dge-ba #  dang lung dum bstan-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams kyis bon yod-bzhin-du #  gtan mi-skye-ba #  thob-pa # s / / de-yang #  so-sor-brtags-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i 'gog-par #  'gyur ro zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  / / de ni gang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  med-pa # r phung-po #  rnams gtan-du #  mi-skye-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  /
Bavati ayam hi sati api kuSala akuSala avyAkRta skanDa bIja sadBAvena vinA kleSa pratipakzeNa laByate iti pratisaFKyA niroDaH eva ayam na apratisaFKyA niroDaH
# 'di-la #  dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'i phung-po # 'i sa-bon #  yod-du-zin-kyang #  / / nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  med-pa # r mi-thob-pa # s so-so #  brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  nyid de / / 'di ni so-so # r ma-brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  ma yin no /
evam sopaDi SezaH nirupaDi SezaH canirvANa DAtuH pratisaFKyA niroDaH iti uktam Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang phung-po # 'i lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i dbyings ni so-sor-brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  zhes bstan-pa #  yin no /
kleSa pratipakzaH atra anAsravaH mArgaH aBipretaH
# nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  ni 'dir zag-pa-med-pa # 'i lam-du #  bzhed do /
atyantam anutpAdaH iti atyanta grahaNam upapatti samApatti niroDa vyavacCeda arTam
# gtan-du #  mi-skye-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la gtan-du #  smos-pa #  ni skye-ba #  dang snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  las rnam-par-dbye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sahi anutpAdoBavatina tu atyantam punar citta cEtta utpAda sadBAvAt / anutpAdaH iti anitya tA niroDAt / anitya tA niroDaH hi vartamAnasyana ca vartamAnasya anutpAdaH asti kim tarhi anAgatasya eva iti / tat yaTA eka rUpa prakAra vyAsakta cakzuH vijQAnasya yAni vizaya antarANi utpattimanti rUpa prakAra antarANi catada AlambanEH paQcaBiH vijQAna kAyEH na Sakyam utpattum vartamAnezu samanantara pratyaya aBAvAt atItezu Alambana pratyaya aBAvAt / atas tezAm apratisaFKyA niroDaH prApyate
# de-dag #  mi-skye-ba #  yin la gtan-du #  ma-yin-pa #  ste / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyang-'byung-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro / / mi-skye-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  kyi 'gog-pa #  las rnam-pa # r 'byed de / / mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  kyi 'gog-pa #  ni de-ltar #  yod-la #  mi-skye-ba #  ni da-ltar #  med-pa # s ma-'ongs-pa #  yin pa nyid de / / dper-na #  gzugs kyi rnam-pa #  gcig la mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  yengs pa yul gzhan dang gzugs kyi rnam-pa #  gzhan 'das-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni dmigs-pa #  de'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs lnga bskyed-pa # r mi nus te / / da-ltar #  gyi rnam-pa #  la ni de-ma-thag-pa # 'i rkyen med cing / / 'das-pa #  rnams la ni dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  la so-sor-brtags-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i 'gog-par #  'gyur ro /
pratisaFKyA niroDaH katamaH iti
# so-sor-brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  gang zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  la /
kpratisaFKyAnam pratisaFKyA Anantarya mArga saFgRhItaH prajQA viSezaH iti arTaH / pratisaFKyayA prApyaH niroDaH maDya pada lopAt / yaH niroDa eti sarva niroDa prasaFgaH iti Aha sa cavisaMyoga eti / evam hi SezeByaH caturByaH / niroDeByaH vyavacCinnaH Bavati tezAm avisaMyoga Atmaka tvAt
# so-sor-rtog-pa #  ni so-sor-brtags-pa #  ste / / bar-chad-med-pa'i-lam #  gyis shes-rab #  kyi khyad-par #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / so-sor-brtags-pa # s thob-par-bya-ba # 'i 'gog-pa #  ni so-sor-brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  ste / / tshig bar-ma #  ma smos so / / gang 'gog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'gog-pa #  thams-cad-du #  thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba # s / / de ni 'brel-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de-ltar-na #  'gog-pa #  lhag-ma #  bzhi-po #  las rnam-par-phye-ba #  yin te /
visaMyogam eva nirUpayati sa punar yaH kleSa pratipakzeNa skanDAnAm atyantam anutpAdaH iti
# de-dag #  ni 'bral-ba # 'i bdag-nyid #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-po # s phung-po #  gtan-du #  mi-skye-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'bral-ba #  nyid dpyod-pa #  ste /
ayam hi ASrayaH / niravaSeza trEDAtuka kleSa bIja anusyUtaH pravartate
# lus 'di ni khams-gsum-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  nam lus pa dang rjes-su-'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'o /
tatra yasya yayasya yaH yaH mArga kzaNaH pratipakzaH tasmin mArgaH utpannesaH ASraya kzaNaH tad praheya kleSa bIja anugata mnantarasya ASrayasya kzaNa antaram utpAdayitum na Saknoti tad utpatti virudDa pratyaya sAnniDyAt
# de-la #  gang-dang-gang #  gi gnyen-po #  lam gyi skad-cig #  gang-dang-gang #  yin pa'i lam de 'byung na lus kyi skad-cig #  de ni des spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sa-bon-dang-ldan-pa # 'i phyi-ma #  lus kyi skad-cig #  gzhan 'byung-ba #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i rkyen-du-gyur-pa #  dang phyi-ma #  lus kyi skad-cig #  gzhan skyed-pa # r mi nus te / / de 'byung-ba #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i rkyen nye-bar-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kim tarhitat praheya kleSa bIja vyAvRtti Atmakasya eva kAraNam Bavati tad utpatti anuguNa pratyaya sadBAvAt
# 'on-kyang #  des spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  ldog-pa #  bdag-nyid #  kho-na # 'i rgyur 'gyur te / / de byung-ba #  dang mthun-pa # 'i rkyen yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
saH eva mArga kzaNaH tad praheya kleza bIja anugatasya kzaNa antarasya utpattaye viguNaH pratyayaH itarasya anuguNaH veditavyaH
# lam gyi skad-cig #  de nyid ni des spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sa-bon-dang-ldan-pa # 'i skad-cig #  gzhan 'byung-ba #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i rkyen-du-gyur-pa #  dang cig shos dang mthun-par #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
evam yAvat BAvanA heyasya mRdu mRdoH kleSa prakArasya pratipakzaH utpanne saH ASraya uniH avaSeza trEDAtuka darSana BAvanA prahAtavya kleSa bIja vyAvR tti Atmakasya eva kzaNa antarasya kAraNIBavati
# de-bzhin-du #  bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i srid-pa # 'i rtse mo'i nyon-mongs-pa #  chung du chung-ngu # 'i bar gyi gnyen-po #  byung na lus de khams-gsum-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  mthong-ba #  dang bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i sa-bon #  ma-lus-par #  ldog-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  kho-na # 'i skad-cig #  gzhan gyi rgyur 'gyur ro /
evam yasyayasya kleSasya ASraya apravRttitaH bIjam udDRtam Bavati tasya tasya tad samprayuktAnAm ca DarmANa aMkleSa pratipakzeNa atyantam anutpAdaH prAptaH Bavati / sa capratisaFKyA niroDaH visaMyogaH ca iti ucyate
# de-bzhin-du #  nyon-mongs-pa #  gang-dang-gang #  gi lus mi-'byung-ba # s sa-bon #  bton par gyur-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  de-dag #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  kyang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-po # s gtan-du #  mi-skye-ba # r 'byung ste / / so-sor-brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  de ni 'bral-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  /
pratisaFKyA niroDAt anantaram taTatA uddizwA iti atas tad nirdeSa anantaram taTatA avaboDa arTam praSnaH taTatA
# so-sor-brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  de-bzhin-nyid #  bstan-pa # s de'i-phyir #  de bshad-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  de-bzhin-nyid #  khong-du-chud-pa # r 'dod nas / / de-bzhin-nyid #  gang zhe na zhes 'dri'o /
katamA iti / yAH DarmANAm Darma tA Darma nErAtmyam iti tad nirdeSaH / ananyaTAtvena taTatA
# gang chos-rnams #  kyi chos-nyid #  dang chos-bdag-med-pa #  nyid do zhes-bya-ba #  de ni de'i bshad-pa #  ste / / gzhan ma-yin-pa # 'i don-gyi-phyir #  de-bzhin-nyid #  do /
DarmANAm iti rUpa vedanA saQjQA saMskAra vijQAnAnAm / DarmANAm BAvaH Darma tA yATAtmyam BUta prakarzaH
# chos-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams so / / chos-rnams #  kyi dngos bo ni chos-nyid #  de ji-lta-ba #  bzhin gyi bdag-nyid #  dang yang-dag-pa # 'i mthar-thug-pa # 'o /
DarmANAm kArya anitya tA AdayaH api Darma tA vidyante iti atas Aha Darma nErAtmyam iti
# chos-nyid #  ni chos-rnams #  kyi 'bras-bu #  mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  yang chos-rnams #  la yod de / / de'i-phyir #  chos-bdag-med-pa #  nyid ces bya-ba #  smos so /
DarmAH hi yena rUpeNa jQAna aBiDAnayoH vizayIBavanti tat tezAm AtmA / tasmAt AtmanaH nirgatAH atatsvaBAva tvAt iti nirAtmAnaH / tad BAva oDarmanEH Atmyam / tat punar BAva anAMkalpita svaBAva SUnyatA / atra tu vicAryamANe bahu vaktavyaMjAyate iti alam prasaFgena prastutam eva AraByate / kena arTena AyatanAni / Ayatana SabdaH hi cakzuH Adizu
# chos ni rang-bzhin #  gang-gis #  shes-pa #  dang brjod-pa #  gnyis kyi yul du 'gyur-ba #  de de-dag #  gi bdag ste / / de'i-rang-bzhin #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir bdag de dang bral-ba #  ni bdag-med-pa # 'o / / de'i dngos-po #  ni bdag-med-pa #  nyid do / / de ni dngos-po #  rnams rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  gyi stong-pa-nyid #  do / / 'di-la #  dpyad na brjod-pa #  mang-du #  'byung ste / / de thal-ba # r 'gyur-ba # s kyang chog gi skabs nyid brtsam mo / / ci'i-phyir #  skye-mched #  ces bya zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  la /
paraspara viBinna rUpezu aviSezeNa pravartate iti atas tezu tena sAmAnyam arTam upAdAya pravartitavyam sa ca na vijQAyata eti praSnaH kena arTena Ayatanani iti / vijQAnAya dvAra arTena iti / Aya ucyate AgamaH
# skye-mched #  kyi sgra ni mig la-sogs-pa #  rang-gi #  ngo bo phan tshun tha-dad-pa #  rnams la yang bye-brag-med-par #  'byung-ba # s de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  la des spyi'i don rgyur byas-na # s 'jug go / / de-yang #  mi-shes-pa # s ci'i-phyir #  skye-mched #  ces bya zhes 'dri'o / / rnam-pa # r shes ba skye-ba # 'i sgo'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  la / / skye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'byung-ba #  ste /
vijQAnAnAm utpattiH Atma lABaH

nirvacanAt citta cEttAnAm Ayam tanvanti vistRNvanti iti AyatanAni
# sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyi 'byung-ba #  mched par byed cing rgyas-par-byed-pa # s skye-mched #  rnams te /

# bdag thob-par-byed-pa #  rgyun-du #  'jog ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /

# de-dag #  'dus-ma-byas #  nam-mkha' #  la-sogs-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  ni chos-kyi-skye-mched #  dang chos-kyi-khams #  so / / ci'i-phyir #  khams zhes bya zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / skye-mched #  bzhin-du #  rgya-cher #  brjod-pa # r bya'o / / byed-pa #  med la rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  'dzin-pa # 'i phyir khams so /
na hikzaNikAnAm vyApAraH samBavati iti pUrvam eva uktam / yaH eva DarmAH skanDAH iti deSitAH te eva punar Ayatana tvena DAtutvena ca iti atas pRcCati kimarTam / skanDa Adi deSanA iti / sarvA hi deSanA BagavatA aMbudDAnAm sa prayojanA sattva arTa pravRtta tvAt kleSa pratipakzeNa ca / na ca atra prayojanam vijQAyate punar punar tezAm eva DarmANAm anyena anyena ca prakAreNa deSanA iti kimarTam skanDa Adi deSanA iti prayojana Mvaktavyam iti atas Aha triviDAtma grAha pratipakzeNa iti

# de'i-phyir #  bdag-tu-'dzin-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gyi gnyen-po # r zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / de-la #  bdag-tu-'dzin-pa #  gsum dang gang-gi #  gnyen-po # r bshad-pa #  yang mi-shes-pa # s de'i-phyir #  go-rims #  bzhin no zhes-bya-ba #  smos te /

# gang dag gzugs-kyi-phung-po # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do zhes-bya-ba #  de-dag #  ni khams bcu ste /
cakzuH DAtuH yAvat kAyaDAtuH rUpaDAtuH yAvat prazwavya DAtuH
# mig gi khams nas lus kyi bar dang gzugs-kyi-khams #  nas reg-bya # 'i khams kyi bar-du # 'o /
avijQapti rUpe sati api na DarmaDAtoH Upi tva prasaFgaH tasya ASraya ASrita rUpa aBAvAt rUpaNa aBAvAt rUpa skanDa AsaFgrahAt ca / kati arUpiNaH / SezAH / rUpi viparyayeNa ye
# rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa #  gzugs su yod-du-zin-kyang #  chos-kyi-khams #  gzugs-can #  nyid-du #  thal-ba # r mi 'gyur te / / de-la #  rten dang brten-pa # 'i gzugs-med-pa #  dang gzugs su yod-pa #  med-pa #  dang gzugs-kyi-phung-po # r gtogs su zin-kyang #  gzugs su yod-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gzugs-can-ma-yin-pa #  du zhe na / / lhag-ma #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  la gzugs-can #  las ldog-pa #  ni gzugs-can-ma-yin-pa #  ste /
te punar / azwO sapta citta DAtavaH DarmaDAtuH ca / kati sa nidarSanA iti / azwAdaSAnAm DAtUnAm iti
# de-dag #  ni brgyad de / / sems kyi khams bdun dang chos-kyi-khams #  so / / bstan-du-yod-pa #  du zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin-pas #  der sbyar ro /
prakRta tvAt sambaDyate / ekaH rUpaDAtuH iti / idam iha amutra iti ayam ayam eva vyapadeSaH nidarSanam / tena sahavartate iti sa nidarSanaH sa Alambana vat
# gzugs-kyi-khams #  gcig ste zhes-bya-ba #  la 'di ni 'di na'o zhes / / pha bi ni pha bi na'o zhes bstan du rung-ba #  de ni bstan-pa # 'o / / de dang lhan-cig #  pa ni bstan-du-yod-pa #  ste / / dmigs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  bzhin no /
idam eva nidarSana arTam praBAvayan= Aha deSa nidarSanena iti / tasmin= tasmin deSe nidarSyate anena iti deSa nidarSanam / ekasya eva rUpaDAtoH sa nidarSana tvena parigrahAt Seza aHsaptat aSa cakzuH Adi DAtavaH paQca Sabda Adi DAtavaH catvAroDarma DAtuH ekaH sapta citta DAtavaH anidarSanAH iti sidDam / kati sa pratiGAH / azwAdaSAnAm DAtUnAm prakRta tvAt / sarvatra sambaDyate
# bstan-du-yod-pa #  'di nyid rab-tu-bstan-pa # 'i phyir / / yul bstan-du-yod-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / yul de-dang-der #  'dis bstan-du-yod-pa # s yul bstan-du-yod-pa # 'o zhes-bya'o #  / / gzugs-kyi-khams #  gcig kho-na #  bstan-du-yod-pa #  nyid-du #  smos-pa # s lhag-ma #  khams bcu bdun ni bstan-du-med-pa # r grub bo / / thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  du zhen zhes-bya-ba #  ni khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin-pas #  thams-cad-du #  yang sbyar ro / / gzugs-can-ma-yin-pa #  rnam-pa # r gcad-pa # 'i phyir gzugs-can #  smos so /
DarmaDAtO= api avijQapti rUpa sadBAvAt asti rUpi vyapadeSaH itidaSa iti Aha / arUpi vyavacCeda arTaMrUpi grahaNam
# chos-kyi-khams #  la yang rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa # 'i gzugs yod-pa # s / / gzugs-can #  yod-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir bcu zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
te punar cakzuH Adi indriya DAtavaH paQca tad vizayAH rUpa Adi DAtavaH capaQca / pratiGAtaH pratiGaH / tena saha vartante iti sapratiGAH
# de-dag #  kyang mig la-sogs-pa #  dbang-po # 'i khams rnams dang de-dag #  gi yul gzugs-can #  gyi khams lnga'o / / go gcod-pa # s thogs-pa #  ste / / de dang lhan-cig #  pa ni thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'o /
dpratiGAtaH tri prakAraH vizaya Alambana AvaraNa pratiGAta BedAt
# go gcod-pa #  ni yul dang dmigs-pa #  dang sgrib-pa # s go gcod-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-gsum #  mo /
iha tu AvaraNa pratiGAtena eva sa pratiGa tvam izwam iti pratipAdayan= Aha yatra yaH ca pratihanyate iti
# 'dir ni sgrib-pa # 'i go gcod-pa #  nyid thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa # r 'dod-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir gang-la #  gang thogs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
AvaraNa pratiGAtaH hi sva deSe parasya utpatti pratibanDaH
# sgrib-pa # 'i go gcod-pa #  ni rang-gi-yul #  du gzhan 'byung-ba # 'i gegs su gyur-pa # 'o /
evaMca yena anyasya sva deSe utpattiH pratibaDyate yasya ca pratibaDyate tat uBayam api sa pratiGam iti jQApita MBavati
# de-ltar-na #  gang-gis #  rang-gi-yul #  du gzhan 'byung-ba # 'i gegs-byed-pa #  dang gang-la #  gegs-byed-pa #  de-gnyi-ga #  yang-thog # s pa dang bcas-pa #  zhes bstan-pa #  yin no /
etena ca daSa rUpiNaH DAtavaH parasparasya sva deSa Otpattim pratibaDnanti iti AvaraNa pratiGAtena sa pratiGAH SezAH sapta citta DAtavaH DarmaDAtuH ca apratiGAiti / sidDam / kati sa AsravAH / DAtUnAm iti prakRtam / paQcadaSa / trayANAm ca paScimAnAm BAgaH iti / cakzuH AdayaH / paQca indriya DAtavaH rUpa AdayaH paQca vizaya DAtavaH paQca cakzuH Adi vijQAna DAtavaH ca ete paQcadaSa ekAntena sa AsravAH eva iva iva eva / AdyAH api trayaH vidyante cakzUrUpa cakzuH vijQAna DAtavEti atas Aha paScimAnAm iti / paScimAH traya manoDAtuH DarmaDAtuH manaH vijQAna DAtuH ca / tezAm api BAgaH aMSaH sa AsravaH na tu cakzuH Adi vat sarve eva sa AsravAH / tezAm punar yaH namArga satya asaMskRta svaBAvaH BAgaH saH eva sa AsravaH / sa AsravEH saha vartante iti sa AsravAH / atas eva Aha tezu kleSaH tpattitaH iti / tezu yasmAt kleSAH utpadyante tezAm Asrava iti
# khams gzugs-can #  bcu po de-dag #  kyang rang-rang-gi #  yul du 'byung-ba #  la gcig-la-gcig #  gegs-byed-pa # s sgrib cing go gcod-pa # 'i phyir thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  rnams so / / lhag-ma #  sems kyi khams bdun dang chos-kyi-khams #  ni thogs-pa-med-pa # r grub po zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  du zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni khams kyi skabs yin no / / bco lnga dang tha-ma #  gsum gyi cha ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni mig la-sogs-pa #  dbang-po-lnga # 'i khams dang gzugs la-sogs-pa #  yul lnga'i khams dang mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  lnga ste / / khams bco lnga po dag ni gcig-tu #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  nyid do / / dang-po #  la yang gsum yod de / / mig dang gzugs dang mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  yin-pas #  de'i-phyir #  tha-ma #  zhes smos so / / tha-ma #  gsum ni yid kyi khams dang chos-kyi-khams #  dang yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  so / / de-dag #  gi cha ni cha-shas #  te / / zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'o / / mig la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  thams-cad #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  nyid ni ma yin no / / de-dag #  las kyang lam gyi bden-pa #  dang 'dus-ma-byas #  kyi rang-bzhin #  gyi cha-ma-yin-pa #  de nyid zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  ste / / zag-pa #  dang lhan-cig #  pas zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'o / / de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  nyon-mongs-pa #  skye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos te / / 'di-ltar #  de-dag #  las nyon-mongs-pa #  skye-ba # s de'i-phyir #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
cakzuH Adi vijQAnAnAm avikalpaka tvAt kaTam rUpa Adizu kleSa utpattiH
# mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams ni / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  yin-pas #  ji-ltar #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  rnams la nyon-mongs-pa #  skyed ce na /
na ucyate cakzuH Adi vijQAnEH eva saha rUpa Adizu kleSAH utpadyante itikim tarhi pratyakza gocara tAm upAdAya rUpa Adizu kleSa utpattiH ucyate
# nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams dang lhan-cig-tu #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la 'byung-ba #  zhes mi bya mod kyi / / 'on-kyang #  mngon-sum #  gyi spyod yul gyi phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa # s nyon mongs la skyed-pa #  ste /
taTA hi cakzuH capratItya rUpANi ca pratItya cakzuH vijQAnam utpadyata cakzuH vijQAna anuBUtAni rUpANi manaH vijQAnena vikalpyantevi kalpAt ca kleSAH utpadyante iti / evam Sezezu api vAcyam / kati anAsravAH / trayANAm paScimAnAm / BAgaH / manaH Darma manaH vijQAna DAtUnAm yomArga satya asaMskRta saFgRhItaH pradeSaH saH anAsravaH iti / kati kAma pratisaMyuktAH / azwAdaSAnAm DAtUnAm / iti sambaDyate / paQca rUpa AdayaH vizayAH kAmyante iti kAmAH / tad praDAnaH DAtuH kAmaDAtuH / tad pratisaMyuktAH kAma pratisaMyuktAH iti ucyante
# 'di-ltar #  mig la brten-cing #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la brten-nas #  mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung ste / / mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa # s myong-ba # 'i gzugs rnams la yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # s rnam-par-rtog-pa # r byed-pa # s rnam-par-rtog-pa #  las nyon-mongs-pa #  'byung ste / / de-bzhin-du #  lhag-ma #  rnams la yang brjod-pa # r bya'o / / zag-pa-med-pa #  du zhe na / / tha-ma #  gsum gyi cha'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni yid dang chos dang yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  rnams kyi'o / / lam gyi bden-pa #  dang 'dus-ma-byas #  su gtogs-pa # 'i phyogs gang-yin-pa #  de ni zag-pa-med-pa # 'o / / 'dod-pa-dang-ldan-pa #  du zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni khams bco brgyad ces bya-ba #  dang sbyar te / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  yul lnga ni 'dod-par-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  'dod-pa #  rnams te / / de gces su byed-pa # 'i khams rnams ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  su shes-pa # r bya'o /
aTavA akAma DAtu pratisaMyuktAH iti vaktavye DAtu Sabda lopAt kAma pratisaMyuktAH iti uktAH
# yang-na #  'dod-pa'i-khams #  dang ldan-pa #  du zhe na zhes brjod-pa # 'i rigs-pa #  las khams zhes-bya-ba # 'i sgra ma smos-pa #  'dod-pa-dang-ldan-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
kAma pratisaMyuktAH kAmaDAtu saFgRhItAH kAmaDAtu svaBAvAH iti arTaH
# 'dod-pa'i-khams #  dang ldan-pa #  dag ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  kyis bsdus-pa #  rnams te / / 'dod-pa'i-khams #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
taTA atra kAma tRzNA samudAcAraH tat sarvaMkAma DAtu saFgRhItam / te punar sarve zaX indriya DAtavaH zakRt vizaya DAtavaH zaX vijQAna DAtavaH ca / kati rUpa pratisaMyuktAH / caturdaSa
# 'di-ltar #  gang-du #  'dod-pa'i-sred-pa #  kun du 'byung-ba #  thams-cad #  'dod-pa'i-khams #  su bsdus-pa # 'o / / de-dag #  kyang dbang-po # 'i khams drug dang yul gyi khams drug dang rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  drug go / / gzugs-dang-ldan-pa #  du zhe na / / bcu bzhi ste /
tatra zaX / cakzuH Srotra GrANa jihvA kAya manEndriya DAtavaH catvAraH vizaya DAtavaH tad vizaya vijQAna DAtavaH catvAraH ete caturdaSa rUpaDAtu pratisaMyuktAH
# mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang; lce dang lus dang yid-kyi-dbang-po # 'i khams dang yul bzhi dang yul de'i rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  bzhi ste / / bcu bzhi-po #  de-dag #  ni gzugs-kyi-khams #  dang ldan-pa # 'o /
kim punar kAraNaMganDa rasayaH rUpaDAtO na BAvaH tad vijQAnayoH ca
# ci'i-phyir #  gzugs-kyi-khams #  na dri dang ro dang de'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  gnyis kyang med ce na /
ganDarasO hi ekAntena kavaXIkAra AhAra svaBAvO= eva na tu sparSa vedanA AhAra svaBAvO / api cakava XIkAra AhAra vIta rAgAH ca rUpaDAtO= upapadyanteya dvIpa rAgAH ca yatra upapadyante tatra tasya aBAvaH tad yaTArUpa vIta rAgANAm ArUpya ApattO cakzuH AdInAm / vizaya aBAvAt ca ganDa rasa vijQAnayoH api aBAvaH
# dri dang ro ni gcig-tu #  kham gyi zas kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  yin gyi reg-pa #  dang sems-pa # 'i zas kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  ma yin no / / yang kham gyi zas kyi 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  rnams ni gzugs-kyi-khams #  su skye ste / / gang-gi #  'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  rnams gang-du #  skyes-pa #  de na med de / / dper-na #  / / 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  gzugs-med-par-skyes-pa # 'i mig la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  yul med-pa # 'i phyir dri dang ro'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  gnyis kyang med do /
kati ArUpya pratisaMyuktAH / paScimAH / trayaH
# gzugs-med-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  du zhe na / / tha-ma #  gsum zhes-bya-ba #  ni /
manoDAtuH Darma DAtuH manaH vijQAna DAtuH ca
# yid kyi khams dang; chos-kyi-khams #  dang yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  so /
rUpavIta rAgAH hi ArUpya DAtO= utpadyante / atas tatra daSa rUpa svaBAvAH DAtavaH tad ASraya AlambanAH ca paQca vijQAna DAtavaH na santi / kati apratisaMyuktAH / ye anAsravAH / ye / kAma rUpA rUpya tRzNABiH na Alambyante
# gzugs-kyi-'dod-chags #  dang bral-ba #  rnams ni gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  su skye ste / / de'i-phyir #  de na gzugs kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi khams bcu dang de-la #  brten-pa #  dang dmigs-pa #  rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  lnga med do / / mi-ldan-pa #  du zhe na gsum gyi cha'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang dag 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa # 'i sred-pa #  rnams kyis ma dmigs-pa #  ste /
DAtu traya viyukta tvAt apratisaMyuktAH / yemArga satya asaMskRta svaBAva manaH Darma manaH vijQAna DAtavaH te anAsravAH / kati kuSalAH / kati akuSalAH / kati / avyAkRtAH
# khams-gsum #  dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir mi-ldan-pa # 'o / / lam gyi bden-pa #  dang 'dus-ma-byas #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  gang-yin-pa # 'i yid dang chos dang yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  de-dag #  ni zag-pa-med-pa # 'o / / dge-ba #  du /
azwAdaSAnAm DAtUnAm iti prakRta tvAt sambaDyate
# mi-dge-ba #  du / / lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  du zhe na / / khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin-pas #  der sbyar ro /
tatra kutsitAt Calitam iti kuSalam gatam iti arTaH / kuSA iti vA prajQA paryAyaH / lAH AdAne
# de-la #  ngan-pa #  bsnyil-ba # 'i phyir dge-ba #  ste / / song zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / yang-na #  ku sha ni shes-rab #  kyi rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa # 'o / / la ni len-pa #  ste /
prajQA parigRhItAH prajQA parigrAhakAH vA kuSalAH / kutsitena vAkAreNa SerataH iti kuSAH CedakAH veDakAH ca iti / lAH AdAne
# shes-rab #  kyis yongs-su-zin-pa # 'am / / shes-rab #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  ni dge-ba #  rnams so / / yang-na #  ngan-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r 'dug-pa #  ni rtsva ku sha ste /
yaH Cedana veDana parihAreNa kuSAn Adatte sa kuSalaH iti ucyate / evam anyaH api yasyAm kriyAyAm praSaMsAm arhati sa kuSalaH tatra ucyate
# gcod-pa #  dang 'bigs-pa # 'o / / la ni len-pa #  ste / / su zhig gcod-pa #  dang 'bigs-pa #  spangs-te #  / / rtsva ku sha rnams len-pa #  de ni mkhas-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de-bzhin-du #  gzhan bya-ba #  gang-la #  bsngags-pa # r 'os-pa #  de ni dge-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  /
etena akuSalam vyAKyAtam / kuSala akuSala BAvena avyAkaraNAt avyAkRtAH
# 'dis mi-dge-ba #  bzlog-ste #  bshad do / / dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i dngos-po # r lung du bstan-pa #  med-pa # s ma bstan-pa # 'o /
daSa triviDAH / iti kuSalAH api akuSalAH api avyAkRtAH api
# bcu ni rnam-pa-gsum #  char te zhes-bya-ba #  ni dge-ba #  yang yin / / mi-dge-ba #  yang yin / / lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  yang yin no /

atra citta DAtUnAm samprayogataH kuSala akuSala tvam na svatas kuSala akuSala mUlAnAm ca iti
# de-la #  sems kyi khams rnams ni mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # s dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  nyid yin gyi / / ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi ni ma yin te / / dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba rnams dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # s so /
tatra sapta citta DAtavaH aloBa adveza amoha samprayuktAH kuSalAH
# de-la #  sems kyi khams bdun ma-chags-pa #  dang zhe-sdang #  med-pa #  dang gti-mug #  med-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  rnams ni dge-ba # 'o /
loBa dveza moha samprayukta akuSalAH
# chags-pa #  dang zhe-sdang #  dang gti-mug #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  rnams ni mi-dge-ba # 'o /

# gzugs dang sgra'i khams lus dang ngag gi rnam-par-rig-byed #  du bsdus-pa #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba'i-sems #  kyis kun-nas-bslang-ba #  ni dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'o / / de-las-gzhan-pa #  ni lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'o /

# chos-kyi-khams #  kyang ma-chags-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang kun-nas-bslang-ba #  dang so-sor-brtags-pa # 'i 'gog-pa #  dang de-bzhin-nyid #  ni dge-ba # 'o /
loBa Adi svaBAva samprayukta samutTaH akuSalaH

# dre dang ro dang reg-bya #  dang mig la-sogs-pa #  lnga'o / / de-dag #  ni lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  nyid de / / don-dam-pa #  dang ngo-bo-nyid #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang kun-nas-bslang-ba # s dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# nang gi du zhe na; khams bco brgyad ces bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
sambaDyate / dvAdaSa / te tu na prajQAyante katame dvAdaSa iti Aha rUpa Sabda ganDa rasa sprazwavya DarmaDAt / Un sTApayitvA iti / Seza aHzaX indriya DAtavaH zaXni vijQAna DAtavaH iti ete dvAdaSa ADyAtmikAH
# bcu gnyis te bcu gnyis gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  kyang mi-shes-pa # s / / gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg-bya #  dang chos-kyi-khams #  ma gtogs so zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / lhag-ma #  dbang-po # 'i khams drug dang rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  drug ste / / bcu gnyis po de-dag #  ni nang gi'o /
kati DAtavaH bAhyAH / zax / te tu na vijQAyante iti atas Aha / ye sTApitAH / ete bAhyAH iti bodDavyAH
# khams rnams las phyi-rol #  gyi du zhe na drug ste / / de-dag #  kyang mi shes-nas #  / / de'i-phyir #  gang dag ma-gtogs-pa #  rnams so zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / 'di dag ni phyi'i yin par shes-pa # r bya'o /
ke ca sTApitAH / rUpa Sabda ganDa rasa sprazwavya Darma DAtavaH
# ma-gtogs-pa #  rnams gang zhe na / / gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg-bya #  dang chos-kyi-khams #  rnams so /
aDi AtmAnam aDyAtmam / aDyAtmam eva ADyAtmikam
# bdag-gi #  dbang-du-byas-pa #  ni nang zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / nang nyid nang ngo /
Atmani asati kaTam ADyAtmikam bAhyam vABavati
# bdag-nyid #  med na nang ngam phyi zhes-bya-ba # r ji-ltar #  'gyur te /
na hi SIle asati aDiSIlam SikzA yujyate
# tshul-khrims #  med na tshul-khrims #  kyi dbang-du-byas-pa # 'i bslab-pa #  mi-rung-ba #  bzhin no zhe na /
ahaFkAra sanniSrita tvAt cittam AtmA iti upacaryate
# ngar-'dzin-pa # 'i gnas yin pa'i phyir sems la bdag ces 'dogs so /
ahaFkAra sanniSrayaH hi Atma vAdiBiH AtmA iti aBiDIyate / taTA hi Atma guNa tvena Atma vizaya tvena ca ahaFkAram pratipannAH
# ngar-'dzin-pa # 'i gzhi ni bdag-tu-smra-ba #  rnams kyis bdag ces brjod de / / 'di-ltar #  bdag-gi #  yon-tan #  nam / / bdag yul nyid-du #  ngar-'dzin-pa #  rtogs so /
ahaFkAraH ca citta sanniSritaH tad vyatirikta Atma aBAvAt / AhitaH ahaMmAnaH etasmin= iti AtmA
# ngar-'dzin-pa #  yang sems la brten-pa #  ste / / de-las-gud-na #  bdag-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-la #  nga'o snyam-du #  nga-rgyal #  skyed-pa # s bdag ste /
cittam eva cEttAnAm ASrayaH iti cittam eva Atma tvena upacaryate / kaTam punar etat gamyate atra Atma tvena cittam aBipretam iti
# sems nyid sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyi gnas yin-pas #  sems nyid la bdag tu 'dogs so / / 'dir sems la bdag ces bya-ba # r bzhed-pa # r 'di ci mngon zhe na /
uktam hi BagavatA AtmanA hi su dAntena svargam prApnoti paNXitA eti
# bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis / / bdag ni legs-par #  dul gyur na / / mkhas-pa # s mtho-ris #  thob-pa # r 'gyur / / zhes gsungs so /
cittasya ca anyatra damanam uktam cittasya damanam sADu cittam dAntam suKa Avaham iti
# gzhan nas kyang sems 'dul-ba #  gsungs te / / sems 'dul-ba #  ni legs-pa #  ste / / sems 'dul bde-ba #  thob-pa # r byed / / ce'o /
atra hi cittasya damanam cittam eva dAntam suKa Avaham iti uktam
# 'dir sems 'dul-ba #  dang sems nyid-du # l na bde-ba #  thob-pa # r byed / / ces gsungs-pa # s de'i-phyir #  /
atas atra api AtmanA hi sudAntena svargam prApnoti paNXitaH iti cittam eva aBipretam iti vijQAyate
# bdag ni legs-par #  dul gyur na / / mkhas-pa # s mtho-ris #  thob-pa # r 'gyur / / zhes-bya-ba #  'dir yang sems nyid la bya-ba # r bzhed-pa # r mngon no /
atas ca Atma BUtasya cittasya ASraya BAvena pratyAsanna tvAt cakzuH AdInAm ADyAtmika tvam
# de'i-phyir #  bdag-tu-lta-ba # 'i sems kyi rten gyi dngos-po # r nye-bar-gyur-pa # 'i phyir mig la-sogs-pa #  ni nang gi nyid do /
rUpa AdInAm ca vizaya BAvAt bAhya tvam
# gzugs la-sogs-pa #  yul-gyi-dngos-po # r gyur-pa #  ni phyi'i nyid do /
evam tarhi zaX vijQAna DAtavaH ADyAtmikAH na prApnuvanti nahi ete manaH DAtu tvam aprAptAH cittasya ASrayIBavanti iti iti / yat AtadA te eva te Bavanti iti lakzaNam na ativartanta eti
# de-ltar-na #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  drug nang gir mi 'gyur te / / de-dag #  yid kyi khams nyid-du #  ma gyur gyi bar-du #  sems kyi rten du mi-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro zhe na / / nam du yang rung ste / / de-dag-nyid #  nad yin-pas #  mtshan-nyid #  las 'da' ba med do /
kati sAlambanA DAtavaH iti prakRtam / atas Aha saptA iti
# dmigs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  du zhe na zhes-bya-ba #  ni khams kyi skabs yin-pas #  de'i-phyir #  bdun zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
te api na jQAyante katame sapta iti atas Aha citta DAtavyA eti / kim ete eva sa AlambanAH / na kim tarhi Darma DAtu pradeSaH ca
# bdun po de-dag #  kyang gang yin mi-shes-pa # s de'i-phyir #  sems kyi khams zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / dmigs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  'di dag nyid-du #  zad dam zhe na / / ma yin te / / chos-kyi-khams #  kyi phyogs-gcig #  kyang yin te /
caSabdaH samuccaye sapta citta DAtavaH DarmaDAtu pradeSaH ca sa AlambanaH iti / asti amIzAm Alambanam iti sa AlambanAH
# kyang gi sgra ni bsdu'o / / sems kyi khams bdun dang chos-kyi-khams #  kyi gcig kyang dmigs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  yin te / / 'di dag la dmigs-pa #  yod-pa # s dmigs-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'o /
vizayaH gocaraH Alambanam iti paryAyAH
# yul dang spyod yul dang dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa # 'o /
sapta citta DAtavaH cakzuH Srotra GrANa rasana kAya manaH vijQAna manoDAtavaH DarmaDAtu pradeSaH ca yaH cEtasika svaBAvaH / kati anAlambanAH / SezAH
# sems kyi khams bdun ni mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams so / / chos-kyi-khams #  kyi phyogs-gcig #  ni gang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do / / dmigs-pa-med-pa #  du zhe na / / lhag-ma #  rnams te /
te punar daSa
# de-dag #  kyang bcu ste /
paQca indriya DAtavaH cakzuH AdayaH paQca vizaya DAtavaH rUpa AdayaH DarmaDAtu pradeSaH cayaH na cEtasika svaBAvaH / kati vikalpakAH
# mig la-sogs-pa #  dbang-po # 'i khams lnga dang gzugs la-sogs-pa #  yul gyi khams lnga'o / / chos-kyi-khams #  kyi phyogs gang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ma-yin-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  du zhe na /
azwAdaSAnAm DAtUnAm iti
# khams bco brgyad ces bya-ba # r sbyar ro /
sambaDyate / manaH DAtuH manaH vijQAna DAtuH Darma DAtoH ca pradeSoyaH samprayuktaH
# yid kyi khams dang yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  dang; chos-kyi-khams #  kyi phyogs so zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'o /
etO / hi aBinirUpaNa anusmaraNa vikalpAByAm samprayuktO tO= eva vikalpakO na itarO tAByAm asamprayogAt / Darma DAtu pradeSaH api samprayuktaH na itaraH
# 'di gnyis ni mngon-pa # r dpyod-pa #  dang rjes-su-dran-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ste / / de nyid rnam-par-rtog-pa #  yin gyi gzhan ni ma yin te / / de gnyis dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / chos-kyi-khams #  kyi phyogs ni mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  can te / / gzhan ni ma yin no /
tatra anusmaraNa vikalpaH smRtiH eva mAnasI anub hUtA lamb anAH ampuH amoz AkAr AH
# de-la #  rjes-su-dran-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni dran-pa #  nyid la bya ste / / yid kyi myong-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ma brjed-pa #  rnams so /
trEyaDvika parokza arTa aByuhana AkAraH idam evam na evam iti prajQA viSezaH cetanA vA aBirUpa NA vikalpaH
# dus-gsum #  gyi don lkog-tu-gyur-pa #  la mngon-pa # r dpyod-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  'di ni 'di lta yin gyi de lta ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  shes-rab #  kyi khyad-par #  la'am / / sems-pa #  ni mngon-pa # r dpyod-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ste /
yaTA uktam aBiDarma samuccaye anusmaraNa vikalpaH katamaH / yaH anuBUta pUrva saMskAra AkAraH
# chos-mngon-pa #  kun las btus pa las ji-skad-du #  / / rjes-su-dran-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  gang zhe na / / gang sngon myong-ba #  la 'du-byed #  bskyed-pa # 'o /
aBinirUpaNa avikalpaH katamaH
# mngon-pa # r dpyod-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  gang zhe na /
yaH atIta anAgata vartamAnezu viparokzezu aByUhana AkAraH vikalpaH
# gang 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  dang da-ltar #  gyi don lkog-tu-gyur-pa #  rnams la mngon-pa # r dpyod-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o zhes bshad-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
SezAH avikalpakAH iti sidDam
# lhag-ma #  rnams ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # r 'grub ste /
te punar paQcadaSa DAtavaH / DarmaDAtoH ca pradeSaH / ete hi avikalpakAH eva
# de-dag #  kyang khams bco lnga ste / / chos-kyi-khams #  kyi phyogs te / / de-dag #  ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid do /
azwAdaSAnAm DAtUn AMkati upAttAH / paQca ADyAtmikAH
# khams bco brgyad las zin-pa #  du zhe na / / nang gi lnga ste /
te punar cakzuH Srotra GrANa rasana kAya DAtavaH / ete hi upAttAH eva / nanu ca anyatra ete dviDA nirdizwAH
# de-dag #  ni mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi khams te / / de-dag #  ni zin-pa #  nyid do / / gzhan-las #  'di dag gnyis su ma bstan tam /
satyam nirdizwAH tatra hi atIta anAgatAH anupAtta uktAH te ca na santi eva
# bstan mod kyi de-la #  yang 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  ni zin-pa #  ma-yin-pa # r brjod de / / de ni med-pa #  nyid do /
na ca asatOpAtta tvam anupAt tatvam vA yujyate
# med-pa #  ni zin-pa # 'am ma-zin-pa #  yin par brjod du mi rung ngo /
vartamAnAH tusvasat tA aDyAsita tvAt citta cEttEH ca upAtta tvAt upAttAH eva cakzuH AdayaH na anupAttAH
# da-ltar #  ni rang yod-pa # r gnas-pa #  dang sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyis zin-pa # 'i phyir zin-pa #  nyid de / / mig la-sogs-pa #  ni ma-zin-pa #  ma yin no /
kim cakzuH AdayaH eva paQca upAttAH
# ci mig la-sogs-pa #  lnga po nyid zin-pa #  dag gang zhe na / / ma yin te /
na kim tarhi caturNAm ca pradeSaH / katamezAMcaturNAm iti atra Aha rUpa rasa ganDa sprazwavyAnAm iti
# bzhi'i phyogs te / / bzhi-po #  de-dag #  gang yin snyam pa la de'i-phyir #  / / gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg-bya #  rnams kyi'o zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tatra ye / srUpa ganDa rasa sprazwavya DAtavaH indriya vinirBAga vartinaH te indriya vat upAttAH
# de-la #  gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg-bya # 'i khams dbang-po #  las tha dad du mi-'jug-pa #  gang dag yin pa de-dag #  dbang-po #  dag bzhin-du #  zin-pa #  rnams so / / gzhan dag ni ma-zin-pa #  dag ste /
anye anupAttAH tat yaTA mUla varjyezu keSa roma naKa dantezu viz mUtra Kewa siFGANaka SoNita Adizu BUmi udaka Adizu ca
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / drung ma-gtogs-pa # 'i skra dang spu dang sen-mo #  dang so dang phyi-sa-dang-gcin #  dang mchil-ma #  dang snabs dang khrag la-sogs-pa #  dang sa dang chu la-sogs-pa #  rnams so /
upAttam iti kaH arTaH / yat citta cEttEH aDizWAna BAvena upagRhItam anugraha upaGAtAByAm anyonya anuviDAnAt / yat lokesacetanam iti ucyate / kati anupAttAH
# zin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i don ci zhe na / / phan-pa #  dang gnod-pa #  gnyis kyis phan tshun rjes su 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir gang sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  de rnams kyis byin-gyis-brlabs-pa # 'i gnas-kyi-dngos-po # r zin-pa #  dang 'jig-rten #  na sems bcas-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / zin-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  du zhe na /
SezAH nava caturNAm ca / pradeSaH / upayukteByaH ye anye te SezAH / atas saptacitta DAtavaH DarmaDAtuH SabdaDAtuH ca
# lhag-ma #  dgu dang bzhi'i phyogs zhes-bya-ba #  ni bshad-zin #  pa rnams las gzhan gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  lhag-ma # 'o / / de'i-phyir #  sems kyi khams bdun dang chos-kyi-khams #  dang sgra'i khams so; /
caturNAm capradeSaH iti rUpa ganDa rasa sparSAnAm / sa punar yA indriyA vinirBAga vartinam BAgam sTApayitvA mUla varjyezu keSa roma Adizu vartate / kati saBAgAH / azwAdaSAnAm DAtUnAm iti prakRta tvAt / aBisambaDyate / tezAm ADyAtmikA iti
# bzhi'i phyogs zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg-pa #  rnams kyi'o / / de-yang #  dbang-po #  dang tha dad du mi-'jug-pa # 'i cha ma-gtogs-pa #  dang drung ma-gtogs-pa # 'i skra dang spu la-sogs-pa #  yod-pa # 'o / / sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  du zhe na / / khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin-pas #  der sbyar ro /
dvAdaSa ADyAtmikAH uktAH / tezAm na vijQAyate katame paQca iti atas Aha rUpiNA eti te punar cakzuH Srotra GrANa rasana sparSana DAtavaH
# nang gi gzugs-can #  lnga zhes-bya-ba #  ni nang gi bcu gnyis bstan-pa # s de-dag #  gi nang na gang-yin-pa #  gtol med-pa # s lnga zhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / gzugs-can #  zhes-bya-ba #  de-dag #  ni mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi khams so /
kasya saBAgAH kena prakAreNa saBAgAH iti na vijQAyate atas Aha sva vijQAnEH vizaya sAmAnya tAm upAdAya iti
# gang-gi #  sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  dang rnam-pa #  gang-gis #  sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  yang mi-shes-pa # s de'i-phyir #  / / rang-gi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  dag dang yul thun-mong-ba #  nyid kyi phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  smos so /
tatra cakzuzaH sva vijQAnam cakzuH vijQAnam
# de-la #  mig gi rang-gi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste /
tena sva vijQAnena cakzuH sva vizayeNa rUpeNa samAnam
# rang-gi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  de dang mig rang-gi-yul #  gzugs su mtshungs te /
dvayoH api cakzuH vijQAna utpattO= anuguNa tvAt samAnam
# gnyi-ga #  yang / / mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  skye-ba #  dang mthun-pa # 'i phyir mtshungs-pa # 'o /
sAmAnya tAm upAdAya iti gRhItvA cakzuH sva vizayeNa rUpeNa sa BAgam ucyate
# thun mong pa nyid kyi phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni bzung-ba #  ste / / mig gi rang-gi-yul #  gzugs dang sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
evam Srotra AdInAm api sva vizayEH saBA gatA vaktavyA
# de-bzhin-du #  rna-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  yang / / rang-gi-yul #  rnams dang sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  zhes brjod-pa # r bya'o /
etat uktam Bavati ye cakzuH AdayaH sva vijQAnEH aDyAsitAH tesa BAgAH / tat eva cakzuH AdayaH sva vijQAna SUnyAH / tad saBAgAH / kimarTam punar te tad saBAgAH iti ucyante / sva jAti sAmAnya tAm upAdAya iti
# de ni 'di-skad-du #  / / mig la-sogs-pa #  gang dag rang-gi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams dang gnas-pa #  de-dag #  sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro; / / de-dag #  dang mtshungs-pa #  du zhe na / / mig la-sogs-pa #  de-dag-nyid #  rang-gi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # s stong-pa-nyid #  de de-dag #  dang mtshungs-pa # 'o / / ci'i-phyir #  de-dag #  ni de-dag #  dang mtshungs-pa #  zhes bya zhe na / / rang-gi-rigs #  dang mthun-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ste /
sva vijQAna SUnyAH / cakzuH AdayaH te saBAgAnAm cakzuH AdInAm cakzuH Adi jAtyA samAnAH iti tEH sadRSa tvAt tad sa BAgAH iti ucyante / ete hi asADAraNa tvAt yaH ekasya saBAgAH tad sa BAgAH vA tesarva sattvAnAm api iti niyatam ezAm saBA gata tsaBAga tvam / rUpa AdInAm tu pratisantAne saBA gata tsaBAga tvam iti anavasTitam / na ca vijQAnAt anyat kAritram asti iti na anyeza aMsa BAga tad saBA ga tvam uktam / paQca skanDaka viBAzA samAptA / kRtiH AcArya sTira mateH
# rang-gi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  stong-pa # 'i mig la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  ni sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa # 'i mig la-sogs-pa #  dang mig la-sogs-pa # r ris-mthun-pa #  ste / / de-dag #  dang 'dra-ba # 'i phyir de-dag #  dang mtshungs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de-dag #  ni thun-mong-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir gcig gi sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  dang de-dag #  dang mtshungs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni / / sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi yang yin-pas #  / / 'di dag gi sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  dang de-dag #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ni nges-pa # 'o / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  ni so-so # 'i rgyud la sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  dang de-dag #  dang mtshungs-pa #  nyid-du #  gnas so / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  las-byed-pa #  gzhan med-pa # 'i phyir / / gzhan dag la ni sten-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  de-dang-de-dag #  dang mtshungs-pa #  zhes ma brjod do / / phung-po #  lnga'i rab tu byed-pa #  bye-brag #  tu bshad-pa #  / / slob-dpon #  blo-gros #  brtan-pa #  sthi ra ma tis mdzad-pa #  rdzogs so /
